
-----title
射洪 (出生地)

href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=659&endYear=659')">659年</a>　是年子昂生于四川梓州。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=660&endYear=675')">660-675年</a>　居乡。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=676&endYear=676')">676年</a>　年少以富家子驰侠使气，至此始慨然立志，闭门谢客，发愤读书。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=677&endYear=677')">677年</a>　居家闭门读书。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=678&endYear=678')">678年</a>　居家闭门读书，该览百家，专精坟典。<br /><a ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=683&endYear=683')">683年</a>　隐居射洪，随父研习黄老，幽观星象，辟谷饵食，求仙学道，与僧道游。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=683&endYear=683')">683年</a>　隐居射洪，春游金华观，有诗叙神仙之兴。作品：《春日登金华观》<span class='inlineComment2'>（金华观，即玉京观。《舆地纪胜》卷一百五十四：“玉京观，在射洪县北金华山上……有老君像，唐明皇所铸。有陈拾遗读书堂、刘蜕诗及卢藏用《祭文》。”《新修潼川府志》卷六：“玉京观在射洪县北金华山，本名金华观，宋治平二年赐名玉京。”）</span><div id='poem_34670' class='_poem'><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_1_34732'>纷群翠之鸿溶，又似蓬瀛海水之周流。<div id='poem_sentence_1_34732_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_2_34732'>信夫人之好道，爱云山以<span class='link' id='poem_sentence_3_34732'></div><div id='poem_sentence_3_34732_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=683&endYear=683')">683年4月</a>　隐居射洪，与左近真谛寺晖上人游，四月于寺内作序饯别齐少府入京。作品：《晖上人房饯齐少府使入京府序》<span class='inlineComment2'>（上人，对和尚的尊称。齐少府，名未详。《射洪县志》卷二载，晖上人房在真谛寺内，寺处“县东七里武东山下，陈子昂故宅在其左，有晖上人者，子昂时与之往还”。）</span><div id='poem_1364537' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1364537' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1364537?labeling=true' target='_blank'>晖上人房饯齐少府使入京府序</a><span class='authorDate'>（683年4月）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 唐初 · </span><a class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1364537'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1364537'>永淳二年。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1364537_comment'></div>四月孟夏。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1364537_comment'></div>东海齐子。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1364537_comment'></div>宦于此州。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1364537_comment'></div>虽黄绶位轻。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1364537_comment'></div>而青云器重。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1364537_comment'></div>故能委邦君而坐啸。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1364537_comment'></div>屈刺史而知名。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1364537_comment'></div>属乎銮驾巡方。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1364537_comment'></div>诸侯纳贡。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1364537_comment'></div>将欲对扬天子。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1364537_comment'></div>命我行人。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1364537_comment'></div>执玉帛而当朝。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1364537_comment'></div>拥騑骖而戒道。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1364537_comment'></div>指途河渭。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1364537_comment'></div>发引岷嵎。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1364537_comment'></div>粤以丙丁之日。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_16_1364537_comment'></div>次于晖公别舍。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_17_1364537_comment'></div>盖言离也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_18_1364537_comment'></div>尔其岩泉列坐。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_19_1364537_comment'></div>竹树交筵。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_20_1364537_comment'></div>吐青蔼于轩窗。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_21_1364537_comment'></div>栖白云于左右。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_22_1364537_comment'></div>参差池榭。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_23_1364537_comment'></div>乱山水之清阴。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_24_1364537_comment'></div>缭绕阶庭。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_25_1364537_comment'></div>杂峰崖之异势。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_26_1364537_comment'></div>入<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_27_1364537", 1364537, "Clauses/27/Comments/0")'>禅林</span>而避暑。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_27_1364537_comment'></div>肃风景于中林。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_28_1364537_comment'></div>开水殿而追凉。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_29_1364537_comment'></div>彻氛埃于户外。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_30_1364537_comment'></div>瑶琴合奏。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_31_1364537_comment'></div>翠斝时行。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_32_1364537_comment'></div>谭窈窕于天人。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_33_1364537_comment'></div>极留连于晷刻。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_34_1364537_comment'></div>既而欢乐极。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_35_1364537_comment'></div>良辰征。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_36_1364537_comment'></div>攀白日而不回。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_37_1364537_comment'></div>唱浮云而告别。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_38_1364537_comment'></div>山光黯黯。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_39_1364537_comment'></div>凝绿树之将曛。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_40_1364537_comment'></div>岚气沈沈。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_41_1364537_comment'></div>结苍云而遂晚。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_42_1364537_comment'></div>虽<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_43_1364537", 1364537, "Clauses/43/Comments/0")'>同交</span>未阻。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_43_1364537_comment'></div>风月可留。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_44_1364537_comment'></div>岐路方乖。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_45_1364537_comment'></div>关山成恨。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_46_1364537_comment'></div>嗟乎。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_47_1364537_comment'></div>朝廷子入。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_48_1364537_comment'></div>期富贵于<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_49_1364537", 1364537, "Clauses/49/Comments/0")'>崇朝</span>。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_49_1364537_comment'></div>林岭吾栖。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_50_1364537_comment'></div>学神仙而未毕。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_51_1364537_comment'></div><span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_52_1364537", 1364537, "Clauses/52/Comments/0")'>青霞</span>路绝。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_52_1364537_comment'></div><span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_53_1364537", 1364537, "Clauses/53/Comments/0")'>朱绂</span>途遥。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_53_1364537_comment'></div>言此会之何时。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_54_1364537_comment'></div>愿相逢而谁代。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_55_1364537_comment'></div>永怀千古。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_56_1364537_comment'></div>岂知仁者之交。<div ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=683&endYear=683')">683年</a>　隐居射洪，荆州府崔兵曹奉使至，子昂与宴，作诗并序。作品：《秋日遇荆州府崔兵曹使宴并序》<span class='inlineComment2'>（崔兵曹，名未详。）</span><div id='poem_34711' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_34711' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/34711?labeling=true' target='_blank'>秋日遇荆州府崔兵曹使宴</a><span class='authorDate'>（683年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 唐初 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(20887, "唐初", "陈子昂", "poem_title_34711")'>陈子昂</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'>五言排律</div></div><div id='poem_title_34711_comment'></div><div class='titleComment' id='poem_preface_34711'>若夫尊卑位隔，荣贱途分，使卿士大夫，倚轩裳而傲物，山栖木食，负林壑而骄人，未能有屈富贵于沈冥，杂薜萝于簪芴。天人坐契，相从云雾之游；风雨不疲，高纵琴樽之赏。崔兵曹紫庭公胄，青云贵人，以钟鼎不足以致奇才，烟霞可以交名士。皇华昭国，怀凤綍而高寻；白桂追游，邀兔罝而下顾。大矣哉，生平未识，一见而交道遂存，此日披怀，千载之风期坐合。支道林之雅论，妙理沈微，崔子玉之雄才，斯文未丧，属乎金龙掌气。石雁惊秋，天泬寥而烟日无光，野寂寞而山川变色，芸其黄矣。悲白露于苍葭，木叶落兮，惨红霜于绿野，尔其高兴洽。芳酒阑，顿羲和而不留，顾华堂而欲晚。长歌何托，思传稽古之文，爰命小人。率记当时之事，人探一字，六韵成篇。</div><div id='poem_preface_34711_comment'></div><div class='titleComment' id='poem_allusion_34711'><span class='label'>引用典故：</span><span class='link' onclick='ShowAllusionComment(2005, class='inline' id='poem_sentence_36_1364546_comment'></div>祖德于。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_37_1364546_comment'></div>北齐著作郎。<div class='inline' "Clauses/40/Comments/1")'>芸扃</span><span class='inlineComment2'>（一作编）</span>睹奥。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_40_1364546_comment'></div>见天下之图。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_41_1364546_comment'></div>石桂闻琴。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_42_1364546_comment'></div>知君子之化。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_43_1364546_comment'></div>父安寿。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_44_1364546_comment'></div>皇朝尚衣直长怀州司马豪<span class='inlineComment2'>（一作濠）</span>州刺史湖州刺史。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_45_1364546_comment'></div>良二千石。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_46_1364546_comment'></div>闻乎共理之尊。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_47_1364546_comment'></div>肇十二州。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_48_1364546_comment'></div>荣多刺举之首。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_49_1364546_comment'></div>公则使君第某子也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_50_1364546_comment'></div>冲和诞命。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_51_1364546_comment'></div>光大含章。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_52_1364546_comment'></div>实公侯之子孙。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_53_1364546_comment'></div>有山河之气象。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_54_1364546_comment'></div>明不外饰。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_55_1364546_comment'></div>默昭于元机。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_56_1364546_comment'></div>敏实内融。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_57_1364546_comment'></div>养蒙于用晦。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_58_1364546_comment'></div>故其廉不直物。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_59_1364546_comment'></div>恕不由衷。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_60_1364546_comment'></div>崇善足以利仁。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_61_1364546_comment'></div>自彊足以从事。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_62_1364546_comment'></div>有朋友之信焉。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_63_1364546_comment'></div>有闺门之肃焉。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_64_1364546_comment'></div>非夫恭人。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_65_1364546_comment'></div>其孰能景行行之者也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_66_1364546_comment'></div>年始若干。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_67_1364546_comment'></div>为国子生。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_68_1364546_comment'></div>言从太学之游。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_69_1364546_comment'></div>以观先王之道。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_70_1364546_comment'></div>某年以明经擢第。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_71_1364546_comment'></div>解褐守恒州参军。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_72_1364546_comment'></div>秩满。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_73_1364546_comment'></div>补许州司法参军。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_74_1364546_comment'></div>许惟旧国。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_75_1364546_comment'></div>陈实多巫。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_76_1364546_comment'></div>君子<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_77_1364546", 1364546, "Clauses/77/Comments/0")'>丰明</span>。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_77_1364546_comment'></div>利用乎狱。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_78_1364546_comment'></div>载以课最。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_79_1364546_comment'></div>累加秩焉。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_80_1364546_comment'></div>又转洺州司兵参军。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_81_1364546_comment'></div>丛台袨服。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_82_1364546_comment'></div>一旦成市。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_83_1364546_comment'></div>非利器者。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_84_1364546_comment'></div>政以多荒。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_85_1364546_comment'></div>公实佐之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_86_1364546_comment'></div>官无留事。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_87_1364546_comment'></div>信矣乎。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_88_1364546_comment'></div>能其理者有其任。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_89_1364546_comment'></div>济其业者享其功。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_90_1364546_comment'></div>我岂蒙求。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_91_1364546_comment'></div>物思其理。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_92_1364546_comment'></div>某年选补临邛县令。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_93_1364546_comment'></div>夫蜀都<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_94_1364546", 1364546, "Clauses/94/Comments/0")'>天府之国</span>。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_94_1364546_comment'></div>金城铁冶。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_95_1364546_comment'></div>而俗以财雄。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_96_1364546_comment'></div>弋猎田池。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_97_1364546_comment'></div>而士多豪侈。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_98_1364546_comment'></div>此邦之政。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_99_1364546_comment'></div>旧难其人。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_100_1364546_comment'></div>公按辔清途。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_101_1364546_comment'></div>下车而宰。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_102_1364546_comment'></div>览其谣俗。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_103_1364546_comment'></div>永叹于良图。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_104_1364546_comment'></div>想其风流。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_105_1364546_comment'></div>慨然于惠化。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_106_1364546_comment'></div>以为太上之理。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_107_1364546_comment'></div>因人者也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_108_1364546_comment'></div>通变之机。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_109_1364546_comment'></div>随时者也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_110_1364546_comment'></div>必使无讼。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_111_1364546_comment'></div>不亦由吾。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_112_1364546_comment'></div>用乎利贞。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_113_1364546_comment'></div>夫何在物。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_114_1364546_comment'></div>于是谋其教令。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_115_1364546_comment'></div>肃其仪刑。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_116_1364546_comment'></div>敬其事以顺其人。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_117_1364546_comment'></div>正其文以利其义。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_118_1364546_comment'></div>以为昔者圣人之务本也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_119_1364546_comment'></div>在乎稼穑。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_120_1364546_comment'></div>有稼穑然后可以养人。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_121_1364546_comment'></div>故公之劝人也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_122_1364546_comment'></div>用天之道。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_123_1364546_comment'></div>分地之利。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_124_1364546_comment'></div>以为昔者圣人之利用也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_125_1364546_comment'></div>实在财货。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_126_1364546_comment'></div>有财货然后可以聚人。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_127_1364546_comment'></div>故公之<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_128_1364546", 1364546, "Clauses/128/Comments/0")'>化居</span>也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_128_1364546_comment'></div>贸迁有无。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_129_1364546_comment'></div>和其众寡。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_130_1364546_comment'></div>以为昔者圣人之事生也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_131_1364546_comment'></div>谨其制度。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_132_1364546_comment'></div>然后可以富。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_133_1364546_comment'></div>故公之节用。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_134_1364546_comment'></div>饮食有节。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_135_1364546_comment'></div>车服有数。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_136_1364546_comment'></div>以为昔者圣人之事死也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_137_1364546_comment'></div>慎其丧祭。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_138_1364546_comment'></div>有丧祭然后可以睦人。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_139_1364546_comment'></div>故公之送死也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_140_1364546_comment'></div>葬之以礼。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_141_1364546_comment'></div>祭之以礼。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_142_1364546_comment'></div>以为昔者圣人之用狱也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_143_1364546_comment'></div>崇其法制。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_144_1364546_comment'></div>有法制然后可以禁人。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_145_1364546_comment'></div>故公之恤刑也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_146_1364546_comment'></div>唯齐非齐。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_147_1364546_comment'></div>有伦有要。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_148_1364546_comment'></div>夫如是者。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_149_1364546_comment'></div>岂苟其利哉。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_150_1364546_comment'></div>唯欲洁乎其源。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_151_1364546_comment'></div>正乎其本。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_152_1364546_comment'></div>慎之于谋始。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_153_1364546_comment'></div>要之于用终。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_154_1364546_comment'></div>将使敚𭤑矫虔而是以息。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_155_1364546_comment'></div>孤寡不谷而是以宁者哉。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_156_1364546_comment'></div>夫然后磨之以仁。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_157_1364546_comment'></div>琢之以义。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_158_1364546_comment'></div>使男女异路。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_159_1364546_comment'></div>班白不提。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_160_1364546_comment'></div>熙乎其若春。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_161_1364546_comment'></div>肃乎其若神。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_162_1364546_comment'></div>然后文以礼乐。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_163_1364546_comment'></div>几乎以淳朴。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_164_1364546_comment'></div>道岂远乎。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_165_1364546_comment'></div>呜呼。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_166_1364546_comment'></div>昊天不悦。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_167_1364546_comment'></div>降此荼毒。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_168_1364546_comment'></div>某年以太夫人忧去职。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_169_1364546_comment'></div>于时公之莅。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_170_1364546_comment'></div>始逾年矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_171_1364546_comment'></div>然三载考绩。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_172_1364546_comment'></div>是用未成。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_173_1364546_comment'></div>百姓哀惶。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_174_1364546_comment'></div>人吏嗟咨。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_175_1364546_comment'></div>咸云我父去矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_176_1364546_comment'></div>而人悴矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_177_1364546_comment'></div><span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_178_1364546", 1364546, "Clauses/178/Comments/0")'>乡望</span>老人前某官等五百馀人。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_183_1364546_comment'></div>诉之上官。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_184_1364546_comment'></div>冀夺其哀。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_185_1364546_comment'></div>摧礼终秩。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_186_1364546_comment'></div>不谋而同者日有百数。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_187_1364546_comment'></div>司马元公。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_188_1364546_comment'></div>帝王之裔也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_189_1364546_comment'></div>康歌协化。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_190_1364546_comment'></div>盛德在人。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_191_1364546_comment'></div>悯烝庶之求思。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_192_1364546_comment'></div>嘉我君之懿绩。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_193_1364546_comment'></div>以为古之借寇者何以踰是哉。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_194_1364546_comment'></div>遂用畴咨旧章。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_195_1364546_comment'></div>允怀氓诵。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_196_1364546_comment'></div>夺之公礼。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_197_1364546_comment'></div>上之于<span class='inline' id='poem_sentence_199_1364546_comment'></div>慰彼黎庶。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_200_1364546_comment'></div>君子之教。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_201_1364546_comment'></div>而日见之哉。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_202_1364546_comment'></div>班白之老。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_203_1364546_comment'></div>胥吏之徒。<div id='poem_sentence_207_1364546_comment'></div>谁其嗣之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_208_1364546_comment'></div>千馀人复连表诣阙投匦。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_209_1364546_comment'></div>乞君以墨缞从事。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_210_1364546_comment'></div>遑遑焉若有望而未至也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_211_1364546_comment'></div><span id='poem_sentence_215_1364546_comment'></div>乃相与言曰。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_216_1364546_comment'></div>昔者君子思其人而爱其树。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_217_1364546_comment'></div>蒙其泽则歌其诗。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_218_1364546_comment'></div>封君之仁。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_219_1364546_comment'></div>我无金石乎。<div id='poem_sentence_223_1364546_comment'></div>刀笔之能。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_224_1364546_comment'></div>永思清风。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_225_1364546_comment'></div>叹息仁化。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_226_1364546_comment'></div>尉安定梁慎盈。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_227_1364546_comment'></div>知名之士也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_228_1364546_comment'></div>墨妙几于草圣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_229_1364546_comment'></div>文义总于辞雄。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_230_1364546_comment'></div>昔仕京畿。<div id='poem_sentence_233_1364546_comment'></div>承封君之德有年矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_234_1364546_comment'></div>夫其忠信之教。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_235_1364546_comment'></div>宽猛之机。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_236_1364546_comment'></div>古之官人。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_237_1364546_comment'></div>君其<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_238_1364546", 1364546, "Clauses/238/Comments/0")'>殆庶</span>乎。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_238_1364546_comment'></div>父老之请允矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_239_1364546_comment'></div>余朅来旧国。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_240_1364546_comment'></div>传据其实。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_241_1364546_comment'></div>恭闻其去思。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_242_1364546_comment'></div>而亲睹其遗爱。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_243_1364546_comment'></div>余所备者。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_244_1364546_comment'></div>敢述斯文。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_245_1364546_comment'></div>犹惧后生有言。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_246_1364546_comment'></div>以为口实。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_247_1364546_comment'></div>河东薛稷。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_248_1364546_comment'></div>隋内史公之孙也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_249_1364546_comment'></div>文章之伯。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_250_1364546_comment'></div>而时所宗。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_251_1364546_comment'></div>故凭其实录。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_252_1364546_comment'></div>寄之为颂。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_253_1364546_comment'></div>其词曰。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_254_1364546_comment'></div></div><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_255_1364546'>天地之閒。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_255_1364546_comment'></div>有渤海焉。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_256_1364546_comment'></div>伯宗伯谷。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_257_1364546_comment'></div>神山在焉。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_34779_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_10_34779'></div><div id='poem_sentence_10_34779_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=693&endYear=693')">693年</a>　居蜀守制，友许州参军李崇嗣使蜀，过梓州，子昂于晖上人房饯宴赠别并序。作品：《夏日晖上人房别李参军崇嗣并序》<div id='poem_34745' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_34745' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/34745?labeling=true' target='_blank'>夏日晖上人房别李参军崇嗣<span class='inlineComment2'>（并序。序内缺二字）</span></a><span class='authorDate'>（693年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 唐初 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(20887, "唐初", "陈子昂", "poem_title_34745")'>陈子昂</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_34745_comment'></div><div class='titleComment' id='poem_preface_34745'>考察天人，旁罗变动。东西南北，贤圣不能定其居；寒署晦明，阴阳不能革其数，莫不云离雨散，奔驰于宇宙之间，宋远燕遥，泣别于关山之际。自古来矣，李参军白云英胄，紫气仙人，爱江海而高寻，顿风尘而未息，来从许下，月旦出于龙泉，言入蜀中，星文见于牛斗，野亭相遇，逆旅承欢，谢鲲之山水暂开，乐广之云天自乐。思道林而不见，怅若有亡，诣祇树而从游，□然旧款，高僧展袂，大士临筵。披□路之天书，坐琉璃之宝地，帘帷后辟，拂鹦鹉之香林，栏槛前开，照芙蓉之绿水。讨论儒墨，探览真玄，觉周孔之犹迹（觉周孔之犹迷），知老庄之未晤（知老庄之未悟），遂欲高攀宝座，伏奏金仙，开不二之法门，观大千之世界。欢娱恍晚，离别行催，红霞生而白日归，青气凝而碧山暮，骊歌断引，抗手将辞，江汉浩浩而长流，天地居然而不动。嗟乎！色为何色，悲观忽而因生，谁去谁来，离会纷而妄作，俗之迷也，不亦烦乎？各述所怀，不拘章韵。</div><div id='poem_preface_34745_comment'></div><div class='titleComment' id='poem_allusion_34745'><span class='label'>引用典故：</span><span class='link' onclick='ShowAllusionComment(4889, "poem_allusion_34745")'>金台</span>　<span class='link' onclick='ShowAllusionComment(9843, "poem_allusion_34745")'>一十三死生</span></div><div id='poem_allusion_34745_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_34745'><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_34745'>四十九变化，<span class='link' onclick='ShowAllusionComment(9843, "poem_sentence_0_34745")'>一十三死生</span>。<div id='poem_sentence_0_34745_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_1_34745'>翕忽玄黄里，驱驰风雨情。<div id='poem_sentence_1_34745_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_2_34745'>是非纷妄作，<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_2_34745", 34745, "Clauses/5/Comments/0")'>宠辱</span>坐相惊。<div id='poem_sentence_2_34745_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_3_34745'>至人独幽鉴<span class='inlineComment2'>（一作览）</span>，窈窕随昏明。<div id='poem_sentence_3_34745_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_4_34745'>咫尺山河道，轩窗日月庭。<div id='poem_sentence_4_34745_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_8_34745'>户牖观天地，阶基上杳冥。<div id='poem_sentence_8_34745_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_9_34745'>自超三界乐，安知万里征。<div id='poem_sentence_9_34745_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_10_34745'>中国要荒内，人寰宇宙荣。<div id='poem_sentence_10_34745_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_11_34745'>弦望如朝夕，宁嗟蜀道行。<div id='poem_sentence_11_34745_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_12_34745'></div><div id='poem_sentence_12_34745_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=693&endYear=693')">693年</a>　居蜀守制，为叔祖陈嗣入葬撰碑文。作品：《梓州射洪县武东山故居士陈君碑》<span class='inlineComment2'>（陈嗣，子昂叔祖。）</span><div id='poem_1364545' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1364545' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1364545?labeling=true' target='_blank'>梓州射洪县武东山故居士陈君碑</a><span class='authorDate'>（693年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 唐初 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(20887, "唐初", class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1364545'>君讳嗣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1364545_comment'></div>字宏嗣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1364545_comment'></div>其先陈国人也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1364545_comment'></div>汉末沦丧。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1364545_comment'></div>八代祖祗。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1364545_comment'></div>自汝南仕蜀为尚书令。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1364545_comment'></div>其后蜀为晋所灭。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1364545_comment'></div>子孙避晋不仕。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1364545_comment'></div>居涪南武东山。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1364545_comment'></div>与唐胡白赵五姓置立新城郡。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1364545_comment'></div>剖制二县。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1364545_comment'></div>而四姓宗之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1364545_comment'></div>代为郡长。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1364545_comment'></div>萧齐之末。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1364545_comment'></div>有太平者。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1364545_comment'></div>兄弟三人。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1364545_comment'></div>为郡豪杰。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_16_1364545_comment'></div>梁武帝受禅。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_17_1364545_comment'></div>网罗英豪。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_18_1364545_comment'></div>拜太平为新城郡守。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_19_1364545_comment'></div>寻加本州别驾。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_20_1364545_comment'></div>弟太乐太蒙。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_21_1364545_comment'></div>蒙为黎州长史都督护南梁二郡太守。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_22_1364545_comment'></div>乐为本郡司马。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_23_1364545_comment'></div>即君之高祖父也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_24_1364545_comment'></div>生曾祖方庆。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_25_1364545_comment'></div>好道。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_26_1364545_comment'></div>不乐为仕。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_27_1364545_comment'></div>得墨子五行秘书。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_28_1364545_comment'></div>而隐于武东山。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_29_1364545_comment'></div>生烈祖汤。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_30_1364545_comment'></div>汤仕郡为主簿。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_31_1364545_comment'></div>遇梁季丧乱。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_32_1364545_comment'></div>避时不仕。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_33_1364545_comment'></div>生皇考广迥。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_34_1364545_comment'></div>迥早卒。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_35_1364545_comment'></div>君即迥之第二子也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_36_1364545_comment'></div>少孤而有纯德。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_37_1364545_comment'></div>恭己饰行。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_38_1364545_comment'></div>一日三省。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_39_1364545_comment'></div>家代本以清白崇德。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_40_1364545_comment'></div>迨君之孤。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_41_1364545_comment'></div>素业空矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_42_1364545_comment'></div>君有仁兄。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_43_1364545_comment'></div>养母以孝。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_44_1364545_comment'></div>君克顺至行。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_45_1364545_comment'></div>同勤苦节。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_46_1364545_comment'></div>夏不避暑。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_47_1364545_comment'></div>冬不避寒。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_48_1364545_comment'></div>蒸蒸服事。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_49_1364545_comment'></div>行年四十有五。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_50_1364545_comment'></div>入则孝。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_51_1364545_comment'></div>出则弟。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_52_1364545_comment'></div>谨而信。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_53_1364545_comment'></div>汎爱众而亲仁。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_54_1364545_comment'></div>无馀力也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_55_1364545_comment'></div>以是不忧于道。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_56_1364545_comment'></div>逮亲终殁。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_57_1364545_comment'></div>春秋巳高。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_58_1364545_comment'></div>从事不可以养矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_59_1364545_comment'></div>乃辍干禄之学。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_60_1364545_comment'></div>修养生之道。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_61_1364545_comment'></div>山壑高居。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_62_1364545_comment'></div>农野永岁。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_63_1364545_comment'></div>雅闻汉有王丹者。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_64_1364545_comment'></div>放居不仕。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_65_1364545_comment'></div>家累千金以自奉。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_66_1364545_comment'></div>田稼勤者。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_67_1364545_comment'></div>载酒肴从之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_68_1364545_comment'></div>乡里承化。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_69_1364545_comment'></div>以相惩沮。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_70_1364545_comment'></div>乃叹曰。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_71_1364545_comment'></div>彼王丹者。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_72_1364545_comment'></div>是为政矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_73_1364545_comment'></div>奚其为政也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_74_1364545_comment'></div>由是始考林泽。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_75_1364545_comment'></div>辟良田。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_76_1364545_comment'></div>习山书。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_77_1364545_comment'></div>务农政。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_78_1364545_comment'></div>天道时变。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_79_1364545_comment'></div>地道化成。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_80_1364545_comment'></div>邱陵泉薮。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_81_1364545_comment'></div>星岁云物。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_82_1364545_comment'></div>靡不用心也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_83_1364545_comment'></div>原田莓莓。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_84_1364545_comment'></div>黍稷漠漠。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_85_1364545_comment'></div>汶阳之稼如云矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_86_1364545_comment'></div>春日载华。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_87_1364545_comment'></div>岁聿其秋。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_88_1364545_comment'></div>白露时降。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_89_1364545_comment'></div>百谷<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_90_1364545", 1364545, "Clauses/90/Comments/0")'>收熟</span>。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_90_1364545_comment'></div>君常乘肩舆。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_91_1364545_comment'></div>省农夫。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_92_1364545_comment'></div>馈田畯。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_93_1364545_comment'></div>刑以肃惰。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_94_1364545_comment'></div>悦以劳勤。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_95_1364545_comment'></div>若孙吴之用兵。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_96_1364545_comment'></div>鸷鸟之搏击也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_97_1364545_comment'></div>卓彼甫田。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_98_1364545_comment'></div>岁取十千。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_99_1364545_comment'></div>仓库实。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_100_1364545_comment'></div>崇礼节。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_101_1364545_comment'></div>恤茕寡。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_102_1364545_comment'></div>赈穷乏。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_103_1364545_comment'></div>九族以亲之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_104_1364545_comment'></div>乡党以欢之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_105_1364545_comment'></div>居十馀年。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_106_1364545_comment'></div>家累千金矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_107_1364545_comment'></div>其邻国有媮衣食。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_108_1364545_comment'></div>带刀剑。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_109_1364545_comment'></div>推埋胠箧之类。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_110_1364545_comment'></div>斗鸡走狗之豪。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_111_1364545_comment'></div>莫不靡下风。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_112_1364545_comment'></div>驯素节。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_113_1364545_comment'></div>曰里有仁焉。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_114_1364545_comment'></div>吾何从之也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_115_1364545_comment'></div>遂顿浮窳之节。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_116_1364545_comment'></div>肃恭俭之规。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_117_1364545_comment'></div>修孝悌。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_118_1364545_comment'></div>饰廉耻。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_119_1364545_comment'></div>将欲效君之素业也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_120_1364545_comment'></div>君时年巳耳顺。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_121_1364545_comment'></div>素无经世之情。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_122_1364545_comment'></div>林园遗老。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_123_1364545_comment'></div>元默忘岁。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_124_1364545_comment'></div>遂保先君武东山之故居。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_125_1364545_comment'></div>行不由径。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_126_1364545_comment'></div>非公事未尝至于州县也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_127_1364545_comment'></div>昔襄阳有庞德公。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_128_1364545_comment'></div>谷口有郑子真。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_129_1364545_comment'></div>东海王霸。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_130_1364545_comment'></div>西山蜀才。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_131_1364545_comment'></div>皆避人养德。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_132_1364545_comment'></div>退耕求志。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_133_1364545_comment'></div>轩冕不可得而羁。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_134_1364545_comment'></div>忧患不可得而累。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_135_1364545_comment'></div>逮于我君。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_136_1364545_comment'></div>作者五人矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_137_1364545_comment'></div>于戏。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_138_1364545_comment'></div>古者至人。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_139_1364545_comment'></div>不利苟得。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_140_1364545_comment'></div>不务近贵。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_141_1364545_comment'></div>量腹而食。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_142_1364545_comment'></div>度身而衣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_143_1364545_comment'></div>非其道。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_144_1364545_comment'></div>万钟不足丰也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_145_1364545_comment'></div>非其荣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_146_1364545_comment'></div>五鼎不足饪也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_147_1364545_comment'></div>躬勤耕稼。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_148_1364545_comment'></div>植其杖而耘。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_149_1364545_comment'></div>不荅子路之问者。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_150_1364545_comment'></div>岂我君之徒与。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_151_1364545_comment'></div>绵绵罗网。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_152_1364545_comment'></div>冥冥高鸿。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_153_1364545_comment'></div><span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_154_1364545", 1364545, "Clauses/154/Comments/0")'>趯趯</span>竹竿。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_154_1364545_comment'></div>穆穆幽龙。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_155_1364545_comment'></div>其与祸败之辽绝如胡越哉。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_156_1364545_comment'></div>然则两龚不免于兰焚。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_157_1364545_comment'></div>二老不免于薇叹。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_158_1364545_comment'></div>其近贵利邪。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_159_1364545_comment'></div>夫上无忧悔。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_160_1364545_comment'></div>下无饥寒。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_161_1364545_comment'></div>含道以制嗜欲。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_162_1364545_comment'></div>达命以顺生死。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_163_1364545_comment'></div>仁以爱身。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_164_1364545_comment'></div>智以养德。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_165_1364545_comment'></div>俾尔耆而艾。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_166_1364545_comment'></div>俾尔昌而炽。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_167_1364545_comment'></div>君子保之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_168_1364545_comment'></div>以永寿考。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_169_1364545_comment'></div>非我君者乎。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_170_1364545_comment'></div>享年八十有五。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_171_1364545_comment'></div>太岁壬辰五月十三日。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_172_1364545_comment'></div>考终厥命。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_173_1364545_comment'></div>临终戒曰。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_174_1364545_comment'></div>启子足。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_175_1364545_comment'></div>启子手。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_176_1364545_comment'></div>吾闻古人有言。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_177_1364545_comment'></div>珠玉而瘗之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_178_1364545_comment'></div>是暴骸于中原也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_179_1364545_comment'></div>古者不封不树。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_180_1364545_comment'></div>后代圣人易之以棺椁。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_181_1364545_comment'></div>吾不敢违圣人。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_182_1364545_comment'></div>可具棺椁而已。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_183_1364545_comment'></div>敛以常服。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_184_1364545_comment'></div>坟无邱陇。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_185_1364545_comment'></div>吾将庶几以奉先人之清业也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_186_1364545_comment'></div>有子某等。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_187_1364545_comment'></div>皆能祗奉遗训。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_188_1364545_comment'></div>聿从先志。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_189_1364545_comment'></div>长寿二年龙集癸巳某月某朔日。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_190_1364545_comment'></div>元月载踰。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_191_1364545_comment'></div>卜兆时吉。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_192_1364545_comment'></div>始启殡昭告。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_193_1364545_comment'></div>奉迁于旧茔武东山之阳。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_194_1364545_comment'></div>礼也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_195_1364545_comment'></div>乡里会葬者千馀人。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_196_1364545_comment'></div>皆涕泣号慕。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_197_1364545_comment'></div>悲纯德之不见。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_198_1364545_comment'></div>咸曰。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_199_1364545_comment'></div>君子没矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_200_1364545_comment'></div>仁何以名。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_201_1364545_comment'></div>陵谷不朽。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_202_1364545_comment'></div>匪唯颂声。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_203_1364545_comment'></div>小子不敏。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_204_1364545_comment'></div>谨述乡人之教。<div id='poem_sentence_207_1364545'>肃肃我祖。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_207_1364545_comment'></div>国始于陈。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_208_1364545_comment'></div>中裔沦丧。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_209_1364545_comment'></div>洎此江滨。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_210_1364545_comment'></div>山川<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_211_1364545", 1364545, "Clauses/211/Comments/0")'>隆郁</span>。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_211_1364545_comment'></div>旂鼎氛氲。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_212_1364545_comment'></div>生我君子。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_213_1364545_comment'></div>于铄元真。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_214_1364545_comment'></div>惟孝肃悌。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_215_1364545_comment'></div>惟仁善邻。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_216_1364545_comment'></div>乐我耕稼。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_217_1364545_comment'></div>忘我搢绅。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_218_1364545_comment'></div>茫茫田薮。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_219_1364545_comment'></div>岁也其春。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_220_1364545_comment'></div>农人肃事。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_221_1364545_comment'></div>君子犒勤。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_222_1364545_comment'></div>孰为夫子。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_223_1364545_comment'></div>植杖而耘。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_224_1364545_comment'></div>弋者何慕。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_225_1364545_comment'></div>鸿飞高云。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_226_1364545_comment'></div>楚狂惧殆。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_227_1364545_comment'></div>夷叔求仁。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_228_1364545_comment'></div>良时<span class='inlineComment2'>（一作图）</span>终矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_229_1364545_comment'></div>不考于身。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_230_1364545_comment'></div>我异于是。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_231_1364545_comment'></div>非隐非沦。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_232_1364545_comment'></div>抚化随运。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_233_1364545_comment'></div>安排屈伸。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_234_1364545_comment'></div>大年既没。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_235_1364545_comment'></div>长夜何辰。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_236_1364545_comment'></div>圣达不免。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_237_1364545_comment'></div>宇宙同尘。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_238_1364545_comment'></div>桐棺三寸。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_239_1364545_comment'></div>岂我窭贫。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_240_1364545_comment'></div>自古有死。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_241_1364545_comment'></div>吾从圣人。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_242_1364545_comment'></div>嗟尔百代。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_243_1364545_comment'></div>子子孙孙。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_244_1364545_comment'></div>骄奢自咎。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_245_1364545_comment'></div>天道无亲。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_246_1364545_comment'></div>思我松柏。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_247_1364545_comment'></div>恭俭是遵。</div><div id='poem_sentence_248_1364545_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=693&endYear=693')">693年</a>　居蜀守制，时郭震在梓州通泉尉任，其姬薛氏卒，子昂为撰墓志。作品：《馆陶郭公姬薛氏墓志铭》<div id='poem_1364560' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1364560' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1364560?labeling=true' target='_blank'>馆陶郭公姬薛氏墓志铭</a><span class='authorDate'>（693年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 唐初 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(20887, "唐初", "陈子昂", "poem_title_1364560")'>陈子昂</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1364560_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1364560'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1364560'>姬人姓薛氏。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1364560_comment'></div>本东明国王金氏之允也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1364560_comment'></div>昔金王有爱子。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1364560_comment'></div>别食于薛。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1364560_comment'></div>因为姓焉。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1364560_comment'></div>世不与金氏为姻。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1364560_comment'></div>其高曾皆金王贵臣大人也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1364560_comment'></div>父永冲。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1364560_comment'></div>有唐高宗时。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1364560_comment'></div>与金仁问归国。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1364560_comment'></div>帝畴厥庸。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1364560_comment'></div>拜左武卫大将军。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1364560_comment'></div>姬人幼有玉色。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1364560_comment'></div>发于秾华。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1364560_comment'></div>若彩云朝升。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1364560_comment'></div>微月宵映也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1364560_comment'></div>故家人美之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_16_1364560_comment'></div>少号仙子。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_17_1364560_comment'></div>闻<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_18_1364560", 1364560, "Clauses/18/Comments/0")'>嬴台</span>有孔雀凤凰之事。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_18_1364560_comment'></div><span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_19_1364560", 1364560, "Clauses/19/Comments/0")'>瑶情</span>悦之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_19_1364560_comment'></div>年十五。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_20_1364560_comment'></div>大将军薨。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_21_1364560_comment'></div>遂剪发出家。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_22_1364560_comment'></div>将学金仙之道。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_23_1364560_comment'></div>而见宝手菩萨。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_24_1364560_comment'></div>静心六年。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_25_1364560_comment'></div>青莲不至。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_26_1364560_comment'></div>乃谣曰。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_27_1364560_comment'></div>化云心兮思淑真。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_28_1364560_comment'></div>洞寂灭兮不见人。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_29_1364560_comment'></div>瑶草芳兮思葐蒀。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_30_1364560_comment'></div>将柰何兮青春。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_31_1364560_comment'></div>遂<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_32_1364560", 1364560, "Clauses/32/Comments/0")'>返初服</span>。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_32_1364560_comment'></div>而归我郭公。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_33_1364560_comment'></div>郭公豪荡而好奇者也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_34_1364560_comment'></div>杂佩以迎之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_35_1364560_comment'></div>宝瑟以友之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_36_1364560_comment'></div>其相得如青鸟翡翠之婉娈矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_37_1364560_comment'></div>华繁艳歇。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_38_1364560_comment'></div>乐极悲来。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_39_1364560_comment'></div>以长寿二年太岁癸巳二月十七日。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_40_1364560_comment'></div>遇暴疾而卒于通泉县之官舍。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_41_1364560_comment'></div>呜呼哀哉。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_42_1364560_comment'></div>郭公恍然犹若未亡也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_43_1364560_comment'></div>宝珠以含之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_44_1364560_comment'></div>锦衾而举之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_45_1364560_comment'></div>故国途遥。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_46_1364560_comment'></div>言归未迨。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_47_1364560_comment'></div>留殡于县之惠普寺之南园。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_48_1364560_comment'></div>不忘真也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_49_1364560_comment'></div>铭曰。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_50_1364560_comment'></div></div><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_51_1364560'>高邱之白云兮。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_51_1364560_comment'></div>愿一见之何期。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_52_1364560_comment'></div>哀淑人之永逝。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_53_1364560_comment'></div>感<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_54_1364560", 1364560, "Clauses/54/Comments/0")'>绀园</span>之春时。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_54_1364560_comment'></div>愿作青鸟长比翼。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_55_1364560_comment'></div>魂魄归来游故国。</div><div id='poem_sentence_56_1364560_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=694&endYear=694')">694年1月</a>　居蜀守制，一月为堂弟陈孜入葬撰墓志。作品：《堂弟孜墓志铭》<div id='poem_1364558' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1364558' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1364558?labeling=true' target='_blank'>堂弟孜墓志铭</a><span class='authorDate'>（694年1月）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 唐初 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(20887, "唐初", "陈子昂", "poem_title_1364558")'>陈子昂</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1364558_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1364558'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1364558'>君讳孜。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1364558_comment'></div>字无怠。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1364558_comment'></div>其先陈国人也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1364558_comment'></div>六代祖太乐。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1364558_comment'></div>梁大同中为本郡大司马。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1364558_comment'></div>生五代祖方庆。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1364558_comment'></div>属梁乱。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1364558_comment'></div>始居新城郡武东山。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1364558_comment'></div>生高祖汤。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1364558_comment'></div>为郡主簿。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1364558_comment'></div>生曾祖通。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1364558_comment'></div>早卒。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1364558_comment'></div>通生皇祖辩。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1364558_comment'></div>少习儒学。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1364558_comment'></div>然以豪英刚烈著闻。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1364558_comment'></div>是以名节为州国所服。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1364558_comment'></div>皇祖生考元爽。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_16_1364558_comment'></div>保植先人茂德。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_17_1364558_comment'></div>降生于君。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_18_1364558_comment'></div>君幼孤。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_19_1364558_comment'></div>天资雄植。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_20_1364558_comment'></div>英秀独迈。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_21_1364558_comment'></div>性严而尚倜傥之奇。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_22_1364558_comment'></div>爱廉贞而不拘介独之操。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_23_1364558_comment'></div>始通诗礼。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_24_1364558_comment'></div>略观史传。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_25_1364558_comment'></div>即怀轨物之标。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_26_1364558_comment'></div>希旷代之业。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_27_1364558_comment'></div>故言不<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_28_1364558", 1364558, "Clauses/28/Comments/0")'>宿诺</span>。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_28_1364558_comment'></div>行不<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_29_1364558", 1364558, "Clauses/29/Comments/0")'>苟从</span>。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_29_1364558_comment'></div>率身克己。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_30_1364558_comment'></div>服道崇德。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_31_1364558_comment'></div>闺门穆穆如也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_32_1364558_comment'></div>乡党恂恂如也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_33_1364558_comment'></div>至乃雄以济义。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_34_1364558_comment'></div>勇以存仁。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_35_1364558_comment'></div>贞以立事。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_36_1364558_comment'></div>毅以守节。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_37_1364558_comment'></div>独断于心。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_38_1364558_comment'></div>每若由已。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_39_1364558_comment'></div>实为时辈所高。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_40_1364558_comment'></div>而莫敢与伦也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_41_1364558_comment'></div>是以乡里长幼。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_42_1364558_comment'></div><span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_43_1364558", 1364558, "Clauses/43/Comments/0")'>望风而靡</span>。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_43_1364558_comment'></div>邦国贤豪。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_44_1364558_comment'></div>闻名而悦服。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_45_1364558_comment'></div>方谓拂羽乔木。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_46_1364558_comment'></div>缅升高云。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_47_1364558_comment'></div>而遭命大过。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_48_1364558_comment'></div>栋桡而殒。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_49_1364558_comment'></div>呜呼。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_50_1364558_comment'></div>天咎予乎。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_51_1364558_comment'></div>时年三十五。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_52_1364558_comment'></div>是岁龙集癸巳。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_53_1364558_comment'></div>有周天授二年秋七月。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_54_1364558_comment'></div>卜兆不吉。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_55_1364558_comment'></div>权殡于真谛寺之北园。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_56_1364558_comment'></div>始以今甲午岁献春一月己酉朔二十五日己酉。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_57_1364558_comment'></div>定于石溪山之北冈。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_58_1364558_comment'></div>陪考坟也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_59_1364558_comment'></div>君家世坟垄在武东山。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_60_1364558_comment'></div>昭穆崇封。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_61_1364558_comment'></div>松柏列盛。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_62_1364558_comment'></div>至君考遗令。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_63_1364558_comment'></div>独爱石溪之冈。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_64_1364558_comment'></div>故君从先志。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_65_1364558_comment'></div>祔葬于此。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_66_1364558_comment'></div>呜呼哀哉。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_67_1364558_comment'></div>始君伯父。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_68_1364558_comment'></div>海内之文人也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_69_1364558_comment'></div>含纯刚之德。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_70_1364558_comment'></div>有高代之行。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_71_1364558_comment'></div>每见君叹曰。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_72_1364558_comment'></div>吾家代虽儒术传嗣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_73_1364558_comment'></div>然豪英雄秀。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_74_1364558_comment'></div>济济不泯。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_75_1364558_comment'></div>常惧后来光烈。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_76_1364558_comment'></div>不象先风。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_77_1364558_comment'></div>每一见尔。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_78_1364558_comment'></div>慰吾家道。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_79_1364558_comment'></div>实谓君有逸群之骨。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_80_1364558_comment'></div>拔俗之标。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_81_1364558_comment'></div>超山越壑。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_82_1364558_comment'></div>可以骏迈也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_83_1364558_comment'></div>岂其夭绝。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_84_1364558_comment'></div>丧兹良图。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_85_1364558_comment'></div>呜呼。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_86_1364558_comment'></div>其元命欤。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_87_1364558_comment'></div>遭命欤。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_88_1364558_comment'></div>天不忱欤。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_89_1364558_comment'></div>道固谬欤。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_90_1364558_comment'></div><span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_91_1364558", 1364558, "Clauses/91/Comments/0")'>大圆</span>苍苍。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_91_1364558_comment'></div><span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_92_1364558", 1364558, "Clauses/92/Comments/0")'>大方</span>茫茫。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_92_1364558_comment'></div>贤圣同此。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_93_1364558_comment'></div>尔之何伤。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_94_1364558_comment'></div>古人有言。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_95_1364558_comment'></div>珠玉而瘗。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_96_1364558_comment'></div>是暴骸于中原。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_97_1364558_comment'></div>况吾家道尚俭。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_98_1364558_comment'></div>名训未坠。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_99_1364558_comment'></div>封树之礼。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_100_1364558_comment'></div>吾敢过焉。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_101_1364558_comment'></div>是用锡尔瓦木之器。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_102_1364558_comment'></div>涂刍之灵。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_103_1364558_comment'></div>尧舜之典。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_104_1364558_comment'></div>忠孝之经。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_105_1364558_comment'></div>昭示后代。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_106_1364558_comment'></div>以安尔形。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_107_1364558_comment'></div>铭曰。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_108_1364558_comment'></div></div><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_109_1364558'>我祖之葳蕤兮邈于陈。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_109_1364558_comment'></div>缅遥裔兮此江濆。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_110_1364558_comment'></div>五代崇光兮至夫君。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_111_1364558_comment'></div>徽烈英曜兮始葐蒀。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_112_1364558_comment'></div>何意严霜兮降青春。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_113_1364558_comment'></div>玉树摧落兮成黄尘。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_114_1364558_comment'></div>南山无隙兮永幽沦。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_115_1364558_comment'></div>悠悠昭代兮卜尔辰。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_116_1364558_comment'></div>吾恸感伤兮号苍旻。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_117_1364558_comment'></div>问之蓍策兮立兹坟。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_118_1364558_comment'></div>乃言千载兮衣冠来臻。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_119_1364558_comment'></div><span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_120_1364558", 1364558, "Clauses/120/Comments/0")'>黄头</span>之子白服人。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_120_1364558_comment'></div>嗟尔<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_121_1364558", 1364558, "Clauses/121/Comments/0")'>黄头</span>兮勿伤神。</div><div id='poem_sentence_121_1364558_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=694&endYear=694')">694年</a>　学士陈该归葬绵州故乡，子昂为撰墓志。作品：《周故内供奉学士怀州河内县尉陈君硕人墓志铭》<div id='poem_1364559' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1364559' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1364559?labeling=true' target='_blank'>周故内供奉学士怀州河内县尉陈君石人铭</a><span class='authorDate'>（694年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 唐初 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(20887, "唐初", "陈子昂", "poem_title_1364559")'>陈子昂</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1364559_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1364559'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1364559'>君讳该。字彦表。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1364559_comment'></div>绵州显武人也。其先自颍川迁蜀矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1364559_comment'></div>曾祖寄。祖曾。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1364559_comment'></div>考永贵。皆养高不仕。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1364559_comment'></div>君少好学。能属文。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1364559_comment'></div>上元元年州贡进士。对策高第。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1364559_comment'></div>释褐授将仕郎。其明年制敕天下文儒。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1364559_comment'></div>司属少卿杨守讷荐君应词殚文律。对策高第。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1364559_comment'></div>敕授茂州石泉县主簿。开耀元年制举。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1364559_comment'></div>太子舍人司议郎大府少卿元知让应制荐君于朝堂。对策高第。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1364559_comment'></div>敕授隆州苍溪县主簿。垂拱四年又应制学综古今。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1364559_comment'></div>对策高第。敕授怀州河内县尉。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1364559_comment'></div>凡历所职。皆以清廉仁爱著闻。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1364559_comment'></div>有周革命。天授三年恩敕自河内追入閤供奉。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1364559_comment'></div>居未期。不幸遇疾。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1364559_comment'></div>于神都积善坊考终厥命。年六十三。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1364559_comment'></div>归葬于豆圌山之阳原。礼也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_16_1364559_comment'></div>呜呼哀哉。古人有云。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_17_1364559_comment'></div>饰颜夷之行。不逢青云之士。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_18_1364559_comment'></div>而声名磨灭者有之矣。呜呼。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_19_1364559_comment'></div>我陈君敦懿元默。洁清温良。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_20_1364559_comment'></div>驯道执志。好学博古。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_21_1364559_comment'></div>恂恂焉行高职卑。不改其操。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_22_1364559_comment'></div>学优禄薄。不怨于天。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_23_1364559_comment'></div>四举有道。三历下位。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_24_1364559_comment'></div>宴如也。非谆谆淑人。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_25_1364559_comment'></div>其谁能涅此而不渝哉。夫知命可谓君子矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_26_1364559_comment'></div>好学可谓为文矣。丹书不藏于勋府。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_27_1364559_comment'></div>青史不昭于方册。于戏。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_28_1364559_comment'></div>一绝故老之口。孰知夫子之贤哉。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_29_1364559_comment'></div>吾与君族人也。服美其德。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_30_1364559_comment'></div>尚矣。昔子云称李元。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_31_1364559_comment'></div>常璩叙令伯。皆没而不朽。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_32_1364559_comment'></div>后代称之。斯非若人之徒欤。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_33_1364559_comment'></div>吾岂默而无述。其铭曰。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_34_1364559_comment'></div></div><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_35_1364559'>訚訚君子。好斯文兮。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_35_1364559_comment'></div>缛藻<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_36_1364559", 1364559, "Clauses/72/Comments/0")'>鞶章</span>。潜卿云兮。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_36_1364559_comment'></div>栖迟下位。允升闻兮。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_37_1364559_comment'></div>金署玉堂。见吾君兮。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_38_1364559_comment'></div>鸾阶鸿渐。期紫氛兮。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_39_1364559_comment'></div>钟鸣漏尽。竟<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_40_1364559", 1364559, "Clauses/81/Comments/0")'>兰焚</span>兮。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_40_1364559_comment'></div>儒行墨节。将何云兮。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_41_1364559_comment'></div>恭承遗言。立石人兮。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_42_1364559_comment'></div><span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_43_1364559", 1364559, "Clauses/86/Comments/0")'>金刻</span>丹书。记岁辰兮。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_43_1364559_comment'></div>青龙甲午。铭兹坟兮。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_44_1364559_comment'></div></div><div id='poem_sentence_45_1364559_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=694&endYear=694')">694年3月</a>　居蜀守制，三月服阕，离蜀赴都。<br /></div><div class='label1' ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=698&endYear=698')">698年10月</a>　归田侍养。十月，方出游，偶遇巴西姜主簿来访，诗酒盘桓，赋诗并序赠别。作品：《偶遇巴西姜主簿序》<div id='poem_1364539' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1364539' class='poemTitle class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1364539'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1364539'>予疲尔永久。未尝解颜。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1364539_comment'></div>正欲登高山。望远壑。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1364539_comment'></div>挥斥幽痗。以劘太清。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1364539_comment'></div>姜主簿倏自绵中。至于林下。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1364539_comment'></div>乃饰琴酒之事。杂文章之娱。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1364539_comment'></div>将蠲我忧。颓靡取乐。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1364539_comment'></div>夫浩浩之白。不可独也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1364539_comment'></div>青春之诗。又谁咎也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1364539_comment'></div>逢太平之化。寄当年之欢。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1364539_comment'></div><span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_9_1364539", 1364539, ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=698&endYear=698')">698年10月</a>　归田侍养。十月，喜忘年故友荆州仓曹马择来访，琴书诗酒，陶然山水之间，醉歌释心逞志之乐。作品：《喜马参军相遇醉歌并序》<div id='poem_34749' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_34749' </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(20887, "唐初", "陈子昂", "poem_title_34749")'>陈子昂</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_34749_comment'></div><div class='titleComment' id='poem_preface_34749'>吾无用久矣，进不能以义补国，退不能以道隐身。天子哀衿，居于侍省，且欲以芝桂为伍，麋鹿同曹，轩裳钟鼎，如梦中也。南荣曝背，北林设罝，有客叩门，云吾道存，孺子孺子，黄中通理。时玄冬遇夜，微月在天，白云半山，志逸海上，酒既醉，琴方清，陶然玄畅，浩尔太素，则欲狎青鸟，寄丹丘矣。日月云迈，蟋蟀谓何，夫诗可以比兴也，不言曷者。时醉书散洒，乃昏见清庙台令，如此有蜀云气也。毕大拾遗、陆六侍御、崔议司、崔兵曹、鲜于晋、崔湎子、怀一道人当知吾此评是实录也，若东莱王仲烈见之，必以为真醉，歌曰。</div><div id='poem_preface_34749_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_34749'><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_34749'>独幽默以三月兮，深林潜居。<div id='poem_sentence_0_34749_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_1_34749'>时岁忽兮，孤愤遐吟。<div id='poem_sentence_1_34749_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_2_34749'>谁知我心，孺子孺子，其可与理分。</div><div id='poem_sentence_2_34749_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=699&endYear=699')">699年</a>　家居侍养。撰《后史记》，粗立纲纪。七月七日，父元敬卒。十月葬父武东山。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=699&endYear=699')">699年2月</a>　归田侍养。春二月，故友冀珪、崔泰之奉使蜀中，过梓州，琴樽谭咏数日，赋诗并序。作品：《喜遇冀侍御珪崔司议泰之二使并序》<div id='poem_34684' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_34684' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/34684?labeling=true' target='_blank'>喜遇冀侍御圭崔司议泰之二使</a><span class='authorDate'>（699年2月）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 唐初 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(20887, "唐初", "陈子昂", "poem_title_34684")'>陈子昂</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_34684_comment'></div><div class='titleComment' id='poem_preface_34684'>余独坐一隅，孤愤五蠹，虽身在江海，而心驰魏阙。岁时仲春，幽卧未起，忽闻二星入井，四牡临亭，邀使者之车，乃故人之驾，隐几一笑，把臂入林。既闻朝廷之乐，复此琴樽之事，山林幽寂，钟鼎旧游，语默谭咏，今复一得，况北堂夜永。西轩月微，巴山有望别之嗟，洛阳无寄载之客，江关离曾，三千馀里，名位宠辱，一百年中，欢娱如何，日月其迈，不为目前之赏，以增别后之思，蟋蟀笑人，夫子何叹。</div><div id='poem_preface_34684_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_34684'><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_34684'>谢病南山下，幽卧不知春。<div id='poem_sentence_0_34684_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_1_34684'>使星入东井，云是故交亲。<div id='poem_sentence_1_34684_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_2_34684'>惠风吹宝瑟，微月忆清真。<div id='poem_sentence_2_34684_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_3_34684'>凭轩一留醉，江海寄情人。<div ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=699&endYear=699')">699年2月</a>　归田侍养。春二月，故友冀珪、崔泰之使蜀，过访数日别去，子昂赋诗并序赠别，言养真理身，进退皆安，并以之为《巴山别引》，附寄房融、陆馀庆、毕构等朝中诸友，邀他日相聚。作品：《赠别冀侍御崔司议并序》<div id='poem_34782' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_34782' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/34782?labeling=true' target='_blank'>赠别冀侍御崔司议</a><span class='authorDate'>（699年2月）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 唐初 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(20887, "唐初", "陈子昂", "poem_title_34782")'>陈子昂</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_34782_comment'></div><div class='titleComment' id='poem_preface_34782'>朝廷欢娱，山林幽痗，思魏阙魂已九飞，饮岷江情复三乐，进不忘匡救于国，退不惭无闷在林。冀侍御、崔司议至公至平，许我以语默于是矣。夫达者以公济天下，穷者以大道理身。嗟乎！子昂岂敢负古人哉？蜀国酒醨，无以娱客，至于挟清瑟，登高山。白云在天，清江涵月，可以散孤愤，可以游太清。一世之逸人，寄千里之道友，吾欲不谢于崔冀二公矣。所恨酒未醒，琴方清，王事靡盬，驿骑遄速，不尽平原十日之饮。又谢叔度累日之欢，云山悠悠，叹不及也。载想房陆毕子为轩冕之人，不知蜀山有云，巴水可兴，暌阙良会，我心惄然，请以此酣，寄谢诸子，为巴山别引也。</div><div id='poem_preface_34782_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_34782'><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_34782'>有道君匡国，无闷<span class='inlineComment2'>（一作机）</span>余在林。<div ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=699&endYear=699')">699年</a>　归田侍养。故友珠英学士王无竞探访，子昻赋诗赠别。作品：《送东莱王学士无竞》<div id='poem_34674' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_34674' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=699&endYear=699')">699年</a>　归田侍养。荆州道士孟安排以武则天之父灵榇曾驻观七月，请奏修饰遗迹，乃重修宫观，赐名大崇福观。子昂受托撰刊石记。作品：《荆州大崇福观记》<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=699&endYear=699')">699年</a>　归田侍养。尝著《江上人文论》，遭家难亡之。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=699&endYear=699')">699年</a>　归田侍养。尝恨国史芜杂，乃自汉孝武之后以迄于唐，撰《后史记》，遭忧中废。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=699&endYear=699')">699年</a>　归田侍养，七月七日，父元敬卒，十月己酉，葬武东山石佛谷中冈。子昂遂庐于墓侧，哀号柴毁，杖而后起。作品：《我府君有周君士文林郎陈公墓志文》<div id='poem_1364561' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1364561' class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1364561'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1364561'>公讳元敬。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1364561_comment'></div>字某。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1364561_comment'></div>其先陈国人也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1364561_comment'></div>五世祖太乐。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1364561_comment'></div>梁大同中为新城郡司马。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1364561_comment'></div>生高祖方庆。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1364561_comment'></div>方庆好道。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1364561_comment'></div>得墨子五行秘书白虎七变法。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1364561_comment'></div>遂隐于郡武东山。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1364561_comment'></div>生曾祖汤。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1364561_comment'></div>汤为郡主簿。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1364561_comment'></div>汤生祖通。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1364561_comment'></div>通早卒。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1364561_comment'></div>生皇考辩。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1364561_comment'></div>为郡豪杰。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1364561_comment'></div>公河目海口。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1364561_comment'></div><span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_16_1364561", 1364561, "Clauses/16/Comments/0")'>燕颔虎头</span>。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_16_1364561_comment'></div>性英雄而志尚元默。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_17_1364561_comment'></div>群书秘学。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_18_1364561_comment'></div>无所不览。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_19_1364561_comment'></div>年弱冠。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_20_1364561_comment'></div>早为州闾所服。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_21_1364561_comment'></div>耆老童幼。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_22_1364561_comment'></div>见之若大宾。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_23_1364561_comment'></div>二十二乡贡明经擢第。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_24_1364561_comment'></div>拜文林郎。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_25_1364561_comment'></div>属忧艰不仕。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_26_1364561_comment'></div>潜道育德。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_27_1364561_comment'></div>穆其清风。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_28_1364561_comment'></div>邦人驯致。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_29_1364561_comment'></div>如众鸟之从凤也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_30_1364561_comment'></div>时有决讼。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_31_1364561_comment'></div>不取州郡之命。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_32_1364561_comment'></div>而信公之言。<div
