/><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=699&endYear=699')">699年</a>　庐墓守制。十月，为申州司马王济撰墓志。作品：《申州司马王府君墓志》<div id='poem_1364552' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1364552' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1364552?labeling=true' target='_blank'>申州司马王府君墓志</a><span class='authorDate'>（699年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 唐初 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(20887, "唐初", "陈子昂", "poem_title_1364552")'>陈子昂</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1364552_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1364552'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1364552'>君讳某。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1364552_comment'></div>字某。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1364552_comment'></div>其先太原人也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1364552_comment'></div>昔周文王有圣人之德。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1364552_comment'></div>甲子受图。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1364552_comment'></div>至我灵王。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1364552_comment'></div>诞膺丕显。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1364552_comment'></div>太子晋得凤凰之瑞。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1364552_comment'></div>恭揖群后。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1364552_comment'></div>上为帝宾。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1364552_comment'></div>绵绵生人。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1364552_comment'></div>作我王氏。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1364552_comment'></div>迨秦有贲剪。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1364552_comment'></div>并吞诸侯。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1364552_comment'></div>晋有浑祥。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1364552_comment'></div>功格帝室。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1364552_comment'></div>魏至慧龙。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_16_1364552_comment'></div>为贵种矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_17_1364552_comment'></div>十二代祖卓。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_18_1364552_comment'></div>晋常山公主子也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_19_1364552_comment'></div>始公主汤沐邑在汾阳。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_20_1364552_comment'></div>永嘉沦夷。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_21_1364552_comment'></div>不及南度。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_22_1364552_comment'></div>因树枌槚而结庐焉。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_23_1364552_comment'></div>卒葬于长寿原。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_24_1364552_comment'></div>至今乡有太原之号也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_25_1364552_comment'></div>曾祖亮。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_26_1364552_comment'></div>周开府仪同上大将军。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_27_1364552_comment'></div>隋信州刺史。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_28_1364552_comment'></div>樽俎之师也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_29_1364552_comment'></div>祖俭。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_30_1364552_comment'></div>隋离石郡守唐石州刺史。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_31_1364552_comment'></div>赠岳州总管广武烈侯。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_32_1364552_comment'></div>社稷之器也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_33_1364552_comment'></div>父谌。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_34_1364552_comment'></div>唐虞部郎中荆州大都督司马商壁鄜许冀五州刺史加银青光禄大夫泸州都督金水敏侯上柱国。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_35_1364552_comment'></div>廊庙之才也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_36_1364552_comment'></div>敏侯有功于国。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_37_1364552_comment'></div>始赐土田。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_38_1364552_comment'></div>白茅苴之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_39_1364552_comment'></div>在鄠之曲。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_40_1364552_comment'></div>因食菜。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_41_1364552_comment'></div>今为雍州人。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_42_1364552_comment'></div>君即敏侯之元子。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_43_1364552_comment'></div>炳灵珍粹。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_44_1364552_comment'></div>辉采幽黄。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_45_1364552_comment'></div>愿而以恭。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_46_1364552_comment'></div>宽而以栗。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_47_1364552_comment'></div>青衿闻道。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_48_1364552_comment'></div>已光大矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_49_1364552_comment'></div>天子立太学。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_50_1364552_comment'></div>所以养贤。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_51_1364552_comment'></div>公子齿上庠。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_52_1364552_comment'></div>所以观国。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_53_1364552_comment'></div>君休烈泉塞。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_54_1364552_comment'></div>志业云翔。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_55_1364552_comment'></div>年若干为国子生。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_56_1364552_comment'></div>其中射策甲科。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_57_1364552_comment'></div>解褐补吴王府参军事。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_58_1364552_comment'></div>时吴王帝之爱子。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_59_1364552_comment'></div>国选英寮。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_60_1364552_comment'></div>君三德允章。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_61_1364552_comment'></div><span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_62_1364552", 1364552, "Clauses/62/Comments/0")'>六行</span>既穆。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_62_1364552_comment'></div>与某郡刘孝孙首光此举。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_63_1364552_comment'></div>诵诗三百。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_64_1364552_comment'></div>和淑其仁。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_65_1364552_comment'></div>而醴酒不恭。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_66_1364552_comment'></div>楚筵亦废。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_67_1364552_comment'></div>坐除滑州录事参军。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_68_1364552_comment'></div>又转陇州录事参军。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_69_1364552_comment'></div>时乐成公刘仁轨以宰相之贵。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_70_1364552_comment'></div>持节此州。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_71_1364552_comment'></div>暧然推中主诺责。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_72_1364552_comment'></div>下君提纲。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_73_1364552_comment'></div>未几。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_74_1364552_comment'></div>群辖载孚。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_75_1364552_comment'></div>刘公坐啸。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_76_1364552_comment'></div>以为能也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_77_1364552_comment'></div>举迁汾州平遥县令。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_78_1364552_comment'></div>其地有台骀之怪。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_79_1364552_comment'></div>蟋蟀之人。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_80_1364552_comment'></div>君黄鼎分中。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_81_1364552_comment'></div>鸣琴不下。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_82_1364552_comment'></div>钟鼓既考。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_83_1364552_comment'></div>风俗允和。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_84_1364552_comment'></div>帝曰良哉。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_85_1364552_comment'></div>而格我政。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_86_1364552_comment'></div>加朝散大夫。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_87_1364552_comment'></div>迁岐州扶风县令。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_88_1364552_comment'></div>昔尹翁归以文武之干。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_89_1364552_comment'></div>缉熙此邦。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_90_1364552_comment'></div>黄图虽宁。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_91_1364552_comment'></div><span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_92_1364552", 1364552, "Clauses/92/Comments/0")'>赤丸</span>未乂。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_92_1364552_comment'></div>君以先庚断甲。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_93_1364552_comment'></div>设距投钩。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_94_1364552_comment'></div><span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_95_1364552", 1364552, "Clauses/95/Comments/0")'>赭裾</span>始绳。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_95_1364552_comment'></div>垩面咸革。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_96_1364552_comment'></div>丁我敏侯艰。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_97_1364552_comment'></div>遂茹哀苫庐。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_98_1364552_comment'></div>衔恤终祀。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_99_1364552_comment'></div>是岁申国不理。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_100_1364552_comment'></div>元寮伫才。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_101_1364552_comment'></div>制加朝请大夫。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_102_1364552_comment'></div>授申州司马。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_103_1364552_comment'></div>属太夫人有羸老之疾。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_104_1364552_comment'></div>去官不之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_105_1364552_comment'></div>白华增勤。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_106_1364552_comment'></div>䌽衣是慕。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_107_1364552_comment'></div>至于朝盥夕膳。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_108_1364552_comment'></div>色承欢。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_109_1364552_comment'></div>夔夔斋慄。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_110_1364552_comment'></div>蒸蒸不匮。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_111_1364552_comment'></div>有若楚老莱子之为婴儿也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_112_1364552_comment'></div>呜呼。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_113_1364552_comment'></div>昊天不吊。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_114_1364552_comment'></div>降我鞠凶。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_115_1364552_comment'></div>太夫人以眉寿薨。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_116_1364552_comment'></div>时君年已七十二矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_117_1364552_comment'></div>礼以饮酒。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_118_1364552_comment'></div>而君绝浆。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_119_1364552_comment'></div>虞以降哀。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_120_1364552_comment'></div>而君泣血。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_121_1364552_comment'></div>茕茕在疚。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_122_1364552_comment'></div>栾棘其心。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_123_1364552_comment'></div>新谷未升。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_124_1364552_comment'></div>匪莪以殒。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_125_1364552_comment'></div>以某年青龙癸巳。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_126_1364552_comment'></div>薨于某里第之正寝。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_127_1364552_comment'></div>孝之终也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_128_1364552_comment'></div>呜呼哀哉。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_129_1364552_comment'></div>昔圣人五十而慕。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_130_1364552_comment'></div>先子谓之至德。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_131_1364552_comment'></div>今君七十二而尽其哀。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_132_1364552_comment'></div>非敦笃允元深仁淑德者。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_133_1364552_comment'></div>畴能离此哉。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_134_1364552_comment'></div>夫人宏农杨氏。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_135_1364552_comment'></div>隋内史侍郎丹川公演之孙女也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_136_1364552_comment'></div>幼有淑德。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_137_1364552_comment'></div>而美令仪。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_138_1364552_comment'></div>采蘩昭华。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_139_1364552_comment'></div>秾荷比秀。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_140_1364552_comment'></div>至于内严阃训。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_141_1364552_comment'></div>外匡君子。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_142_1364552_comment'></div>麟趾以穆。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_143_1364552_comment'></div>鸡鸣有章。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_144_1364552_comment'></div>诚可道映公宫。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_145_1364552_comment'></div>事宣彤管。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_146_1364552_comment'></div>晚年以儒因未究。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_147_1364552_comment'></div>冥业惟深。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_148_1364552_comment'></div>遂揭无生之筌。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_149_1364552_comment'></div>将遗有漏之屣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_150_1364552_comment'></div>颛洁道行。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_151_1364552_comment'></div>受莲花经。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_152_1364552_comment'></div>理极翻三。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_153_1364552_comment'></div>心灭不二。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_154_1364552_comment'></div>形亡缘尽。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_155_1364552_comment'></div>归真化冥。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_156_1364552_comment'></div>岁在丁酉。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_157_1364552_comment'></div>处顺而往。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_158_1364552_comment'></div>始我府君以悬车之岁。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_159_1364552_comment'></div>从负米之勤。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_160_1364552_comment'></div>夫人亦能肃恭晨昏。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_161_1364552_comment'></div>严祗左右。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_162_1364552_comment'></div>夫至行莫大于孝。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_163_1364552_comment'></div>崇义莫显乎忠。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_164_1364552_comment'></div>君克勤于家。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_165_1364552_comment'></div>尽力于国。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_166_1364552_comment'></div>刑于妻子。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_167_1364552_comment'></div>至于朝廷。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_168_1364552_comment'></div>夫矜而不与。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_169_1364552_comment'></div>物或有违。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_170_1364552_comment'></div>广而无适。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_171_1364552_comment'></div>义所以比。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_172_1364552_comment'></div>君好谦达礼。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_173_1364552_comment'></div>研几成务。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_174_1364552_comment'></div>摹其<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_175_1364552", 1364552, "Clauses/175/Comments/0")'>法器</span>无不驯。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_175_1364552_comment'></div>从其事政无不理。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_176_1364552_comment'></div>夫用我者。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_177_1364552_comment'></div>而岂徒哉。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_178_1364552_comment'></div>嗟夫。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_179_1364552_comment'></div>矜而能廉。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_180_1364552_comment'></div>利而不浼。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_181_1364552_comment'></div>百行允备。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_182_1364552_comment'></div>三事不阶。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_183_1364552_comment'></div>臧文仲其窃位与。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_184_1364552_comment'></div>柳下惠其直道与。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_185_1364552_comment'></div>有子四人。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_186_1364552_comment'></div>长曰某。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_187_1364552_comment'></div>官至武连县令。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_188_1364552_comment'></div>先公而卒。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_189_1364552_comment'></div>次子某等。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_190_1364552_comment'></div>皆肃奉严训。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_191_1364552_comment'></div>景行高山。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_192_1364552_comment'></div>达于家邦。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_193_1364552_comment'></div>光于礼乐。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_194_1364552_comment'></div>永号罔极。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_195_1364552_comment'></div>泣血旻天。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_196_1364552_comment'></div>始府君临终。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_197_1364552_comment'></div>遗令薄葬。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_198_1364552_comment'></div>墨龟未食。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_199_1364552_comment'></div><span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_200_1364552", 1364552, "Clauses/200/Comments/0")'>青乌</span>不封。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_200_1364552_comment'></div>权殡于某所。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_201_1364552_comment'></div>需吉兆也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_202_1364552_comment'></div>龙集己亥。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_203_1364552_comment'></div>律躔应钟。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_204_1364552_comment'></div>金鸡鸣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_205_1364552_comment'></div>玉狗吠。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_206_1364552_comment'></div>黄肠密启。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_207_1364552_comment'></div>丹旐徐飞。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_208_1364552_comment'></div>始迁神于某原之阳。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_209_1364552_comment'></div>礼也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_210_1364552_comment'></div>青龙在左。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_211_1364552_comment'></div>朱凤居前。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_212_1364552_comment'></div>双衾共封。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_213_1364552_comment'></div>二室同宛。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_214_1364552_comment'></div>珠玉不瘗。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_215_1364552_comment'></div>邱陇谁传。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_216_1364552_comment'></div>刻此金石。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_217_1364552_comment'></div>以旌后贤。</div><div id='poem_sentence_218_1364552_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=700&endYear=700')">700年</a>　家居守制。县令段简附会文法，罗织陷狱，忧愤而卒。享年四十二，葬射洪独坐山。<br /></div>
-----end



-----title
合川（石镜）
-----detail
<div class='label1' id='08cbdc9bf07b48f8897a75a5c4417d5d_label'><a href='javascript: DetailSwitch("08cbdc9bf07b48f8897a75a5c4417d5d");'><span id='08cbdc9bf07b48f8897a75a5c4417d5d_link' class='switch'>—</span></a><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=679&endYear=679')">679年</a>，21岁</div><div id='08cbdc9bf07b48f8897a75a5c4417d5d' class='detail'><span style='margin: 0 0.5em; color: gray;'>▪</span>出蜀赴京途中，历合州由水路出蜀赴长安。<br /><span style='margin: 0 0.5em; color: gray;'>▪</span>出蜀赴京途中，初入巴峡遇大风，作诗寄故乡亲友。作品：《初入峡苦风寄故乡亲友》<span class='inlineComment2'>（按：巴峡，即重庆合川区以下一段嘉陵江，有沥鼻峡、温塘峡、观音峡，称“嘉陵江小三峡”。）</span><div id='poem_34659' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_34659' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/34659?labeling=true' target='_blank'>初入峡苦风寄故乡亲友</a><span class='authorDate'>（679年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 唐初 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(20887, "唐初", "陈子昂", "poem_title_34659")'>陈子昂</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'>五言绝句</div></div><div id='poem_title_34659_comment'></div><div class='titleComment' id='poem_allusion_34659'><span class='label'>引用典故：</span><span class='link' onclick='ShowAllusionComment(7803, "poem_allusion_34659")'>石尤风</span></div><div id='poem_allusion_34659_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_34659'><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_34659'>故乡今日友，欢会坐应同。<div id='poem_sentence_0_34659_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_1_34659'>宁知巴峡路，辛苦<span class='link' onclick='ShowAllusionComment(7803, "poem_sentence_1_34659")'><span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_1_34659", 34659, "Clauses/3/Comments/1")'>石尤风</span></span>。<div id='poem_sentence_1_34659_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_2_34659'></div><div id='poem_sentence_2_34659_comment'></div></div></div><br /></div><div class='label1' id='5edfc756cf6943e888a344f9d617d960_label'><a href='javascript: DetailSwitch("5edfc756cf6943e888a344f9d617d960");'><span id='5edfc756cf6943e888a344f9d617d960_link' class='switch'>—</span></a><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=683&endYear=683')">683年</a>，25岁</div><div id='5edfc756cf6943e888a344f9d617d960' class='detail'><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=683&endYear=683')">683年</a>　再出蜀赴京途中，过合州。<br /></div>
-----end



-----title
北碚（巴县）
-----detail
<div class='label1' id='aae587ecf23b427e8107b9166d803a16_label'><a href='javascript: DetailSwitch("aae587ecf23b427e8107b9166d803a16");'><span id='aae587ecf23b427e8107b9166d803a16_link' class='switch'>—</span></a><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=679&endYear=679')">679年</a>，21岁</div><div id='aae587ecf23b427e8107b9166d803a16' class='detail'><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=679&endYear=679')">679年</a>　出蜀赴京途中，入东阳峡，与友人李姓县令船前后不相及，有诗抒怀。作品：《入东阳峡与李明府船前后不相及》<span class='inlineComment2'>（李明府，李姓县令，名未详。东阳峡，即温汤峡，又名温塘峡。）</span><div id='poem_34699' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_34699' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/34699?labeling=true' target='_blank'>入东阳峡与李明府舟前后不相及</a><span class='authorDate'>（679年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 唐初 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(20887, "唐初", "陈子昂", "poem_title_34699")'>陈子昂</a></span><br id='poem_sentence_4_34699_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_5_34699'>倏忽犹疑及，差池复两分。<div id='poem_sentence_5_34699_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' -----title
忠县（临江）
-----detail
<div class='label1' id='03fd1f921bb4455abfdd42829ffbf12b_label'><a href='javascript: DetailSwitch("03fd1f921bb4455abfdd42829ffbf12b");'><span id='03fd1f921bb4455abfdd42829ffbf12b_link' ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=679&endYear=679')">679年</a>　出蜀赴京途中，过忠州。<br /></div><div class='label1' id='afcbcc17c4fd4981bd25e28949e04be2_label'><a href='javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=683&endYear=683')">683年</a>　再出蜀赴京途中，过忠州，遇故友吴参军、牛司仓，欣余有作。作品：《忠州江亭喜遇吴参军牛司仓序》<div id='poem_1364536' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1364536' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1364536?labeling=true' target='_blank'>忠州江亭喜重遇吴参军牛司仓序</a><span class='authorDate'>（683年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 唐初 · </span><a class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1364536'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1364536'>日月交分。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1364536_comment'></div>春秋代谢。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1364536_comment'></div>昔岁居单阏。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1364536_comment'></div>适言别于兹都。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1364536_comment'></div>今龙集昭阳。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1364536_comment'></div>复相逢于此地。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1364536_comment'></div>山川未改。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1364536_comment'></div>容貌俱非。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1364536_comment'></div>叙名宦而犹嗟。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1364536_comment'></div>问乡关而不乐。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1364536_comment'></div>云天遂解。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1364536_comment'></div>琴酒还开。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1364536_comment'></div>新交与旧识俱欢。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1364536_comment'></div>林壑共烟霞对赏。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1364536_comment'></div>江亭回瞰。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1364536_comment'></div>罗新树于阶基。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1364536_comment'></div>山榭遥临。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_16_1364536_comment'></div>列群峰于户牖。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_17_1364536_comment'></div>尔其丹藤绿筱。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_18_1364536_comment'></div>俯映长筵。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_19_1364536_comment'></div>翠渚洪澜。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_20_1364536_comment'></div>交流合座。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_21_1364536_comment'></div>神融兴洽。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_22_1364536_comment'></div>望真情高。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_23_1364536_comment'></div>觉清溪之仙洞不遥。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_24_1364536_comment'></div>见苍海之神山乍出。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_25_1364536_comment'></div>既而行舟有限。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_26_1364536_comment'></div>嗟此会之难留。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_27_1364536_comment'></div>别日无期。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_28_1364536_comment'></div>叹分岐之易远。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_29_1364536_comment'></div>徘徊北渚。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_30_1364536_comment'></div>惆怅南津。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_31_1364536_comment'></div>江陵之道路方赊。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_32_1364536_comment'></div>巴徼之云山渐异。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_33_1364536_comment'></div>嗟乎。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_34_1364536_comment'></div>离言可赠。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_35_1364536_comment'></div>所愿保于千金。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_36_1364536_comment'></div>别曲何谣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_37_1364536_comment'></div>各请陈于五际。</div><div id='poem_sentence_38_1364536_comment'></div></div></div><br /></div>

-----title
万州（武宁）
-----detail
<div class='label1' id='eb7dc752a45f4aedb3b73509b0321ef6_label'><a href='javascript: DetailSwitch("eb7dc752a45f4aedb3b73509b0321ef6");'><span id='eb7dc752a45f4aedb3b73509b0321ef6_link' ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=679&endYear=679')">679年</a>　出蜀赴京途中，江上与友人萧四刘三暂别又再逢，欣喜有诗。作品：《江上暂别萧四刘三旋欣接遇》<span class='inlineComment2'>（萧四，名未详。刘三，名未祥。另按：诗云“昨夜沧江别，言乖天汉游，宁期此相遇，尚接武陵州。”即暂别相约再遇之地尚未至，不意在武陵洲附近即提前相遇。武陵洲，彭谱云“四川万县南有武陵场，今名武陵镇，滨临大江，疑即武陵洲。”可信。故系作此诗之地为万州武宁县，今重庆万州区武陵镇。）</span><div id='poem_34705' onclick='ShowAllusionComment(9147, "poem_allusion_34705")'>衔杯对刘</span>　<span class='link' onclick='ShowAllusionComment(9753, "poem_allusion_34705")'>野人舟</span></div><div 奉节

class='poemContent' id='poem_content_34702'><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_34702'>日落沧江晚，停桡问土风。<div id='poem_sentence_0_34702_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_1_34702'>城临<span class='link' onclick='ShowAllusionComment(199, "poem_sentence_1_34702")'>巴子国</span>，台没汉王宫。<div id='poem_sentence_1_34702_comment'></div></div><div id='poem_sentence_2_34702_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_3_34702'>岩悬青壁断，地险碧流通。<div id='poem_sentence_3_34702_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' -----title
荆门（乐乡）
-----detail
<div class='label1' id='bc4208776f2749ea8a776090f0cd7d54_label'><a href='javascript: DetailSwitch("bc4208776f2749ea8a776090f0cd7d54");'><span id='bc4208776f2749ea8a776090f0cd7d54_link' ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=679&endYear=679')">679年</a>　出蜀赴京途中，晚宿乐乡县，有孤旅之思。作品：《晚次乐乡县》<span class='inlineComment2'>（按：此诗徐谱据诗中恨如猿啼语系此诗为永淳元年（682）子昂落第归乡途中作,见《陈子昂论考》42页。非是。据子昂诗《宿襄河驿浦》，子昂落第返乡取汉江水路无疑，与本诗中“川原迷旧国，道路入边城”情形不符。且乐乡县故址在今湖北荆门北九十里，离汉水尚远，不可能夜宿乐乡县城。故仍从彭说，系本年。）</span><div id='poem_34682' id='poem_sentence_6_34731'></div><div id='poem_sentence_6_34731_comment'></div></div></div><br /><span style='margin: 0 0.5em; color: gray;'>▪</span>在长安游太学，族叔县尉陈某赴边从军，子昂饯别作序。作品：《饯陈少府从军序》<span class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1364540'>夫岁月易得。古人疾没代不称。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1364540_comment'></div>功业未成。君子以自强不息。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1364540_comment'></div>岂非怀其宝。思其用。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1364540_comment'></div>然后以取海内之名。以定当年之策。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1364540_comment'></div>展其才力。受以驱驰。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1364540_comment'></div>少府叔凤彩龙章。才高位下。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1364540_comment'></div>班超远慕。每言关塞之勋。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1364540_comment'></div>梁竦长怀。耻为州县之职。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1364540_comment'></div>属胡兵犯塞。汉将临边。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1364540_comment'></div>商君用耕战之谋。充国起屯田之策。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1364540_comment'></div>皇华出使。言收疆埸之功。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1364540_comment'></div>白水开筵。遂为云雨之别。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1364540_comment'></div>尔其苍龙<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_12_1364540", 1364540, "Clauses/24/Comments/0")'>解角</span>。朱鸟<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_12_1364540", 1364540, "Clauses/25/Comments/0")'>司辰</span>。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1364540_comment'></div><span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_13_1364540", 1364540, "Clauses/26/Comments/1")'>溽景</span>薰<span class='inlineComment2'>（一作蒸）</span>天。炎光折地。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1364540_comment'></div>山川渐远。行人动游子之歌。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1364540_comment'></div>樽酒未空。送客起贫交之赠。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1364540_comment'></div>嗟乎。杨朱所以泣岐路。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_16_1364540_comment'></div>苏武所以悲绝国。古之来矣。<div class='inline' style='margin: 0 0.5em; color: gray;'>▪</span>在长安游太学，隐士田游岩征为太子洗马，在东宫无所规益，右卫副率蒋俨以书责之。子昂作诗为田氏辩。作品：《题田洗马游岩桔槔》<span class='inlineComment2'>（田游岩，生卒年不详，行二，京兆三原人。初补太学生，罢归，游于太白山二十余年。后隐箕山许由庙东，自称许由东邻。调露中，高宗幸其宅，携归京，授崇文馆学士。文明中，拜太子洗马。垂拱初，坐与裴炎交结，放还山。《旧唐书》卷一九二，《新唐书》卷一九六有传。）</span><div id='poem_34661' class='_poem'><div id='poem_sentence_3_1364529_comment'></div>太牢斯烹。安可荐羹藜之味。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1364529_comment'></div>然则文章薄伎。固弃于<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_5_1364529", id='poem_sentence_8_1364529_comment'></div>虽有劳人之歌。怅尔咏怀。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1364529_comment'></div>曾无阮藉之思。徒恨迹荒淫丽。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1364529_comment'></div>岂不幸甚。伏惟君侯星云诞<span class='inlineComment2'>（一作挺）</span>秀。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1364529_comment'></div>金玉閒成。衣冠礼乐。<div class='inline' /><span style='margin: 0 0.5em; color: gray;'>▪</span>落第返乡途中，在长安，送别故友梁李二明府，有诗。作品：《送梁李二明府》<span class='inlineComment2'>（梁李二明府，梁姓李姓县令，名未详。另按：此诗彭谱云“当作于落第归途之中”，但此次送别未详于何地。审诗题为“送”，而非“别”，似非子昂于归途中与故友相逢于途再别之情形，或子昂落第西还长安，曾稍作盘桓，适故友离京，故送之。送别之地姑系于长安。）</span><div id='poem_34676' class='_poem'><div id='poem_note_34663_comment'></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=680&endYear=680')">680年1月</a>　在东洛，晦日与韩仲宣等共二十一人宴于高正臣之林亭，赋诗并序。作品：《晦日宴高氏林亭并序》<div id='poem_34683' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_34683' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/34683?labeling=true' target='_blank'>晦日宴高氏林亭<span class='inlineComment2'>（并序。序内缺一字）</span></a><span class='authorDate'>（680年1月）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 唐初 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(20887, "唐初", "陈子昂", "poem_title_34683")'>陈子昂</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'>五言律诗</div></div><div id='poem_title_34683_comment'></div><div class='titleComment' id='poem_preface_34683'>夫天下良辰美景，园林池观（园亭池观），古来游宴欢娱众矣。然而地或幽偏，未睹皇居之圣，时终交丧，多阻升平之道，岂知光华启旦。朝野资欢，有渤海之宗英，是平阳之贵戚，发挥形胜，出凤台之啸侣，幽赞芳辰，指鸡川而留宴，列珍羞于绮席，珠翠琅玕，奏丝管于芳园；秦筝赵瑟，冠璎济济，多延戚里之宾。鸾凤锵锵，自有文雄之客，总都畿而写望，通汉苑之楼台，控伊洛而斜□，临神仙之浦溆，则有都人士女。侠客游童，出金市而连镳，入铜街而结驷。香车绣毂，罗绮生风，宝盖雕鞍，珠玑耀日，于时律穷太簇，气淑中京，山河春而霁景华，城阙丽而年光满，淹留自乐，玩花鸟以忘归，欢赏不疲，对林泉而独得。伟矣！信皇州之盛观也，岂可使晋京才子，孤摽洛下之游，魏室群公，独擅邺中之会，盍各言志，以记芳游，同探一字，以华为韵。</div><div id='poem_preface_34683_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_34683'><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_34683'><span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_0_34683", 34683, "Clauses/0/Comments/0")'>寻春</span>游上路，追宴入山家。<div id='poem_sentence_0_34683_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_1_34683'>主第簪缨满，皇州景望华。<div id='poem_sentence_1_34683_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_2_34683'>玉池初<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_2_34683", 34683, "Clauses/4/Comments/0")'>吐溜</span>，珠树始开花。<div id='poem_sentence_2_34683_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_3_34683'>欢娱方未极，林阁散馀霞。<div id='poem_sentence_3_34683_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_4_34683'></div><div id='poem_sentence_4_34683_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=680&endYear=680')">680年1月</a>　在东洛，晦日与韩仲宣等共九人重宴高正臣之林亭，同赋诗。作品：《晦日重宴高氏林亭》<div class='inlineComment2'>（东平，即东平王李续。《新唐书·纪王慎传》：“七子……续与秀最知名。续王东平，历和州刺史，薨。”）</span><div id='poem_1364530' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1364530' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a id='poem_content_1364530'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1364530'>昔者汉朝卿士。供帐饯于东都。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1364530_comment'></div>晋国名贤。倾城祖于西郊。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1364530_comment'></div>虽时称盛观。而人非帝族。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1364530_comment'></div>东平紫微英冑。朱邸天人。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1364530_comment'></div>蕴岐嶷之瑰姿。得山河之宝气。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1364530_comment'></div>刘君爱士。常致礼于幽人。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1364530_comment'></div>曹植论文。每交欢于数子。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1364530_comment'></div>属銮舆拜日。来朝太室之前。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1364530_comment'></div>玉检停刊。言返章华之路。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1364530_comment'></div>群公以眷深王粲。思邀<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_9_1364530", 1364530, "Clauses/19/Comments/0")'>祖道</span>之欢。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1364530_comment'></div>下走以遇重荀慈。谬奉芳筵之醴。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1364530_comment'></div>于时青阳二月。黄鸟群飞。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1364530_comment'></div>残霞将落日交晖。远树与<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_12_1364530", 1364530, "Clauses/25/Comments/0")'>孤烟</span>共色。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1364530_comment'></div>江山万里。眇然荆楚之涂。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1364530_comment'></div>城邑三春。去矣伊瀍之地。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1364530_comment'></div>既而朱轩不驻。绿盖行遥。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1364530_comment'></div>琴樽之清宴巳疲。珠玉之芳言未赠。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_16_1364530_comment'></div>请各陈志。以序离襟。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_17_1364530_comment'></div></div><div id='poem_sentence_18_1364530_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: class='inlineComment4'>（点击查看或隐藏评注）</span></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=684&endYear=684')">684年</a>　在洛阳，献书谏太学废散等政理事。作品：《谏政理书》<div id='poem_1364517' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1364517' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1364517?labeling=true' target='_blank'>谏政理书</a><span class='authorDate'>（684年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 唐初 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(20887, "唐初", "陈子昂", "poem_title_1364517")'>陈子昂</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1364517_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1364517'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1364517'>月日。梓州射洪县草莽愚臣陈子昂谨冒死稽首再拜献书阙下。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1364517_comment'></div>臣子昂西蜀草茅贱臣也。以事亲馀暇得读书。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1364517_comment'></div>窃少好三皇五帝霸王之经。历观邱坟。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1364517_comment'></div>旁览<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_3_1364517", 1364517, "Clauses/6/Comments/0")'>代史</span>。原其政理。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1364517_comment'></div>察其兴亡。自伏羲神农之初。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1364517_comment'></div>至于周隋之际。驰骋数百年。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1364517_comment'></div>虽未得其详。而略可知也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1364517_comment'></div>莫不先本人情。而后化之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1364517_comment'></div>过此已往。亦无神异。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1364517_comment'></div>独轩辕氏之代。欲问广成子以至道之精理于天下。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1364517_comment'></div>臣虽奇之。然其说不经。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1364517_comment'></div>未足信也。至殷高宗亦延问傅说。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1364517_comment'></div>然才救弊。未能宏远。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1364517_comment'></div>自此之后。殆不足称。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1364517_comment'></div>臣每在山谷。有愿朝廷。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1364517_comment'></div>常恐没代而不得见也。岂知沾沐圣化。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1364517_comment'></div>未夭天年。幸得游京师。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_16_1364517_comment'></div>睹皇风。亲逢大圣之诏布于天下。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_17_1364517_comment'></div>问于贤士大夫曰。何道可以调<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_18_1364517", 1364517, "Clauses/37/Comments/0")'>元气</span>。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_18_1364517_comment'></div>贱臣孤陋。诚未足知。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_19_1364517_comment'></div>然臣窃观自古帝王。开政之原备矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_20_1364517_comment'></div>未有能深思远虑独绝古今如陛下者也。故贱臣不胜区区。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_21_1364517_comment'></div>愿竭固陋。以闻见言之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_22_1364517_comment'></div>虽未足对扬天休。然或万一有可观者。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_23_1364517_comment'></div>敢冒昧阙庭奏书以闻。伏惟皇太后陛下少加察焉。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_24_1364517_comment'></div>臣闻之于师曰。<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_25_1364517", 1364517, "Clauses/51/Comments/0")'>元气</span>者。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_25_1364517_comment'></div>天地之始。万物之祖。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_26_1364517_comment'></div>王政之<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_27_1364517", 1364517, "Clauses/54/Comments/0")'>大端</span>也。天地之道。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_27_1364517_comment'></div>莫大乎阴阳。万物之灵。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_28_1364517_comment'></div>莫大乎黔首。王政之贵。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_29_1364517_comment'></div>莫大乎安人。故人安则阴阳和。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_30_1364517_comment'></div>阴阳和则天地平。天地平则<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_31_1364517", 1364517, "Clauses/63/Comments/0")'>元气</span>正矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_31_1364517_comment'></div>是以古先帝代。见人之通于天也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_32_1364517_comment'></div>天之应乎人也。天人相感。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_33_1364517_comment'></div>阴阳相和。灾害之所以不生。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_34_1364517_comment'></div><span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_35_1364517", 1364517, "Clauses/70/Comments/1")'>嘉祥</span>之所以遂<span class='inlineComment2'>（一作并）</span>作。则<span class='inlineComment2'>（一作遂）</span>观象于天。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_35_1364517_comment'></div>察法于地。财成天地之道。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_36_1364517_comment'></div>辅相天地之宜。以左右人。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_37_1364517_comment'></div>于是养成群生。奉顺天德。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_38_1364517_comment'></div>故人得安其俗。乐其业。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_39_1364517_comment'></div>甘其食。美其服。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_40_1364517_comment'></div>阴阳大和。<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_41_1364517", 1364517, "Clauses/83/Comments/0")'>元气</span>以正。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_41_1364517_comment'></div>天瑞降。地符升。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_42_1364517_comment'></div>风雨以时。草木不落。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_43_1364517_comment'></div>龟龙麟凤。在郊薮矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_44_1364517_comment'></div>洎颛顼唐虞之閒。不敢荒宁。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_45_1364517_comment'></div>亦克用理。故其书曰。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_46_1364517_comment'></div>百姓昭明。协和万邦。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_47_1364517_comment'></div>黎人于变时雍。乃命羲和。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_48_1364517_comment'></div>钦若昊天。历象日月星辰。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_49_1364517_comment'></div>敬授人时。和之得也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_50_1364517_comment'></div>至夏德衰亡。殷政微丧。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_51_1364517_comment'></div>桀纣昏暴。乱于天道。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_52_1364517_comment'></div>杀戮无罪。放弃忠良。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_53_1364517_comment'></div>遂竭天下之力。殚天下之货。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_54_1364517_comment'></div>作为瑶台。起乎琼室。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_55_1364517_comment'></div>极荒淫之乐。穷耳目之玩。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_56_1364517_comment'></div>倾宫之女。至数千人。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_57_1364517_comment'></div>奇伎淫巧。以亿万计。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_58_1364517_comment'></div>信巫鬼。听谗邪。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_59_1364517_comment'></div>遂为糟邱酒池炮烙之刑。一朝牛饮者三千人。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_60_1364517_comment'></div>龙逢不胜其忧。谏而死。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_61_1364517_comment'></div>箕子不堪其愤。囚为奴。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_62_1364517_comment'></div>是以阴阳大乖。天地震怒。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_63_1364517_comment'></div>山川鬼神。发见灾异。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_64_1364517_comment'></div>疾疫大兴。妖孽并作。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_65_1364517_comment'></div>而桀纣不悔。卒乃灭亡。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_66_1364517_comment'></div>和之失也。逮周文武创业。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_67_1364517_comment'></div>顺天应人。诚信忠厚。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_68_1364517_comment'></div>加于百姓。德泽休泰。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_69_1364517_comment'></div>兴乎颂声。成康之时。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_70_1364517_comment'></div>刑措三十馀年。天人之道始和矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_71_1364517_comment'></div>幽厉之末。复乱厥常。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_72_1364517_comment'></div>苛慝暴虐。诟黩天地。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_73_1364517_comment'></div>百川沸腾。山冢崒崩。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_74_1364517_comment'></div>人以愁怨。疾厉为作。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_75_1364517_comment'></div>故其诗曰。昊天不佣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_76_1364517_comment'></div>降此鞫凶。昊天不惠。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_77_1364517_comment'></div>降此大戾。不先不后。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_78_1364517_comment'></div>为瘥为瘵。天地生人之理。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_79_1364517_comment'></div>复悖于兹矣。呜呼。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_80_1364517_comment'></div>岂不哀哉。岂不哀哉。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_81_1364517_comment'></div>近者有隋氏。亦不克终厥初。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_82_1364517_comment'></div>隋高帝之有天下也。以六合为家。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_83_1364517_comment'></div>方将对越天人。传之万代。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_84_1364517_comment'></div>至炀帝承平。自以贵为天子。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_85_1364517_comment'></div>富有四海。欲穷宇宙之观。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_86_1364517_comment'></div>极游宴之乐。以为人主之急务也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_87_1364517_comment'></div>于是乃凿御渠。决黄河。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_88_1364517_comment'></div>自伊洛之閒而属之扬州。生人之力既弊。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_89_1364517_comment'></div>天地之藏又泄。炀帝方欣然以为得计。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_90_1364517_comment'></div>将后宫䌽女数百千人。遂泛龙舟。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_91_1364517_comment'></div>游三江五湖之閒。当其得意也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_92_1364517_comment'></div>视天下如脱屣尔。其后百姓<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_93_1364517", 1364517, "Clauses/187/Comments/0")'>骚弊</span>。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_93_1364517_comment'></div>灾变数兴。吏人贪暴。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_94_1364517_comment'></div>其政日乱。阴阳感怒。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_95_1364517_comment'></div>彗孛以出。炀帝不悟。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_96_1364517_comment'></div>自以为天下安于泰山。方率百万之师。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_97_1364517_comment'></div>而有事于辽东。当时山东。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_98_1364517_comment'></div>父子不得相保也。天厌暴政。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_99_1364517_comment'></div>人怀乱亡。故辽东之役未归。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_100_1364517_comment'></div>而中国之难已起。身死逆手。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_101_1364517_comment'></div>宗庙以隳。其故何哉。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_102_1364517_comment'></div>逆天人之理也。是以臣每察天人之际。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_103_1364517_comment'></div>观祸乱之由。迹帝王之事。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_104_1364517_comment'></div>念先师之说。昭然著明信不欺尔。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_105_1364517_comment'></div>不意陛下以大圣之虑。见天人之心。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_106_1364517_comment'></div>将欲调<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_107_1364517", 1364517, "Clauses/214/Comments/0")'>元气</span>之纲。返淳和之治。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_107_1364517_comment'></div>自非陛下合天地之德。有日月之明。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_108_1364517_comment'></div>谁能眇然远思。欲求大和于<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_109_1364517", 1364517, "Clauses/219/Comments/0")'>元气</span>哉。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_109_1364517_comment'></div>此昔者伏羲氏之所以本天人而为三皇首也。愚臣暗昧。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_110_1364517_comment'></div>不胜大愿。愿陛下为大唐建万代之策。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_111_1364517_comment'></div>恢三圣之功。传乎子孙。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_112_1364517_comment'></div>永作鸿业。千百年閒。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_113_1364517_comment'></div>使继文之主有所守也。非甚无道。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_114_1364517_comment'></div>不失厥嗣。陛下可不务之哉。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_115_1364517_comment'></div>臣伏见天皇大帝得天地之统。封于泰山。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_116_1364517_comment'></div>盛德大业。与天比崇矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_117_1364517_comment'></div>然尚未建明堂之宫。遂朝上帝。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_118_1364517_comment'></div>使万代鸿业。今犹阙然。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_119_1364517_comment'></div>臣愚意者。岂非天皇大帝知陛下圣明。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_120_1364517_comment'></div>必能起中兴之化。留此盛德。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_121_1364517_comment'></div>以发挥陛下哉。不然。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_122_1364517_comment'></div>何所与让而未作也。今陛下欲调<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_123_1364517", 1364517, "Clauses/247/Comments/0")'>元气</span>。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_123_1364517_comment'></div>睦人伦。跻俗仁寿。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_124_1364517_comment'></div>兴风礼让。舍此道也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_125_1364517_comment'></div>于何理哉。故臣不胜区区蝼蚁之诚思。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_126_1364517_comment'></div>愿陛下念先帝之休意。恢大唐之鸿业。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_127_1364517_comment'></div>于国南郊建立明堂。使宇宙黎元。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_128_1364517_comment'></div>遐荒夷貊。昆虫草木。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_129_1364517_comment'></div>天地鬼神。粲然知陛下方兴三皇五帝之事。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_130_1364517_comment'></div>与天下更始。不其盛哉。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_131_1364517_comment'></div>昔者黄帝合宫。有虞总章。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_132_1364517_comment'></div>唐尧衢室。夏后世室。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_133_1364517_comment'></div>群圣之所以调<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_134_1364517", 1364517, "Clauses/268/Comments/0")'>元气</span>理阴阳于此教也。臣虽未学。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_134_1364517_comment'></div>窃尝闻明堂之制也。有天地之则焉。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_135_1364517_comment'></div>有阴阳之统焉。二十四气八风十二月四时五行二十八宿。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_136_1364517_comment'></div>莫不率备。故顺其时月而为政。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_137_1364517_comment'></div>则风雨时。寒暑平。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_138_1364517_comment'></div>万物茂畅。五谷登稔。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_139_1364517_comment'></div><span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_140_1364517", 1364517, "Clauses/280/Comments/0")'>元气</span>不错。阴阳以和。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_140_1364517_comment'></div>逆其时而为政也。则水旱兴。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_141_1364517_comment'></div>疾疫起。虫螟为害。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_142_1364517_comment'></div>霜雹成灾。阴阳不和。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_143_1364517_comment'></div><span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_144_1364517", 1364517, "Clauses/288/Comments/0")'>元气</span>以错。故昔者圣人所以为教之大业也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_144_1364517_comment'></div>是以臣愿陛下为大唐建万代之策者。意在兹乎。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_145_1364517_comment'></div>意在兹乎。陛下若不以臣微而废其言。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_146_1364517_comment'></div>乞以臣此章与三公九卿贤士大夫议之于庭。倘事便于今。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_147_1364517_comment'></div>道不违古。即请陛下徵天下鸿生钜儒。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_148_1364517_comment'></div>贤良豪杰之士。博通古今皇王政理之术者。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_149_1364517_comment'></div>与之按周礼月令而建之。臣必知天下庶人子来。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_150_1364517_comment'></div>不日而成也。乃正月孟春。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_151_1364517_comment'></div>陛下乘銮舆。驾苍龙。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_152_1364517_comment'></div>载青旂。佩苍玉。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_153_1364517_comment'></div>从三公九卿贤士大夫。鸿儒硕老衣冠之伦。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_154_1364517_comment'></div>朝于青阳左个。负斧扆。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_155_1364517_comment'></div>凭玉几。南面以听天下之政。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_156_1364517_comment'></div>于是遂发大号。宣布四方。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_157_1364517_comment'></div>使各顺十二月之令。无敢有违。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_158_1364517_comment'></div>乃命太史守典。奉法司天。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_159_1364517_comment'></div>日月星辰之行。无失经纪。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_160_1364517_comment'></div>以初为常。陛下遂躬藉田亲蚕。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_161_1364517_comment'></div>以劝天下之农桑。养三老五更。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_162_1364517_comment'></div>以教天下之孝悌。明讼恤狱。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_163_1364517_comment'></div>以息天下之<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_164_1364517", 1364517, "Clauses/328/Comments/0")'>淫刑</span>。除害去虐。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_164_1364517_comment'></div>以正天下之仁寿。修文尚德。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_165_1364517_comment'></div>以止天下之干戈。察孝兴廉。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_166_1364517_comment'></div>以除天下之贪吏。矜寡孤独。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_167_1364517_comment'></div>疲癃羸老。不能自存者。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_168_1364517_comment'></div>赈恤之。后宫美人。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_169_1364517_comment'></div>非三妃九嫔八十一御女之数者。出嫁之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_170_1364517_comment'></div>珠玉锦绣雕琢技巧之饰。非益于理者。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_171_1364517_comment'></div>悉弃之。巫鬼淫祀。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_172_1364517_comment'></div>诳惑良人者。禁杀之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_173_1364517_comment'></div>陛下务以至诚。躬服质素。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_174_1364517_comment'></div>以为天下先。愚臣以为不出数年之閒。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_175_1364517_comment'></div>将见太平之化也。天人之际既洽。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_176_1364517_comment'></div>鬼神之望允塞。然后作雅乐。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_177_1364517_comment'></div>洁粢盛。宗祀天皇于明堂以配上帝。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_178_1364517_comment'></div>使万国各以其职来祭。岂不休哉。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_179_1364517_comment'></div>臣伏惟陛下至德明圣。未有能越行此道者也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_180_1364517_comment'></div>故臣窃以为此化一成。则人伦之道自睦。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_181_1364517_comment'></div>刑罚之原自息。兵革之事不兴。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_182_1364517_comment'></div>还淳之途可见。仁寿礼让。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_183_1364517_comment'></div>稼穑农桑。不言而自致也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_184_1364517_comment'></div>是以贱臣未得为陛下一二论之。何者。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_185_1364517_comment'></div>圣人之教在于可大可久者。故臣欲陛下<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_186_1364517", 1364517, "Clauses/373/Comments/0")'>振领提纲</span>。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_186_1364517_comment'></div>使天下自理也。然臣窃独有私恨。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_187_1364517_comment'></div>陛下方欲兴崇大化。而不知国家太学之废。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_188_1364517_comment'></div>积岁月矣。堂宇芜秽。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_189_1364517_comment'></div>殆无人踪。诗书礼乐。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_190_1364517_comment'></div>䍐闻习者。陛下明诏尚未及之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_191_1364517_comment'></div>愚臣所以有私恨也。臣闻天子立太学。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_192_1364517_comment'></div>可以聚天下英贤。为政教之首。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_193_1364517_comment'></div>故君臣上下之礼。于是兴焉。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_194_1364517_comment'></div>揖让樽俎之节。于此生焉。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_195_1364517_comment'></div>是以天子得贤臣。由此道也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_196_1364517_comment'></div>今则荒废。委而不论。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_197_1364517_comment'></div>而欲睦人伦。兴礼让。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_198_1364517_comment'></div>失之于本。而求之于末。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_199_1364517_comment'></div>岂可得哉。况君子三年不为礼。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_200_1364517_comment'></div>礼必坏。三年不为乐。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_201_1364517_comment'></div>乐必崩。柰何天子之政而轻礼乐哉。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_202_1364517_comment'></div>臣所以独窃有私恨者也。陛下何不诏天下冑子。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_203_1364517_comment'></div>使归太学而习业乎。斯亦国家之大务也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_204_1364517_comment'></div>臣愚蒙所言。事未曲尽者。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_205_1364517_comment'></div>恐烦圣览。必陛下恕臣昏愚。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_206_1364517_comment'></div>请赐他日。别具奏闻。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_207_1364517_comment'></div></div><div id='poem_sentence_208_1364517_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=684&endYear=684')">684年</a>　在洛阳，时高宗灵驾将西还长安归葬，子昂诣阙上书谏止。作品：《谏灵驾入京书》<div id='poem_1364514' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1364514' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1364514?labeling=true' target='_blank'>谏灵驾入京书</a><span class='authorDate'>（684年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 唐初 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(20887, "唐初", "陈子昂", "poem_title_1364514")'>陈子昂</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1364514_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1364514'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1364514'>梓州射洪县草莽愚臣陈子昂谨顿首冒死献书阙下。臣闻明主不恶<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_0_1364514", 1364514, "Clauses/1/Comments/0")'>切直</span>之言以纳忠。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1364514_comment'></div>烈士不惮死亡之诛以极谏。故有非常之策者。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1364514_comment'></div>必待非常之时。有非常之时者。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1364514_comment'></div>必待非常之主。然后<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_3_1364514", 1364514, "Clauses/7/Comments/0")'>危言正色</span>。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1364514_comment'></div><span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_4_1364514", 1364514, "Clauses/8/Comments/0")'>抗议</span>直辞。赴汤镬而不回。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1364514_comment'></div>至诛夷而无悔。岂徒欲<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_5_1364514", 1364514, "Clauses/11/Comments/0")'>诡世</span>誇俗。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1364514_comment'></div>厌生乐死者哉。实以为杀身之害小。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1364514_comment'></div>存国之利大。故审计定议而甘心焉。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1364514_comment'></div>况乎得非常之时。遇非常之主。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1364514_comment'></div>言必获用。死亦何惊。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1364514_comment'></div>千载之迹。将不朽于今日矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1364514_comment'></div>伏惟大行皇帝遗天下。弃群臣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1364514_comment'></div>万国震惊。百姓<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_12_1364514", 1364514, "Clauses/25/Comments/0")'>屠裂</span>。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1364514_comment'></div>陛下以<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_13_1364514", 1364514, "Clauses/26/Comments/0")'>徇齐</span>之圣。承宗庙之重。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1364514_comment'></div>天下之望。喁喁如也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1364514_comment'></div>莫不冀蒙圣化。以保馀年。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1364514_comment'></div>太平之主。将复在于今日矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_16_1364514_comment'></div>况皇太后又以文母之贤。协轩宫之耀。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_17_1364514_comment'></div>军国大事。遗诏决之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_18_1364514_comment'></div>唐虞之际。于斯盛矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_19_1364514_comment'></div>臣伏见诏书。<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_20_1364514", 1364514, "Clauses/41/Comments/0")'>梓宫</span>将迁坐京师。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_20_1364514_comment'></div>銮舆亦欲陪幸。计非上策。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_21_1364514_comment'></div>智者失图。庙堂未闻有骨鲠之谋。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_22_1364514_comment'></div>朝廷多见有顺从之议。愚臣窃惑。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_23_1364514_comment'></div>以为过矣。伏自思之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_24_1364514_comment'></div>生圣日。沐皇风。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_25_1364514_comment'></div>摩顶至踵。莫非亭育。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_26_1364514_comment'></div>不能历丹凤。抵濯龙。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_27_1364514_comment'></div>北面玉阶。东望金屋。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_28_1364514_comment'></div>抗音而正谏者。圣王之罪人也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_29_1364514_comment'></div>所以不顾万死。乞献一言。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_30_1364514_comment'></div>愿蒙听览。甘就鼎镬。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_31_1364514_comment'></div>伏惟陛下察之。臣闻秦据咸阳之时。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_32_1364514_comment'></div>汉都长安之日。山河为固。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_33_1364514_comment'></div>天下服矣。然犹北假胡宛之利。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_34_1364514_comment'></div>南资巴蜀之饶。自渭入河。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_35_1364514_comment'></div>转关东之粟。踰沙绝漠。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_36_1364514_comment'></div>致山西之宝。然后能削平天下。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_37_1364514_comment'></div><span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_38_1364514", 1364514, "Clauses/76/Comments/0")'>弹压</span>诸侯。长辔利策。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_38_1364514_comment'></div>横制宇宙。今则不然。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_39_1364514_comment'></div>燕代迫匈奴之侵。巴陇婴吐蕃之患。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_40_1364514_comment'></div>西蜀疲老。千里赢粮。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_41_1364514_comment'></div>北国<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_42_1364514", 1364514, "Clauses/84/Comments/0")'>丁男</span>。十五乘塞。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_42_1364514_comment'></div>岁月奔命。其弊不堪。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_43_1364514_comment'></div>秦之首尾。今为阙矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_44_1364514_comment'></div>即所馀者。独三辅之閒尔。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_45_1364514_comment'></div>顷遭荒馑。人被荐饥。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_46_1364514_comment'></div>自河而西。无非赤地。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_47_1364514_comment'></div>循陇以北。䍐逢青草。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_48_1364514_comment'></div>莫不父兄转徙。妻子流离。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_49_1364514_comment'></div>委家丧业。膏原润莽。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_50_1364514_comment'></div>此朝廷之所备知也。赖以宗庙神灵。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_51_1364514_comment'></div>皇天悔祸。去岁薄稔。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_52_1364514_comment'></div>前秋稍登。使<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_53_1364514", 1364514, "Clauses/107/Comments/0")'>羸饿</span>之馀。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_53_1364514_comment'></div>得保<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_54_1364514", 1364514, "Clauses/108/Comments/0")'>沈命</span>。天下幸甚。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_54_1364514_comment'></div>可谓厚矣。然而流人未返。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_55_1364514_comment'></div>田野尚芜。白骨纵横。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_56_1364514_comment'></div>阡陌无主。至于蓄积。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_57_1364514_comment'></div>犹可哀伤。陛下不料其难。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_58_1364514_comment'></div>贵从先意。遂欲长驱大驾。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_59_1364514_comment'></div>按节秦京。千乘万骑。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_60_1364514_comment'></div>何方取给。况山陵初制。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_61_1364514_comment'></div><span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_62_1364514", 1364514, "Clauses/124/Comments/0")'>穿复</span>未央。土木工匠。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_62_1364514_comment'></div>必资徒役。今欲率疲弊之众。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_63_1364514_comment'></div>兴数万之军。徵发近畿。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_64_1364514_comment'></div>鞭朴羸老。凿山采石。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_65_1364514_comment'></div>驱以就功。但恐春作无时。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_66_1364514_comment'></div>秋成绝望。凋瘵<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_67_1364514", 1364514, "Clauses/135/Comments/0")'>遗噍</span>。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_67_1364514_comment'></div>再罹饥苦。倘不堪弊。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_68_1364514_comment'></div>必有逋逃。子来之颂。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_69_1364514_comment'></div>其将何词以述。此亦宗庙之大机。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_70_1364514_comment'></div>不可不深图也。况国无<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_71_1364514", 1364514, "Clauses/143/Comments/0")'>兼岁</span>之储。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_71_1364514_comment'></div>家鲜<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_72_1364514", 1364514, "Clauses/144/Comments/0")'>匝时</span>之蓄。一旬不雨。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_72_1364514_comment'></div>犹可深忧。忽加水旱。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_73_1364514_comment'></div>人何以济。陛下不深察始终。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_74_1364514_comment'></div>独违群议。臣恐三辅之弊。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_75_1364514_comment'></div>不止如前日矣。且天子以四海为家。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_76_1364514_comment'></div>圣人包六合为宇。历观邃古。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_77_1364514_comment'></div>以至于今。何尝不以三王为仁。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_78_1364514_comment'></div>五帝为圣。故虽周公制作。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_79_1364514_comment'></div>夫子著名。莫不祖述尧舜。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_80_1364514_comment'></div>宪章文武。为百王之鸿烈。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_81_1364514_comment'></div>作千载之雄图。然而舜死陟方。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_82_1364514_comment'></div>葬苍梧而不返。禹会群后。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_83_1364514_comment'></div>殁稽山而永终。岂其爱蛮夷之乡而鄙中国哉。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_84_1364514_comment'></div>实将欲示圣人之无外也。故能使坟籍以为美谈。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_85_1364514_comment'></div>帝王以为高范。况我巍巍大圣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_86_1364514_comment'></div>轹帝登皇。日月所临。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_87_1364514_comment'></div>莫不率俾。何独秦丰之地。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_88_1364514_comment'></div>可置山陵。河洛之都。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_89_1364514_comment'></div>不堪<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_90_1364514", 1364514, "Clauses/180/Comments/0")'>园寝</span>。陛下岂可不察之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_90_1364514_comment'></div>愚臣窃为陛下惜也。且景山崇丽。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_91_1364514_comment'></div>秀冠群峰。北对嵩邙。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_92_1364514_comment'></div>西望汝海。居祝融之故地。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_93_1364514_comment'></div>连太昊之遗墟。帝王图迹。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_94_1364514_comment'></div>纵横左右。园陵之美。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_95_1364514_comment'></div>复何加焉。陛下曾未察之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_96_1364514_comment'></div>谓其不可。愚臣鄙见。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_97_1364514_comment'></div>良足尚矣。况瀍涧之中。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_98_1364514_comment'></div>天地交会。北有太行之险。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_99_1364514_comment'></div>南有宛叶之饶。东压江淮。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_100_1364514_comment'></div>食湖海之利。西驰崤渑。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_101_1364514_comment'></div>据关河之宝。以聪明之主。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_102_1364514_comment'></div>养淳粹之人。天下和平。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_103_1364514_comment'></div>恭己正南面而巳。陛下不思瀍洛之壮观。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_104_1364514_comment'></div>关陇之荒芜。遂欲弃太山之安。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_105_1364514_comment'></div>履焦原之险。忘神器之大宝。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_106_1364514_comment'></div>徇曾闵之小节。愚臣闇昧。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_107_1364514_comment'></div>以为甚也。陛下何不览诤臣之策。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_108_1364514_comment'></div>采行路之谣。咨谋太后。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_109_1364514_comment'></div>平章宰辅。使苍生之望。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_110_1364514_comment'></div>知有所安。天下岂不幸甚。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_111_1364514_comment'></div>昔者平王迁周。光武都洛。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_112_1364514_comment'></div>山陵寝庙。不在东京。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_113_1364514_comment'></div>宗社坟茔。并居西土。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_114_1364514_comment'></div>然而春秋美为始王。汉书载为代祖。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_115_1364514_comment'></div>岂其不愿孝哉。何圣贤褒贬。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_116_1364514_comment'></div>于斯滥矣。实以时有不可。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_117_1364514_comment'></div>事有必然。盖欲遗小存大。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_118_1364514_comment'></div>去祸归福。圣人所以为贵也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_119_1364514_comment'></div>夫小不忍则乱大谋。仲尼之至诫。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_120_1364514_comment'></div>愿陛下察之。若以臣愚不用。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_121_1364514_comment'></div>朝议遂行。臣恐关陇之忧。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_122_1364514_comment'></div>无时休息。臣又闻太原蓄钜万之仓。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_123_1364514_comment'></div>洛口积天下之粟。国家之宝<span class='inlineComment2'>（一作资）</span>。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_124_1364514_comment'></div>斯为大矣。今欲舍而不顾。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_125_1364514_comment'></div>背以长驱。使有识惊嗟。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_126_1364514_comment'></div>天下失望。倘鼠窃狗盗。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_127_1364514_comment'></div>万一不图。西入陜州之郊。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_128_1364514_comment'></div>东犯武牢之镇。盗敖仓一抔之粟。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_129_1364514_comment'></div>陛下何以遏之。此天下之至机。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_130_1364514_comment'></div>不可不深惧也。虽则盗未旋踵。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_131_1364514_comment'></div>诛刑已及。灭其九族。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_132_1364514_comment'></div>焚其妻子。泣辜虽恨。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_133_1364514_comment'></div>将何及焉。故曰先谋后事者逸。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_134_1364514_comment'></div>先事后图者失。国之利器。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_135_1364514_comment'></div>不可以示人。斯言不徒设也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_136_1364514_comment'></div>愿陛下念之。臣西蜀野人。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_137_1364514_comment'></div>本在林薮。幸属交泰。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_138_1364514_comment'></div>得游王国。故知不在其位者。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_139_1364514_comment'></div>不谋其政。亦欲退身岩谷。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_140_1364514_comment'></div>灭迹朝廷。窃感娄敬委辂。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_141_1364514_comment'></div>干非其议。图汉策于万全。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_142_1364514_comment'></div>取鸿名于千古。臣何独怯。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_143_1364514_comment'></div>而不及之哉。所以敢触龙鳞。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_144_1364514_comment'></div>死而无恨。庶万有一中。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_145_1364514_comment'></div>或垂察焉。臣子昂诚惶诚恐顿首顿首死罪死罪。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_146_1364514_comment'></div></div><div id='poem_sentence_147_1364514_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=684&endYear=684')">684年</a>　在洛阳，田逸人见寻，子昂回访不遇题诗于壁。作品：《酬田逸人见寻不遇题隐居里壁》<span class='inlineComment2'>（田逸人，名未详。按：徐谱据田游岩未仕系此诗于调露元年子昂游太子时，见徐文茂《陈子昂论考》，上海古籍出版社2002年版29页。恐非是。诗云：“游人献书去，薄暮返灵台。传道神仙友，青囊卖卜来。”子昂调露元年初入京游太学，似未有献书事。且田游岩行状，亦非青囊卖卜者流。彭谱认为此田逸人当是另一人，非田游岩。故仍从彭说，系此诗于本年。）</span><div id='poem_34727' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_34727' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/34727?labeling=true' target='_blank'>酬田逸人游岩见寻不遇题隐居里壁</a><span class='authorDate'>（684年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 唐初 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(20887, "唐初", "陈子昂", "poem_title_34727")'>陈子昂</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'>五言排律</div></div><div id='poem_title_34727_comment'></div><div class='titleComment' id='poem_allusion_34727'><span class='label'>引用典故：</span><span class='link' onclick='ShowAllusionComment(2730, "poem_allusion_34727")'>闻莺</span>　<span class='link' onclick='ShowAllusionComment(2748, "poem_allusion_34727")'>题凤</span>　<span class='link' onclick='ShowAllusionComment(3038, "poem_allusion_34727")'>缝掖</span>　<span class='link' onclick='ShowAllusionComment(4513, "poem_allusion_34727")'>灵台</span>　<span class='link' onclick='ShowAllusionComment(4572, "poem_allusion_34727")'>洛阳才</span>　<span class='link' onclick='ShowAllusionComment(7036, "poem_allusion_34727")'>青囊</span></div><div id='poem_allusion_34727_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_34727'><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_34727'>游人献书去，薄暮返<span class='link' onclick='ShowAllusionComment(2730, "poem_sentence_2_34727")'>闻莺</span>忽相访，<span class='link' onclick='ShowAllusionComment(2748, "poem_sentence_2_34727")'>题凤</span>久裴回。<div id='poem_sentence_2_34727_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_3_34727'>石髓空盈握，<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_3_34727", 34727, "Clauses/7/Comments/0")'>金经</span>秘不开。<div id='poem_sentence_3_34727_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_4_34727'>还疑<span class='link' onclick='ShowAllusionComment(3038, "poem_sentence_4_34727")'>缝掖</span>子，复似<span class='link' onclick='ShowAllusionComment(4572, "poem_sentence_4_34727")'>洛阳才</span>。<div id='poem_sentence_4_34727_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_5_34727'></div><div id='poem_sentence_5_34727_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=684&endYear=684')">684年</a>　在洛阳，子昂上《谏灵驾入京书》，武后奇其才，召见金华殿，擢麟台正字。子昂释褐。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=684&endYear=684')">684年</a>　居官东都，太子司直宗秦客宴宾客于金谷亭，子昂席上赋麈尾。作品：《麈尾赋》<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=684&endYear=684')">684年</a>　居官东都，是年赵贞固年二十七，褐衣游洛阳，与子昂、卢藏用、司马承祯，魏元忠、陆馀庆、宋之问等交游，士争向慕。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=685&endYear=685')">685年</a>　居官东都，于解三处见东方虬《咏孤桐篇》，感其雅制，慨然作《修竹篇并序》以传示知音。并于序中陈述其诗歌主张，开唐诗革新之先。<span class='inlineComment2'>（徐谱以为此诗当为本年及稍前后之作，姑系本年。解三，徐谱以为即解琬，《旧唐书》卷一九四、《新唐书》卷一三〇有传。）</span><div id='poem_34730' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_34730' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/34730?labeling=true' target='_blank'>与东方左史虬修竹篇<span class='inlineComment2'>（并书）</span></a><span class='authorDate'>（685年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 唐初 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(20887, "唐初", "陈子昂", "poem_title_34730")'>陈子昂</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_34730_comment'></div><div class='titleComment' id='poem_preface_34730'>并书：东方公足下，文章道弊，五百年矣。汉魏风骨，晋宋莫传，然而文献有可徵者。仆尝暇时观齐梁间诗，彩丽竞繁，而兴寄都绝，每以永叹，思古人，尝恐逦逶颓靡（尝恐逶迤颓靡），风雅不作，以耿耿也。一昨于解三处，见明公咏《孤桐篇》，骨气端翔，因情顿挫。光英朗练（光映朗练），有金石声，遂用洗心饰视，发挥幽郁，不图正始知音，复睹于兹。可使建安作者，相视而笑。解君云、张茂先、何敬祖、东方生与其比肩，仆亦以为知言也。故感叹雅制，作《修竹诗》一首，当有知音已传示之。</div><div id='poem_preface_34730_comment'></div><div class='titleComment' id='poem_allusion_34730'><span class='label'>引用典故：</span><span class='link' onclick='ShowAllusionComment(1565, "poem_allusion_34730")'>丹凤城</span>　<span class='link' onclick='ShowAllusionComment(5710, "poem_allusion_34730")'>学凤鸣</span></div><div id='poem_allusion_34730_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_34730'><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_34730'><span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_0_34730", 34730, "Clauses/0/Comments/1")'>龙种</span><span "Clauses/2/Comments/0")'>崇崒</span>，烟雨下<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_1_34730", 34730, "Clauses/3/Comments/0")'>微冥</span>。<div id='poem_sentence_1_34730_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_2_34730'>夜闻鼯鼠叫，昼聒泉鹤声。<div id='poem_sentence_2_34730_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_3_34730'>春风正<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_3_34730", 34730, "Clauses/6/Comments/0")'>淡荡</span>，白露已清泠。<div id='poem_sentence_3_34730_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_4_34730'>哀响激<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_4_34730", 34730, id='poem_sentence_5_34730_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_6_34730'>岂不厌凝洌，羞比春木荣。<div id='poem_sentence_6_34730_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_7_34730'>春木有<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_7_34730", 34730, "Clauses/14/Comments/0")'>荣歇</span>，此节无凋零。<div id='poem_sentence_7_34730_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_8_34730'>始愿与金石，终古保坚贞。<div id='poem_sentence_8_34730_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_9_34730'>不意伶伦子，吹之<span class='link' onclick='ShowAllusionComment(5710, "poem_sentence_9_34730")'>学凤鸣</span>。<div id='poem_sentence_9_34730_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_10_34730'>遂偶云和瑟，张乐奏天庭。<div id='poem_sentence_10_34730_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_11_34730'>妙曲方千变，箫韶亦九成。<div id='poem_sentence_11_34730_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_12_34730'>信蒙雕斲美，常愿事仙灵。<div id='poem_sentence_12_34730_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_13_34730_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_14_34730'>结交<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_14_34730", 34730,
