id='poem_sentence_16_34730_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_17_34730'>永随众仙逝，三山游玉京。<div id='poem_sentence_17_34730_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_18_34730'></div><div id='poem_sentence_18_34730_comment'></div></div><div class='poemComment' id='poem_comment_34730'><a href='javascript: ShowPoemComment(34730)'>评注</a><span class='inlineComment4'>（点击查看或隐藏评注）</span></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=685&endYear=685')">685年11月16日</a>　居官东都，十一月十六日，武后召见，赐纸笔，令于中书省条上利害，子昂对出使、牧宰、人机三事。作品：《上军国利害事三条》<div id='poem_1364501' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1364501' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1364501?labeling=true' target='_blank'>上军国利害事<span class='inlineComment2'>（三条）</span><span style='margin: 0 0.5em'> 其三 </span>人机</a><span class='authorDate'>（685年11月16日）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 唐初 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(20887, "唐初", "陈子昂", "poem_title_1364501")'>陈子昂</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1364501_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1364501'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1364501'>臣闻天下有危机。祸福因之而生。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1364501_comment'></div>机静则有福。机动则有祸。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1364501_comment'></div>天下百姓是也。夫百姓安则乐其生。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1364501_comment'></div>不安则轻其死。轻其死。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1364501_comment'></div>则无所不至也。故曰人不可使穷。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1364501_comment'></div>穷之则奸宄生。人不可数动。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1364501_comment'></div>动之则灾变起。奸宄不息。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1364501_comment'></div>灾变日兴。叛逆乘衅。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1364501_comment'></div>天下乱矣。当今天下百姓。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1364501_comment'></div>虽未穷困。军旅之弊。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1364501_comment'></div>不得安者。向五六年矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1364501_comment'></div>夫妻不得相保。父子不得相养。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1364501_comment'></div>自剑以南。爰至河陇秦凉之閒。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1364501_comment'></div>山东则有青徐曹汴。河北则有沧瀛恒赵。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1364501_comment'></div>莫不或被饥荒。或遭水旱。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1364501_comment'></div>兵役转输。疾疫死亡。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1364501_comment'></div>流离分散。十至四五。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_16_1364501_comment'></div>可谓不安矣。幸得陛下以仁圣之恩。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_17_1364501_comment'></div>悯其失业。所在边境有兵战之役。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_18_1364501_comment'></div>一切且停。遂使穷困之人。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_19_1364501_comment'></div>尚得与妻子相见。父兄相保。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_20_1364501_comment'></div>各复其业。获以救穷。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_21_1364501_comment'></div>人心稍安。殆半年矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_22_1364501_comment'></div>天下可谓幸甚。愚臣窃贺陛下得天下之机。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_23_1364501_comment'></div>能密静之。非陛下至圣大明。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_24_1364501_comment'></div>不能如此也。愚臣今所以为陛下更论天下之危机者。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_25_1364501_comment'></div>恐将相有贪夷狄之利。又说陛下以广地彊武为威。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_26_1364501_comment'></div>谋动甲兵。以事边塞。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_27_1364501_comment'></div>陛下或未知天下有危机。万一听之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_28_1364501_comment'></div>臣惧机失祸搆。则天下有不可柰何也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_29_1364501_comment'></div>诗不云乎。人亦劳止。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_30_1364501_comment'></div>汔可小康。惠此中国。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_31_1364501_comment'></div>以绥四方。故臣愿陛下垂衣裳。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_32_1364501_comment'></div>修文德。去刑罚。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_33_1364501_comment'></div>劝农桑。以息天下之人。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_34_1364501_comment'></div>务与之共安。然后使遐荒蛮夷。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_35_1364501_comment'></div>自知中国有圣人。重译而入贡。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_36_1364501_comment'></div>愚臣窃以为当今天下之大计也。伏惟陛下念之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_37_1364501_comment'></div>近者隋炀帝不知天下有危机。自以为威德广大。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_38_1364501_comment'></div>欲建万代之业。动天下之众。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_39_1364501_comment'></div>殚万人之力。兵役相仍。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_40_1364501_comment'></div>转输不绝。北讨胡貊。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_41_1364501_comment'></div>东伐辽人。于是天下百姓穷困。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_42_1364501_comment'></div>人不堪命。机动祸搆。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_43_1364501_comment'></div>遂丧天下。此是不知天下有危机。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_44_1364501_comment'></div>而信贪佞之臣。冀收夷狄之利。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_45_1364501_comment'></div>卒以灭亡者也。隋氏之失。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_46_1364501_comment'></div>可以<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_47_1364501", 1364501, "Clauses/94/Comments/0")'>殷鉴</span>。岂不大哉。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_47_1364501_comment'></div>伏惟陛下察之。国家所伐吐蕃。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_48_1364501_comment'></div>有大失策。中国之众。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_49_1364501_comment'></div>半天下受其弊。然遂事不谏。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_50_1364501_comment'></div>当复何言。陛下不以臣愚。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_51_1364501_comment'></div>刍荛可采。一赐召臣至玉陛。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_52_1364501_comment'></div>得以口论。天下幸甚。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_53_1364501_comment'></div>臣子昂言。臣本下愚。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_54_1364501_comment'></div>未知大体。今月十六日。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_55_1364501_comment'></div>特奉恩敕。赐臣纸笔。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_56_1364501_comment'></div>遣于中书言天下利害。天之降命。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_57_1364501_comment'></div>敢不对扬。而孤负圣恩。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_58_1364501_comment'></div>万一无补。死罪死罪。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_59_1364501_comment'></div>谨率愚见。封进以闻。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_60_1364501_comment'></div>尘听玉阶。伏阙累息。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_61_1364501_comment'></div>臣子昂诚惶诚恐顿首顿首。谨言。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_62_1364501_comment'></div></div><div id='poem_sentence_63_1364501_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=685&endYear=685')">685年</a>　居官东都，于乔偘处阅晋人洪崖子《鸾鸟诗》，与诸君属和，并撰序。作品：《洪崖子鸾鸟诗序》<span class='inlineComment2'>（徐谱以为此诗序当为本年及稍前后之作，姑系本年。乔侃：《旧唐书》卷一九〇载，乔侃为乔知之第。）</span><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=685&endYear=685')">685年</a>　居官东都，为故朝议大夫杨越作碑铭。作品：《唐故朝议大夫梓州长史杨府君碑》<span class='inlineComment2'>（徐谱以此文作于守秘书正字前期，姑系本年。）</span><div id='poem_1364544' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1364544' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1364544?labeling=true' target='_blank'>唐故朝议大夫梓州长史杨府君碑铭</a><span class='authorDate'>（685年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 唐初 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(20887, "唐初", "陈子昂", "poem_title_1364544")'>陈子昂</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1364544_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1364544'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1364544'>君讳越。字复圭。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1364544_comment'></div>宏农仙掌人也。其先帝高辛氏之裔。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1364544_comment'></div>周有天下。晋授其封。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1364544_comment'></div>至宣公伯乔。早基杨国。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1364544_comment'></div>若乃彤弓旅矢。巨鬯<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_4_1364544", 1364544, "Clauses/9/Comments/0")'>赤茀</span>。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1364544_comment'></div>则礼命之。乐歌之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1364544_comment'></div>崇天王之宠光。保元侯之休祉。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1364544_comment'></div>其后十六代。有杨宝者。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1364544_comment'></div>天锡黄鸟。授以白环。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1364544_comment'></div>若曰命君子孙。世登三事。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1364544_comment'></div>迨震秉彪赐。四代五公。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1364544_comment'></div>烈光昭于汉室。盛德充于海内。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1364544_comment'></div>金圭铭鼎。至今为宏农世家也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1364544_comment'></div>高祖椿。魏尚书右仆射开府仪同三司司徒公。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1364544_comment'></div>进位太保。加侍中。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1364544_comment'></div>给后部鼓吹。致仕归邑。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1364544_comment'></div>赐安车驷马。传制二人。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_16_1364544_comment'></div>可谓国之元老。帝之师臣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_17_1364544_comment'></div>功成名遂。社稷之宝。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_18_1364544_comment'></div>曾祖思善。齐通直散骑常侍。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_19_1364544_comment'></div>赠中书侍郎。祖敬通。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_20_1364544_comment'></div>镇远将军郑州治中邛州别驾。父君同。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_21_1364544_comment'></div>随蒲州芮城县令。皆国书旧史。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_22_1364544_comment'></div>烈乎名节。公即芮城府君之第二子也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_23_1364544_comment'></div>少而冲嶷。苦节真素。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_24_1364544_comment'></div>礼非玉帛。室有琴书。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_25_1364544_comment'></div>闻少连之风而悦之。庶乎身中权。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_26_1364544_comment'></div>行<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_27_1364544", 1364544, "Clauses/54/Comments/0")'>中清</span>。上以察乎道。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_27_1364544_comment'></div>下以敦乎物。不应州郡之命。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_28_1364544_comment'></div>而有金玉之心。尝叹曰。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_29_1364544_comment'></div>以明月珠。弹千仞雀。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_30_1364544_comment'></div>吾不能也。于是观宝龟之象。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_31_1364544_comment'></div>心灭<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_32_1364544", 1364544, "Clauses/64/Comments/0")'>朵颐</span>。探金虎之爻。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_32_1364544_comment'></div>志存<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_33_1364544", 1364544, "Clauses/66/Comments/0")'>幽履</span>。遂去家遁于嵩山。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_33_1364544_comment'></div>经十馀年。丹山白云之志眇然矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_34_1364544_comment'></div>属太宗文武圣皇帝初临天下。物色幽人。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_35_1364544_comment'></div>焚山榜道。网罗遗逸。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_36_1364544_comment'></div>君子若曰。天下有道。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_37_1364544_comment'></div>可以见矣。于是始以<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_38_1364544", 1364544, "Clauses/77/Comments/0")'>角巾</span>应命。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_38_1364544_comment'></div>褐衣诣阙。陈大道之宏谟。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_39_1364544_comment'></div>论至言之阃奥。帝曰俞。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_40_1364544_comment'></div>尔言乃可厎行。若岁大旱。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_41_1364544_comment'></div>用汝作霖雨。今南山近塞。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_42_1364544_comment'></div>北漠连胡。石州边烽。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_43_1364544_comment'></div>皇化未谧。汝往钦哉。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_44_1364544_comment'></div>辑乃人。御乃敌。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_45_1364544_comment'></div>以息匈奴之患。始解褐。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_46_1364544_comment'></div>授石州方山县令。樽俎在堂。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_47_1364544_comment'></div>干旄在阶。布大信于獯戎。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_48_1364544_comment'></div>示折冲于衽席。威名震曜。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_49_1364544_comment'></div>乃升闻也。有敕徵授宪台监察御史。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_50_1364544_comment'></div>绣衣始拜。珥笔升朝。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_51_1364544_comment'></div>台阁以之生风。豪贵由其敛手。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_52_1364544_comment'></div>又敕直中书待制。未几。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_53_1364544_comment'></div>又迁秘书郎。直中书省如故。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_54_1364544_comment'></div>游凤凰之池。观蓬莱之府。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_55_1364544_comment'></div>是天下之<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_56_1364544", 1364544, "Clauses/112/Comments/0")'>荣践</span>也。又转宗正寺丞。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_56_1364544_comment'></div>居岁馀。帝思南史之才。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_57_1364544_comment'></div>将崇东观之美。又迁起居郎。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_58_1364544_comment'></div>加骑都尉。龙朔中。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_59_1364544_comment'></div>天子将观兵于东夷。以复先帝之业。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_60_1364544_comment'></div>凡居中者。多出守旁郡。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_61_1364544_comment'></div>是岁授公朝散大夫。除冀州司马。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_62_1364544_comment'></div>又转魏州司马。皆知州事。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_63_1364544_comment'></div>于时天下雌韩而雄魏。壮武而柔文。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_64_1364544_comment'></div>公始厌承明。初临外郡。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_65_1364544_comment'></div>探丸垩面。犯禁崇奸。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_66_1364544_comment'></div>欲尝朱博之能。以观龚遂之政。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_67_1364544_comment'></div>公深钩潜往。英机立断。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_68_1364544_comment'></div>短服<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_69_1364544", 1364544, "Clauses/138/Comments/0")'>赭裾</span>。于是乎理。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_69_1364544_comment'></div>麟德初兼梓州长史。盖在华之南区。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_70_1364544_comment'></div>彭之北鄙。人豪俗侈。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_71_1364544_comment'></div>政削公朘。攒六国之遗氓。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_72_1364544_comment'></div>杂三巴之奥壤。公下车问俗。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_73_1364544_comment'></div>观风立政。先之礼让。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_74_1364544_comment'></div>教以诗书。抑<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_75_1364544", 1364544, "Clauses/151/Comments/0")'>浮窳</span>。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_75_1364544_comment'></div>禁<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_76_1364544", 1364544, "Clauses/152/Comments/0")'>蟊食</span>。至于堂叩钟磬。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_76_1364544_comment'></div>家擅山川。莫不为之节制。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_77_1364544_comment'></div>行其典礼。来暮之颂。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_78_1364544_comment'></div>复起于斯。时高宗大帝方接千载之统。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_79_1364544_comment'></div>升中太山。玉帛云趋。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_80_1364544_comment'></div>朝者万国。公预陪金跸。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_81_1364544_comment'></div>侍拜瑶坛。白云既封。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_82_1364544_comment'></div>皇庆斯洽。加朝散<span class='inlineComment2'>（一作议）</span>大夫。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_83_1364544_comment'></div>馀官如故。东山拜命。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_84_1364544_comment'></div>西驾未归。逢太岁之临辰。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_85_1364544_comment'></div>感殷楹之梦奠。遇疾薨于官舍。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_86_1364544_comment'></div>时年六十四。呜呼哀哉。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_87_1364544_comment'></div>遗令薄葬。不藏珠玉。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_88_1364544_comment'></div>唯孝经一卷。尧典一篇。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_89_1364544_comment'></div>昭示后嗣。不忘圣道。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_90_1364544_comment'></div>即以某年月日。葬于西岳习仙乡登仙里之西麓。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_91_1364544_comment'></div>遵遗命也。嗣子嘉宾等。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_92_1364544_comment'></div>哀号泣血。柴骨栾心。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_93_1364544_comment'></div>缅惟罔极之恩。思崇永锡之道。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_94_1364544_comment'></div>以为吾邱子<span class='inlineComment2'>（疑一作于）</span>没。无助冥因。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_95_1364544_comment'></div>季由之叹。空勤负米。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_96_1364544_comment'></div>于是考群圣之典。探众妙之门。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_97_1364544_comment'></div>求所以昭报幽扃。赞祉冥籍。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_98_1364544_comment'></div>则云金仙慈救。宝手来迎。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_99_1364544_comment'></div>若德崇于此。则功济于彼。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_100_1364544_comment'></div>是用归诚真谛。祈祐能仁。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_101_1364544_comment'></div>钳铁围而写容。现金莲而得像。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_102_1364544_comment'></div>遂于登仙麓茔之侧。造阿弥陁像一躯。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_103_1364544_comment'></div>坐高三丈。并象变菩萨。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_104_1364544_comment'></div>天人毕备。全金涌出。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_105_1364544_comment'></div>众宝装严。云仙鬼神。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_106_1364544_comment'></div>周罗上界。珠幡羽盖。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_107_1364544_comment'></div>围绕中天。所以丕显尊灵。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_108_1364544_comment'></div>光昭惠业。达人之能事毕矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_109_1364544_comment'></div>孝子之事亲终矣。铭曰。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_110_1364544_comment'></div></div><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_111_1364544'>岩岩大岳。浼浼长河。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_111_1364544_comment'></div><span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_112_1364544", 1364544, "Clauses/224/Comments/0")'>歊云</span>滃雾。含灵伫和。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_112_1364544_comment'></div>杨侯之国。宛其中阿。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_113_1364544_comment'></div>子孙瓜瓞。轩盖骈罗。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_114_1364544_comment'></div>四代五公。自于伯起。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_115_1364544_comment'></div>蝉联彪懿。令闻不已。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_116_1364544_comment'></div>二千户侯。三十刺史。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_117_1364544_comment'></div>世济其荣。至我君子。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_118_1364544_comment'></div>峨峨君子。皎有令光。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_119_1364544_comment'></div>不宠我组。而括其囊。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_120_1364544_comment'></div>洗心岩遁。抗迹云翔。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_121_1364544_comment'></div>冥鸿不远。白驹在场。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_122_1364544_comment'></div>解其萝袂。绾我墨职。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_123_1364544_comment'></div><span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_124_1364544", 1364544, "Clauses/248/Comments/0")'>边朔</span>多虞。猃狁孔棘。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_124_1364544_comment'></div>之子之往。允威允德。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_125_1364544_comment'></div>干旄在阶。烽火罢色。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_126_1364544_comment'></div>行行骏马。绣衣之光。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_127_1364544_comment'></div>烈烈董狐。司史之良。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_128_1364544_comment'></div>而我君子。总其徽章。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_129_1364544_comment'></div>出同严助。政穆王祥。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_130_1364544_comment'></div>雄魏既康。郪蜀犹侈。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_131_1364544_comment'></div>揽辔言迈。题舆载理。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_132_1364544_comment'></div>尺兵允戢。乱绳攸靡。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_133_1364544_comment'></div>天子登封。拜服玉趾。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_134_1364544_comment'></div>大礼既毕。归路迟迟。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_135_1364544_comment'></div>岁亦秋止。天不憖遗。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_136_1364544_comment'></div>呜呼氓吏。号泣涟洏。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_137_1364544_comment'></div>曷其往矣。来暮歌思。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_138_1364544_comment'></div>茕茕孤子。棘心哀疚。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_139_1364544_comment'></div>永号昊天。眇泣冥祐。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_140_1364544_comment'></div>莲花之国。金池玉霤。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_141_1364544_comment'></div>崇此香缘。生彼秾秀。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_142_1364544_comment'></div>全金既涌。众宝斯庄。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_143_1364544_comment'></div>考坟其左。叔茔其旁。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_144_1364544_comment'></div>香花围绕。松柏成行。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_145_1364544_comment'></div>千秋万岁。祚祉无疆。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_146_1364544_comment'></div></div><div id='poem_sentence_147_1364544_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=686&endYear=686')">686年</a>　居官东都，春，从乔知之护刘敬同军，北征金徽州都督仆固始。<br /></div><div class='label1' id='31b7806ef91b41d0849d4d9c83401444_label'><a href='javascript: DetailSwitch("31b7806ef91b41d0849d4d9c83401444");'><span id='31b7806ef91b41d0849d4d9c83401444_link' class='switch'>—</span></a><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=686&endYear=691')">686-691年</a>，28-33岁</div><div id='31b7806ef91b41d0849d4d9c83401444' class='detail'><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=686&endYear=686')">686年</a>　居东都，上书论西蕃边州安危事。作品：《上西蕃边州安危事三条》<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=686&endYear=686')">686年</a>　居东都，为苏令本上书舅父内史岑长倩求升迁。作品：《为苏令本与岑内史启》<span class='inlineComment2'>（徐谱考此文作于686年冬至689年冬，姑系本年。）</span><div id='poem_1364528' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1364528' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1364528?labeling=true' target='_blank'>为苏令本与岑内史启</a><span class='authorDate'>（686年）</span><span class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1364528_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1364528'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1364528'>某启。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1364528_comment'></div>某闻子以母贵。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1364528_comment'></div>自古通方。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1364528_comment'></div>礼以亲荣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1364528_comment'></div>在昔恒理。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1364528_comment'></div>岂非奉上之道。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1364528_comment'></div>休泰必同。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1364528_comment'></div>膝下之恩。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1364528_comment'></div>亲爱先及。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1364528_comment'></div>伏惟尊舅宠居密戚。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1364528_comment'></div>位列崇班。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1364528_comment'></div>实富贵于当今。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1364528_comment'></div>允尊荣于前代。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1364528_comment'></div>居得言之地。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1364528_comment'></div>据至要之途。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1364528_comment'></div>九族同欣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1364528_comment'></div>皆凭于<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_16_1364528", 1364528, "Clauses/16/Comments/0")'>奖眄</span>。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_16_1364528_comment'></div>六亲咸赖。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_17_1364528_comment'></div>仰沐于恩波。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_18_1364528_comment'></div>莫不拂拭其羽仪。<div ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=687&endYear=687')">687年</a>　居东都，守麟台正字。冬，武后谋自雅州开山出击生羌，因以袭吐蕃。子昂作诗述忧思，斥当政之失。作品：《感遇 其二十九》<div id='poem_34768' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_34768' class='poemTitle ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=687&endYear=687')">687年</a>　居东都，守麟台正字。冬，武后谋自雅州开山出击生羌，因以袭吐蕃。子昂上书谏止。作品：《谏雅州讨生羗书》<div id='poem_1364515' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1364515' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1364515?labeling=true' target='_blank'>谏雅州讨生羌书</a><span class='authorDate'>（687年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 唐初 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(20887, "唐初", "陈子昂", "poem_title_1364515")'>陈子昂</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1364515_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1364515'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1364515'>将仕郎守麟台正字臣陈子昂昧死上言。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1364515_comment'></div>窃闻道路云。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1364515_comment'></div>国家欲开蜀山。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1364515_comment'></div>自雅州道入讨生羌。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1364515_comment'></div>因以袭击吐蕃。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1364515_comment'></div>执事者不审图其利害。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1364515_comment'></div>遂发梁凤巴蜒兵以徇之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1364515_comment'></div>臣愚以为西蜀之祸。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1364515_comment'></div>自此结矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1364515_comment'></div>臣闻乱生必由怨起。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1364515_comment'></div>雅之边羌。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1364515_comment'></div>自国初已来。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1364515_comment'></div>未尝一日为盗。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1364515_comment'></div>今一旦无罪受戮。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1364515_comment'></div>其怨必甚。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1364515_comment'></div>怨甚惧诛。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1364515_comment'></div>必蜂骇西山。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_16_1364515_comment'></div>西山盗起。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_17_1364515_comment'></div>则蜀之边邑。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_18_1364515_comment'></div>不得不连兵备守。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_19_1364515_comment'></div>兵久不解。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_20_1364515_comment'></div>则蜀之祸搆矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_21_1364515_comment'></div>昔后汉末西京丧败。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_22_1364515_comment'></div>盖由此诸羌。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_23_1364515_comment'></div>此一事也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_24_1364515_comment'></div>且臣闻吐蕃桀黠之虏。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_25_1364515_comment'></div>君长相信而多奸谋。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_26_1364515_comment'></div>自敢抗天诛。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_27_1364515_comment'></div>迩来向二十馀载。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_28_1364515_comment'></div>大战则大胜。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_29_1364515_comment'></div>小战则小胜。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_30_1364515_comment'></div>未尝败一队亡一矢。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_31_1364515_comment'></div>国家往以薛仁贵郭待封为<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_32_1364515", 1364515, "Clauses/32/Comments/0")'>虓武</span>之将。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_32_1364515_comment'></div>屠十万众于大非之川。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_33_1364515_comment'></div>一甲不归。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_34_1364515_comment'></div>又以李敬元刘审礼为廊庙之宰。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_35_1364515_comment'></div>辱十八万众于青海之泽。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_36_1364515_comment'></div>身为囚虏。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_37_1364515_comment'></div>是时精甲勇士。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_38_1364515_comment'></div>势如云雷。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_39_1364515_comment'></div>然竟不能擒一戎馘一丑。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_40_1364515_comment'></div>至今而关陇为空。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_41_1364515_comment'></div>今乃欲以李处一为将。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_42_1364515_comment'></div>驱憔悴之兵。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_43_1364515_comment'></div>将袭吐蕃。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_44_1364515_comment'></div>臣窃忧之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_45_1364515_comment'></div>而为此虏所笑。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_46_1364515_comment'></div>此二事也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_47_1364515_comment'></div>且夫事有求利而得害者。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_48_1364515_comment'></div>则蜀昔时不通中国。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_49_1364515_comment'></div>秦惠王欲帝天下而并诸侯。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_50_1364515_comment'></div>以为不兼賨不取蜀。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_51_1364515_comment'></div>势未可举。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_52_1364515_comment'></div>乃用张仪计。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_53_1364515_comment'></div>饰<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_54_1364515", 1364515, "Clauses/54/Comments/0")'>美女</span>。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_54_1364515_comment'></div>谲金牛。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_55_1364515_comment'></div>因閒以啖蜀侯。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_56_1364515_comment'></div>蜀侯果贪其利。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_57_1364515_comment'></div>使五丁力士凿山通谷。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_58_1364515_comment'></div>栈褒斜置道于秦。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_59_1364515_comment'></div>自是险阻不关。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_60_1364515_comment'></div>山谷不闭。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_61_1364515_comment'></div>张仪蹑踵乘便。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_62_1364515_comment'></div>纵兵大破之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_63_1364515_comment'></div>蜀侯诛。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_64_1364515_comment'></div>賨邑灭。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_65_1364515_comment'></div>至今蜀为<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_66_1364515", 1364515, id='poem_sentence_68_1364515_comment'></div>且臣闻吐蕃羯虏。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_69_1364515_comment'></div>爱蜀之珍富。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_70_1364515_comment'></div>欲盗之久有日矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_71_1364515_comment'></div>然其势不能举者。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_72_1364515_comment'></div>徒以山川阻绝。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_73_1364515_comment'></div>障隘不通。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_74_1364515_comment'></div>此其所以顿饿狼之喙。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_75_1364515_comment'></div>而不得窃食也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_76_1364515_comment'></div>今国家乃撤边羌。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_77_1364515_comment'></div>开隘道。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_78_1364515_comment'></div>使其收奔亡之种。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_79_1364515_comment'></div>为<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_80_1364515", 1364515, "Clauses/80/Comments/0")'>向导</span>以攻边。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_80_1364515_comment'></div>是乃借寇兵而为贼除道。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_81_1364515_comment'></div>举全蜀以遗之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_82_1364515_comment'></div>此四事也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_83_1364515_comment'></div>臣窃观蜀为西南一都会。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_84_1364515_comment'></div>国家之<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_85_1364515", 1364515, "Clauses/85/Comments/0")'>宝库</span>。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_85_1364515_comment'></div>天下珍货。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_86_1364515_comment'></div>聚出其中。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_87_1364515_comment'></div>又人富粟多。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_88_1364515_comment'></div>顺江而下。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_89_1364515_comment'></div>可以兼济中国。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_90_1364515_comment'></div>今执事者乃图侥倖之利。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_91_1364515_comment'></div>悉以委事西羌。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_92_1364515_comment'></div>得西羌。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_93_1364515_comment'></div>地不足以稼穑。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_94_1364515_comment'></div>财不足以富国。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_95_1364515_comment'></div>徒杀无辜之众。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_96_1364515_comment'></div>以伤陛下之仁。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_97_1364515_comment'></div>糜费随之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_98_1364515_comment'></div>无益圣德。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_99_1364515_comment'></div>又况侥倖之利。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_100_1364515_comment'></div>未可图哉。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_101_1364515_comment'></div>此五事也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_102_1364515_comment'></div>夫蜀之所宝。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_103_1364515_comment'></div>恃险者也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_104_1364515_comment'></div>人之所安。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_105_1364515_comment'></div>无役者也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_106_1364515_comment'></div>今国家乃开其险。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_107_1364515_comment'></div>役其人。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_108_1364515_comment'></div>险开则便寇。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_109_1364515_comment'></div>人役则伤财。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_110_1364515_comment'></div>臣恐未及见羌戎。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_111_1364515_comment'></div>而已有奸盗在其中矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_112_1364515_comment'></div>往年益州长史李崇真将图此<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_113_1364515", 1364515, "Clauses/113/Comments/0")'>奸利</span>。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_113_1364515_comment'></div>传檄称吐蕃欲寇松州。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_114_1364515_comment'></div>遂使国家盛军以待之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_115_1364515_comment'></div>转饷以备之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_116_1364515_comment'></div>未二三年。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_117_1364515_comment'></div>巴蜀二十馀州骚然大弊。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_118_1364515_comment'></div>竟不见吐蕃之面。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_119_1364515_comment'></div>而崇真赃钱已计巨万矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_120_1364515_comment'></div>蜀人残破。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_121_1364515_comment'></div>几不堪命。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_122_1364515_comment'></div>此乃近事。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_123_1364515_comment'></div>犹在人口。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_124_1364515_comment'></div>陛下所亲知。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_125_1364515_comment'></div>臣愚意者。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_126_1364515_comment'></div>得非有奸臣欲图此利。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_127_1364515_comment'></div>复以生羌为计者哉。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_128_1364515_comment'></div>此六事也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_129_1364515_comment'></div>且蜀人尪孱<span class='inlineComment2'>（一作劣）</span>。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_130_1364515_comment'></div>不习兵战。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_131_1364515_comment'></div>一虏持矛。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_132_1364515_comment'></div>百人莫敢当。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_133_1364515_comment'></div>又山川阻旷。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_134_1364515_comment'></div>去中夏精兵处远。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_135_1364515_comment'></div>今国家若击西羌。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_136_1364515_comment'></div>掩吐蕃。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_137_1364515_comment'></div>遂能破灭其国。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_138_1364515_comment'></div>奴虏其人。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_139_1364515_comment'></div>使其君长系首北阙。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_140_1364515_comment'></div>计亦可矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_141_1364515_comment'></div>若不到如此。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_142_1364515_comment'></div>臣方见蜀之边陲不守。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_143_1364515_comment'></div>而为羌夷所横暴。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_144_1364515_comment'></div>昔辛有见被发而祭伊川者。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_145_1364515_comment'></div>以为不出百年。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_146_1364515_comment'></div>此其为戎乎。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_147_1364515_comment'></div>臣恐不及百年。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_148_1364515_comment'></div>而蜀为戎。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_149_1364515_comment'></div>此七事也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_150_1364515_comment'></div>且国家近者废安北。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_151_1364515_comment'></div>拔单于。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_152_1364515_comment'></div>弃龟兹。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_153_1364515_comment'></div>放疏勒。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_154_1364515_comment'></div>天下翕然谓之盛德。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_155_1364515_comment'></div>所以者何。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_156_1364515_comment'></div>盖以陛下务在仁。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_157_1364515_comment'></div>不在广。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_158_1364515_comment'></div>务在养。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_159_1364515_comment'></div>不在杀。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_160_1364515_comment'></div>将以此息边鄙。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_161_1364515_comment'></div>休甲兵。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_162_1364515_comment'></div>行乎三皇五帝之事者也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_163_1364515_comment'></div>今又徇贪夫之议。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_164_1364515_comment'></div>谋动兵戈。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_165_1364515_comment'></div>将诛无罪之戎。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_166_1364515_comment'></div>而遗全蜀之患。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_167_1364515_comment'></div>将何以令天下乎。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_168_1364515_comment'></div>此愚臣所甚不悟者也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_169_1364515_comment'></div>况当今山东饥。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_170_1364515_comment'></div>关陇弊。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_171_1364515_comment'></div>历岁枯旱。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_172_1364515_comment'></div>人有流亡。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_173_1364515_comment'></div>诚是圣人宁静思和天人之时。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_174_1364515_comment'></div>不可动甲兵兴大役。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_175_1364515_comment'></div>以自生乱。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_176_1364515_comment'></div>臣又流闻西军失守。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_177_1364515_comment'></div>北军不利。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_178_1364515_comment'></div>边人忙动。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_179_1364515_comment'></div>情有不安。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_180_1364515_comment'></div>今者复驱此兵。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_181_1364515_comment'></div>投之不测。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_182_1364515_comment'></div>臣闻自古国亡家败。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_183_1364515_comment'></div>未尝不由黩兵。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_184_1364515_comment'></div>今小人议夷狄之利。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_185_1364515_comment'></div>非帝王之至德也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_186_1364515_comment'></div>又况弊中夏哉。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_187_1364515_comment'></div>臣闻古人善为天下者。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_188_1364515_comment'></div>计大而不计小。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_189_1364515_comment'></div>务德而不务刑。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_190_1364515_comment'></div>图其安则思其危。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_191_1364515_comment'></div>谋其利则虑其害。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_192_1364515_comment'></div>然后能享福禄。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_193_1364515_comment'></div>伏愿陛下熟计之。</div><div id='poem_sentence_194_1364515_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=688&endYear=688')">688年</a>　居东都，守麟台正字。自光宅元年徐敬业扬州叛乱后，朝中告密罗织之风大盛，子昂上《谏用刑书》<div id='poem_1364518' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1364518' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1364518?labeling=true' target='_blank'>谏用刑书</a><span class='authorDate'>（688年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 唐初 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(20887, "唐初", "陈子昂", "poem_title_1364518")'>陈子昂</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1364518_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1364518'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1364518'>将仕郎守麟台正字臣陈子昂谨顿首冒死诣阙上疏。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1364518_comment'></div>臣本蜀之匹夫。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1364518_comment'></div>宦不望达。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1364518_comment'></div>陛下<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_3_1364518", 1364518, "Clauses/3/Comments/0")'>过意</span>。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1364518_comment'></div>擢臣草莽之下。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1364518_comment'></div>升在麟台之阁。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1364518_comment'></div>光宠自天。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1364518_comment'></div>卓若日月。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1364518_comment'></div>微臣固陋。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1364518_comment'></div>将何克负。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1364518_comment'></div>然臣闻忠臣事君。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1364518_comment'></div>有死无二。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1364518_comment'></div>怀佞不谏。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1364518_comment'></div>罪莫大焉。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1364518_comment'></div>况在明圣之朝。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1364518_comment'></div>当不讳之日。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1364518_comment'></div>方复<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_16_1364518", 1364518, "Clauses/16/Comments/0")'>钳口</span>下列。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_16_1364518_comment'></div>俛仰偷荣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_17_1364518_comment'></div>非臣之始愿也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_18_1364518_comment'></div>不胜愚惑。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_19_1364518_comment'></div>辄奏狂昧之说。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_20_1364518_comment'></div>伏惟陛下少加察焉。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_21_1364518_comment'></div>臣闻古之御天下者。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_22_1364518_comment'></div>其政有三。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_23_1364518_comment'></div>王者化之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_24_1364518_comment'></div>用仁义也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_25_1364518_comment'></div>霸者威之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_26_1364518_comment'></div>盛权智也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_27_1364518_comment'></div>强国胁之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_28_1364518_comment'></div>务刑罚也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_29_1364518_comment'></div>是以化之不足。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_30_1364518_comment'></div>然后威之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_31_1364518_comment'></div>威之不变。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_32_1364518_comment'></div>然后刑之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_33_1364518_comment'></div>故至于刑。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_34_1364518_comment'></div>则非王者所贵矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_35_1364518_comment'></div>况欲光宅天下。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_36_1364518_comment'></div>追功上皇。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_37_1364518_comment'></div>专任刑杀。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_38_1364518_comment'></div>以为威断。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_39_1364518_comment'></div>可谓策之失者也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_40_1364518_comment'></div>臣伏睹陛下圣德聪明。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_41_1364518_comment'></div>游心太古。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_42_1364518_comment'></div>将制静宇宙。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_43_1364518_comment'></div>保乂黎人。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_44_1364518_comment'></div>发号施令。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_45_1364518_comment'></div>出于<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_46_1364518", 1364518, "Clauses/46/Comments/0")'>诚慊</span>。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_46_1364518_comment'></div>天下苍生。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_47_1364518_comment'></div>莫不想望圣风。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_48_1364518_comment'></div>冀见神化。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_49_1364518_comment'></div>道德为政。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_50_1364518_comment'></div>将待于陛下矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_51_1364518_comment'></div>且臣闻之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_52_1364518_comment'></div>圣人出治。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_53_1364518_comment'></div>必有驱除。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_54_1364518_comment'></div>盖天人之符应休命也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_55_1364518_comment'></div>日者东南微孽。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_56_1364518_comment'></div>敢谋乱常。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_57_1364518_comment'></div>陛下顺天行诛。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_58_1364518_comment'></div>罪恶咸服。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_59_1364518_comment'></div>岂非天意欲彰陛下神武之功哉。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_60_1364518_comment'></div>而执事者不察天心。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_61_1364518_comment'></div>以为人意。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_62_1364518_comment'></div>恶其<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_63_1364518", 1364518, "Clauses/63/Comments/0")'>首乱</span>倡祸。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_63_1364518_comment'></div>法合诛屠。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_64_1364518_comment'></div>将息奸源。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_65_1364518_comment'></div>穷其党与。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_66_1364518_comment'></div>遂使陛下大开诏狱。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_67_1364518_comment'></div>重设严刑。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_68_1364518_comment'></div>冀以惩创。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_69_1364518_comment'></div>观于天下。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_70_1364518_comment'></div>逆党亲属。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_71_1364518_comment'></div>及其交游。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_72_1364518_comment'></div>有迹涉嫌疑。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_73_1364518_comment'></div>辞相逮引。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_74_1364518_comment'></div>莫不<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_75_1364518", 1364518, "Clauses/75/Comments/0")'>穷捕</span>考讯。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_75_1364518_comment'></div>枝叶<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_76_1364518", 1364518, "Clauses/76/Comments/0")'>蟠拿</span>。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_76_1364518_comment'></div>大或流血。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_77_1364518_comment'></div>小御魑魅。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_78_1364518_comment'></div>至有奸人荧惑。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_79_1364518_comment'></div>乘险相诬。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_80_1364518_comment'></div>纠告疑似。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_81_1364518_comment'></div>冀图爵赏。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_82_1364518_comment'></div>叫<span class='inlineComment2'>（一作刑）</span>于阙下者。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_83_1364518_comment'></div>日有数矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_84_1364518_comment'></div>于时朝廷<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_85_1364518", 1364518, "Clauses/85/Comments/0")'>偟偟</span>。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_85_1364518_comment'></div>莫能自固。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_86_1364518_comment'></div>海内倾听。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_87_1364518_comment'></div>以相惊恐。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_88_1364518_comment'></div>赖陛下仁慈。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_89_1364518_comment'></div>悯斯危惧。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_90_1364518_comment'></div>赐以恩诏。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_91_1364518_comment'></div>许其大功已上。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_92_1364518_comment'></div>一切勿论。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_93_1364518_comment'></div>时人获泰。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_94_1364518_comment'></div>谓生再造。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_95_1364518_comment'></div>愚臣窃亦欣然。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_96_1364518_comment'></div>贺陛下圣明。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_97_1364518_comment'></div>得天下之机也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_98_1364518_comment'></div>不谓议者异见。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_99_1364518_comment'></div>又执前图。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_100_1364518_comment'></div>比者刑狱。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_101_1364518_comment'></div>纷纷复起。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_102_1364518_comment'></div>陛下不深思天意。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_103_1364518_comment'></div>以顺休期。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_104_1364518_comment'></div>尚以督察为理。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_105_1364518_comment'></div>威刑为务。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_106_1364518_comment'></div>使前者之诏。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_107_1364518_comment'></div>不信于人。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_108_1364518_comment'></div>愚臣昧焉。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_109_1364518_comment'></div>窃恐非三皇五帝伐罪吊人之意也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_110_1364518_comment'></div>臣窃观当今天下百姓。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_111_1364518_comment'></div>思安久矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_112_1364518_comment'></div>曩属北胡侵塞。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_113_1364518_comment'></div>西戎寇边。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_114_1364518_comment'></div>兵革相屠。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_115_1364518_comment'></div>向历十载。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_116_1364518_comment'></div>关河自北。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_117_1364518_comment'></div>转输幽燕。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_118_1364518_comment'></div>秦蜀之西。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_119_1364518_comment'></div>驰骛湟海。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_120_1364518_comment'></div>当时天下疲极矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_121_1364518_comment'></div>重以大兵之后。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_122_1364518_comment'></div>屡遭凶年。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_123_1364518_comment'></div>流离饥饿。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_124_1364518_comment'></div>死丧略半。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_125_1364518_comment'></div>幸赖陛下以至圣之德。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_126_1364518_comment'></div>抚宁兆人。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_127_1364518_comment'></div>边境获安。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_128_1364518_comment'></div>中国无事。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_129_1364518_comment'></div>阴阳大顺。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_130_1364518_comment'></div>年谷累登。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_131_1364518_comment'></div>天下父子始得相养矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_132_1364518_comment'></div>故扬州搆祸。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_133_1364518_comment'></div>殆有五旬。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_134_1364518_comment'></div>而海内晏然。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_135_1364518_comment'></div>纤尘不动。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_136_1364518_comment'></div>岂非天下<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_137_1364518", 1364518, "Clauses/137/Comments/0")'>蒸庶</span>厌凶乱哉。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_137_1364518_comment'></div>臣以此卜之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_138_1364518_comment'></div>知百姓思安久矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_139_1364518_comment'></div>今陛下不务元默。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_140_1364518_comment'></div>以救疲人。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_141_1364518_comment'></div>而反任威刑。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_142_1364518_comment'></div>以失其望。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_143_1364518_comment'></div>欲以察察为政。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_144_1364518_comment'></div>肃理寰区。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_145_1364518_comment'></div>臣愚暗昧。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_146_1364518_comment'></div>窃有大惑。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_147_1364518_comment'></div>且臣闻刑者。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_148_1364518_comment'></div>政之末节也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_149_1364518_comment'></div>先王以禁暴整乱。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_150_1364518_comment'></div>不得已而用之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_151_1364518_comment'></div>今天下幸安。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_152_1364518_comment'></div>万物思泰。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_153_1364518_comment'></div>陛下乃以末节之法。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_154_1364518_comment'></div><span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_155_1364518", 1364518, "Clauses/155/Comments/0")'>察理</span>平人。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_155_1364518_comment'></div>臣愚以为非适变随时之议也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_156_1364518_comment'></div>顷年以来。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_157_1364518_comment'></div>伏见诸方<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_158_1364518", 1364518, "Clauses/158/Comments/0")'>告密</span>囚累百千辈。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_158_1364518_comment'></div>大抵所告皆以扬州为名。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_159_1364518_comment'></div>及其穷究。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_160_1364518_comment'></div>百无一实。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_161_1364518_comment'></div>陛下仁恕。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_162_1364518_comment'></div>又屈法容之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_163_1364518_comment'></div>傍讦他事。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_164_1364518_comment'></div>亦为推劾。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_165_1364518_comment'></div>遂使奸恶之党。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_166_1364518_comment'></div>决意相雠。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_167_1364518_comment'></div>睚眦之嫌。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_168_1364518_comment'></div>即称有密。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_169_1364518_comment'></div>一人被讼。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_170_1364518_comment'></div>百人满狱。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_171_1364518_comment'></div>使者推捕。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_172_1364518_comment'></div>冠盖如云。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_173_1364518_comment'></div>或谓陛下爱一人而害百人。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_174_1364518_comment'></div>天下喁喁。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_175_1364518_comment'></div>莫知<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_176_1364518", 1364518, "Clauses/176/Comments/0")'>宁所</span>。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_176_1364518_comment'></div>臣闻自非圣人。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_177_1364518_comment'></div>不有外患。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_178_1364518_comment'></div>必有内忧。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_179_1364518_comment'></div>物理之自然也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_180_1364518_comment'></div>臣不敢以远古言之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_181_1364518_comment'></div>请借隋而况。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_182_1364518_comment'></div>臣闻<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_183_1364518", 1364518, "Clauses/183/Comments/0")'>长老</span>言。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_183_1364518_comment'></div>隋之末代。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_184_1364518_comment'></div>天下犹平。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_185_1364518_comment'></div>炀帝<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_186_1364518", 1364518, "Clauses/186/Comments/0")'>不龚</span>。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_186_1364518_comment'></div>穷毒威武。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_187_1364518_comment'></div>厌居皇极。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_188_1364518_comment'></div>自总元戎。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_189_1364518_comment'></div>以百万之师。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_190_1364518_comment'></div>观兵辽海。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_191_1364518_comment'></div>天下始骚然矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_192_1364518_comment'></div>遂使杨元感挟不臣之势。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_193_1364518_comment'></div>有大盗之心。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_194_1364518_comment'></div>欲因人谋以窃皇业。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_195_1364518_comment'></div>乃称兵中夏。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_196_1364518_comment'></div>将据洛阳。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_197_1364518_comment'></div><span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_198_1364518", 1364518, "Clauses/198/Comments/0")'>哮阚</span>之势。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_198_1364518_comment'></div>倾宇宙矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_199_1364518_comment'></div>然乱未踰月。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_200_1364518_comment'></div>而首足异处。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_201_1364518_comment'></div>何者。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_202_1364518_comment'></div>天下之弊。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_203_1364518_comment'></div>未有土崩。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_204_1364518_comment'></div>蒸人之心。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_205_1364518_comment'></div>犹望乐业。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_206_1364518_comment'></div>炀帝不悟。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_207_1364518_comment'></div>暗忽人机。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_208_1364518_comment'></div>自以为元恶既诛。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_209_1364518_comment'></div>天下无巨猾也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_210_1364518_comment'></div>皇极之任。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_211_1364518_comment'></div>可以刑罚理之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_212_1364518_comment'></div>遂使兵部尚书樊子盖专行屠戮。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_213_1364518_comment'></div>大穷党与。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_214_1364518_comment'></div>海内豪士。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_215_1364518_comment'></div>无不罹殃。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_216_1364518_comment'></div>遂至杀人如麻。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_217_1364518_comment'></div>血流成泽。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_218_1364518_comment'></div>天下靡然。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_219_1364518_comment'></div>始思为乱矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_220_1364518_comment'></div>于是萧铣朱粲起于荆南。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_221_1364518_comment'></div>李密窦建德乱于河北。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_222_1364518_comment'></div>四海<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_223_1364518", 1364518, "Clauses/223/Comments/0")'>云摇</span>。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_223_1364518_comment'></div>遂并起而亡隋族矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_224_1364518_comment'></div>岂不哀哉。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_225_1364518_comment'></div><span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_226_1364518", 1364518, "Clauses/226/Comments/0")'>长老</span>至今谈之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_226_1364518_comment'></div>委曲如是。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_227_1364518_comment'></div>臣窃以此上观三代夏殷周兴亡。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_228_1364518_comment'></div>下逮秦汉魏晋理乱。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_229_1364518_comment'></div>莫不皆以毒刑而致败坏也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_230_1364518_comment'></div>夫大狱一起。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_231_1364518_comment'></div>不能无滥。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_232_1364518_comment'></div>何者。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_233_1364518_comment'></div>刀笔之吏。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_234_1364518_comment'></div>寡识大方。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_235_1364518_comment'></div>断狱能者。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_236_1364518_comment'></div>名在<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_237_1364518", 1364518, "Clauses/237/Comments/0")'>急刻</span>。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_237_1364518_comment'></div><span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_238_1364518", 1364518, "Clauses/238/Comments/0")'>文深网密</span>。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_238_1364518_comment'></div>则共称至公。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_239_1364518_comment'></div>爰及人主。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_240_1364518_comment'></div>亦谓其奉法。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_241_1364518_comment'></div>于是利在杀人。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_242_1364518_comment'></div>害在平恕。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_243_1364518_comment'></div>故狱吏相戒。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_244_1364518_comment'></div>以杀为词。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_245_1364518_comment'></div>非憎于人也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_246_1364518_comment'></div>而利在己。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_247_1364518_comment'></div>故上以希人主之旨。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_248_1364518_comment'></div>下以图荣身之利。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_249_1364518_comment'></div>徇利既多。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_250_1364518_comment'></div>则不能无滥。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_251_1364518_comment'></div>滥及良善。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_252_1364518_comment'></div>则淫刑逞矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_253_1364518_comment'></div>夫人情莫不自爱其身。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_254_1364518_comment'></div>陛下以此察之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_255_1364518_comment'></div>岂能无滥也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_256_1364518_comment'></div>冤人吁嗟。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_257_1364518_comment'></div>感伤和气。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_258_1364518_comment'></div>和气悖乱。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_259_1364518_comment'></div>群生疠疫。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_260_1364518_comment'></div>水旱随之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_261_1364518_comment'></div>则有凶年。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_262_1364518_comment'></div>人既失业。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_263_1364518_comment'></div>则祸乱之心。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_264_1364518_comment'></div>怵然而生矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_265_1364518_comment'></div>顷来亢阳僭。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_266_1364518_comment'></div>密云不雨。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_267_1364518_comment'></div>农夫释耒。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_268_1364518_comment'></div>瞻望嗷嗷。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_269_1364518_comment'></div>岂不由陛下之有圣德。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_270_1364518_comment'></div>而不降泽于下人也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_271_1364518_comment'></div>倘旱遂过春。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_272_1364518_comment'></div>废于时种。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_273_1364518_comment'></div>今年稼穑。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_274_1364518_comment'></div>必有损矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_275_1364518_comment'></div>陛下何不敬承天意。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_276_1364518_comment'></div>以泽恤人。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_277_1364518_comment'></div>臣闻古者明王。<div id='poem_sentence_280_1364518_comment'></div>书不云乎。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_281_1364518_comment'></div>与其杀不辜。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_282_1364518_comment'></div>宁失不经。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_283_1364518_comment'></div>陛下柰何以堂堂之圣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_284_1364518_comment'></div>犹务强霸之威哉。<div class='inline' class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_290_1364518", 1364518, "Clauses/290/Comments/0")'>起奸</span>。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_290_1364518_comment'></div>倘大狱未休。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_291_1364518_comment'></div>支党日广。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_292_1364518_comment'></div>天下疑惑。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_293_1364518_comment'></div>相恐无辜。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_294_1364518_comment'></div>人情之变。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_295_1364518_comment'></div>不可不察。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_296_1364518_comment'></div>昔汉武帝时。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_297_1364518_comment'></div>巫蛊狱起。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_298_1364518_comment'></div>江充行诈。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_299_1364518_comment'></div>作乱京师。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_300_1364518_comment'></div>致使太子奔走。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_301_1364518_comment'></div>兵交宫阙。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_302_1364518_comment'></div>无辜被害者以千万数。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_303_1364518_comment'></div>刘氏宗庙。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_304_1364518_comment'></div>几倾覆矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_305_1364518_comment'></div>赖武帝得壶关三老上书。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_306_1364518_comment'></div>廓然感悟。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_307_1364518_comment'></div>夷江充三族。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_308_1364518_comment'></div>馀狱不论。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_309_1364518_comment'></div>天下少以安尔。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_310_1364518_comment'></div>臣读汉书至此。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_311_1364518_comment'></div>未尝不为戾太子流涕也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_312_1364518_comment'></div>古人云。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_313_1364518_comment'></div>前事之不忘。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_314_1364518_comment'></div>后事之师。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_315_1364518_comment'></div>伏愿陛下念之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_317_1364518_comment'></div>以蝼蚁之命。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_318_1364518_comment'></div>轻触宸严。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_319_1364518_comment'></div>臣非不恶死而贪生也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_320_1364518_comment'></div>诚恐负陛下恩遇。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_321_1364518_comment'></div>臣不敢以微命蔽塞聪明。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_322_1364518_comment'></div>亦非敢欲陛下顿息刑罚。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_323_1364518_comment'></div>望在<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_324_1364518", 1364518, "Clauses/324/Comments/0")'>恤刑</span>尔。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_324_1364518_comment'></div>乞与三事大夫图其可否。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_325_1364518_comment'></div>往者不可谏。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_326_1364518_comment'></div>来者犹可追。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_327_1364518_comment'></div>无以臣微而忽其奏。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_328_1364518_comment'></div>天下幸甚。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_329_1364518_comment'></div>臣子昂诚惶诚恐死罪死罪。</div><div id='poem_sentence_330_1364518_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=688&endYear=688')">688年</a>　居东都，守麟台正字。为丰国夫人作皇太子诞庆表。作品：《为丰国夫人庆皇太子诞表》<span class='inlineComment2'>（徐谱考此文作于文明元年子昂入仕至本年五月武后加“圣母神皇”尊号之前，姑系本年。）</span><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1364454'>臣妾某言。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1364454_comment'></div>今月日。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1364454_comment'></div>伏承轩宫载诞。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1364454_comment'></div>皇嗣克昌。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1364454_comment'></div>品物咸欢。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1364454_comment'></div>天人交庆。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1364454_comment'></div>臣妾闻圣人多子。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1364454_comment'></div>祝美于尧年。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1364454_comment'></div>螽羽宜孙。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1364454_comment'></div>称道乎周颂。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1364454_comment'></div>自非璿图配永。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1364454_comment'></div>宝祚灵长。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1364454_comment'></div>何以茂对天休。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1364454_comment'></div>光绍大业。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1364454_comment'></div>伏惟皇太后陛下星虹授祉。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_19_1364454_comment'></div>其窃宠中姻。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_20_1364454_comment'></div>承恩外戚。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_21_1364454_comment'></div>涂山之庆。<div id='poem_sentence_33_1364454_comment'></div>洗心而荐。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_34_1364454_comment'></div>窃希瑶席之珍。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_35_1364454_comment'></div>洁意而羞。<div ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=688&endYear=688')">688年</a>　居东都，守麟台正字。时诏令怀远军郎将曹仁师出征突厥，子昂以仓猝未备，恐劳师无功，上书谏止。作品：《谏曹仁师出军书》<div id='poem_1364520' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1364520' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1364520?labeling=true' target='_blank'>谏曹仁师出军书</a><span class='authorDate'>（688年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 唐初 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(20887, "唐初", "陈子昂", "poem_title_1364520")'>陈子昂</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1364520_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1364520'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1364520'>臣伏见诏书发怀远军。令郎将曹仁师讯勒以征凶丑。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1364520_comment'></div>臣闻古之天子。方建大礼。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1364520_comment'></div>必先<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_2_1364520", 1364520, "Clauses/4/Comments/0")'>振兵释旅</span>。以告成功。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1364520_comment'></div>故汉孝武皇帝将封禅。乃徵精卒十万。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1364520_comment'></div>北巡朔方。略地而还。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1364520_comment'></div>此盖遵古先哲王之礼也。今神皇陛下应天受箓。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1364520_comment'></div>将欲郊祭天地。巡拜河洛。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1364520_comment'></div>建明堂。朝万国。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1364520_comment'></div>斯<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_8_1364520", 1364520, "Clauses/16/Comments/0")'>迈古</span>之盛礼也。诚合式遵旧典。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1364520_comment'></div>耀武塞上。毕境而还。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1364520_comment'></div>臣犹虑曹仁师未识典礼。肆兵长驱。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1364520_comment'></div>穷极砂碛。不恤士马。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1364520_comment'></div>专以务得为利。不以全兵为上。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1364520_comment'></div>今朝廷百寮。虽有疑者。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1364520_comment'></div>无敢言之。臣诚愚昧。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1364520_comment'></div>不识忌讳。曾闻事君之道。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1364520_comment'></div>所贵尽心。心以为非。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_16_1364520_comment'></div>安可不言。臣料仁师到云内城发兵之日。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_17_1364520_comment'></div>合至九月初到突利城。回兵之日。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_18_1364520_comment'></div>合至十月初。胡地隆冬。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_19_1364520_comment'></div>草枯泉涸。南中士马。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_20_1364520_comment'></div>不耐祁寒。计仁师所将之马。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_21_1364520_comment'></div>从灵州常时所发之处。却回到云内城。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_22_1364520_comment'></div>已行四千馀里。云内城中又先未支度。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_23_1364520_comment'></div>马既疲瘦。经冬无粟。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_24_1364520_comment'></div>以臣愚算。十不存二。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_25_1364520_comment'></div>若送南中。散就诸州。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_26_1364520_comment'></div><span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_27_1364520", 1364520, "Clauses/54/Comments/0")'>路程</span>益远。疲瘦更极。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_27_1364520_comment'></div>以臣愚算。十不存五。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_28_1364520_comment'></div>紫蒙之军。类例相似。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_29_1364520_comment'></div>且仁师此行。计迟发速至。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_30_1364520_comment'></div>于应会不甚精备。以臣计料。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_31_1364520_comment'></div>恐未成功。<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_32_1364520", 1364520, "Clauses/65/Comments/0")'>脱若</span>功未克成。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_32_1364520_comment'></div>士马先丧尽。中土求市。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_33_1364520_comment'></div>卒又难得。且自古与匈奴战。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_34_1364520_comment'></div>非士马相资不可。臣恐马既虚用致尽。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_35_1364520_comment'></div>贼又窜远未平。但虑后之谋臣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_36_1364520_comment'></div>悔于今事。且古来绝漠。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_37_1364520_comment'></div>多丧士马。非臣<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_38_1364520", 1364520, "Clauses/77/Comments/0")'>臆度</span>。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_38_1364520_comment'></div>辄敢陈闻。昔汉室以卫青出塞。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_39_1364520_comment'></div>是时汉马三十万疋。旋师之日。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_40_1364520_comment'></div>唯馀四万。四十年不得事匈奴。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_41_1364520_comment'></div>盖由此也。臣愿陛下考验前古。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_42_1364520_comment'></div>取臣愚诚。望与三公大臣审更详议。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_43_1364520_comment'></div></div><div id='poem_sentence_44_1364520_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=688&endYear=688')">688年</a>　居东都，守麟台正字。陈御史上奉和秋景观竞渡应制诗，子昂为其草表。作品：《为陈御史上奉和秋景观竞渡诗表》<div id='poem_1364460' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1364460' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1364460?labeling=true' target='_blank'>为陈御史上奉和秋景观竞渡诗表</a><span class='authorDate'>（688年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 唐初 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(20887, "唐初", "陈子昂", "poem_title_1364460")'>陈子昂</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1364460_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1364460'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1364460'>臣某言。伏见某月日御制。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1364460_comment'></div>秋景务馀。聊观竞渡。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1364460_comment'></div>故陈先作。式伫来篇。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1364460_comment'></div>凡六韵。天文爰降。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1364460_comment'></div>品汇咸亨。金简潜开。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1364460_comment'></div>瑞图斯见。臣闻白云兴咏。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1364460_comment'></div>汉游汾水之祠。黄竹申歌。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1364460_comment'></div>周舞瑶池之驾。然而志崇远辙。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1364460_comment'></div>事或劳人。故文思之化未光。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1364460_comment'></div>太清之道犹阙。伏惟圣母神皇陛下太虹齐圣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1364460_comment'></div>感月含神。元德茂于皇阶。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1364460_comment'></div>文明照于天下。用能提玉斗。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1364460_comment'></div>挹璿衡。百神景从。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1364460_comment'></div>三灵协赞。青云出洛。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1364460_comment'></div>爰开受命之符。<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_14_1364460", 1364460, "Clauses/29/Comments/0")'>赤甲</span>荣河。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1364460_comment'></div>终御兴王之宝。非穷神之至德者。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1364460_comment'></div>其孰能与于是哉。既而黄屋务闲。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_16_1364460_comment'></div>紫机时暇。洞庭张乐。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_17_1364460_comment'></div>思接轸于轩游。妫水披图。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_18_1364460_comment'></div>想同骖于尧辇。然而远而劳物者。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_19_1364460_comment'></div>未若近而安人。动而勤巳者。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_20_1364460_comment'></div>岂比静而泰神。于是从<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_21_1364460", 1364460, "Clauses/43/Comments/0")'>金跸</span>。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_21_1364460_comment'></div>鸣玉鸾。清禁林。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_22_1364460_comment'></div>御池殿。肃波神<span class='inlineComment2'>（一作臣）</span>而戒事。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_23_1364460_comment'></div>命舟子为水嬉。彩鹢莲歌。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_24_1364460_comment'></div>乍起江吴<span class='inlineComment2'>（一作吴江）</span>之引。青龙桂楫。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_25_1364460_comment'></div>时摇瓯越<span class='inlineComment2'>（一作时讴越女）</span>之风。鸟逝虬惊。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_26_1364460_comment'></div>沸珠潭而竞逐。云飞电集。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_27_1364460_comment'></div>横玉浦而流光。信可以娱乐惟灵。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_28_1364460_comment'></div>发挥文物。皇欢允洽。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_29_1364460_comment'></div>白日俄光。于是奏薰风于管弦。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_30_1364460_comment'></div>咏丛云于林籞。帝歌爰作。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_31_1364460_comment'></div><span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_32_1364460", 1364460, "Clauses/64/Comments/0")'>天藻</span>攸彰。黼帐帷宫。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_32_1364460_comment'></div>缛文房之绣䌽。祥云瑞景。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_33_1364460_comment'></div>霏翰苑之荣光。信探道<span class='inlineComment2'>（一作赜）</span>于元包。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_34_1364460_comment'></div>得斯文于紫极。太平允矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_35_1364460_comment'></div>元首康哉。方欲朝明堂之宫。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_36_1364460_comment'></div>辑群后之瑞。尊崇显号。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_37_1364460_comment'></div>光启圣图。封玉嵩邱。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_38_1364460_comment'></div>以接千年之统。泥金少室。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_39_1364460_comment'></div>攸增万岁之规。卓哉煌煌。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_40_1364460_comment'></div>圣君之表也。微臣<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_41_1364460", 1364460, "Clauses/83/Comments/0")'>曲学</span>蓬户。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_41_1364460_comment'></div>窃位兰台。未闻骢马之谣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_42_1364460_comment'></div>非有雕龙之思。鞠躬<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_43_1364460", 1364460, "Clauses/87/Comments/0")'>霜署</span>。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_43_1364460_comment'></div>谬睹于天章。逖听<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_44_1364460", 1364460, "Clauses/89/Comments/0")'>钧台</span>。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_44_1364460_comment'></div>侧闻于帝乐。天文尊贵<span class='inlineComment2'>（一作贲）</span>。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_45_1364460_comment'></div>不远于下臣。帝宝珍崇。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_46_1364460_comment'></div>曲宣于近贵。窃以君唱臣和。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_47_1364460_comment'></div>固不隔于尊卑。宫变商从。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_48_1364460_comment'></div>方允谐于金石。辄用斋心扣寂。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_51_1364460_comment'></div></div><div id='poem_sentence_52_1364460_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=688&endYear=688')">688年</a>　居东都，守麟台正字。王美畅兄降授亳州司马，子昂为其草谢官表。作品：《为王美畅谢兄官表》<div id='poem_1364485' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1364485' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1364485?labeling=true' target='_blank'>为王美畅谢兄官表</a><span class='authorDate'>（688年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 唐初 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(20887, "唐初", "陈子昂", "poem_title_1364485")'>陈子昂</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1364485_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1364485'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1364485'>臣某言。臣兄某前某官。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1364485_comment'></div>特蒙恩诏。擢授豫州司马。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1364485_comment'></div>未及赴任。即以某月日改亳州司马。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1364485_comment'></div>再三策命。叨荷恩私。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1364485_comment'></div>在臣宗门。实为庆幸。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1364485_comment'></div>中谢。臣兄自解巾从仕。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1364485_comment'></div>三十馀年。五为县宰。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1364485_comment'></div>三迁州佐。政皆通显。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1364485_comment'></div>职实恭勤。直道在公。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1364485_comment'></div>有终始之节。平心应物。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1364485_comment'></div>无造次之愆。在于周行。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1364485_comment'></div>颇蒙推荐。近属虺贞搆逆。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1364485_comment'></div>惑乱豫州。诖误平人。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1364485_comment'></div>自贻<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_13_1364485", 1364485, "Clauses/26/Comments/0")'>枭灭</span>。陛下悯荆河之俗。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1364485_comment'></div>遭此无辜。吊汝濆之人。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1364485_comment'></div>使其昭庆。以为奉扬皇化者必藉其才。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1364485_comment'></div>抚驭穷人者亦资有德。臣兄贞固。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_16_1364485_comment'></div>滥承天奖。迁授豫州。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_17_1364485_comment'></div>在于天恩。实为超擢。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_18_1364485_comment'></div>今者未及赴任。复降授亳州。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_19_1364485_comment'></div>重謺承恩。翻同贬降。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_20_1364485_comment'></div>朝廷体例。实亦为尤。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_21_1364485_comment'></div>臣兄弟叨荣。滥窃非据。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_22_1364485_comment'></div>天慈改授。不合冒闻。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_23_1364485_comment'></div>但以始者承恩。蒙越抽擢。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_24_1364485_comment'></div>今有何过。遂同左迁。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_25_1364485_comment'></div>区区恳诚。辄敢祈诉天泽。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_26_1364485_comment'></div>伏愿皇慈有裕。降昭奖之恩。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_27_1364485_comment'></div>臣兄竭忠。获展才之地。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_28_1364485_comment'></div>小臣死日。犹生之年。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_29_1364485_comment'></div></div><div id='poem_sentence_30_1364485_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=688&endYear=688')">688年</a>　居东都，守麟台正字。宿卫将军程处弼以侄构逆，坐流放遐荒，子昂为其草谢恩表。作品：《为程处弼辞放流表》<div id='poem_1364465' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1364465'
