</span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(20887, "唐初", "陈子昂", "poem_title_1364465")'>陈子昂</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1364465_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1364465'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1364465'>粪土臣某言。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1364465_comment'></div>臣以殃衅。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1364465_comment'></div>侄构凶逆。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1364465_comment'></div>臣合宗族诛戮。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1364465_comment'></div>以显国刑。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1364465_comment'></div>不谓天慈哀矜。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1364465_comment'></div>宥从宽典。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1364465_comment'></div>全臣骸骨。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1364465_comment'></div>生窜遐荒。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1364465_comment'></div>穷魂再造。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1364465_comment'></div>以崩以跃。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1364465_comment'></div>中谢。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1364465_comment'></div>臣闻忠臣事君。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1364465_comment'></div>如子事父。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1364465_comment'></div>穷痛之至。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1364465_comment'></div>则呼所亲。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1364465_comment'></div>何者。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_16_1364465_comment'></div>君父恩深。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_17_1364465_comment'></div>臣子恳切。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_18_1364465_comment'></div>况臣蒙陛下恩遇。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_19_1364465_comment'></div>如子于母。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_20_1364465_comment'></div>今为子不孝。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_21_1364465_comment'></div>为臣不忠。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_22_1364465_comment'></div>长辞阙庭。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_23_1364465_comment'></div>永没<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_24_1364465", 1364465, "Clauses/24/Comments/0")'>荒裔</span>。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_24_1364465_comment'></div>悲穷痛恨。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_25_1364465_comment'></div>荼毒谁依。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_26_1364465_comment'></div>即使朽骨埋魂。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_27_1364465_comment'></div>长灭泉壤。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_28_1364465_comment'></div>恳诚莫展。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_29_1364465_comment'></div>幽翳明恩。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_30_1364465_comment'></div>实恐隐匿于君。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_31_1364465_comment'></div>不尽臣节。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_32_1364465_comment'></div>明神诛殛。<div id='poem_sentence_35_1364465_comment'></div>罄竭诚恳。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_36_1364465_comment'></div>残喘冒死。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_37_1364465_comment'></div>期以少谢。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_38_1364465_comment'></div>伏惟圣母神皇陛下哀怜垂察。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_39_1364465_comment'></div>中谢。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_40_1364465_comment'></div>臣闻犬马贱畜。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_41_1364465_comment'></div>尚知主恩。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_42_1364465_comment'></div>草木无心。<div id='poem_sentence_45_1364465_comment'></div>不足比人。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_46_1364465_comment'></div>负荣怀恩。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_47_1364465_comment'></div>能无感激。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_48_1364465_comment'></div>臣山东孤贱。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_49_1364465_comment'></div>朝无亲故。<div class='inline' class='inline' id='poem_sentence_53_1364465_comment'></div>饰行轨物。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_54_1364465_comment'></div>假借名誉。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_55_1364465_comment'></div>为时吹嘘。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_56_1364465_comment'></div>遂得宿卫阶墀。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_57_1364465_comment'></div>忝职郎将。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_63_1364465_comment'></div>于此可见。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_64_1364465_comment'></div>而贪冒荣宠。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_70_1364465_comment'></div>擢任中郎。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_71_1364465_comment'></div>委以心膂。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_72_1364465_comment'></div>在职未几。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_73_1364465_comment'></div>即检校将军。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_74_1364465_comment'></div>才逾一年。<div class='inline' class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1364489_comment'></div>以臣为凤阁舍人。荣命自天。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1364489_comment'></div>宠章非次。祇奉惶越。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1364489_comment'></div>徒以时逢昭泰。迹忝周行。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1364489_comment'></div>非有君子瑚琏之材。通儒青紫之秀。<div class='inline' 1364489, "Clauses/39/Comments/0")'>龙池</span>。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_19_1364489_comment'></div>愚臣何人。敢冒天造。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_20_1364489_comment'></div>臣闻紫机务重。青锁任隆。<div id='poem_sentence_23_1364489_comment'></div>将何以光赞帝猷。奉扬休命。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_24_1364489_comment'></div>物无异议。政允其中。<div class='inline' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1364456' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1364456?labeling=true' target='_blank'>为程处弼庆拜洛表</a><span class='authorDate'>（689年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 唐初 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(20887, "唐初", "陈子昂", "poem_title_1364456")'>陈子昂</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1364456_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1364456'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1364456'>臣某言。臣粪土残魂。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1364456_comment'></div>合窜荒裔。特蒙陛下施再生之德。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1364456_comment'></div>赦万死之诛。<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_2_1364456", 1364456, "Clauses/5/Comments/0")'>起骨</span>九泉。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1364456_comment'></div>同列编户。臣诚万死。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1364456_comment'></div>无以上答。况恩全贱命。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1364456_comment'></div>生在帝乡。伏见陛下至德配天。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1364456_comment'></div>化及草木。天不爱宝。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1364456_comment'></div>洛出瑞图。地不藏珍。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1364456_comment'></div>河开秘箓。陛下恭承天命。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1364456_comment'></div>因顺子来。建立明堂。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1364456_comment'></div>式尊显号。成之匪日。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1364456_comment'></div>功若有神。万国咸欢。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1364456_comment'></div>百灵同庆。元正肇祚。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1364456_comment'></div>品物惟新。陛下郊祭旻天。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1364456_comment'></div>总受群瑞。神灵庆戴。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1364456_comment'></div>万福攸宜。斯实<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_15_1364456", 1364456, "Clauses/31/Comments/0")'>旷古</span>莫闻。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1364456_comment'></div>于今始见。喙飞蠕动。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_16_1364456_comment'></div>莫不欢心。臣以粪土穷骸。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_17_1364456_comment'></div>不合辄同朝贺。以古来大礼。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_18_1364456_comment'></div>莫盛于今。昔登封泰山。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_19_1364456_comment'></div>七十四主。明堂布政。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_20_1364456_comment'></div>无三数君。诚以陛下道冠古今。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_21_1364456_comment'></div>恩溢天地。昆虫草木。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_22_1364456_comment'></div>犹或相欢。况臣久蒙驱策。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_23_1364456_comment'></div>今日又拔死为生。沟壑残骸。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_24_1364456_comment'></div>而得再造。遂得恭闻大礼。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_25_1364456_comment'></div>侧听鸿名。臣伏惟宇宙之中。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_26_1364456_comment'></div>含气之类。蒙恩负德。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_27_1364456_comment'></div>独臣最甚。向非陛下慈造。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_28_1364456_comment'></div>曲被鸿私。臣巳灰灭遐荒。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_29_1364456_comment'></div>肝涂<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_30_1364456", 1364456, "Clauses/60/Comments/0")'>边壤</span>。岂得尚存骸骨。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_30_1364456_comment'></div>恭闻圣庆。臣所以匍匐冒死。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_31_1364456_comment'></div>不避诛戮。冀申蝼蚁之情。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_32_1364456_comment'></div>以同燕雀之庆。然臣自惟罪累。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_33_1364456_comment'></div>不可比人。在于礼经。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_34_1364456_comment'></div>尤宜自绝。所以屏营粪土。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_35_1364456_comment'></div>不敢先闻。今既万国礼终。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_36_1364456_comment'></div>百神庆毕。昆虫鸟兽。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_37_1364456_comment'></div>亦并欢宁。故臣蝼蚁之诚。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_38_1364456_comment'></div>始敢冒死上贺。臣伏知冒礼违法。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_39_1364456_comment'></div>罪合诛夷。臣生见明时。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_40_1364456_comment'></div>豫闻嘉庆。臣今即殒灭。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_41_1364456_comment'></div>实万死为荣。不胜欢踊戴贺之诚。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_42_1364456_comment'></div></div><div id='poem_sentence_43_1364456_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=689&endYear=689')">689年</a>　居东都，守麟台正字。为永昌父老草追赠武士彟帝号表。作品：《为永昌父老劝追尊忠孝王表》<span class='inlineComment2'>（徐谱考表当作于二月丁酉（十四）之前。）</span><div id='poem_1364468' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1364468' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1364468?labeling=true' target='_blank'>为永昌父老劝追尊中山王表</a><span class='authorDate'>（689年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 唐初 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(20887, "唐初", "陈子昂", class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1364468'>臣闻子贵亲荣。圣人典礼。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1364468_comment'></div>故姬文受命。尊太王之名。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1364468_comment'></div>汉祖登宸。加上皇之号。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1364468_comment'></div>而皆事美帝籍。业盛昌图。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1364468_comment'></div>臣伏见中山大王道合先天。功成佐命。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1364468_comment'></div>昔高祖神尧皇帝义旗爰建。大号初兴。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1364468_comment'></div>首赞皇基。定策京邑。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1364468_comment'></div>用能神驱电扫。应天顺人。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1364468_comment'></div>龙跃紫微。光宅区夏。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1364468_comment'></div>实赖大王之德。翼成高祖之勋。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1364468_comment'></div>开国成家。犹未奉答。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1364468_comment'></div>况陛下应命受天。协运披图。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1364468_comment'></div>正显位于明堂。昭大明于天下。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1364468_comment'></div>功崇五帝。业盛三皇。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1364468_comment'></div>可谓宝极洪名。尊崇光大。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1364468_comment'></div>今者追尊之义。犹阙于显陵。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1364468_comment'></div>荣亲之典。未闻于帝号。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_16_1364468_comment'></div>臣闻商周革命。封宋之君。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_17_1364468_comment'></div>春秋正名。美虞晋之祀。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_18_1364468_comment'></div>夫以兴王继绝。尚不阙于礼经。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_19_1364468_comment'></div>况乎大孝尊亲。岂可亏于祀典。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_20_1364468_comment'></div>臣等餐和白屋。沐庆元门。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_21_1364468_comment'></div>幸为可封之人。叨遇永昌之运。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_22_1364468_comment'></div>伏见陛下则天法地。崇孝临人。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_23_1364468_comment'></div>方且示天下以事亲。正皇猷以达礼。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_24_1364468_comment'></div>苍生之庆。实赖惟新。<div class='inline' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1364487' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1364487?labeling=true' target='_blank'>为百官谢追尊魏国大王表</a><span class='authorDate'>（689年2月）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 唐初 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(20887, "唐初", "陈子昂", "poem_title_1364487")'>陈子昂</a></span><br /><div id='poem_sentence_0_1364487'>臣等昨陈愚恳。请上魏国大王尊号。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1364487_comment'></div>天慈恩孝。降顺群情。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1364487_comment'></div>宇宙咸欢。品物知泰云云。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1364487_comment'></div>臣闻一人有庆。万国欢心。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1364487_comment'></div>况乎道洽奉先。义光尊号。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1364487_comment'></div>伏惟圣母神皇陛下镳官受命。宝极披图。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1364487_comment'></div>以大孝而居尊。勤至仁而育物。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1364487_comment'></div>用能光于四海。化及万方。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1364487_comment'></div>缅惟尊祖之仪。实美前王之典。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1364487_comment'></div>宸心载穆。盛百辟之诚求。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1364487_comment'></div>帝册终开。见千年之盛礼。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1364487_comment'></div>苍氓以之禔福。皇极由其永昌。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1364487_comment'></div>凡在含灵。孰不欢庆。<div class='inline' ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=689&endYear=689')">689年3月19日</a>　居东都，守麟台正字。三月十九日，武后召见，使论为政之要，子昂退而上《答制问事八条》<div id='poem_1364512' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1364512' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1364512?labeling=true' target='_blank'>荅制问事<span class='inlineComment2'>（八条）</span><span style='margin: 0 0.5em'> 其八 </span>请息兵科</a><span class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1364512'>臣伏以当今国家事最大者。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1364512_comment'></div>在兵甲岁兴。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1364512_comment'></div>赋役不省。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1364512_comment'></div>神皇欲安人思化。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1364512_comment'></div>理不可得。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1364512_comment'></div>何者。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1364512_comment'></div>兵之所聚。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1364512_comment'></div>必有所资。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1364512_comment'></div>千里运粮。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1364512_comment'></div>万里应敌。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1364512_comment'></div>十万兵在境。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1364512_comment'></div>则百万家不得安业。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1364512_comment'></div>以此徭役。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1364512_comment'></div>人何敢安。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1364512_comment'></div>臣伏见国家自有事北狄。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1364512_comment'></div>于今十有馀年。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1364512_comment'></div>兵甲岁兴。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_16_1364512_comment'></div>竟不闻其利。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_17_1364512_comment'></div>岂中国无制胜之策。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_18_1364512_comment'></div>朝廷无奇画之臣哉。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_19_1364512_comment'></div>臣窃谓不然。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_20_1364512_comment'></div>是未计之庙算尔。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_21_1364512_comment'></div>臣伏惟神皇圣武天威若神。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_22_1364512_comment'></div>突厥小丑。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_23_1364512_comment'></div>何足诛灭。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_24_1364512_comment'></div>然今未灭者。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_25_1364512_comment'></div>臣恐庸将无智。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_26_1364512_comment'></div>未审庙算之机。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_27_1364512_comment'></div>故使兵甲日多。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_28_1364512_comment'></div>徭役日广。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_29_1364512_comment'></div>今国家又命将出师。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_30_1364512_comment'></div>臣愿神皇审图庙算。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_31_1364512_comment'></div>量其损益。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_32_1364512_comment'></div>计其利害。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_33_1364512_comment'></div>若事必不可请兵不虚行。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_34_1364512_comment'></div>兵不虚行。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_35_1364512_comment'></div>赋役自省。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_36_1364512_comment'></div>以此安人。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_37_1364512_comment'></div>得贤可理。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_38_1364512_comment'></div>若失之于此。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_39_1364512_comment'></div>而救之于彼。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_40_1364512_comment'></div>臣恐人日以疲劳。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_41_1364512_comment'></div>不得安息。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_42_1364512_comment'></div>伏愿熟察臣言。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_43_1364512_comment'></div>审图庙算。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_44_1364512_comment'></div>则夷狄不足灭。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_45_1364512_comment'></div>中国可永宁。</div><div class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1364497' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1364497?labeling=true' target='_blank'>上益国事</a><span class='authorDate'>（689年）</span><span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_0_1364497", 1364497, "Clauses/0/Comments/0")'>富国彊兵</span>。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1364497_comment'></div>未尝不用山泽之利。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1364497_comment'></div>臣伏见西戎未灭。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1364497_comment'></div>兵镇用广。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1364497_comment'></div>内少资储。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1364497_comment'></div>外勒转饷。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1364497_comment'></div>山泽之利。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1364497_comment'></div>伏而未通。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1364497_comment'></div>臣愚不识大体。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1364497_comment'></div>伏见剑南诸山。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1364497_comment'></div>多有铜矿。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1364497_comment'></div>采之铸钱。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1364497_comment'></div>可以富国。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1364497_comment'></div>今诸山皆闭。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1364497_comment'></div>官无采铸。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1364497_comment'></div>军国资用。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1364497_comment'></div>惟敛下人。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_16_1364497_comment'></div>乃使公府虚竭。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_17_1364497_comment'></div>私室贫弊。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_18_1364497_comment'></div>而天地珍藏。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_19_1364497_comment'></div>委废不论。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_20_1364497_comment'></div>以臣所见。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_21_1364497_comment'></div>请依旧式。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_22_1364497_comment'></div>尽令剑南诸州准前采铜。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_23_1364497_comment'></div>于益府铸钱。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_24_1364497_comment'></div>其松潘诸军所须用度。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_25_1364497_comment'></div>皆取以资给用。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_26_1364497_comment'></div>有馀者。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_27_1364497_comment'></div>然后使缘江诸州递运。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_28_1364497_comment'></div>散纳荆衡沔鄂诸州。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_29_1364497_comment'></div>每岁便以和籴。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_30_1364497_comment'></div>令漕运委神都太仓。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_31_1364497_comment'></div>此皆顺流乘便。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_32_1364497_comment'></div>无所劳扰。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_33_1364497_comment'></div>外得以事西山诸军。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_34_1364497_comment'></div>内得以实中都仓廪。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_35_1364497_comment'></div>蜀之百姓。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_36_1364497_comment'></div>免于赋敛。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_37_1364497_comment'></div>军国大利。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_38_1364497_comment'></div>公私所切要者。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_39_1364497_comment'></div>非神皇大圣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_40_1364497_comment'></div>谁能用之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_41_1364497_comment'></div>管仲云。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_42_1364497_comment'></div>圣人用无穷之府。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_43_1364497_comment'></div>盖言此也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_44_1364497_comment'></div>臣某言。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_45_1364497_comment'></div>臣伏见神皇陛下恭已受图。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_46_1364497_comment'></div>遐想至理。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_47_1364497_comment'></div>将欲制御戎狄。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_48_1364497_comment'></div>永安黎元。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_49_1364497_comment'></div>不欲烦挠蒸人。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_50_1364497_comment'></div>故为无益。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_51_1364497_comment'></div>贱臣朝不坐。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_52_1364497_comment'></div>宴不豫。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_53_1364497_comment'></div>军国大事。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_54_1364497_comment'></div>非臣合言。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_55_1364497_comment'></div>伏见松潘军粮。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_56_1364497_comment'></div>费扰过甚。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_57_1364497_comment'></div>太平百姓。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_58_1364497_comment'></div>未得安居。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_59_1364497_comment'></div>臣参班一命。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_60_1364497_comment'></div>庶几仁类。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_61_1364497_comment'></div>不敢自见避讳。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_62_1364497_comment'></div>忍之不言。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_63_1364497_comment'></div>所以不惧身诛。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_64_1364497_comment'></div>区区上奏。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_65_1364497_comment'></div>冒越非次。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_66_1364497_comment'></div>伏待显戮。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_67_1364497_comment'></div>惶悚死罪死罪。</div><div id='poem_sentence_68_1364497_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=689&endYear=689')">689年</a>　居东都，守麟台正字。秩满，随常牒补右卫胄曹参军。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=689&endYear=689')">689年</a>　李司农坐徐敬真谋逆事下狱，获赦官复原职，子昂为其作让官表。作品：《为司农李卿让本官表》<span class='inlineComment2'>（徐谱考此表撰于本年七月之前，姑系此。）</span><div id='poem_1364488' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1364488' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1364488?labeling=true' target='_blank'>为司农李卿让本官表</a><span class='authorDate'>（689年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 唐初 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(20887, "唐初", "陈子昂", "poem_title_1364488")'>陈子昂</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1364488_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1364488'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1364488'>臣某言。伏奉月日恩制。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1364488_comment'></div>依旧授臣中大夫守司农卿。臣枯骨再生。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1364488_comment'></div>更蒙宠命。魂魄竞越。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1364488_comment'></div>不知所图。臣某中谢。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1364488_comment'></div>臣实庸愚。本无名节。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1364488_comment'></div>庇身公族。窃轩冕之馀。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1364488_comment'></div>假翼宗枝。滥衣冠之末。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1364488_comment'></div>因循宠服。累历荣班。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1364488_comment'></div>素餐之责每深。效拙之勤未补。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1364488_comment'></div>横被逆贼徐敬真以私雠架祸诬臣。云与叔孝逸交通逆竖。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1364488_comment'></div>狱官执法。寘以极刑。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1364488_comment'></div>臣腰领之诛。巳甘灰粉。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1364488_comment'></div>泉壤之魄。分隔幽冥。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1364488_comment'></div>不图天地之恩。再生枯骨。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1364488_comment'></div>日月之照。曲被幽泉。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1364488_comment'></div>察臣非辜。慜臣无罪。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1364488_comment'></div>不牵文法之议。特垂赦宥之慈。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_16_1364488_comment'></div>蝼蚁微躯。复得全活。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_17_1364488_comment'></div>自非陛下克明克圣。至德至仁。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_18_1364488_comment'></div>臣之魂骸。不保今日。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_19_1364488_comment'></div>臣免死为幸。岂敢期荣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_20_1364488_comment'></div>陛下重加宠章。还臣旧职。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_21_1364488_comment'></div>典司宗伯。以睦周亲。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_22_1364488_comment'></div>愚臣胡颜。敢冒朝典。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_23_1364488_comment'></div>况臣叔孝逸推使未回。在于臣愚。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_24_1364488_comment'></div>更深待罪。安敢私<span class='inlineComment2'>（一作讼）</span>职。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_25_1364488_comment'></div>以玷国章。伏乞天恩。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_26_1364488_comment'></div>照臣愚恳。不胜感戴生荣之至云云。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_27_1364488_comment'></div></div><div id='poem_sentence_28_1364488_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=689&endYear=689')">689年</a>　居东都，守右卫胄曹参军。有感于酷吏罗织，大狱频起，人人自危，成诗以讽。作品：《感遇 其二十二》<div id='poem_34765' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_34765' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/34765?labeling=true' target='_blank'>感遇诗三十八首<span style='margin: 0 0.5em'> 其二十二 </span></a><span class='authorDate'>（689年）</span><span id='poem_sentence_0_34765'>微霜知岁晏，斧柯始青青。<div id='poem_sentence_0_34765_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_1_34765'>况乃金天夕，浩露沾群英。<div id='poem_sentence_1_34765_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_2_34765'>登山望宇宙，白日已西暝。<div id='poem_sentence_2_34765_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_4_34765'></div><div id='poem_sentence_4_34765_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=689&endYear=689')">689年闰9月</a>　居东都，守右卫胄曹参军。其时大狱增多，子昂上书极谏宽刑。作品：《谏刑书》<div id='poem_1364516' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1364516' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1364516?labeling=true' target='_blank'>谏刑书</a><span class='authorDate'>（689年闰9月）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 唐初 · </span><a class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1364516'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1364516'>承务郎守右卫曹参军臣陈子昂谨顿首昧死上言。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1364516_comment'></div>臣闻昔者圣人务理天下者。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1364516_comment'></div>美在太平。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1364516_comment'></div>太平之美者。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1364516_comment'></div>在于刑措。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1364516_comment'></div>臣伏见陛下务太平之理。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1364516_comment'></div>而未美太平之功。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1364516_comment'></div>贱臣顽微。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1364516_comment'></div>窃惑下列。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1364516_comment'></div>臣前蒙天恩召见。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1364516_comment'></div>恩制赐臣曰。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1364516_comment'></div>既遇非常之主。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1364516_comment'></div>何不进非常之策。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1364516_comment'></div>臣<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_13_1364516", 1364516, "Clauses/13/Comments/0")'>草木</span>微品。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1364516_comment'></div>天恩降休。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1364516_comment'></div>伏刻肌骨。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1364516_comment'></div>不敢忘舍。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_16_1364516_comment'></div>今陛下创三皇之业。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_17_1364516_comment'></div>务三皇之理。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_18_1364516_comment'></div>大统已集。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_19_1364516_comment'></div>神化光明。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_20_1364516_comment'></div>虽伏羲神农。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_21_1364516_comment'></div>昔有天下。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_22_1364516_comment'></div>诚未足比。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_23_1364516_comment'></div>臣敢不竭节以效愚忠。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_24_1364516_comment'></div>臣闻自古圣王谓之大圣者。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_25_1364516_comment'></div>皆云尚德崇礼。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_26_1364516_comment'></div>贵仁贱刑。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_27_1364516_comment'></div>刑措不用。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_28_1364516_comment'></div>谓之圣德。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_29_1364516_comment'></div>不称严刑猛制。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_30_1364516_comment'></div>用狱为理者也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_31_1364516_comment'></div>故周有天下八百馀岁。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_32_1364516_comment'></div>而惟颂成康。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_33_1364516_comment'></div>汉有天下四百馀岁。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_34_1364516_comment'></div>而独称文景。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_35_1364516_comment'></div>皆由几致刑措者也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_36_1364516_comment'></div>何则。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_37_1364516_comment'></div>刑者政之末节。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_38_1364516_comment'></div>非太平之资。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_39_1364516_comment'></div>臣窃考之于天。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_40_1364516_comment'></div>天贵生成。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_41_1364516_comment'></div>验之于人。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_42_1364516_comment'></div>人爱生育。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_43_1364516_comment'></div>旁稽于圣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_44_1364516_comment'></div>圣务胜残。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_45_1364516_comment'></div>皆不云以刑为德者。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_46_1364516_comment'></div>然则圣王养天下者。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_47_1364516_comment'></div>固当上务顺天。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_48_1364516_comment'></div>下务济人。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_49_1364516_comment'></div>不天不人。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_50_1364516_comment'></div>不可谓理。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_51_1364516_comment'></div>故曰惟天为大。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_52_1364516_comment'></div>唯尧则之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_53_1364516_comment'></div>又曰唯天地万物父母。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_54_1364516_comment'></div>唯人万物之灵。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_55_1364516_comment'></div>亶聪明作元后。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_56_1364516_comment'></div>元后作人父母。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_57_1364516_comment'></div>然则为人父母。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_58_1364516_comment'></div>固当贵于德养。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_59_1364516_comment'></div>不可务于刑杀。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_60_1364516_comment'></div>臣伏惟陛下圣德至大矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_61_1364516_comment'></div>应天受命。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_62_1364516_comment'></div>有三皇之功。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_63_1364516_comment'></div>顺人正位。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_64_1364516_comment'></div>有三皇之业。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_65_1364516_comment'></div>拜图巡洛。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_66_1364516_comment'></div>有三皇之符。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_67_1364516_comment'></div><span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_68_1364516", 1364516, "Clauses/68/Comments/0")'>专名</span>显号。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_68_1364516_comment'></div>有三皇之册。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_69_1364516_comment'></div>明堂神构。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_70_1364516_comment'></div>万象宣威。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_71_1364516_comment'></div>风雨顺时。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_72_1364516_comment'></div>百谷<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_73_1364516", 1364516, "Clauses/73/Comments/0")'>昌熟</span>。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_73_1364516_comment'></div>可谓足为万代之规也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_74_1364516_comment'></div>今天下百姓。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_75_1364516_comment'></div>抱孙弄子。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_76_1364516_comment'></div>鼓腹以望太平之政矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_77_1364516_comment'></div>陛下为天地父母。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_78_1364516_comment'></div>固将务德以顺养之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_79_1364516_comment'></div>登于太和。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_80_1364516_comment'></div>以协皇极。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_81_1364516_comment'></div>今陛下之政。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_82_1364516_comment'></div>虽尽善矣。<div id='poem_sentence_201_1364516_comment'></div>辄投<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_202_1364516", 1364516, "Clauses/202/Comments/0")'>谏匦</span>昧死上闻。</div><div id='poem_sentence_202_1364516_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=689&endYear=689')">689年</a>　居东都，守右卫胄曹参军。袁司刑获升迁，上表请让与某人，子昂为其草让官表。作品：《为司刑袁卿让官表》<span class='inlineComment2'>（徐谱考此表当作于本年1至10月间。）</span><div id='poem_1364490' class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 唐初 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(20887, "唐初", "陈子昂", "poem_title_1364490")'>陈子昂</a></span><br /><div id='poem_sentence_2_1364490_comment'></div>祇拜宠光。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1364490_comment'></div>魂首飞越。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1364490_comment'></div>中谢。<div id='poem_sentence_7_1364490_comment'></div>天下允平。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1364490_comment'></div>取兹廷尉。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1364490_comment'></div>苟非其任。<div id='poem_sentence_12_1364490_comment'></div>名术无纪。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1364490_comment'></div>皆缘际会。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1364490_comment'></div>昭遇盛明。<div id='poem_sentence_53_1364490_comment'></div>名不失实。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_54_1364490_comment'></div>圣明有得人之盛。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_55_1364490_comment'></div>愚臣无冒贵之讥。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_56_1364490_comment'></div>实在圣慈。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_57_1364490_comment'></div>鉴非虚谬。</div><div id='poem_sentence_58_1364490_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=689&endYear=689')">689年</a>　居东都，守右卫胄曹参军。子昂宗人凤阁舍人陈嘉言遭诬获罪，子昂上书为其申冤。作品：《申宗人冤狱书》<span class='inlineComment2'>（徐谱考此表当作于武则天拜洛受图而未逾岁之内。姑系此。）</span><div id='poem_1364519' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1364519' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1364519?labeling=true' target='_blank'>申宗人冤狱书</a><span class='authorDate'>（689年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 唐初 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(20887, "唐初", "陈子昂", "poem_title_1364519")'>陈子昂</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1364519_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1364519'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1364519'>臣闻古人言。为国忠臣者半死。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1364519_comment'></div>而为国谏臣者必死。然而至忠之臣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1364519_comment'></div>不避死以谏主。至圣之主。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1364519_comment'></div>不恶直以废忠。臣幸逢陛下至圣大明。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1364519_comment'></div>好忠爱直。每正言极谏。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1364519_comment'></div>特见优容。今陛下方御宝图。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1364519_comment'></div>以临<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_6_1364519", 1364519, "Clauses/12/Comments/0")'>阳馆</span>。崇阐元化。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1364519_comment'></div>宁济苍生。固臣精心洁意。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1364519_comment'></div>愿陛下至德与三皇比矣。然臣伏见陛下有至圣之德。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1364519_comment'></div>左右无至忠之臣。使上下不通。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1364519_comment'></div>内外壅隔。臣窃惧之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1364519_comment'></div>恐后代或以为圣朝无至忠之臣。故臣敢冒万死。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1364519_comment'></div>越职上奏。伏乞天恩宽臣喘息。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1364519_comment'></div>毕尽忠言。臣闻上有圣君。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1364519_comment'></div>下无枉臣。昔舜诛四凶。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1364519_comment'></div>尧不罪舜。周公诛管蔡。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1364519_comment'></div>成王不罪周公。霍光诛燕王。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_16_1364519_comment'></div>昭帝不罪子孟。何者。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_17_1364519_comment'></div>此数公皆为国讨贼。为君殄雠。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_18_1364519_comment'></div>假虽擅权。犹不可罪。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_19_1364519_comment'></div>况奉君命而执法者乎。臣伏见宗人嘉言。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_20_1364519_comment'></div>有至忠之诚。抱<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_21_1364519", 1364519, "Clauses/43/Comments/0")'>徇公</span>之节。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_21_1364519_comment'></div>执法不挠。为国殄雠。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_22_1364519_comment'></div><span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_23_1364519", 1364519, "Clauses/46/Comments/0")'>顷者</span>逆子贼臣。阴搆祸难。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_23_1364519_comment'></div>潜图密计。将危社稷。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_24_1364519_comment'></div>当时逆节初露。朝野震惊。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_25_1364519_comment'></div>赖陛下神武之威。天机<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_26_1364519", 1364519, "Clauses/53/Comments/0")'>电断</span>。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_26_1364519_comment'></div>得奉圣决。恭顺天诛。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_27_1364519_comment'></div>不顾躯命。不避彊御。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_28_1364519_comment'></div>唯法是守。唯恶是雠。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_29_1364519_comment'></div>幸能察罪明辜。穷奸极党。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_30_1364519_comment'></div>使伏法者自首情实。<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_31_1364519", 1364519, "Clauses/63/Comments/0")'>天衢</span>得以清泰。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_31_1364519_comment'></div>万国得以欢宁。<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_32_1364519", 1364519, "Clauses/65/Comments/0")'>诚是</span>陛下神断之明。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_32_1364519_comment'></div>抑亦尽忠之效。陛下所以自监察御史擢拜为凤閤舍人者。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_33_1364519_comment'></div>岂不以表其臣节。报其竭诚。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_34_1364519_comment'></div>使天下之人知其忠恳者也。当此之时。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_35_1364519_comment'></div>忠必见信。行必见明。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_36_1364519_comment'></div>自谓专一事君无贰也。今乃遭诬罔之罪。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_37_1364519_comment'></div>被搆架之词。陷见疑之辜。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_38_1364519_comment'></div>困无验之告。幽穷诏狱。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_39_1364519_comment'></div>吏不见明。肝血赤心。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_40_1364519_comment'></div>无所控告。母年八十。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_41_1364519_comment'></div>老病在床。抱疾喘息。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_42_1364519_comment'></div>朝不保夕。今日身幽狱户。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_43_1364519_comment'></div>死生断绝。朝蒙国荣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_44_1364519_comment'></div>夕为孤囚。臣窃痛之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_45_1364519_comment'></div><span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_46_1364519", 1364519, "Clauses/92/Comments/0")'>顷者</span>至忠。而今日受赂。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_46_1364519_comment'></div>辜负圣主。忧及慈亲。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_47_1364519_comment'></div>诚足痛恨。臣比者固知不免此祸。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_48_1364519_comment'></div>不能度德量力。贪荣昧进。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_49_1364519_comment'></div>以讼受服。谁能免尤。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_50_1364519_comment'></div>向使辞宠让荣。陈力就列。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_51_1364519_comment'></div>雷同众辈。勤恪在公。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_52_1364519_comment'></div>与全躯保妻子之臣恭默圣代。臣固知今日未招此患。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_53_1364519_comment'></div>何者。古人云。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_54_1364519_comment'></div>盗憎主人。被尧诛者。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_55_1364519_comment'></div>不能无怨。顷来执法诛罪。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_56_1364519_comment'></div>多是国之权豪。父雠子怨。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_57_1364519_comment'></div>岂可胜道。亲党阴结。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_58_1364519_comment'></div>同恶相从。假使为脯肉。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_59_1364519_comment'></div>为菹醢。宗诛族灭。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_60_1364519_comment'></div>肝脑涂地。彼凶雠也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_61_1364519_comment'></div>未足以快其心。况蒙国宠荣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_62_1364519_comment'></div>位显朝列。凶雠切齿。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_63_1364519_comment'></div>怨黩何穷。臣窃恐今日之辜。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_64_1364519_comment'></div>已是雠怨者相结搆矣。陛下至圣明察。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_65_1364519_comment'></div>岂不为之降照哉。倘万一雠诬滥罪。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_66_1364519_comment'></div>使凶嚚者得计。忠正者见辜。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_67_1364519_comment'></div>为贼报雠。岂不枉苦。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_68_1364519_comment'></div>夫孤直者众邪之所憎。至公者群恶之所疾。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_69_1364519_comment'></div><span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_70_1364519", 1364519, "Clauses/140/Comments/0")'>寡不敌众</span>。孤不胜群。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_70_1364519_comment'></div>群诬成罪。圣不能救。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_71_1364519_comment'></div>自古所有。非止于今。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_72_1364519_comment'></div>古者吴起事楚。<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_73_1364519", 1364519, "Clauses/147/Comments/0")'>抑削</span><span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_73_1364519", 1364519, "Clauses/147/Comments/1")'>庶族</span>。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_73_1364519_comment'></div>以尊楚君。楚国既强。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_74_1364519_comment'></div>吴起蒙戮。商鞅事秦。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_75_1364519_comment'></div>专讨庶孽。以明秦法。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_76_1364519_comment'></div>秦国既霸。商鞅极刑。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_77_1364519_comment'></div>晁错事汉。诸侯威彊。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_78_1364519_comment'></div>七国骄奢。将淩王室。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_79_1364519_comment'></div>错削弱其势以尊汉。景帝不悟。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_80_1364519_comment'></div>惑奸臣之说。遂族灭晁氏。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_81_1364519_comment'></div>以此三臣。岂不尽忠愿保其君。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_82_1364519_comment'></div>然而身死族亡。为雠者所快。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_83_1364519_comment'></div>皆当代不觉。而后代伤之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_84_1364519_comment'></div>圣主明君。可不谓之痛伤邪。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_85_1364519_comment'></div>臣以嘉言虽无三子之智。窃恐获罪或与之同。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_86_1364519_comment'></div>伏惟陛下仁慈矜怜。悯察其忠。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_87_1364519_comment'></div>且臣闻汉高祖谋楚。与陈平四万金。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_88_1364519_comment'></div>及其为帝。不问金之出入。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_89_1364519_comment'></div>何者。立大功者不求小疵。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_90_1364519_comment'></div>有大忠者不求小过。所谓圣主之至道者也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_91_1364519_comment'></div>陛下豁达大度。至圣宽仁。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_92_1364519_comment'></div>观于汉祖。固已远矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_93_1364519_comment'></div>龌龊小吏。何足为陛下深责哉。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_94_1364519_comment'></div>伏愿天恩矜愚赦罪。念功补过。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_95_1364519_comment'></div>乞将终养老母。获尽馀年。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_96_1364519_comment'></div>岂非圣主之恩。仁君之惠。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_97_1364519_comment'></div>有礼有训。善始善终哉。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_98_1364519_comment'></div>臣于嘉言。亲非骨肉。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_99_1364519_comment'></div>同姓相善。臣知其忠。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_100_1364519_comment'></div>然非是<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_101_1364519", 1364519, "Clauses/202/Comments/0")'>丘园</span>之贤。道德之茂。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_101_1364519_comment'></div>大雅明哲。能保其身。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_102_1364519_comment'></div>假使获罪于天。身首异处。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_103_1364519_comment'></div>盖如一蝼蚁尔。亦何足可称。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_104_1364519_comment'></div>然臣念其曾一日承恩。蒙圣主驱使。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_105_1364519_comment'></div>而不以赤诚取信。今乃负罪见疑。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_106_1364519_comment'></div>臣实痛之。恐累圣主之明。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_107_1364519_comment'></div>伤其老母之寿。身污明法。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_108_1364519_comment'></div>为后代所悲。臣知其忠。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_109_1364519_comment'></div>岂能无惜。所以敢冒万死。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_110_1364519_comment'></div>乞见矜怜。臣若言非至忠。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_111_1364519_comment'></div>苟有侥倖。请受诛斩。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_112_1364519_comment'></div>伏表惶怖。魂魄飞扬。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_113_1364519_comment'></div></div><div id='poem_sentence_114_1364519_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=690&endYear=690')">690年</a>　居东都，守右卫胄曹参军。循州司马高琁卒，旅榇北归，子昂为撰墓志。作品：《唐故循州司马申国公高君墓志》<span class='inlineComment2'>（徐谱考此志当作于本年正月至九月九日之前。）</span><div id='poem_1364551' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1364551' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1364551?labeling=true' target='_blank'>唐故循州司马申国公高君墓志</a><span class='authorDate'>（690年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 唐初 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(20887, "唐初", "陈子昂", "poem_title_1364551")'>陈子昂</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1364551_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1364551'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1364551'>君讳某。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1364551_comment'></div>字某。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1364551_comment'></div>渤海蓨人也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1364551_comment'></div>昔周天子命我太公。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1364551_comment'></div>受封东海。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1364551_comment'></div>钟鼎宝玉。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1364551_comment'></div>七百馀年。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1364551_comment'></div>故其公侯。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1364551_comment'></div>代有国祀。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1364551_comment'></div>曾祖励。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1364551_comment'></div>字敬德。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1364551_comment'></div>北齐朔州大行台仆射。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1364551_comment'></div>袭爵清河王。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1364551_comment'></div>改封乐安王。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1364551_comment'></div>周授开府。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1364551_comment'></div>隋授杨楚洮三州刺史。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1364551_comment'></div>我唐有命。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_16_1364551_comment'></div>崇宠典章。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_17_1364551_comment'></div>贞观初赠恒定并赵四州刺史。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_18_1364551_comment'></div>垂拱中又赠特进。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_19_1364551_comment'></div>非明德上公。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_20_1364551_comment'></div>孰享之哉。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_21_1364551_comment'></div>祖宗俭。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_22_1364551_comment'></div>字士廉。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_23_1364551_comment'></div>皇朝太子太傅上柱国申国公。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_24_1364551_comment'></div>食邑三千户。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_25_1364551_comment'></div>赠司徒并州刺史。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_26_1364551_comment'></div>永徽初赠太尉。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_27_1364551_comment'></div>配享太宗文皇帝庙庭。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_28_1364551_comment'></div>谥曰文献。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_29_1364551_comment'></div>昔帝光天下。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_30_1364551_comment'></div>公实佐之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_31_1364551_comment'></div>至是元勋。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_32_1364551_comment'></div>克配清庙。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_33_1364551_comment'></div>父慜。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_34_1364551_comment'></div>字履行。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_35_1364551_comment'></div>秦府军直千牛滑州刺史将作大匠金紫光禄大夫太常卿洪州都督上柱国申国公。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_36_1364551_comment'></div>尚东阳长公主驸马都尉。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_37_1364551_comment'></div>衣冠礼乐。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_38_1364551_comment'></div>尽在是矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_39_1364551_comment'></div>故帝乙归妹。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_40_1364551_comment'></div>尚于中行。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_41_1364551_comment'></div>公则驸马之元子也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_42_1364551_comment'></div>含章丹穴。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_43_1364551_comment'></div>籍宠<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_44_1364551", 1364551, "Clauses/44/Comments/0")'>黄扉</span>。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_44_1364551_comment'></div>承礼训于公庭。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_45_1364551_comment'></div>尽仪刑于士则。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_46_1364551_comment'></div>年若干。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_47_1364551_comment'></div>嗣封申国公。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_48_1364551_comment'></div>十四解巾。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_49_1364551_comment'></div>授干牛备身。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_50_1364551_comment'></div>趍奉紫璋。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_51_1364551_comment'></div>已有光矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_52_1364551_comment'></div>秩满。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_53_1364551_comment'></div>补海监府左果毅都尉。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_54_1364551_comment'></div>再迁游击将军右师府郎将。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_55_1364551_comment'></div>遂升荣禁卫。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_56_1364551_comment'></div>承宠司阶。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_57_1364551_comment'></div>千庐之务式遵。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_58_1364551_comment'></div>八舍之荣攸袭。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_59_1364551_comment'></div>又授朝散大夫尚辇奉御。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_60_1364551_comment'></div>再迁尚衣奉御。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_61_1364551_comment'></div>属扆宫搆难。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_62_1364551_comment'></div>巫蛊祸兴。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_63_1364551_comment'></div>坐堂弟岐左迁循州司马。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_64_1364551_comment'></div>苍梧南极。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_65_1364551_comment'></div>桂海东浮。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_66_1364551_comment'></div>是唯篁竹之区。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_67_1364551_comment'></div>而有山夷之患。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_68_1364551_comment'></div>永隆二年。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_69_1364551_comment'></div>有盗攻南海。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_70_1364551_comment'></div>广州边鄙被其灾。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_71_1364551_comment'></div>皇帝哀洛越之人罹其凶害。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_72_1364551_comment'></div>以公名家之子。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_73_1364551_comment'></div>才足理戎。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_74_1364551_comment'></div>乃命专征。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_75_1364551_comment'></div>且令招慰。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_76_1364551_comment'></div>公奉天子威令。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_77_1364551_comment'></div>以喻越人。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_78_1364551_comment'></div>越人来苏。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_79_1364551_comment'></div>日有千计。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_80_1364551_comment'></div>公乃惟南蛮不讨之日久矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_81_1364551_comment'></div>国有大命。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_82_1364551_comment'></div>将布远方。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_83_1364551_comment'></div>欲巡御象林。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_84_1364551_comment'></div>观兵海裔。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_85_1364551_comment'></div>彼苍不吊。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_86_1364551_comment'></div>夭我良图。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_87_1364551_comment'></div>因追寇至广州。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_88_1364551_comment'></div>遇疾薨于南海之旅次。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_89_1364551_comment'></div>时年若干。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_90_1364551_comment'></div>呜呼哀哉。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_91_1364551_comment'></div>珠鼎之秀。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_92_1364551_comment'></div>邦国之光。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_93_1364551_comment'></div>负才能。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_94_1364551_comment'></div>重书剑。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_95_1364551_comment'></div>方将克崇旧业。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_96_1364551_comment'></div>祗宠前人。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_97_1364551_comment'></div>降年不长。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_98_1364551_comment'></div>永坠厥绪。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_99_1364551_comment'></div>呜呼哀哉。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_100_1364551_comment'></div>夫人京兆韦氏。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_101_1364551_comment'></div>银青光禄大夫太子詹事武阳侯琨之第某女也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_102_1364551_comment'></div>有淑慎之德。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_103_1364551_comment'></div>窈窕之贤。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_104_1364551_comment'></div>长于公宫。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_105_1364551_comment'></div>少习妇道。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_106_1364551_comment'></div>年十六归于申国。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_107_1364551_comment'></div>凤台<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_108_1364551", 1364551, "Clauses/108/Comments/0")'>尊閟</span>。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_108_1364551_comment'></div>鹊巢斯在。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_109_1364551_comment'></div>虽珠玉翡翠。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_110_1364551_comment'></div>职是其仪。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_111_1364551_comment'></div>而浣濯蘋蘩。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_112_1364551_comment'></div>不改其操。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_113_1364551_comment'></div>故我君子琴瑟友之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_114_1364551_comment'></div>年三十。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_115_1364551_comment'></div>仪凤二年先公而殁。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_116_1364551_comment'></div>其年权殡先茔。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_117_1364551_comment'></div>呜呼哀哉。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_118_1364551_comment'></div>始公之适南裔也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_119_1364551_comment'></div>夫人逝矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_120_1364551_comment'></div>死生言别。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_121_1364551_comment'></div>永怀燕越之悲。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_122_1364551_comment'></div>旌旐同归。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_123_1364551_comment'></div>终沦松柏之路。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_124_1364551_comment'></div>先是公有命合葬。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_125_1364551_comment'></div>宏道岁灵榇自南海还。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_126_1364551_comment'></div>嗣子绍等。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_127_1364551_comment'></div>追惟永终。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_128_1364551_comment'></div>仰遵先志。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_129_1364551_comment'></div>粤载初元年岁在摄提格。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_130_1364551_comment'></div>始昭启亡灵。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_131_1364551_comment'></div>改卜迁祔。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_132_1364551_comment'></div>某月日。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_133_1364551_comment'></div>遂合葬于少陵原。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_134_1364551_comment'></div>礼也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_135_1364551_comment'></div>呜呼哀哉。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_136_1364551_comment'></div>霸山南望。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_137_1364551_comment'></div>秦川满目。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_138_1364551_comment'></div>紫台钟鼓。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_139_1364551_comment'></div>方对于青春。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_140_1364551_comment'></div>白杨邱陵。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_141_1364551_comment'></div>独悲于元夜。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_142_1364551_comment'></div>绍等以东西之人。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_143_1364551_comment'></div>惧冈陵之变。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_144_1364551_comment'></div>古不树。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_145_1364551_comment'></div>今则坟焉。</div><div id='poem_sentence_146_1364551_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=690&endYear=690')">690年</a>　居东都，守右卫胄曹参军。上书请变革蜀中松潘通轨军运粮事。作品：《上蜀川军事》<span class='inlineComment2'>（徐谱考此表当作于垂拱四年五月乙亥（十八）至天授元年九月乙酉（十二）之间。姑系此。）</span><div id='poem_1364496' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1364496' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1364496?labeling=true' target='_blank'>上蜀川军事</a><span class='authorDate'>（690年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 唐初 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(20887, "唐初", "陈子昂", "poem_title_1364496")'>陈子昂</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1364496_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1364496'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1364496'>臣伏见剑南诸州。缘通轨军屯在松潘等州。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1364496_comment'></div>千里运粮。百姓困弊。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1364496_comment'></div>臣不自恤。窃为国家惜之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1364496_comment'></div>伏以国家富有巴蜀。是<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_3_1364496", 1364496, "Clauses/7/Comments/0")'>天府</span>之藏。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1364496_comment'></div>自陇右及河西诸州。军国所资。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1364496_comment'></div>邮驿所给。商旅莫不皆取于蜀。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1364496_comment'></div>又京都府库。岁月珍贡。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1364496_comment'></div>尚在其外。此诚蜀国之珍府。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1364496_comment'></div>今边郡主将。乃通轨一军徭役弊之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1364496_comment'></div>使百姓贫穷。国用不赡。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1364496_comment'></div>河西陇右。资给亦减。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1364496_comment'></div>臣伏惟松潘诸军。自屯镇已来。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1364496_comment'></div>于今相继。百十馀年。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1364496_comment'></div>竟未闻盗贼大侵。而有尺寸之效。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1364496_comment'></div>今国家甘心竭力以事之。臣不知其故。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1364496_comment'></div>伏惟念惜。臣闻上有圣君。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1364496_comment'></div>下得直言。贱臣敢越次冒昧以奏。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_16_1364496_comment'></div>臣在蜀时。见相传云。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_17_1364496_comment'></div>闻松潘等州屯军数不逾万。计粮给饷。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_18_1364496_comment'></div>年则不过七万馀石可盈足。边郡主将。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_19_1364496_comment'></div>不审<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_20_1364496", 1364496, "Clauses/40/Comments/0")'>支度</span>。乃每岁向役十六万夫。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_20_1364496_comment'></div>夫担粮轮送。一㪷之米。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_21_1364496_comment'></div>价钱四百。使百姓老弱。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_22_1364496_comment'></div>未得其所。比年以来。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_23_1364496_comment'></div>多以逃亡。臣伏以吐蕃陛下未忍即灭。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_24_1364496_comment'></div>松潘屯兵未可废散。若准此赋敛。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_25_1364496_comment'></div>每年以十六万夫运粮。臣恐更三年吐蕃未殄灭。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_26_1364496_comment'></div>剑南百姓不堪此役。愚臣恐非圣母神皇制敌安人富国彊兵之神算者也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_27_1364496_comment'></div>愚臣窃见蜀中耆老平议。剑南诸州。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_28_1364496_comment'></div>比来以夫运粮者。且一切并停。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_29_1364496_comment'></div>请为九等税钱。以市骡马。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_30_1364496_comment'></div>差州县富户各为𩢀主。税钱者以充脚价。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_31_1364496_comment'></div>各次第四番运辇。不用一年夫运之费。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_32_1364496_comment'></div>可得数年军食盈足。比于常运。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_33_1364496_comment'></div>减省二十馀倍。蜀川百姓。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_34_1364496_comment'></div>永得休息。通轨军人。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_35_1364496_comment'></div>保安边镇。京台府库。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_36_1364496_comment'></div>河西军马。得利供输其资。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_37_1364496_comment'></div>臣伏审计。便宜体大。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_38_1364496_comment'></div>非一二状俱尽。陛下若以此奏非虚。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_39_1364496_comment'></div>或可采者。请勒臣付<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_40_1364496", 1364496, "Clauses/81/Comments/0")'>所司</span>对议得失。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_40_1364496_comment'></div>然后具条目一一奏闻。若臣苟为<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_41_1364496", 1364496, "Clauses/83/Comments/0")'>谬妄</span>。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_41_1364496_comment'></div>无益国家。请罪死不赦。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_42_1364496_comment'></div></div><div id='poem_sentence_43_1364496_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=690&endYear=690')">690年9月</a>　居东都，守右卫胄曹参军。九月则天称帝，武周代唐，子昂撰《大周受命颂》作品：《大周受命颂四章并序》<div id='poem_1364452' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1364452' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1364452?labeling=true' target='_blank'>大周受命颂</a><span class='authorDate'>（690年9月）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 唐初 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(20887, "唐初", "陈子昂", "poem_title_1364452")'>陈子昂</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1364452_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1364452'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1364452'>臣闻大人升阶。神物绍至。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1364452_comment'></div>必有非人力所能存者。上招飞鸟。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1364452_comment'></div>下动泉鱼。古之元皇。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1364452_comment'></div>祗承上帝。所以协人祉。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1364452_comment'></div>匹天休。卓哉神明。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1364452_comment'></div>昭格上下。莫不以之矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1364452_comment'></div>是故物有可则。而道有可宗。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1364452_comment'></div>谓之文献。其原上也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1364452_comment'></div>缅哉有唐。钦崇天命。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1364452_comment'></div>三祖继统。品物咸章。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1364452_comment'></div>元历改。元黄瑞。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1364452_comment'></div>告神皇。出地轴。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1364452_comment'></div>陟天阶。历轩辕。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1364452_comment'></div>登太昊。集乎初始之极。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1364452_comment'></div>以授我皇。符鸟之肇。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1364452_comment'></div>开辟<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_15_1364452", 1364452, "Clauses/30/Comments/0")'>元台</span>。女希氏姓。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1364452_comment'></div>神功大哉。莫不盛于兹日矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_16_1364452_comment'></div>乃察璿玑。稽宝命。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_17_1364452_comment'></div>发元谶。升紫图。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_18_1364452_comment'></div>则天粲然。皇文炳也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_19_1364452_comment'></div>非夫升光之曜。魄宝之精。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_20_1364452_comment'></div>其孰能威神皇赫赫若斯者哉。是时三阶底平。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_21_1364452_comment'></div>百揆时序。天下昌矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_22_1364452_comment'></div>元功溥矣。西土耆老。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_23_1364452_comment'></div>欣然来称曰。至哉天子。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_24_1364452_comment'></div>恤我元元。勤劳下都。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_25_1364452_comment'></div>升闻上帝。臣闻天无二日。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_26_1364452_comment'></div>土无二王。皇帝嗣武。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_27_1364452_comment'></div>以主<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_28_1364452", 1364452, "Clauses/56/Comments/0")'>匕鬯</span>。岂不宜乎。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_28_1364452_comment'></div>神皇窅然。乃登昆崙之台。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_29_1364452_comment'></div>修<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_30_1364452", 1364452, "Clauses/60/Comments/0")'>三统</span>。观五始。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_30_1364452_comment'></div>探命历之纪。则知元气之所造也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_31_1364452_comment'></div>方采钟龙。象鸣凤。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_32_1364452_comment'></div>协<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_33_1364452", 1364452, "Clauses/66/Comments/0")'>林黄</span>之律。以因生赐姓。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_33_1364452_comment'></div>九月戊申朔八日乙卯。神都耆老。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_34_1364452_comment'></div>遐荒夷貊。缁衣黄冠等万有二千馀人。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_35_1364452_comment'></div>云趍诣阙请曰。臣等闻王者受命。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_36_1364452_comment'></div>必有锡氏。轩辕皇帝二十五子。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_37_1364452_comment'></div>班为十二姓。高阳氏才子二八。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_38_1364452_comment'></div>命为十六族。书云。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_39_1364452_comment'></div>祇台德先。不拒朕行。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_40_1364452_comment'></div>然则圣人起则命历昌。必有锡氏之规。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_41_1364452_comment'></div>臣等伏惟陛下受天之符。为人圣母。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_42_1364452_comment'></div>皇帝仁孝。肃恭神明。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_43_1364452_comment'></div>可以纂武承家。以克永代。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_44_1364452_comment'></div>陛下崇锡类。垂宪章。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_45_1364452_comment'></div>不易日月。天人交际。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_46_1364452_comment'></div>斯亦万代之一时。臣等固陋。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_47_1364452_comment'></div>不达大道。敢冒死上闻。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_48_1364452_comment'></div>神皇穆然。方御珍图。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_49_1364452_comment'></div>谦而未许也。越翌日丙辰。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_50_1364452_comment'></div>文武百寮。又与耆老夷貊道俗等五万馀人。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_51_1364452_comment'></div>守阙固请曰。盖臣闻圣人则天以王。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_52_1364452_comment'></div>顺人以昌。今天命陛下以主。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_53_1364452_comment'></div>人以陛下为母。天之丕律。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_54_1364452_comment'></div>元命也。人之大猷。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_55_1364452_comment'></div>定姓也。陛下不应天。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_56_1364452_comment'></div>不顺人。独高谦让之道。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_57_1364452_comment'></div>无所宪法。臣等何所仰则。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_58_1364452_comment'></div>敬冒昧万死固请。是时□踵昆吾。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_59_1364452_comment'></div>有凤鸟从南方来。历端门。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_60_1364452_comment'></div>群鸟数千蔽之。又有赤雀数百从东方来。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_61_1364452_comment'></div>群飞映云。回翔紫闼。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_62_1364452_comment'></div>或止庭树。有黄雀从之者。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_63_1364452_comment'></div>又有庆云。休光半天。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_64_1364452_comment'></div>倾都毕见。群臣咸睹。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_65_1364452_comment'></div>于是众氓云萃。嚣声雷动。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_66_1364452_comment'></div>庆天应之如响。惊象物其犹神。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_67_1364452_comment'></div>咸曰大哉。非至德孰能睹此。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_68_1364452_comment'></div>昔唐虞之瑞逖听矣。今则见也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_69_1364452_comment'></div>天物来。圣人革。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_70_1364452_comment'></div>时哉。况凤者阳鸟。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_71_1364452_comment'></div>赤雀火精。黄雀从之者土也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_72_1364452_comment'></div>土则火之子。子随母。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_73_1364452_comment'></div>所以纂母姓。天意如彼。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_74_1364452_comment'></div>人诚如此。陛下曷可辞之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_75_1364452_comment'></div>昔金天凤凰。镐京黄鸟。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_76_1364452_comment'></div><span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_77_1364452", 1364452, "Clauses/154/Comments/0")'>赤氏</span>朱雁。有吴丹乌。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_77_1364452_comment'></div>皆纪之金册。藏之瑞府。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_78_1364452_comment'></div>以有事也。陛下若遂辞之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_79_1364452_comment'></div>是推天而绝人。将何以训。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_80_1364452_comment'></div>于是皇霈然曰。俞哉。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_81_1364452_comment'></div>此亦天授也。乃命有司正皇典。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_82_1364452_comment'></div>恢帝纲。建大周之统历。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_83_1364452_comment'></div>革旧唐之遗号。在宥天下。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_84_1364452_comment'></div>咸与惟新。赐皇帝姓曰武氏。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_85_1364452_comment'></div>命为嗣皇。崇乎绍天统物。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_86_1364452_comment'></div>其赫胥大庭之上事巳。乃献颂曰。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_87_1364452_comment'></div></div><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_88_1364452'>天命神凤。降祚我周。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_88_1364452_comment'></div>彩容有穆。其仪孔休。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_89_1364452_comment'></div>惟我有周。实保天德。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_90_1364452_comment'></div>上帝临命。纂承皇极。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_91_1364452_comment'></div>人曰天祐。有皇女希。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_92_1364452_comment'></div>造天立极。缅然猷徽。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_93_1364452_comment'></div>赫我皇帝。乃先厥微。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_94_1364452_comment'></div>匪天之命。凤鸟谁归。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_95_1364452_comment'></div>因生锡氏。革号循机。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_96_1364452_comment'></div>岂不顺乎天而应乎人。帝曰俞哉。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_97_1364452_comment'></div></div><div id='poem_sentence_98_1364452_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=690&endYear=690')">690年9月</a>　居东都，守右卫胄曹参军。九月则天称帝，武周代唐，子昂撰《大周受命颂》，作表上呈。作品：《上大周受命颂表》<div id='poem_1364453' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1364453' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1364453?labeling=true' target='_blank'>上大周受命颂表</a><span class='authorDate'>（690年9月）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 唐初 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(20887, "唐初", "陈子昂", "poem_title_1364453")'>陈子昂</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1364453_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1364453'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1364453'>臣子昂言。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1364453_comment'></div>臣闻昔周道昌而颂声作。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1364453_comment'></div>遂能昭配天地。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1364453_comment'></div>光烈祖宗。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1364453_comment'></div>垂之无穷。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1364453_comment'></div>永为代典。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1364453_comment'></div>伏惟神圣皇帝陛下阐元极。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1364453_comment'></div>升紫图。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1364453_comment'></div>光有唐基。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1364453_comment'></div>以启周室。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1364453_comment'></div>不改旧物。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1364453_comment'></div>天下惟新。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1364453_comment'></div>皇王以来。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1364453_comment'></div>未尝睹也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1364453_comment'></div>臣闻仲尼曰。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1364453_comment'></div>圣人邱不得而见之矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1364453_comment'></div>又曰。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_16_1364453_comment'></div>舜禹之有天下。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_17_1364453_comment'></div>邱不豫也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_18_1364453_comment'></div>又曰。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_19_1364453_comment'></div>凤鸟不至。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_20_1364453_comment'></div>河不出图。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_21_1364453_comment'></div>邱巳矣夫。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_22_1364453_comment'></div>皆伤不得见大道之行而郁悒也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_23_1364453_comment'></div>臣草野愚陋。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_24_1364453_comment'></div>生长休明。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_25_1364453_comment'></div>亲逢圣人。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_26_1364453_comment'></div>又睹昌运。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_27_1364453_comment'></div>舜禹之政。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_28_1364453_comment'></div>河洛之图。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_29_1364453_comment'></div>悉皆目见。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_30_1364453_comment'></div>幸亦多矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_31_1364453_comment'></div>今者凤鸟来。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_32_1364453_comment'></div>赤雀至。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_33_1364453_comment'></div>庆云见。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_34_1364453_comment'></div>休气升。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_35_1364453_comment'></div>大周受命之珍符也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_36_1364453_comment'></div>不稽元命。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_37_1364453_comment'></div>探秘文。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_38_1364453_comment'></div>采风谣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_39_1364453_comment'></div>挥象物。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_40_1364453_comment'></div>纪天人之会。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_41_1364453_comment'></div>以协颂声。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_42_1364453_comment'></div>则臣下之过也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_43_1364453_comment'></div>有国彝典。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_44_1364453_comment'></div>其可阙乎。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_45_1364453_comment'></div>臣不揣朴固。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_46_1364453_comment'></div>辄献神凤颂四章。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_47_1364453_comment'></div>以言大周受命之事。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_48_1364453_comment'></div>诚未足以润色鸿业。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_49_1364453_comment'></div>揄扬盛美。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_50_1364453_comment'></div>亦小臣区区丹慊之至。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_51_1364453_comment'></div>谨辄诣洛城南门奉进。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_52_1364453_comment'></div><span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_53_1364453", 1364453, "Clauses/53/Comments/0")'>尘冒</span>旒冕。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_53_1364453_comment'></div>伏表惭惶。</div><div id='poem_sentence_54_1364453_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=690&endYear=690')">690年</a>　居东都，守右卫胄曹参军。郑某拜资州刺史，子昂为之草让官表。作品：《为资州郑使君让官表》<span class='inlineComment2'>（徐谱考表当作于天授元年九月武则天改唐为周后不久。）</span><div id='poem_1364491' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1364491' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1364491?labeling=true' class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1364491'>臣某言。伏奉月日制。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1364491_comment'></div>以臣为资州剌史。恭承玺命。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1364491_comment'></div>祇拜宠章。匪服知惭。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1364491_comment'></div>循荣如失。中谢。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1364491_comment'></div>臣学惭名术。才乏器能。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1364491_comment'></div>而宝历逢时。金章坐忝。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1364491_comment'></div>题舆佐岳。无<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_6_1364491", 1364491, "Clauses/13/Comments/0")'>展骥</span>之庸。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1364491_comment'></div>剖竹专城。阙悬鱼之化。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1364491_comment'></div>坐啸徒积。<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_8_1364491", 1364491, "Clauses/17/Comments/0")'>主诺</span>空惭。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1364491_comment'></div>伏惟陛下革命开基。造天立极。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1364491_comment'></div>六条班政。允属其才。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1364491_comment'></div>臣疲朽巳侵。循良久昧。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1364491_comment'></div>将何式光刺举。允协得人。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1364491_comment'></div>伏愿博选英才。克谐佥议。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1364491_comment'></div>使人光理。政洽惟良。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_16_1364491_comment'></div>大周之命惟新。愚臣之责攸息。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_17_1364491_comment'></div>其所让人。具如别状。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_18_1364491_comment'></div></div><div id='poem_sentence_19_1364491_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=690&endYear=690')">690年9月</a>　居东都，守右卫胄曹参军。李峤上《皇帝丘礼抚事述怀》诗，则天命群臣相和，子昂应制和诗。作品：《奉和皇帝丘礼抚事述怀应制》<span
