id='poem_sentence_10_34738_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=690&endYear=690')">690年</a>　居东都，守右卫胄曹参军。乔知之上表庆武成殿，子昂为之草表。作品：《为乔补阙庆武成殿表》<span class='inlineComment2'>（徐谱考表当撰于九月乙酉（十二）至十月之间。）</span><div id='poem_1364455' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1364455' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1364455?labeling=true' target='_blank'>为乔补阙庆武成殿表</a><span class='authorDate'>（690年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 唐初 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(20887, "唐初", "陈子昂", "poem_title_1364455")'>陈子昂</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1364455_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1364455'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1364455'>臣某言。臣以今月日奉敕。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1364455_comment'></div>于武成殿唤臣入。问骨笃禄等贼请降事。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1364455_comment'></div>臣以愚瞽。得践赤墀。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1364455_comment'></div>对扬天休。具奏其状。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1364455_comment'></div>天恩特赐臣温颜。又降问云。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1364455_comment'></div>洛阳宫室。皆隋朝营制。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1364455_comment'></div>岁月久远。方有隳颓。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1364455_comment'></div>楼阁内殿。凋落者众。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1364455_comment'></div>补一坏百。无可施功。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1364455_comment'></div>唯此武成。确然端立。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1364455_comment'></div>土木丹䌽。光色如新。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1364455_comment'></div>不知何故。得自如此。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1364455_comment'></div>卿之博识。应知其说。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1364455_comment'></div>臣当时造次。略奏其梗概。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1364455_comment'></div>退而再省。未涉万分。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1364455_comment'></div>臣恭惟圣言。缅求神像。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1364455_comment'></div>研几太极。幽赞元符。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_16_1364455_comment'></div>上以稽验神谋。旁以合契冥数。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_17_1364455_comment'></div>信有至道。允在于兹。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_18_1364455_comment'></div>臣闻圣人有言曰。清明在躬。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_19_1364455_comment'></div>志气如神。嗜欲将至。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_20_1364455_comment'></div>有开必先。天降时雨。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_21_1364455_comment'></div>山川出云。此盖言神应。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_22_1364455_comment'></div>必有其物。陛下至尊至神。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_23_1364455_comment'></div>为天下主。宰御群品。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_24_1364455_comment'></div>威统百灵。宸居尊严。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_25_1364455_comment'></div>品物昭泰。自天而祐。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_26_1364455_comment'></div>于是用宁。抑臣又闻物之有灵。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_27_1364455_comment'></div>如人之有神。神之和畅。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_28_1364455_comment'></div>则支体便利。用人繁昌。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_29_1364455_comment'></div>则物必丰茂。所以见其俗知兴废之数。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_30_1364455_comment'></div>睹其气识盛衰之由。服物犹然。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_31_1364455_comment'></div>况其大者。今陛下应天受命。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_32_1364455_comment'></div>括地登枢。先飞名于秘箓。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_33_1364455_comment'></div>终据图于宝座。今则当千载之运。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_34_1364455_comment'></div>得三统之元。帝气氤氲。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_35_1364455_comment'></div>祚基于元命。皇图幽蔼。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_36_1364455_comment'></div>象显于天成。夫以德之休明。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_37_1364455_comment'></div>尚荣草木。化之昭庆。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_38_1364455_comment'></div>且变烟云。况皇皇真君。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_39_1364455_comment'></div>龙居其极。武成合庆。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_40_1364455_comment'></div>土木增荣。独超众殿。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_41_1364455_comment'></div>夫何足怪。臣闻敬其事者必载其文。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_42_1364455_comment'></div>美其业者必颂其德。臣所恨才非<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_43_1364455", 1364455, "Clauses/87/Comments/0")'>墨妙</span>。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_43_1364455_comment'></div>思乏笔精。不能赞扬休祚。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_44_1364455_comment'></div>歌咏圣德。臣请以此事付之史臣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_45_1364455_comment'></div>千代知神。万载知述。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_46_1364455_comment'></div>伏愿天恩。特垂降许。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_47_1364455_comment'></div></div><div id='poem_sentence_48_1364455_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=690&endYear=690')">690年</a>　居东都，守右卫胄曹参军。有感于僧怀义、法明等妄言符命，诛杀诸王大臣，纲常纷乱，子昂究天人之际而不得其解，幽思困苦，赋诗以慨之。作品：《感遇 其八》<div id='poem_34755' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_34755' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/34755?labeling=true' target='_blank'>感遇诗三十八首<span style='margin: 0 0.5em'> 其八 </span></a><span class='authorDate'>（690年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 唐初 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(20887, "唐初", "陈子昂", "poem_title_34755")'>陈子昂</a></span><br id='poem_sentence_0_34755_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_1_34755'>精魄相交会，天壤以罗生。<div id='poem_sentence_1_34755_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_2_34755'>仲尼推太极，老聃贵窈冥。<div id='poem_sentence_2_34755_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_3_34755'>西方金仙子，崇义乃无明。<div ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=690&endYear=690')">690年</a>　居东都，守右卫胄曹参军。有感于奸佞妄陈符命，惑世酿祸，赋诗以讽。作品：《感遇 其九》<div id='poem_34756' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_34756' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=691&endYear=691')">691年1月</a>　居东都，守右卫胄曹参军。春一月，朝集使二千八百人表请封中岳，子昂草劝封禅表。作品：《为赤县父老劝封禅表》<div id='poem_1364467' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1364467' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1364467?labeling=true' target='_blank'>为赤县父老劝封禅表</a><span class='authorDate'>（691年1月）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 唐初 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(20887, "唐初", "陈子昂", "poem_title_1364467")'>陈子昂</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1364467_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1364467'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1364467'>臣闻帝功既乂。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1364467_comment'></div>必昭告于上元。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1364467_comment'></div>元命攸尊。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1364467_comment'></div>必升封于厚载。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1364467_comment'></div>故七十二主能恢万代之规。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1364467_comment'></div>三五六经以为百王之典。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1364467_comment'></div>伏惟陛下应天受命。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1364467_comment'></div>握纪<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_7_1364467", 1364467, "Clauses/7/Comments/0")'>登枢</span>。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1364467_comment'></div>包括乾坤之灵。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1364467_comment'></div>亭毒神明之化。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1364467_comment'></div>故能开天宝。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1364467_comment'></div>阐地珍。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1364467_comment'></div>温洛所以升图。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1364467_comment'></div>荣河由其荐箓。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1364467_comment'></div>群神既赞。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1364467_comment'></div>众瑞交驰。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1364467_comment'></div>讴歌于是大归。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_16_1364467_comment'></div>礼乐以之咸备。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_17_1364467_comment'></div>陛下仰顺天意。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_18_1364467_comment'></div>允答神休。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_19_1364467_comment'></div>垂显号以居宸。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_20_1364467_comment'></div>建明堂而治物。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_21_1364467_comment'></div>百寮惟允。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_22_1364467_comment'></div>万国咸宁。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_23_1364467_comment'></div>然则嵩岳神宗。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_24_1364467_comment'></div>望玉銮而来禅。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_25_1364467_comment'></div>天中仙族。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_26_1364467_comment'></div>伫金驾而崇封。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_27_1364467_comment'></div>实大礼<span class='inlineComment2'>（一作德）</span>之昌期。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_28_1364467_comment'></div>膺告成之茂典。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_29_1364467_comment'></div>况神都为八方之极。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_30_1364467_comment'></div>太室居五岳之尊。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_31_1364467_comment'></div>陛下垂统紫微。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_32_1364467_comment'></div>大昌黄运。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_33_1364467_comment'></div>报功崇德。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_34_1364467_comment'></div>允协神心。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_35_1364467_comment'></div>应天顺人。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_36_1364467_comment'></div>雅符灵望。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_37_1364467_comment'></div>皇图盛业。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_38_1364467_comment'></div>实在于兹。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_39_1364467_comment'></div>臣等叨愿尧封。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_40_1364467_comment'></div>久忘帝力。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_41_1364467_comment'></div>窃闻圣人封禅。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_42_1364467_comment'></div>天下所以会昌。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_43_1364467_comment'></div>山岳成功。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_44_1364467_comment'></div>皇寿由其配永。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_45_1364467_comment'></div>臣等既为陛下赤子。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_46_1364467_comment'></div>陛下又为万姓慈亲。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_47_1364467_comment'></div>实愿上报天功。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_48_1364467_comment'></div>下顺人望。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_49_1364467_comment'></div>勒成嵩岳。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_50_1364467_comment'></div>大显尊名。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_51_1364467_comment'></div>不胜庆幸之至。</div><div id='poem_sentence_52_1364467_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=691&endYear=691')">691年2月1日</a>　居东都，守右卫胄曹参军。为已故袁州李参军妻张氏撰墓志。作品：《唐故袁州参军李府君妻清河张氏墓志铭》<div id='poem_1364554' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1364554' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1364554?labeling=true' target='_blank'>唐故袁州参军李府君妻张氏墓志铭</a><span class='authorDate'>（691年2月1日）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 唐初 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(20887, "唐初", "陈子昂", "poem_title_1364554")'>陈子昂</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1364554_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1364554'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1364554'>夫人讳某。清河郡东武城人也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1364554_comment'></div>昔轩辕锡允。弧矢崇威。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1364554_comment'></div>畏其神者三百年。得其姓者十四族。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1364554_comment'></div>金貂七叶。汉天子之忠臣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1364554_comment'></div>鼎足三公。晋武皇之名相。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1364554_comment'></div>孤卿玉帛。世有其庸。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1364554_comment'></div>曾祖某。北齐太常卿徐兖二州刺史。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1364554_comment'></div>天人之礼。位掌于<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_7_1364554", 1364554, "Clauses/15/Comments/0")'>秩宗</span>。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1364554_comment'></div>侯伯之尊。宠优于露冕。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1364554_comment'></div>祖某。隋汾阴寿春阳城三县令。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1364554_comment'></div>袭公侯之瑞。屈铜墨之班。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1364554_comment'></div>士元非百里之才。太邱有三台之望。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1364554_comment'></div>父某。唐户部侍郎复亳建三州刺史。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1364554_comment'></div>尚书北斗。始赞于南宫。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1364554_comment'></div>方岳专城。终荣于独坐。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1364554_comment'></div>夫人即刺史之第若干女也。禀柔成性。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1364554_comment'></div>蕴粹含章。承礼训于公庭。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_16_1364554_comment'></div>习威仪于<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_17_1364554", 1364554, "Clauses/34/Comments/0")'>壸则</span>。夫其窈窕之秀。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_17_1364554_comment'></div><span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_18_1364554", 1364554, "Clauses/36/Comments/0")'>婉娈</span>之姿。贞节峻于寒松。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_18_1364554_comment'></div><span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_19_1364554", 1364554, "Clauses/38/Comments/0")'>韶仪</span>丽于温玉。铅华不御。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_19_1364554_comment'></div>饰环佩之容。浣濯是衣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_20_1364554_comment'></div>勤黼黻之䌽。自作嫔于君子。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_21_1364554_comment'></div>主中馈于家人。三千之礼不违。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_22_1364554_comment'></div>九十之仪无慝。至乃恭于奉上。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_23_1364554_comment'></div>顺于接下。仁孝以承宗祀。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_24_1364554_comment'></div>慈惠以睦闺门。则雍雍跄跄。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_25_1364554_comment'></div>必由其道矣。呜呼。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_26_1364554_comment'></div>府君不造。遘此闵凶。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_27_1364554_comment'></div>中年不图。早世而殒。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_28_1364554_comment'></div>青松摧折。哀断女萝之心。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_29_1364554_comment'></div><span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_30_1364554", 1364554, "Clauses/60/Comments/0")'>丹节</span>孤高。终守柏舟之誓。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_30_1364554_comment'></div>而府君食先人之德。无厚生之财。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_31_1364554_comment'></div>夫人徇黔娄之贞。阙<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_32_1364554", 1364554, "Clauses/65/Comments/0")'>丹台</span>之产。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_32_1364554_comment'></div>孀居永日。<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_33_1364554", 1364554, "Clauses/67/Comments/0")'>蓬首</span>终年。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_33_1364554_comment'></div>处<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_34_1364554", 1364554, "Clauses/68/Comments/0")'>贫素</span>而弥坚。保幽芳而不昧。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_34_1364554_comment'></div>始府君之逝。有四子焉。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_35_1364554_comment'></div>少遭罔极之哀。未奉过庭之训。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_36_1364554_comment'></div>夫人保持名教。终始礼经。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_37_1364554_comment'></div>既勖之以义方。又申之以远大。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_38_1364554_comment'></div>皆能率由慈训。克荷嘉声。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_39_1364554_comment'></div>箕裘之业载隆。燕翼之谋不霣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_40_1364554_comment'></div>非夫淑明贤懿。圣善温良。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_41_1364554_comment'></div>崇妇道之深规。宏母仪之至范。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_42_1364554_comment'></div>孰能昭宣令问。若斯之盛哉。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_43_1364554_comment'></div>彼苍不忱。歼我眉寿。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_44_1364554_comment'></div>春秋若干。载初元年月日。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_45_1364554_comment'></div>遘疾终于洛州某里之私第。呜呼哀哉。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_46_1364554_comment'></div>夫人令仪有穆。惠问无喧。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_47_1364554_comment'></div>敦雅志于诗书。婉娴情于琴瑟。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_48_1364554_comment'></div>若乃姆师酒食之议。女工纂组之繁。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_49_1364554_comment'></div>莫不总制清衷。宏宣懿则。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_50_1364554_comment'></div>茂蘋蘩之雅训。协沼沚之芳猷。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_51_1364554_comment'></div>虽古称敬姜。诗云淑女。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_52_1364554_comment'></div>论容比德。殆无以过。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_53_1364554_comment'></div>秾华不居。私扃永閟。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_54_1364554_comment'></div>嗣子某等。悲摧栾棘。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_55_1364554_comment'></div>思结寒泉。永惟<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_56_1364554", 1364554, "Clauses/113/Comments/0")'>同穴</span>之仪。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_56_1364554_comment'></div>仰遵归祔之典。以大周天授二年二月日朔。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_57_1364554_comment'></div>迁祔于袁州府君之旧茔。礼也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_58_1364554_comment'></div>合葬非古。奉周公之仪。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_59_1364554_comment'></div>墓而为坟。宗仲尼之训。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_60_1364554_comment'></div>呜呼。鸳鸯之树。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_61_1364554_comment'></div>眇泣于松楸。鼓吹之山。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_62_1364554_comment'></div>缅然于邱垄。原陵何代。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_63_1364554_comment'></div>铭志无文。有哀黄鸟之诗。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_64_1364554_comment'></div>遂勒青乌之兆。铭曰。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_65_1364554_comment'></div></div><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_66_1364554'>诗云淑女。君子好求。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_66_1364554_comment'></div>懿哉令德。嘉仪聿修。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_67_1364554_comment'></div>温容玉映。峻节松楸。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_68_1364554_comment'></div>妙心彤史。洁志玄猷。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_69_1364554_comment'></div>昭宣<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_70_1364554", 1364554, "Clauses/140/Comments/0")'>壸则</span>。惠穆蘋洲。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_70_1364554_comment'></div>共伯早逝。贞姜独留。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_71_1364554_comment'></div>茕居<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_72_1364554", 1364554, "Clauses/144/Comments/0")'>蓬首</span>。哀深柏舟。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_72_1364554_comment'></div>彼苍不憖。此夜长幽。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_73_1364554_comment'></div>怀南风之吹棘。想北陇以同邱。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_74_1364554_comment'></div>青春兮白日。独昭昭以悠悠。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_75_1364554_comment'></div></div><div id='poem_sentence_76_1364554_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=691&endYear=691')">691年</a>　居东都，守右卫胄曹参军。友陈州宛丘高县令改葬先君，迁祔夫人及诸子之柩，子昂为之撰墓志二，祭文二。作品：《唐陈州宛丘县令高府君夫人河南宇文氏墓志铭》《祭外姑宇文夫人文》《上殇高氏墓志铭》《祭黄州高府君文》<div id='poem_1364556' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1364556' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1364556?labeling=true' target='_blank'>唐陈州宛邱县令高府君夫人河南宇文氏墓志铭</a><span class='authorDate'>（691年2月1日）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 唐初 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(20887, "唐初", "陈子昂", "poem_title_1364556")'>陈子昂</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1364556_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1364556'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1364556'>夫人讳某。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1364556_comment'></div>河南郡人也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1364556_comment'></div>昔吾君夏后氏之子。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1364556_comment'></div>霸有幽都。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1364556_comment'></div>皇运北兴。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1364556_comment'></div>鼎图南起。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1364556_comment'></div>开宝符而帝天下。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1364556_comment'></div>抚璿玑而王中国。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1364556_comment'></div>则后周之受命。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1364556_comment'></div>武帝之云孙。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1364556_comment'></div>夫人四代祖也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1364556_comment'></div>曾祖某。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1364556_comment'></div>失周子之封。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1364556_comment'></div>亡山阳之国。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1364556_comment'></div>虽存天子之允。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1364556_comment'></div>已类咸阳布衣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1364556_comment'></div>植德早夭。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_16_1364556_comment'></div>祖某。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_17_1364556_comment'></div>隋朝官澧州澧阳县令。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_18_1364556_comment'></div>父某。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_19_1364556_comment'></div>龙州司法。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_20_1364556_comment'></div>皆承家席宠。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_21_1364556_comment'></div>代有令名。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_22_1364556_comment'></div>夫人贲秾华。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_23_1364556_comment'></div>袭繁祉。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_24_1364556_comment'></div>崇徽惠穆。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_25_1364556_comment'></div>秀色<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_26_1364556", 1364556, "Clauses/26/Comments/0")'>苕荣</span>。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_26_1364556_comment'></div>自于幼年。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_27_1364556_comment'></div>有令仪也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_28_1364556_comment'></div>十四适于高府君。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_29_1364556_comment'></div>夫其温慈惠和。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_30_1364556_comment'></div>信肃修穆。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_31_1364556_comment'></div>行有法度。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_32_1364556_comment'></div>动有礼经。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_33_1364556_comment'></div>严恪以理家人。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_34_1364556_comment'></div><span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_35_1364556", 1364556, "Clauses/35/Comments/0")'>僩瑟</span>以和君子。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_35_1364556_comment'></div>则已含乎光大矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_36_1364556_comment'></div>若乃宗庙衷敬。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_37_1364556_comment'></div>仁孝也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_38_1364556_comment'></div>娣姒祗和。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_39_1364556_comment'></div>谦顺也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_40_1364556_comment'></div>蠲洁酒食。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_41_1364556_comment'></div>妇仪也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_42_1364556_comment'></div>黼黻元黄。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_43_1364556_comment'></div>女工也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_44_1364556_comment'></div>宏此四德。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_45_1364556_comment'></div>而务六亲。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_46_1364556_comment'></div>鞶帨以文之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_47_1364556_comment'></div>杂佩以发之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_48_1364556_comment'></div>猗可以作范母仪。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_49_1364556_comment'></div>昭宣壸则矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_50_1364556_comment'></div>至于训子以睦。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_51_1364556_comment'></div>教女以顺。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_52_1364556_comment'></div>爱下以慈。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_53_1364556_comment'></div>与人以让。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_54_1364556_comment'></div>外以赞府君之德。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_55_1364556_comment'></div>内以光中馈之教。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_56_1364556_comment'></div>皆曰闻其进不见其退也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_57_1364556_comment'></div>呜呼。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_58_1364556_comment'></div>仁而不寿。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_59_1364556_comment'></div>生也永终。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_60_1364556_comment'></div>永淳元年五月。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_61_1364556_comment'></div>遇疾终于宛邱县之官舍。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_62_1364556_comment'></div>时年二十七。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_63_1364556_comment'></div>呜呼哀哉。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_64_1364556_comment'></div>高府君寻以公事罢职。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_65_1364556_comment'></div>山茔未卜。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_66_1364556_comment'></div>旌旐来归。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_67_1364556_comment'></div>府君思北海之魂。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_68_1364556_comment'></div>留东园而殡。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_69_1364556_comment'></div>日月遂往。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_70_1364556_comment'></div>九岁于兹。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_71_1364556_comment'></div>府君方崇树先茔。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_72_1364556_comment'></div>增封旧域。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_73_1364556_comment'></div>以大周天授二年太岁辛卯二月癸卯。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_74_1364556_comment'></div>启殡于东园。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_75_1364556_comment'></div>迁祔于洛州某原。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_76_1364556_comment'></div>礼也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_77_1364556_comment'></div>哀哉夫人。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_78_1364556_comment'></div>雅有高行。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_79_1364556_comment'></div>终而不忘。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_80_1364556_comment'></div>以为厚葬非礼也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_81_1364556_comment'></div>是以珠玉不饰。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_82_1364556_comment'></div>塼瓦是藏。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_83_1364556_comment'></div>高府君聿遵其志。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_84_1364556_comment'></div>率以薄葬。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_85_1364556_comment'></div>于戏。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_86_1364556_comment'></div>非古之明德淑女。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_87_1364556_comment'></div>金玉其光。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_88_1364556_comment'></div>何以跻之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_89_1364556_comment'></div>吾忝门闾之宾。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_90_1364556_comment'></div>睹其家道矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_91_1364556_comment'></div>雍穆<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_92_1364556", 1364556, "Clauses/92/Comments/0")'>懿铄</span>。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_92_1364556_comment'></div>实有清风。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_93_1364556_comment'></div>故叙之而未充德也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_94_1364556_comment'></div>铭曰。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_95_1364556_comment'></div></div><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_96_1364556'>夭夭桃李有华兮。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_96_1364556_comment'></div>灼灼淑人宜家兮。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_97_1364556_comment'></div>修睦妇道不哗兮。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_98_1364556_comment'></div>窈窕嫔仪孔嘉兮。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_99_1364556_comment'></div>荣采之方茂而云亡兮咨嗟。</div><div id='poem_sentence_100_1364556_comment'></div></div></div><div id='poem_1364570' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1364570' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1364570?labeling=true' target='_blank'>祭外姑宇文夫人文</a><span class='authorDate'>（691年2月）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 唐初 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(20887, "唐初", "陈子昂", "poem_title_1364570")'>陈子昂</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1364570_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1364570'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1364570'>维年月日朔。女夫某。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1364570_comment'></div>谨以清酌嘉蔬之奠。奉祭于故高氏河南宇文夫人之灵。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1364570_comment'></div>恭闻夫人有清穆之德。皓洁之行。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1364570_comment'></div>淳懿肃恭。内外仰则。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1364570_comment'></div>而遗风素范。蕙敷兰滋。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1364570_comment'></div>用能惠心光孚。氤氲沼沚。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1364570_comment'></div>崇严<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_6_1364570", 1364570, "Clauses/12/Comments/0")'>壸训</span>。芬郁母仪。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1364570_comment'></div>中馈柔嘉。娣姒有则。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1364570_comment'></div>岂图慈颜幽翳。于今十年。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1364570_comment'></div>毫水巳拱。尊灵廓然。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1364570_comment'></div>今吉辰协应。幽殡方开。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1364570_comment'></div>容象如在。器质巳灰。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1364570_comment'></div>改卜礼典。宅兆方迁。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1364570_comment'></div>山园既列。祖载行焉。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1364570_comment'></div>哀子号咷。女也<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_14_1364570", 1364570, "Clauses/29/Comments/0")'>蝉媛</span>。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1364570_comment'></div>终天永诀。泣血流涟。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1364570_comment'></div>某谬承嘉惠。预叨姻戚。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_16_1364570_comment'></div>生事早睽。送终空积。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_17_1364570_comment'></div>窃闻精意以享。黍稷非馨。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_18_1364570_comment'></div>敢陈薄酹。以献明灵。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_19_1364570_comment'></div>伏惟夫人。明神尚飨。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_20_1364570_comment'></div></div><div id='poem_sentence_21_1364570_comment'></div></div></div><div id='poem_1364555' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1364555' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1364555?labeling=true' target='_blank'>上殇高氏墓志铭</a><span class='authorDate'>（691年2月1日）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 唐初 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(20887, "唐初", "陈子昂", "poem_title_1364555")'>陈子昂</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1364555_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1364555'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1364555'>维唐垂拱二年太岁景戌七月二十日。殇子高氏卒。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1364555_comment'></div>呜呼哀哉。含琼敷而不玉实者有矣夫。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1364555_comment'></div>我观颢元机化出入。夭寿之数。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1364555_comment'></div>荣落之原。皆一受而不易者也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1364555_comment'></div>悲夫古人之仁懿中庸。不幸短命。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1364555_comment'></div>今复见之于高子矣。高子渤海蓨人也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1364555_comment'></div>黄州府君之幼孙。宛邱府君之叔子。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1364555_comment'></div>生而岐嶷。实覃实华。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1364555_comment'></div>越在襁褓。神明滋茂。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1364555_comment'></div>童蒙渊敏。光润玉颜。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1364555_comment'></div>八岁始教方书。受甲子。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1364555_comment'></div>巳知孝悌之道。诗礼之规。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1364555_comment'></div>宛邱府君钟爱之。他日。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1364555_comment'></div>尝趋庭与诸儿戏。神情涵泳。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1364555_comment'></div>绰然如鸿雏<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_14_1364555", 1364555, "Clauses/28/Comments/0")'>鹄子</span>。有青云之意也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1364555_comment'></div>府君美之曰。能光我家者此儿。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1364555_comment'></div>十五通左氏春秋及尚书。飞骞之志。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_16_1364555_comment'></div>日新宏大矣。不幸享年十七。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_17_1364555_comment'></div>遇暴疾而夭。呜呼哀哉。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_18_1364555_comment'></div>宛邱府君感恸。哀过于礼。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_19_1364555_comment'></div>曰。不恨尔寿之不长。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_20_1364555_comment'></div>惜尔器之不彰。夫何苗育。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_21_1364555_comment'></div>今也则亡。呜呼。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_22_1364555_comment'></div>吾将老矣。尔远何哉。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_23_1364555_comment'></div>其年七月。殡于家园。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_24_1364555_comment'></div>日月云徂。六载于兹矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_25_1364555_comment'></div>天授二年龙集辛卯。府君方大崇元域。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_26_1364555_comment'></div>以安先兆。诸子之柩皆祔焉。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_27_1364555_comment'></div>其年二月癸卯朔十八日庚申。启殡归瘗于大茔。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_28_1364555_comment'></div>礼也。铭曰。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_29_1364555_comment'></div></div><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_30_1364555'>来不可遏。去不可止。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_30_1364555_comment'></div>唯死与生。由生以死。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_31_1364555_comment'></div>于戏殇子。噫何往矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_32_1364555_comment'></div>伤慈父之肝情。独冥冥而长巳。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_33_1364555_comment'></div>死而有知可也。若其无知悲尔。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_34_1364555_comment'></div></div><div id='poem_sentence_35_1364555_comment'></div></div></div><div id='poem_1364569' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1364569' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1364569?labeling=true' target='_blank'>祭黄州高府君文</a><span class='authorDate'>（691年2月）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 唐初 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(20887, "唐初", "陈子昂", "poem_title_1364569")'>陈子昂</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1364569_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1364569'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1364569'>维年月日朔。孙女夫某等。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1364569_comment'></div>谨以清酌庶羞之奠。敢昭告于故黄州高府君之灵。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1364569_comment'></div>惟府君含德元亨。保和光大。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1364569_comment'></div>才堪济代。而运属承平。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1364569_comment'></div>器允登台。而命钟流落。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1364569_comment'></div>有瑚琏之宝。无廊庙之资。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1364569_comment'></div>岂图大位不跻。幽灵永昧。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1364569_comment'></div>尊仪潜翳。三十馀年。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1364569_comment'></div>元殡既开。黄肠已古。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1364569_comment'></div>今青乌改卜。丹旐来归。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1364569_comment'></div>窀穸即期。幽明永诀。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1364569_comment'></div>某等忝承嘉惠。奉事门阑。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1364569_comment'></div>兴言追慕。实增感咽。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1364569_comment'></div>窃惟精意以享。黍稷非馨。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1364569_comment'></div>敢陈薄酹。以献明灵。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1364569_comment'></div>呜呼哀哉。伏惟尚飨。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1364569_comment'></div></div><div id='poem_sentence_16_1364569_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=691&endYear=691')">691年</a>　居东都，守右卫胄曹参军。前曹州离孤高县丞卒，子昂为撰墓志。作品：《故宣议郎骑都尉行曹州离孤县丞高府君墓志铭》<div id='poem_1364557' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1364557' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1364557?labeling=true' target='_blank'>故宣议郎骑都尉行曹州离狐县丞高府君墓志铭</a><span class='authorDate'>（691年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 唐初 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(20887, "唐初", "陈子昂", "poem_title_1364557")'>陈子昂</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1364557_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1364557'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1364557'>君讳某。字某。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1364557_comment'></div>其先渤海蓨人也。因仕居洛。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1364557_comment'></div>今为阳翟人。昔赭鞭乘运。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1364557_comment'></div>袭炎帝之宗。苍兕应期。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1364557_comment'></div>承太公之允。崇勋霸业。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1364557_comment'></div>光烈犹存。曾祖某。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1364557_comment'></div>北齐太子中舍人。赠冀州刺史。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1364557_comment'></div>青宫近侍。光宠朝班。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1364557_comment'></div>皂盖追荣。恩崇国礼。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1364557_comment'></div>祖钦仁。隋左亲卫大都督检校秘书郎。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1364557_comment'></div>带七尺剑。始游天子之阶。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1364557_comment'></div>持三寸笔。终入芸香之阁。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1364557_comment'></div>父相。唐江州浔阳县令舒州怀宁县令。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1364557_comment'></div>弦歌之化。身不下堂。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1364557_comment'></div>神明之威。蝗犹避境。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1364557_comment'></div>君即怀宁府君之长子也。黄河一直。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1364557_comment'></div>青松万仞。性惟仁孝。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_16_1364557_comment'></div>行实温恭。文义必以润身。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_17_1364557_comment'></div>名节由其徇物。唐龙朔元年。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_18_1364557_comment'></div>有制举忠鲠。君对策及第。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_19_1364557_comment'></div>试永州湘源县尉。位卑黄绶。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_20_1364557_comment'></div>志在清规。秩满。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_21_1364557_comment'></div>以常调补凤州黄花县丞。梁竦长怀。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_22_1364557_comment'></div>尚劳州县。桓谭不乐。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_23_1364557_comment'></div>空负琴书。又转易州遂城县丞。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_24_1364557_comment'></div>以管辂之材。从赵典之任。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_25_1364557_comment'></div>古人斯在。君子居之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_26_1364557_comment'></div>大周革命。任曹州离狐县丞。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_27_1364557_comment'></div>而春秋已高。日月方出。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_28_1364557_comment'></div>武尽美矣。不得夷齐之臣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_29_1364557_comment'></div>文哉郁乎。自邈夏商之道。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_30_1364557_comment'></div>于是因阶秩满。<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_31_1364557", 1364557, "Clauses/63/Comments/0")'>告老</span>归闲。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_31_1364557_comment'></div>闭郊扉于南野。习岩居于东涧。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_32_1364557_comment'></div>诗书琴酒。以观先达之风。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_33_1364557_comment'></div>山水丘园。将为遗老之赏。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_34_1364557_comment'></div>天授二年岁在单阏七月二十二日。考终厥命。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_35_1364557_comment'></div>卒于陆浑县明高之山庄。时年七十有二。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_36_1364557_comment'></div>呜呼哀哉。君雅尚节义。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_37_1364557_comment'></div>素履元亨。怀古人之远图。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_38_1364557_comment'></div>慕先贤之遗烈。以为桓魋石椁。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_39_1364557_comment'></div>非则于礼经。墨翟桐棺。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_40_1364557_comment'></div>实宜于圣典。遗令薄葬。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_41_1364557_comment'></div>务取随时。即以其年十月日。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_42_1364557_comment'></div>葬于北邙山平乐之原。礼也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_43_1364557_comment'></div>嗣子思恭。孝思罔极。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_44_1364557_comment'></div>丧制过哀。思封树而缅怀。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_45_1364557_comment'></div>恐东西而不志。白楸为椁。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_46_1364557_comment'></div>奚遵古葬之仪。丹漆题封。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_47_1364557_comment'></div>即表永年之记。铭曰。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_48_1364557_comment'></div></div><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_49_1364557'>泱泱大风。其太公兮。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_49_1364557_comment'></div>穆穆君子。绍厥宗兮。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_50_1364557_comment'></div>忠鲠察廉。仕汉宫兮。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_51_1364557_comment'></div>才高位卑。考永终兮。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_52_1364557_comment'></div>哀哀孤子。号苍穹兮。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_53_1364557_comment'></div>归葬平陵。松柏桐兮。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_54_1364557_comment'></div></div><div id='poem_sentence_55_1364557_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=691&endYear=691')">691年</a>　居东都，守右卫胄曹参军。赋诗讥傅游艺辈以符瑞谄谀而至相位旋致身死国笑者。作品：《感遇 其二十四》<div id='poem_34692' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_34692' id='poem_sentence_4_1364531_comment'></div>明月琴樽。即对西园之赏。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1364531_comment'></div>鄙人幽介。酒醴知惭。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1364457_comment'></div>天听自我人听。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1364457_comment'></div>故尧臣放命。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1364457_comment'></div>降震怒之灾。<div id='poem_sentence_6_1364457_comment'></div>先王所以恭畏上下。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1364457_comment'></div>祇奉天人。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1364457_comment'></div>于是有昭德塞违。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1364457_comment'></div>惩恶劝善。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1364457_comment'></div>所以明枉直。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1364457_comment'></div>正典刑。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1364457_comment'></div>一昨伏奉恩敕。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1364457_comment'></div>宣示司农卿宗晋卿所奏。<div id='poem_sentence_21_1364457_comment'></div>元感上恻。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_22_1364457_comment'></div>乃降明制。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_23_1364457_comment'></div>发德音。<div id='poem_sentence_1_1364483_comment'></div>特从放免。伏对恩命。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1364483_comment'></div>魂魄飞扬。中谢。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1364483_comment'></div>臣巴蜀微贱。名教未闻。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1364483_comment'></div>陛下降非常之恩。加不次之命。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1364483_comment'></div>拔臣草野。谬齿衣冠。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1364483_comment'></div>臣私门祖宗。幽显荣庆。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1364483_comment'></div>岂止微臣一身而巳。臣宜肃恭名节。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1364483_comment'></div>上答圣恩。不图误识凶人。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1364483_comment'></div>坐缘逆党。论臣罪累。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1364483_comment'></div>死有馀辜。肝脑涂地。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1364483_comment'></div>不足塞责。陛下宏慈育之典。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1364483_comment'></div>宽再宥之刑。矜臣草莱。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1364483_comment'></div>悯臣愚昧。特恕万死。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1364483_comment'></div>赐以再生。身首获全。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1364483_comment'></div>巳是非分。官服具在。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_16_1364483_comment'></div>臣何敢安。臣若贪冒宠私。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_17_1364483_comment'></div>腼颜恩造。复尘旧职。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_18_1364483_comment'></div>以玷清猷。蝼蚁微心。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_19_1364483_comment'></div>实惭面目。臣伏见西有未宾之虏。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_20_1364483_comment'></div>北有逆命之戎。尚稽天诛。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_21_1364483_comment'></div>未息边戌。臣请束身塞上。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_22_1364483_comment'></div>奋命贼庭。效一卒之力。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_23_1364483_comment'></div>答再生之施。庶陛下威命。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_24_1364483_comment'></div>绥服荒夷。愚臣罪戾。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_25_1364483_comment'></div>时补万一。若臣获死锋镝。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_26_1364483_comment'></div>为厉犬羊。古人结草。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_27_1364483_comment'></div>实臣恳愿。不胜大造再生荷戴之至。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_28_1364483_comment'></div></div><div id='poem_sentence_29_1364483_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=695&endYear=695')">695年</a>　居东都，守右后遗。故友韦君卒，子昂尚在狱中，及出狱，为文祭韦君。作品：《祭临海韦府君文》<div id='poem_1364571' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1364571' id='poem_sentence_1_1364571_comment'></div>谨以少牢清酌之奠。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1364571_comment'></div>致祭故人临海韦君之灵。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1364571_comment'></div>惟君孝友自天。<div id='poem_sentence_6_1364571_comment'></div>怀轨物之量。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1364571_comment'></div>甘心苦节。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1364571_comment'></div>风雨不改。<div id='poem_sentence_1_1364535_comment'></div>琴酒管弦。未穷欢于<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_2_1364535", 1364535, "Clauses/5/Comments/0")'>永夕</span>。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1364535_comment'></div>何功曹旧州耆老。迹尚于沈冥。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1364535_comment'></div>李录事吾土贤豪。义多于游侠。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1364535_comment'></div>高轩置酒。甲第迎宾。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1364535_comment'></div>丝竹纷于绮窗。琅玕盛于雕俎。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1364535_comment'></div>楼台若画。临故国之城池。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1364535_comment'></div>轩盖如云。总名都之车马。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_84_1364549_comment'></div>云栖穷林今五纪。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_85_1364549_comment'></div>圣人以万机为贵。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_86_1364549_comment'></div>而我以天下为累。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_87_1364549_comment'></div>圣人以大宝为尊。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_88_1364549_comment'></div>而我以天下为烦。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_96_1364549_comment'></div>斋心洁意缅相望。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_97_1364549_comment'></div>祈问玉真及玉皇。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_98_1364549_comment'></div>何以得之受天昌。<div </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(20887, "唐初", "陈子昂", "poem_title_1364538")'>陈子昂</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1364538_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1364538'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1364538'>盖北夷不羁之日久矣。天子垂元默。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1364538_comment'></div>穆皇风。而狼居革心。<div id='poem_sentence_5_1364538_comment'></div>不踰青春。复命<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_6_1364538", 1364538, "Clauses/13/Comments/0")'>紫阙</span>。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1364538_comment'></div>其忠臣烈夫之节。感激壮矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1364538_comment'></div>朝廷以赴此绝国。追送近郊。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1364538_comment'></div>登熊山。望燕塞。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1364538_comment'></div>黄云千里。亭皋悠然。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1364538_comment'></div>佥曰赋诗。绝句以赠。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1364538_comment'></div></div><div id='poem_sentence_12_1364538_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=696&endYear=696')">696年7月</a>　居东都，守右拾遗。七月，著作郎崔融、比部郎中唐奉一、考功员外郎李迥秀等从梁王武三思东征，子昂于祖宴赋诗相送。作品：《送著作郎崔融等从梁五东征并序》<div id='poem_34677' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_34677' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/34677?labeling=true' target='_blank'>送著作佐郎崔融等从梁王东征</a><span class='authorDate'>（696年7月）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 唐初 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(20887, "唐初", "陈子昂", "poem_title_34677")'>陈子昂</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'>五言律诗</div></div><div id='poem_title_34677_comment'></div><div class='titleComment' id='poem_preface_34677'>古者凉风至，白露下，天子命将帅，训甲兵，将以外威荒戎，内辑中夏，时义远矣。自我大君受命，百蛮蚁伏，匈奴舍蒲萄之宫，越尝重翡翠之贡，虎符不发，象译攸同，实欲高议灵台，偃兵天下（偃伯天下），而林胡遗孽，渎乱边氓，驱蚊蚋之师，忽雷霆之伐，乃窃海裔，弄燕陲，皇帝哀北鄙之人，罹齐辛螫，以东征之义，降彼偏裨，犹恐威令未孚，亭塞仍梗，乃谋元帅，命佐军，得朱邸之天人，乃黄阁之元老。庙堂授钺，凿门申命，建梁国之旌旗，吟汉庭之箫鼓，东向而拜，北道长驱，蜺旄羽骑之殿，戈翻落日，突鬓蒙轮之勇，剑决浮云。方且猎九都，穷踏顿，存肃慎，吊姑馀，彷徨赤山，巡御日域，以昭我王师，恭天讨也。岁七月，军出国门，天晶无云，朔风清海，时比部郎中唐奉一、考功员外郎李回秀、著作佐郎崔融并参帷幕之宾，掌书记之任，燕南怅别，洛北思欢，顿旌节而少留，倾朝廷而出饯，永昌丞房思玄，衣冠之秀，乃张蕙圃，席兰堂，环曲榭，罗羽觞，写中京之望。纵候庭之赏，尔乃投壶习射，博弈观兵，镗金铙，忧瑶琴，歌易水之慷慨，奏关山以徘徊，颓阳半林，微阴出座，思长风以破浪，恐白日之蹉跎，酒中乐酣，拔剑起舞，则以气横辽碣，志扫獯戎，赋诗以赠。</div><div id='poem_preface_34677_comment'></div><div class='titleComment' id='poem_allusion_34677'><span class='label'>引用典故：</span><span class='link' onclick='ShowAllusionComment(986, ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=696&endYear=696')">696年</a>　居东都，守右拾遗。昭夷子赵贞固卒，京外故友共稽旧行，子昂秉翰，作碑颂。作品：《昭夷子赵氏碑》<span class='inlineComment2'>（徐谱考碑当作于是年九月陈子昂从武攸宜东征之前。）</span><div id='poem_1364550' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1364550' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1364550?labeling=true' target='_blank'>昭夷子赵氏碣颂</a><span class='authorDate'>（696年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 唐初 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(20887, "唐初", "陈子昂", "poem_title_1364550")'>陈子昂</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1364550_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1364550'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1364550'>昭夷子讳元亮<span class='inlineComment2'>（一无亮字）</span>。字贞固。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1364550_comment'></div>汲人也。本居河閒。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1364550_comment'></div>代为大儒。至祖掞。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1364550_comment'></div>尤博雅耽道。隋徵八学士。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1364550_comment'></div>与同郡刘焯俱至京师。补黎阳郡长。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1364550_comment'></div>始居汲焉。有二子。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1364550_comment'></div>礼舆礼辕。舆官至临颍县丞。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1364550_comment'></div>辕为校书郎。并著名当代。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1364550_comment'></div>昭夷即礼舆季子也。<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_8_1364550", 1364550, "Clauses/17/Comments/0")'>元精</span>冲懿。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1364550_comment'></div>有英雄之姿。学不常师。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1364550_comment'></div>志在遐远。年二十七。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1364550_comment'></div>褐衣游洛阳。天下<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_11_1364550", 1364550, "Clauses/23/Comments/0")'>名流</span>。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1364550_comment'></div>翕然宗仰。群蒙以初筮求我。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1364550_comment'></div>昭夷以元毂发机。故<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_13_1364550", 1364550, "Clauses/27/Comments/0")'>蓬居</span>穷巷。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1364550_comment'></div><span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_14_1364550", 1364550, "Clauses/28/Comments/0")'>轩冕</span><span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_14_1364550", 1364550, "Clauses/28/Comments/1")'>结辙</span>。时代议迫阨。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1364550_comment'></div>不容其高。乃屈身泥蟠。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1364550_comment'></div>求禄下位。为幽州宜禄县尉。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_16_1364550_comment'></div>到职逾岁。默然无言。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_17_1364550_comment'></div>唯采药弹琴咏尧舜而已。州将郡守。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_18_1364550_comment'></div>穆然承风。君之道标浩如也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_19_1364550_comment'></div>因巡田入陇山。见乌支丹穴。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_20_1364550_comment'></div>密有<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_21_1364550", 1364550, "Clauses/42/Comments/0")'>潜遁</span>之意。苍龙甲<span class='inlineComment2'>（一作丙）</span>申岁。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_21_1364550_comment'></div>在大梁遭命不造。发<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_22_1364550", 1364550, "Clauses/45/Comments/0")'>痟疾</span>而卒。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_22_1364550_comment'></div>时四<span class='inlineComment2'>（一作三）</span>十九。呜呼哀哉。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_23_1364550_comment'></div>天下士人闻之。知与不知。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_24_1364550_comment'></div>莫不为之垂涕。盖伤其有济时之量。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_25_1364550_comment'></div>而无长驻之年。夫上德道全。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_26_1364550_comment'></div>器无不顺。中庸以降。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_27_1364550_comment'></div>才好则偏。有张也之庄。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_28_1364550_comment'></div>无展也之道。好由也之勇。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_29_1364550_comment'></div>缅回也之仁。侈宰予之言。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_30_1364550_comment'></div>遗澹台之行。务端木之智。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_31_1364550_comment'></div>忘宁武之愚。或正而不奇。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_32_1364550_comment'></div>或达而过杂。君独五味足。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_33_1364550_comment'></div>六气和。通众贤之不兼。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_34_1364550_comment'></div>畅群才之大适。虽不至于圣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_35_1364550_comment'></div>道其殆庶乎。故人无閒言。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_36_1364550_comment'></div>物饱其义。吾尝论人事有十。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_37_1364550_comment'></div>君得其九。一不至者。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_38_1364550_comment'></div>命也夫。于戏。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_39_1364550_comment'></div>名闻天下。而不达于堂上。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_40_1364550_comment'></div>智周万物。而不适乎一人也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_41_1364550_comment'></div>其时欤。其事欤。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_42_1364550_comment'></div>君故人云居沙门释法成嵩山道士河内司马子微终南山人范阳卢藏用御史中丞钜鹿魏元忠监察御史吴郡陆馀庆秦州长史平昌孟诜雍州司功太原王适洛州参军西河宋之问安定主簿博陵崔璩。咸痛君中夭。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_43_1364550_comment'></div>鼎饪不实。百代祀德。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_44_1364550_comment'></div>故老或云。以为名者德之表。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_45_1364550_comment'></div>谥者行之迹。君囊括代道。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_46_1364550_comment'></div>位屯时艰。困乎臲卼。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_47_1364550_comment'></div>光景不耀。乃共稽骘旧行。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_48_1364550_comment'></div>考谥定名。问于元蓍。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_49_1364550_comment'></div>象曰明夷于昭夷。昔叹才位不兼。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_50_1364550_comment'></div>大运有数。尝哀时命。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_51_1364550_comment'></div>而作颂云。诸公以余从君之游最久。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_52_1364550_comment'></div>故秉翰参议。其颂曰。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_53_1364550_comment'></div></div><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_54_1364550'>天道宏运兮物各有时。匪时不生。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_54_1364550_comment'></div>匪运不成。昔者<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_55_1364550", 1364550, "Clauses/111/Comments/0")'>元精</span>回潏。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_55_1364550_comment'></div>阳九滔灾。大人感生。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_56_1364550_comment'></div>尧禹恢能。阴阳既和。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_57_1364550_comment'></div>元帝传家。五百数终。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_58_1364550_comment'></div>桀骜暴邪。子乙提运。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_59_1364550_comment'></div>水火革明。匪贤不昌。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_60_1364550_comment'></div>尹乃阿衡。六百运徂。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_61_1364550_comment'></div>受始淫狂。西伯考元。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_62_1364550_comment'></div>历在躬昌。匪雄不决。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_63_1364550_comment'></div>匪谋不臧。姜牙皓眉。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_64_1364550_comment'></div>实逢其良。投钓指麾。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_65_1364550_comment'></div>奄有八荒。周有天下。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_66_1364550_comment'></div>七百馀年。太公之后。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_67_1364550_comment'></div>不闻大贤。岂无仲尼。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_68_1364550_comment'></div>负道周旋。无势一挈。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_69_1364550_comment'></div>无土一廛。然则大运之所来。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_70_1364550_comment'></div>时哉时哉。时隘业隘。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_71_1364550_comment'></div>运巨功巨。苟非其时。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_72_1364550_comment'></div>草木为伍。昭夷作颂云尔。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_73_1364550_comment'></div>又尝著汲人嚜记。言变化之事。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_74_1364550_comment'></div>且曰请尔灵龟。永晏息乎浩初。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_75_1364550_comment'></div></div><div id='poem_sentence_76_1364550_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=696&endYear=696')">696年9月</a>　居东都，守右拾遗。五月，契丹李陷营州。九月，以同州刺史建安郡王武攸宜为右武威卫大将军，充清边道行军大总管，讨契丹。子昂以本官参谋。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=696&endYear=696')">696年9月</a>　参建安军幕。出师前，为建安王武攸宜草表，请罢募罪奴，稍宽兵期，募山东浮浪三万等事。作品：《上军国机要事》<div id='poem_1364498' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1364498' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1364498?labeling=true' target='_blank'>上军国机要事</a><span class='authorDate'>（696年9月）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 唐初 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(20887, "唐初", "陈子昂", "poem_title_1364498")'>陈子昂</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1364498_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1364498'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1364498'>臣窃闻宗怀昌等军失律者。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1364498_comment'></div>乃被逆贼诈造官军文牒。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1364498_comment'></div>诬召怀昌。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1364498_comment'></div>昌等<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_3_1364498", 1364498, "Clauses/3/Comments/0")'>颛愚</span>无备陷没。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1364498_comment'></div>今诸军败失。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1364498_comment'></div>东蕃固知。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1364498_comment'></div>然恐安东阻隔。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1364498_comment'></div>未审此诈。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1364498_comment'></div>国家若无私契与安东往来。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1364498_comment'></div>臣恐凶贼多端。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1364498_comment'></div>诈伪复设。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1364498_comment'></div>万一被其矫命。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1364498_comment'></div>更失其图。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1364498_comment'></div>乃是资长贼权。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1364498_comment'></div>没陷府城。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1364498_comment'></div>此固宜天恩巳应先有处分。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1364498_comment'></div>然臣愚见。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_16_1364498_comment'></div>不敢不言。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_17_1364498_comment'></div>又贼初胜。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_18_1364498_comment'></div>不即西侵者。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_19_1364498_comment'></div>深恐围略安东。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_20_1364498_comment'></div>以自全计。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_21_1364498_comment'></div>若安东被围略。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_22_1364498_comment'></div>则辽东以来。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_23_1364498_comment'></div>非国所制。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_24_1364498_comment'></div>伏乞天恩早为图之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_25_1364498_comment'></div>臣闻天子义兵不可以怒发。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_26_1364498_comment'></div>怒则众惧。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_27_1364498_comment'></div>急则人摇。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_28_1364498_comment'></div>人摇则贼得其势。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_29_1364498_comment'></div>故昔者圣人守静以制乱。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_30_1364498_comment'></div>持重以服奸。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_31_1364498_comment'></div>大义常存。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_32_1364498_comment'></div>人无疑惧。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_33_1364498_comment'></div>臣伏见恩制免天下罪人及募诸色奴充兵讨击者。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_34_1364498_comment'></div>是<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_35_1364498", 1364498, "Clauses/35/Comments/0")'>捷急</span>之计。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_35_1364498_comment'></div>非天子之兵。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_36_1364498_comment'></div>且比来刑狱久清。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_37_1364498_comment'></div>罪人全少。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_38_1364498_comment'></div>奴多怯弱。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_39_1364498_comment'></div>未惯征行。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_40_1364498_comment'></div>纵其募集。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_41_1364498_comment'></div>未足可用。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_42_1364498_comment'></div>况当今天下忠臣勇士。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_43_1364498_comment'></div>万分未用其一。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_44_1364498_comment'></div>契丹小孽。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_45_1364498_comment'></div>假命待诛。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_46_1364498_comment'></div>何劳免罪赎奴。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_47_1364498_comment'></div>损国大义。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_48_1364498_comment'></div>且陛下富有四海。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_49_1364498_comment'></div>一战未胜。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_50_1364498_comment'></div>遂即免罪募奴。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_51_1364498_comment'></div>若更有他虞。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_52_1364498_comment'></div>复何徵发。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_53_1364498_comment'></div>臣恐此不可威示天下。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_54_1364498_comment'></div>臣闻圣人制事。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_55_1364498_comment'></div>必理未萌。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_56_1364498_comment'></div>所以奸不敢谋。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_57_1364498_comment'></div>贼不得起。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_58_1364498_comment'></div>臣闻吐蕃近日将兵围瓜州。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_59_1364498_comment'></div>数日即退。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_60_1364498_comment'></div>或云此贼通使墨啜。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_61_1364498_comment'></div>恐瓜沙止遏。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_62_1364498_comment'></div>故以此兵送之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_63_1364498_comment'></div>臣虽未信。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_64_1364498_comment'></div>然惟国家比来勍敌。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_65_1364498_comment'></div>在此两蕃。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_66_1364498_comment'></div>至于契丹小丑。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_67_1364498_comment'></div>未足以比类。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_68_1364498_comment'></div>今国家为契丹大发河东道及六胡州绥延丹隰等州稽胡精兵。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_69_1364498_comment'></div>悉赴营州。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_70_1364498_comment'></div>而缘塞空虚。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_71_1364498_comment'></div>灵夏独立。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_72_1364498_comment'></div>今冰生河合。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_73_1364498_comment'></div>草秋马肥。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_74_1364498_comment'></div>秦中北据陇右。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_75_1364498_comment'></div>亦关东邻党。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_76_1364498_comment'></div>凶羯奸谋。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_77_1364498_comment'></div>觇知此隙。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_78_1364498_comment'></div>驱其丑类。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_79_1364498_comment'></div>大盗秦关。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_80_1364498_comment'></div>陇右马群。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_81_1364498_comment'></div>是国所宝。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_82_1364498_comment'></div>防备远策。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_83_1364498_comment'></div>良宜豫图。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_84_1364498_comment'></div>不可竭塞上之兵。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_85_1364498_comment'></div>使凶虏得计。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_86_1364498_comment'></div>伏愿详审。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_87_1364498_comment'></div>臣闻所养非所用。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_88_1364498_comment'></div>所用非所养。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_89_1364498_comment'></div>理家必弊。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_90_1364498_comment'></div>在国必危。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_91_1364498_comment'></div>故明君不畜无用之臣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_92_1364498_comment'></div>慈父不畜无益之子。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_93_1364498_comment'></div>今朝廷三品五品。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_94_1364498_comment'></div>受国宠荣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_95_1364498_comment'></div>天恩赏赐。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_96_1364498_comment'></div>府库虚耗。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_97_1364498_comment'></div>食人之禄。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_98_1364498_comment'></div>死人之事。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_99_1364498_comment'></div>恩养圣朝。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_100_1364498_comment'></div>甚矣厚矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_101_1364498_comment'></div>及边有小贼。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_102_1364498_comment'></div>则云无人驱使。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_103_1364498_comment'></div>又劳圣恩远访外人。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_104_1364498_comment'></div>外人先无宠禄。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_105_1364498_comment'></div>临难又不肯殉节。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_106_1364498_comment'></div>然则国之所养者总无用之臣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_107_1364498_comment'></div>朝之所遗者乃有用之士。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_108_1364498_comment'></div>今不收有用。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_109_1364498_comment'></div>厚养无用。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_110_1364498_comment'></div>欲令忠贤效力。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_111_1364498_comment'></div>凶贼灭亡。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_112_1364498_comment'></div>以臣愚见。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_113_1364498_comment'></div>理不可得。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_114_1364498_comment'></div>近者辽军张立遇等<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_115_1364498", 1364498, "Clauses/115/Comments/0")'>丧律</span>。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_115_1364498_comment'></div>实由内外不同心。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_116_1364498_comment'></div>宰相或卖国树恩。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_117_1364498_comment'></div>近臣或附势私谒。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_118_1364498_comment'></div>禄重者以拱默为智。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_119_1364498_comment'></div>任权者以<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_120_1364498", 1364498, "Clauses/120/Comments/0")'>倾巧</span>为贤。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_120_1364498_comment'></div>群居雷同以殉私为能。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_121_1364498_comment'></div>媚妻保子以奉国为愚。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_122_1364498_comment'></div>陛下又宽刑漏网。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_123_1364498_comment'></div>不循名实。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_124_1364498_comment'></div>遂令纲纪日废。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_125_1364498_comment'></div><span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_126_1364498", 1364498, "Clauses/126/Comments/0")'>奸宄</span>滋多。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_126_1364498_comment'></div>今国家第一要者。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_127_1364498_comment'></div>在稍宽兵期。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_128_1364498_comment'></div>山南淮南去幽州四千里。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_129_1364498_comment'></div>所司使十月上旬到。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_130_1364498_comment'></div>计日行百里。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_131_1364498_comment'></div>四十日方到。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_132_1364498_comment'></div>即今水雨如此。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_133_1364498_comment'></div>又徵符到彼未久。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_134_1364498_comment'></div>当日便发。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_135_1364498_comment'></div>犹不及期。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_136_1364498_comment'></div>况未便发。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_137_1364498_comment'></div>且日行不可百里。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_138_1364498_comment'></div>若违限者死。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_139_1364498_comment'></div>国有常刑。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_140_1364498_comment'></div>到不及期。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_141_1364498_comment'></div>惧罪逃散为贼。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_142_1364498_comment'></div>此更生一患。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_143_1364498_comment'></div>纵倍程<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_144_1364498", 1364498, "Clauses/144/Comments/0")'>趁期</span>。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_144_1364498_comment'></div>亦恐不及。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_145_1364498_comment'></div>若违不诛。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_146_1364498_comment'></div>则军不可统。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_147_1364498_comment'></div>若违必诛。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_148_1364498_comment'></div>则全众皆怨。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_149_1364498_comment'></div>况兵疲不堪用。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_150_1364498_comment'></div>吴广陈胜为盗由此。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_151_1364498_comment'></div>切急切急。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_152_1364498_comment'></div>即日江南淮南诸州租船数千艘。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_153_1364498_comment'></div>巳至巩洛。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_154_1364498_comment'></div>计有百馀万斛。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_155_1364498_comment'></div>所司便勒往幽州纳充军粮。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_156_1364498_comment'></div>其船夫多是客户游手隳业无赖杂色人。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_157_1364498_comment'></div>发家来时。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_158_1364498_comment'></div>唯作入都资料。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_159_1364498_comment'></div>今已到京。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_160_1364498_comment'></div>又勒往幽州。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_161_1364498_comment'></div>幽州去此二千馀里。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_162_1364498_comment'></div>还又二千馀里。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_163_1364498_comment'></div>方寒冰冻。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_164_1364498_comment'></div>一无资粮。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_165_1364498_comment'></div>国家更无优恤。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_166_1364498_comment'></div>但切勒<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_167_1364498", 1364498, "Clauses/167/Comments/0")'>赴限</span>。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_167_1364498_comment'></div>比闻<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_168_1364498", 1364498, "Clauses/168/Comments/0")'>丁夫</span>。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_168_1364498_comment'></div>皆甚愁叹。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_169_1364498_comment'></div>又诸州行纲。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_170_1364498_comment'></div>承前多僦向<span class='inlineComment2'>（一作勾）</span>至都籴纳。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_171_1364498_comment'></div>今傥有此类向沧瀛籴纳。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_172_1364498_comment'></div>则山东米必二百巳上。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_173_1364498_comment'></div>百姓必骚动。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_174_1364498_comment'></div>今国家不优恤。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_175_1364498_comment'></div>又无识事明了人检点勾当。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_176_1364498_comment'></div>知租米现在虚实。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_177_1364498_comment'></div>又未宣恩旨慰劳兵夫。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_178_1364498_comment'></div>惟切勒<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_179_1364498", 1364498, "Clauses/179/Comments/0")'>赴限</span>。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_179_1364498_comment'></div>倘在道逃亡。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_180_1364498_comment'></div>此粮有万一非意损失。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_181_1364498_comment'></div>则东军二十万众。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_182_1364498_comment'></div>坐自取败。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_183_1364498_comment'></div>为贼所图。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_184_1364498_comment'></div>切急切急。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_185_1364498_comment'></div>杨元感以此为乱。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_186_1364498_comment'></div>实军国大命。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_187_1364498_comment'></div>山东百姓。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_188_1364498_comment'></div>国家比以供军。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_189_1364498_comment'></div>矜不点募。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_190_1364498_comment'></div>近闻东军失利。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_191_1364498_comment'></div>山东人骄慢。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_192_1364498_comment'></div>乃谓国家怕其粗豪。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_193_1364498_comment'></div>不敢徵发。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_194_1364498_comment'></div>今街谈巷议。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_195_1364498_comment'></div>多有苟且之心。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_196_1364498_comment'></div>伺国瑕隙。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_197_1364498_comment'></div>颇摇风俗。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_198_1364498_comment'></div>国家大政。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_199_1364498_comment'></div>须人无二心。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_200_1364498_comment'></div>若纵怀二。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_201_1364498_comment'></div>奸乱必渐。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_202_1364498_comment'></div>臣伏思即日山东愚人。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_203_1364498_comment'></div>有亡命不事产业者。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_204_1364498_comment'></div>有游侠聚盗者。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_205_1364498_comment'></div>有奸豪强宗者。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_206_1364498_comment'></div>有交通州县造罪过者。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_207_1364498_comment'></div>如此等色。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_208_1364498_comment'></div>皆是<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_209_1364498", 1364498, "Clauses/209/Comments/0")'>奸雄</span>。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_209_1364498_comment'></div>国家又不以法制役之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_210_1364498_comment'></div>臣恐无赖子弟。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_211_1364498_comment'></div>暴横日广。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_212_1364498_comment'></div>上不为国法所制。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_213_1364498_comment'></div>下不为州县所羁。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_214_1364498_comment'></div>又不从军。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_215_1364498_comment'></div>又不守业。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_216_1364498_comment'></div>坐观成败。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_217_1364498_comment'></div>养其奸心。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_218_1364498_comment'></div>在于国家。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_219_1364498_comment'></div>甚非长计。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_220_1364498_comment'></div>以臣愚见。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_221_1364498_comment'></div>望降墨敕。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_222_1364498_comment'></div>使臣与州县相知。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_223_1364498_comment'></div>子细采访。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_224_1364498_comment'></div>有粗豪游侠亡命奸盗失业浮浪<span class='inlineComment2'>（一作漂食）</span>富族强宗者。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_225_1364498_comment'></div>并稍优与赐物。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_226_1364498_comment'></div>悉募从军。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_227_1364498_comment'></div>仍宣恩旨慰劳。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_228_1364498_comment'></div>以礼发遣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_229_1364498_comment'></div>若如此。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_230_1364498_comment'></div>则山东浮人。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_231_1364498_comment'></div>安于太山。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_232_1364498_comment'></div>一者以慑奸豪异心。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_233_1364498_comment'></div>二者得精兵讨贼。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_234_1364498_comment'></div>不须免奴稽胡等。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_235_1364498_comment'></div>又身既在军。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_236_1364498_comment'></div>则父兄子弟。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_237_1364498_comment'></div>自不敢为过。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_238_1364498_comment'></div>昔汉祖征山东。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_239_1364498_comment'></div>使萧何镇关中。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_240_1364498_comment'></div>汉军数败。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_241_1364498_comment'></div>萧何每发关中子弟以助汉军。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_242_1364498_comment'></div>三秦无盗乱之患。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_243_1364498_comment'></div>汉军有强雄之势。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_244_1364498_comment'></div>盖以此道是也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_245_1364498_comment'></div>夫乱群败众者。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_246_1364498_comment'></div>惟在<span onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_248_1364498", 1364498, "Clauses/248/Comments/0")'>奸雄</span>既羁。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_248_1364498_comment'></div>乱弊自息。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_249_1364498_comment'></div>伏乞圣慈早图之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_250_1364498_comment'></div>诗云。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_251_1364498_comment'></div>无纵诡随。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_252_1364498_comment'></div>式遏寇虐。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_253_1364498_comment'></div>紫袍绯袍绿袍金带牙笏告身金银器物等。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_254_1364498_comment'></div>即日军中巳集。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_255_1364498_comment'></div>入贼有期。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_256_1364498_comment'></div>臣欲募<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_257_1364498", 1364498, "Clauses/257/Comments/0")'>死士</span>三万人。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_257_1364498_comment'></div>长驱贼庭。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_258_1364498_comment'></div>一战扫定。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_259_1364498_comment'></div>军中未有高爵重赏。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_260_1364498_comment'></div>无以励勇使贪。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_261_1364498_comment'></div>伏望天恩赐给前件袍带告身器物二千事。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_262_1364498_comment'></div>庶以劝励士众。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_263_1364498_comment'></div>未敢虚用。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_264_1364498_comment'></div>比来将军不明赏罚。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_265_1364498_comment'></div>所以兵不齐心。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_266_1364498_comment'></div>今聚十五万众。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_267_1364498_comment'></div>戈甲粮饷。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_268_1364498_comment'></div>日费万金。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_269_1364498_comment'></div>不早克定。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_270_1364498_comment'></div>恐所费弥广。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_271_1364498_comment'></div>山东百姓。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_272_1364498_comment'></div>贫弊不可再役。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_273_1364498_comment'></div>特乞天恩允臣所请。</div><div id='poem_sentence_274_1364498_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=696&endYear=696')">696年9月</a>　从军东征，九月出师，子昂为建安王武攸宜撰誓从词。作品：《为建安王誓众词》<div id='poem_1364542' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1364542' class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1364542'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1364542'>诸总管部将旗长队正各听命。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1364542_comment'></div>夫圣人用兵。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1364542_comment'></div>以伐有罪。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1364542_comment'></div><span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_3_1364542", 1364542, "Clauses/3/Comments/0")'>奸慝</span>窃命。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1364542_comment'></div>戎夷不龚。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1364542_comment'></div>则必肆诸市朝。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1364542_comment'></div>大戮原野。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1364542_comment'></div>我皇周子毓万国。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1364542_comment'></div>宠绥百蛮。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1364542_comment'></div>遐荒戎狄。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1364542_comment'></div>莫不率职。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1364542_comment'></div>聚兵帅众。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1364542_comment'></div>非欲劳人。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1364542_comment'></div>盖逆不可纵。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1364542_comment'></div>乱不可长。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1364542_comment'></div>所以屈己推毂。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1364542_comment'></div>垂涕泣辜。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_16_1364542_comment'></div>诚恐苍生。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_17_1364542_comment'></div>颠坠涂炭。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_18_1364542_comment'></div>今契丹凶羯。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_19_1364542_comment'></div>敢乱天常。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_20_1364542_comment'></div>为封豕长蛇。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_21_1364542_comment'></div>荐食上国。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_22_1364542_comment'></div>玉帛皮币。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_23_1364542_comment'></div>弃而不贡。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_24_1364542_comment'></div>名器正朔。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_25_1364542_comment'></div>僭而有谋。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_26_1364542_comment'></div>乃将绐神虐人。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_27_1364542_comment'></div>暴殄天物。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_28_1364542_comment'></div>故皇帝命我。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_29_1364542_comment'></div>肃将王诛。<div id='poem_sentence_32_1364542_comment'></div>公等诸将。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_33_1364542_comment'></div>及士卒已上。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_34_1364542_comment'></div>须各严职事。<div
