id='poem_sentence_37_1364542_comment'></div>本为中国奴隶。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_38_1364542_comment'></div>昏狂不道。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_39_1364542_comment'></div>劳我师徒。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_40_1364542_comment'></div>今与公等及士卒。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_41_1364542_comment'></div>久勤干戈。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_42_1364542_comment'></div>冒犯霜露。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_43_1364542_comment'></div>夫四郊多垒。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_44_1364542_comment'></div>士大夫之耻。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_45_1364542_comment'></div>蕞尔凶狡。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_46_1364542_comment'></div>一钮可屠。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_47_1364542_comment'></div>况皇帝义兵。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_48_1364542_comment'></div>剋期诛剪。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_49_1364542_comment'></div>此犹太山压卵。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_50_1364542_comment'></div>鸿毛在炉。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_51_1364542_comment'></div>今日之伐。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_52_1364542_comment'></div>须如雷霆之震。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_53_1364542_comment'></div>虎豹之击。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_54_1364542_comment'></div>搴旗斩馘。<div ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=696&endYear=696')">696年9月</a>　从军东征，九月出师，子昂赋平叛报国壮志答朝臣相送。作品：《东征答朝臣相送》<div id='poem_34665' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_34665' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=697&endYear=698')">697-698年</a>，39-40岁</div><div id='5254d0d8609a43cf817334a18231de04' class='detail'><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=697&endYear=697')">697年8月</a>　班师归朝，守右拾遗。为河内王武懿宗、建安王武攸宜等撰为将士请功表。作品：《为河内王等论功表》<span class='inlineComment2'>（彭谱云表当作于七月凯旋之后。按：表作于凯旋途中或归朝之后未明，今按河内郡王武懿宗四月十八日出师，六月军至赵州闻契丹将至冀州，南遁相州。六月三十日契丹败亡，七月二十四日武懿宗已在朝因奏折河北从贼百姓事与拾遗王求礼庭争。事见《资治通鉴》卷二百零六。  又六月三十日契丹败亡，七月二十四日建安王武攸宜自幽州凯旋，当是班师启程之日，非归朝到达之日。子昂亦随武攸宜北还，班师途中不可能为不在一地之武懿宗武攸宜同撰论功表。故子昂作此表当为8月班师归朝之后，地点在洛阳。）</span><div id='poem_1364462' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1364462' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1364462?labeling=true' target='_blank'>为河内王等论军功表</a><span class='authorDate'>（697年8月）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 唐初 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(20887, "唐初", "陈子昂", "poem_title_1364462")'>陈子昂</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1364462_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1364462'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1364462'>右。金吾卫大将军兼检校洛州长史河内郡王臣懿宗加爵一等勋五转司宾卿兼羽林大将军建安郡王攸宜加爵一等勋七转臣某等言。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1364462_comment'></div>伏奉月日制书。录臣等在军微功。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1364462_comment'></div>特加前件勋封。嘉命聿至。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1364462_comment'></div>宠渥载优。伏对惭魂。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1364462_comment'></div>殒首颠越云云。臣闻古者名将。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1364462_comment'></div>先士卒而后身。故其功劝。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1364462_comment'></div>末世庸将。穷人力以宠巳。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1364462_comment'></div>故其政乖。然则箪醪投河。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1364462_comment'></div>三军告醉。刓印在手。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1364462_comment'></div>万夫以离。夫与众共功。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1364462_comment'></div>专巳独利。成败之理。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1364462_comment'></div>兴亡继焉。赏者国之大事。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1364462_comment'></div>故不可忽。日者林胡搆孽。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1364462_comment'></div>敢乱燕陲。陛下徵义兵。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1364462_comment'></div>诛不道。天下士庶。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1364462_comment'></div>焱集星驰。皆忘身忧国。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1364462_comment'></div>纾祸郤难。至于躬先矢石。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_16_1364462_comment'></div>血涂草莽。冒艰险。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_17_1364462_comment'></div>历寒温。气腾青云。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_18_1364462_comment'></div>精贯白日。诚亦勤矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_19_1364462_comment'></div>虽圣灵威武。逆虏自灭。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_20_1364462_comment'></div>然士卒戮力。亦尽其劳。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_21_1364462_comment'></div>今大功未酬。众议犹在。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_22_1364462_comment'></div>而臣等驽怯。猥加先封。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_23_1364462_comment'></div>臣等不能折冲虏廷。还师衽席。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_24_1364462_comment'></div>今坐加茅土之赐。以先将士之勤。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_25_1364462_comment'></div>使鹖冠虎臣。将何以劝。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_26_1364462_comment'></div>今战士留滞于外府。军吏咨嗟于<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_27_1364462", 1364462, "Clauses/55/Comments/0")'>下寮</span>。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_27_1364462_comment'></div>臣等胡颜。敢冒天造。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_28_1364462_comment'></div>夫赏一劝百。犹恐未孚。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_29_1364462_comment'></div>利一沮万。其弊谁救。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_30_1364462_comment'></div>爵命不可以招谤国章不可以假人。伏愿天光俯回。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_31_1364462_comment'></div>昭发军礼。请以臣等前件勋封。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_32_1364462_comment'></div>回受战●人及立功将士等。上以明国之大赏。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_33_1364462_comment'></div>下以雪臣等谬功。使人悦忘劳。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_34_1364462_comment'></div>士感知死。然后兵可训励。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_35_1364462_comment'></div>贼可<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_36_1364462", 1364462, "Clauses/72/Comments/0")'>诛屠</span>。此诚国之<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_36_1364462", 1364462, "Clauses/73/Comments/0")'>元经</span>。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_36_1364462_comment'></div>不可苟而利者。臣等不胜区区。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_37_1364462_comment'></div></div><div id='poem_sentence_38_1364462_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=697&endYear=697')">697年</a>　班师归朝，守右拾遗。金吾将军陈令英乞骸骨，子昂为撰请免官表。作品：《为金吾将军陈令英请免官表》<span class='inlineComment2'>（徐谱云表作于七月班师归朝之后。）</span><div id='poem_1364492' class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1364492_comment'></div>臣闻军政不臧。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1364492_comment'></div>春秋责帅。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1364492_comment'></div>故扬干之乱。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1364492_comment'></div>魏绛致戮。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1364492_comment'></div>所以国有明赏。<div class='inlineComment2'>（一作父子）</span>兄弟。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_19_1364492_comment'></div>一门五人。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_20_1364492_comment'></div>皆伏节<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_21_1364492", 1364492, "Clauses/21/Comments/0")'>尽忠</span>。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_21_1364492_comment'></div>身死王事。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_22_1364492_comment'></div>遂超臣不次。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_23_1364492_comment'></div>授原州都督。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_24_1364492_comment'></div>臣时年三十二<span class='inlineComment2'>（一作四十二）</span>。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_25_1364492_comment'></div>职兼五印。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_26_1364492_comment'></div>荣绝一时。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_27_1364492_comment'></div>阶缘此恩。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_28_1364492_comment'></div>累忝藩翰。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_29_1364492_comment'></div>持节统部。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_30_1364492_comment'></div>前后八州。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_31_1364492_comment'></div>皆居塞垣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_32_1364492_comment'></div>当贼冲要。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_33_1364492_comment'></div>国之重寄。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_34_1364492_comment'></div>莫与臣比。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_35_1364492_comment'></div>虽无长策。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_36_1364492_comment'></div>恤戎伏胡。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_37_1364492_comment'></div>恭守朝章。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_38_1364492_comment'></div>保完免失。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_39_1364492_comment'></div>属陛下大圣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_40_1364492_comment'></div>矜老容愚。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_41_1364492_comment'></div>不以臣驽怯。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_42_1364492_comment'></div>更加宠命。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_43_1364492_comment'></div>授以<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_44_1364492", 1364492, "Clauses/44/Comments/0")'>青紫</span>。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_44_1364492_comment'></div>遣督幽州。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_45_1364492_comment'></div>林胡搆凶。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_46_1364492_comment'></div>王师出讨。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_47_1364492_comment'></div>士马云集。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_48_1364492_comment'></div>军务<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_49_1364492", 1364492, "Clauses/49/Comments/0")'>星繁</span>。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_49_1364492_comment'></div>粮馈军甲。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_50_1364492_comment'></div>动以亿计。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_51_1364492_comment'></div>臣无田畴<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_52_1364492", 1364492, "Clauses/52/Comments/0")'>乡导</span>之策。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_52_1364492_comment'></div>又乏杜预度支之才。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_53_1364492_comment'></div>空竭疲驽。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_54_1364492_comment'></div>昼夜不息。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_55_1364492_comment'></div>以勤补拙。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_56_1364492_comment'></div>首尾三<span class='inlineComment2'>（一作二）</span>年。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_57_1364492_comment'></div>弥缝阙漏。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_58_1364492_comment'></div>幸无愆乏。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_59_1364492_comment'></div>张元遇等不谨师律。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_60_1364492_comment'></div>贼得乘机。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_61_1364492_comment'></div>遂敢长驱燕陲。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_62_1364492_comment'></div>深入赵际。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_63_1364492_comment'></div>臣又无李牧东胡之略。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_64_1364492_comment'></div>实愧吴起西河之守。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_65_1364492_comment'></div>使凶狡敚𣀮。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_66_1364492_comment'></div>遂扰边氓。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_67_1364492_comment'></div>论之国宪。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_68_1364492_comment'></div>合刎颈谢罪。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_69_1364492_comment'></div>陛下又不以臣为辜。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_70_1364492_comment'></div>更授清边军副大总管。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_71_1364492_comment'></div>五月恩制。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_72_1364492_comment'></div>六月到军。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_73_1364492_comment'></div>逆虏天亡。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_74_1364492_comment'></div>臣又无效。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_75_1364492_comment'></div>至于军功<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_76_1364492", 1364492, "Clauses/76/Comments/0")'>战籍</span>。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_76_1364492_comment'></div>叙勋定劳。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_77_1364492_comment'></div>副职日浅。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_78_1364492_comment'></div>未及精覆。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_79_1364492_comment'></div>大兵旋旆。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_80_1364492_comment'></div>王师献功。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_81_1364492_comment'></div>而汉庭将军。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_82_1364492_comment'></div>未闻辞第。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_83_1364492_comment'></div>云中太守。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_84_1364492_comment'></div>巳论增级。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_85_1364492_comment'></div>今乃窃功谬赏。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_86_1364492_comment'></div>有忝朝章。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_87_1364492_comment'></div>忠诚殉节。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_88_1364492_comment'></div>不昭国议。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_89_1364492_comment'></div>实由臣滥其职。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_90_1364492_comment'></div>任过其才。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_91_1364492_comment'></div>上不能允副圣心。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_92_1364492_comment'></div>中不能匡正<span class='link' id='poem_sentence_94_1364492_comment'></div>有紊军容。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_95_1364492_comment'></div>臣罪何逃。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_96_1364492_comment'></div>孰执其咎。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_97_1364492_comment'></div>伏愿乞赐骸骨。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_98_1364492_comment'></div>贬归私第。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_99_1364492_comment'></div>式清朝序。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_100_1364492_comment'></div>永睹<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_101_1364492", 1364492, "Clauses/101/Comments/0")'>师贞</span>。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_101_1364492_comment'></div>不胜待罪惶惧之至。</div><div id='poem_sentence_102_1364492_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=697&endYear=697')">697年</a>　居东都，守右拾遗。宴于左奉宸大夫薛曜山亭，子昂撰序。作品：《薛大夫山亭宴序》<span class='inlineComment2'>（徐谱云当作于归朝后八、九月间。）</span><div id='poem_1364532' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1364532' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1364532?labeling=true' target='_blank'>薛大夫山亭宴序</a><span class='authorDate'>（697年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 唐初 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(20887, "唐初", "陈子昂", "poem_title_1364532")'>陈子昂</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1364532_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1364532'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1364532'>夫贫贱之交而不可忘。珠玉满堂而不足贵。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1364532_comment'></div>闭门无事。对黄卷以终年。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1364532_comment'></div>高论不疲。逢故人而永夜。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1364532_comment'></div>薛大夫其人也。<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_3_1364532", 1364532, "Clauses/7/Comments/0")'>下官</span>昔承颜色。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1364532_comment'></div>早蒙车骑之知。晚接恩光。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1364532_comment'></div>不异平津之旧。蔡邕书史。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1364532_comment'></div>许以相资。张载文章。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1364532_comment'></div>见称于代。尔其华堂别业。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1364532_comment'></div>秀木清泉。去朝廷而不遥。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1364532_comment'></div>与江湖而自远。名流不杂。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1364532_comment'></div>既入芙蓉之池。君子有邻。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1364532_comment'></div>还得芝兰之室。披翠微而列坐。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1364532_comment'></div>左对青山。俯盘石而开襟。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1364532_comment'></div>右临<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_13_1364532", 1364532, "Clauses/26/Comments/0")'>澄水</span>。斟绿酒。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1364532_comment'></div>弄<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_14_1364532", 1364532, "Clauses/28/Comments/0")'>清弦</span>。索皓月而按歌。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1364532_comment'></div>追凉风而解带。谈高趣逸。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1364532_comment'></div>体静心闲。神眇眇而临云。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_16_1364532_comment'></div>思飘飘而遇物。林轩寂寞。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_17_1364532_comment'></div>星汉纵横。思欲垂汗漫而群游。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_18_1364532_comment'></div>与真精而合契。欢穷兴洽。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_19_1364532_comment'></div>乐往悲来。怅鸾鹤之不存。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_20_1364532_comment'></div>哀鹴鸠之久没。徘徊永叹。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_21_1364532_comment'></div>慷慨长怀。东方明而毕昴升。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_22_1364532_comment'></div>北阁曙而天云静。悲夫。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_23_1364532_comment'></div>向之所得。巳失于无何。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_24_1364532_comment'></div>今之所游。复羁于有物。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_25_1364532_comment'></div>诗言志也。可得闻乎。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_26_1364532_comment'></div></div><div id='poem_sentence_27_1364532_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=697&endYear=697')">697年10月</a>　居东都，守右拾遗。时张昌宗云得王子晋遗迹，子昂与薛稷为昌宗作《窅冥君古坟记铭》<div id='poem_1364541' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1364541' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1364541?labeling=true' target='_blank'>窅冥君古坟记铭序<span class='inlineComment2'>（为张昌宁作）</span></a><span class='authorDate'>（697年10月）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 唐初 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(20887, "唐初", "陈子昂", "poem_title_1364541")'>陈子昂</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1364541_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1364541'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1364541'>神功元年。龙集丁酉。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1364541_comment'></div>我有周金革道息。宝鼎功成。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1364541_comment'></div>朝廷大宁。天下无事。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1364541_comment'></div>皇帝受紫阳之道。延访玉京。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1364541_comment'></div>群臣从白云之游。载驰瑶水。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1364541_comment'></div>笙歌入至。元鹤飞来。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1364541_comment'></div>时余以银青光禄大夫忝在中侍。拥青旄之节。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1364541_comment'></div>陪翠鸾之旗。昔奉车子侯。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1364541_comment'></div>独随武帝。昌明为御。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1364541_comment'></div>每侍轩游。比之今日。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1364541_comment'></div>未足多幸。是时屡从严祀。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1364541_comment'></div>遥谒秘封。尝睹众灵如云。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1364541_comment'></div>群仙蔽日。乃仰感王子晋。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1364541_comment'></div>俯接浮邱公。行吹洞箫。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1364541_comment'></div>坐弄云凤。窃欲邀羽袂。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1364541_comment'></div>导鸾舆。求不死于金庭。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1364541_comment'></div>保长生于玉册。上以尊圣寿。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_16_1364541_comment'></div>下以息微躬。因登缑山。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_17_1364541_comment'></div>望少室。寻古灵迹。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_18_1364541_comment'></div>拟刻真容。得王子晋之遗墟。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_19_1364541_comment'></div>在永水之层曲。且欲开石室。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_20_1364541_comment'></div>营寿宫。<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_21_1364541", 1364541, "Clauses/43/Comments/0")'>庀徒</span>方兴。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_21_1364541_comment'></div>畚锸攸作。乃得古藏焉。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_22_1364541_comment'></div>其藏上无<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_23_1364541", 1364541, "Clauses/46/Comments/0")'>封壝</span>。内有甓瓦。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_23_1364541_comment'></div>南北长二丈二尺。东西阔八尺。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_24_1364541_comment'></div>中有古剑一。长尺馀。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_25_1364541_comment'></div>铜碗一。并瓦器二。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_26_1364541_comment'></div>其器文彩怪异。非虫篆雕斲所能拟也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_27_1364541_comment'></div>又有古五铢钱朱漆片数十枚。初开时文彩可见。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_28_1364541_comment'></div>及<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_29_1364541", 1364541, "Clauses/58/Comments/0")'>枨拨</span>之。应手灰灭。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_29_1364541_comment'></div>既无年代铭志。不知爵里官族。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_30_1364541_comment'></div>参验其事。已曾为人所开。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_31_1364541_comment'></div>于是抚之永怀。念昔增密。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_32_1364541_comment'></div>始知有形必弊。涉器则毁。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_33_1364541_comment'></div>钟鼎玉帛。非度世之资。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_34_1364541_comment'></div>名位宠章。为累真之府。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_35_1364541_comment'></div>未能独立物表。超世长存。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_36_1364541_comment'></div>与日月齐光。天地比寿。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_37_1364541_comment'></div>非天道乎。君窅窅冥冥。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_38_1364541_comment'></div>久幽珍藏。迨此昭发。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_39_1364541_comment'></div>岂不欲感示元契。奇畅灵期。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_40_1364541_comment'></div>昔<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_41_1364541", 1364541, "Clauses/82/Comments/0")'>王乔</span>古坟。惟留一剑。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_41_1364541_comment'></div>令威荒冢。又叹千年。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_42_1364541_comment'></div>起予道心在乎此。仰惟圣主仁慈。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_43_1364541_comment'></div>恩被草木。阳和<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_44_1364541", 1364541, "Clauses/89/Comments/0")'>掩骼</span>。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_44_1364541_comment'></div>既昭国典。至德埋胔。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_45_1364541_comment'></div>又在周令。今此藏亏露。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_46_1364541_comment'></div>诚感仁恻。谨历吉日。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_47_1364541_comment'></div>协良辰。即以其年十月甲子朔。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_48_1364541_comment'></div>具物备容。还定旧圹。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_49_1364541_comment'></div>豚鸡在奠。牺樽若歆。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_50_1364541_comment'></div>哀其铭志磨灭。姓位不显。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_51_1364541_comment'></div>乃锡之名曰窅冥君。其铭曰<span class='inlineComment2'>（铭入薛稷）</span>。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_52_1364541_comment'></div></div><div id='poem_sentence_53_1364541_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=698&endYear=698')">698年</a>　居东都，守右拾遗。寒食，于毕录事宅宴集，赋诗感时伤春，繁华不乐，归隐之志渐明。作品：《春台引》<div ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=698&endYear=698')">698年</a>　居东都，守右拾遗。子昂自东征归后，意绪索然，自觉仕隐失据，乃书无端帖自惜自嘲。作品：《无端帖》<span class='inlineComment2'>（按：徐谱云“帖约作于本年（神功元年697）冬”，未详何据。据文意当为子昂东征归后，意绪索然，自觉仕隐失据，自怨自惜自嘲，卧病洛阳，沉郁冷落之时所作，作于决意归隐之前，故系入圣历元年上表乞归之前，更为妥贴。）</span><br /><a href="javascript: id='poem_sentence_6_34747_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=698&endYear=698')">698年</a>　居东都，守右拾遗。赋诗言世俗工巧，既失望于世事，已有挂冠之意。作品：《感遇 其十》<span class='inlineComment2'>（按：徐谱据诗中“便便夸毗子，荣耀更相持”之语，以为是讥讽武攸东征无功而夸功邀荣，故系于神功元年秋冬。徐说未免牵强。析诗中之意，当为泛言世俗工巧，非指一事。既失望于道之不行，世事难为，故有挂冠之意。诗当作于上表乞归之前，故系此。）</span><div id='poem_34757' class='_poem'><div ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=698&endYear=698')">698年5月14日</a>　居官东都，守右拾遗。五月十四日上书，言废同昌军后，应选择都督，招纳逃户，整饬吏治等事。作品：《上蜀川安危事三条》<div id='poem_1364494' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1364494' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1364494?labeling=true' target='_blank'>上蜀川安危事<span class='inlineComment2'>（三条）</span><span style='margin: 0 0.5em'> 其二 </span></a><span class='authorDate'>（698年5月14日）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 唐初 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(20887, "唐初", "陈子昂", "poem_title_1364494")'>陈子昂</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1364494_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1364494'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1364494'>蜀中运粮既停。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1364494_comment'></div>百姓更无重役。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1364494_comment'></div>至于租庸。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1364494_comment'></div>合富府库。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1364494_comment'></div>今诸州逃走户有三万馀。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1364494_comment'></div>在蓬渠果合遂等州山林之中。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1364494_comment'></div>不属州县。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1364494_comment'></div>土豪大族。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1364494_comment'></div><span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_8_1364494", 1364494, "Clauses/8/Comments/0")'>阿隐</span>相容。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1364494_comment'></div>徵敛驱役。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1364494_comment'></div>皆入国用。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1364494_comment'></div>其中游手惰业<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_11_1364494", 1364494, "Clauses/11/Comments/0")'>亡命之徒</span>。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1364494_comment'></div>结为光火大贼。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1364494_comment'></div>依凭林险。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1364494_comment'></div>巢穴其中。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1364494_comment'></div>若以甲兵捕之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1364494_comment'></div>则乌散山谷。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_16_1364494_comment'></div>如州县怠慢。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_17_1364494_comment'></div>则劫杀公行。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_18_1364494_comment'></div>比来访闻。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_19_1364494_comment'></div>有人说逃在其中者。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_20_1364494_comment'></div>攻城劫县。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_21_1364494_comment'></div>徒众日多。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_22_1364494_comment'></div>诚可特降严加敕。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_23_1364494_comment'></div>令州县长官与使人设法大招此户。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_24_1364494_comment'></div>则劫贼徒党。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_25_1364494_comment'></div>自然除殄。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_26_1364494_comment'></div>其三万户租赋。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_27_1364494_comment'></div>即可富国。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_28_1364494_comment'></div>若纵而不括。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_29_1364494_comment'></div>以养贼徒。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_30_1364494_comment'></div>蜀川大弊。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_31_1364494_comment'></div>必是未息。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_32_1364494_comment'></div>天恩允此请。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_33_1364494_comment'></div>乞作<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_34_1364494", 1364494, "Clauses/34/Comments/0")'>条例</span>括法。</div><div id='poem_sentence_34_1364494_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=698&endYear=698')">698年</a>　居官东都，守右拾遗。乞归前夕，洛阳丞杜审言贬吉州司户，宋之问等四十五人赋诗相送，子昂为之序。作品：《送吉州杜司户审言序》<div id='poem_1364534' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1364534' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1364534?labeling=true' target='_blank'>送吉州杜司户审言序</a><span class='authorDate'>（698年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 唐初 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(20887, "唐初", "陈子昂", "poem_title_1364534")'>陈子昂</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1364534_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1364534'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1364534'>嗟夫。德则有邻。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1364534_comment'></div>才不必贵。昔有耕于岩石。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1364534_comment'></div>而名动京师。词感帝王。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1364534_comment'></div>乃位卑武骑。夫岂不遭昌运哉。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1364534_comment'></div>盖时命不齐。奇偶有数。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1364534_comment'></div>当用贤之世。贾谊窜于长沙。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1364534_comment'></div>居好文之朝。崔骃放于辽海。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1364534_comment'></div>况大圣提象。群臣守规。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1364534_comment'></div>杜司户<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_8_1364534", 1364534, "Clauses/16/Comments/0")'>炳灵</span>翰林。研几<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_8_1364534", 1364534, "Clauses/17/Comments/0")'>策府</span>。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1364534_comment'></div>有重名于天下。而独秀于朝端。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1364534_comment'></div>徐陈应刘。不得劘其垒。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1364534_comment'></div>何王沈谢。适足靡其旗。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1364534_comment'></div>而载笔下寮。三十馀载。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1364534_comment'></div>秉不羁之操。物莫同尘。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1364534_comment'></div>含<span class='inlineComment2'>（一作合）</span>绝唱之音。人皆寡和。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1364534_comment'></div>群公爱祢衡之俊。留在京师。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1364534_comment'></div>天子以桓谭之非。谪居外郡。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_16_1364534_comment'></div>苍龙阉茂。扁舟入吴。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_17_1364534_comment'></div>告别千秋之亭。回棹五湖之曲。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_18_1364534_comment'></div>朝廷相送。驻旌盖于城隅。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_19_1364534_comment'></div>之子孤游。森风帆于天际。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_20_1364534_comment'></div>白云自出。苍梧渐远。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_21_1364534_comment'></div>帝台半隐。坐隔丹霄。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_22_1364534_comment'></div>巴山一望。魂断绿木。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_23_1364534_comment'></div>于是邀白日。藉青蘋。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_24_1364534_comment'></div>追潇湘之游。寄洞庭之乐。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_25_1364534_comment'></div>吴歈楚舞。右琴左壶。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_26_1364534_comment'></div>将以缓燕客之心。慰越人之思。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_27_1364534_comment'></div>杜君乃挟琴起舞。抗首高歌。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_28_1364534_comment'></div>哀皓首而未遇。恐青春之蹉跎。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_29_1364534_comment'></div>且欲携幽兰。结芳桂。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_30_1364534_comment'></div>饮石泉以节味。咏商山以卒岁。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_31_1364534_comment'></div>返耕饵术。吾将老焉。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_32_1364534_comment'></div>群公嘉之。赋诗以赠。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_33_1364534_comment'></div>凡四十五人。具题爵里。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_34_1364534_comment'></div></div><div id='poem_sentence_35_1364534_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=698&endYear=698')">698年</a>　居官东都，守右拾遗。乞归前夕，病中与韦虚己书，告以命不可强，将归东山。作品：《与韦虚己书》<div id='poem_1364527' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1364527' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1364527?labeling=true' target='_blank'>与韦五虚已书</a><span class='authorDate'>（698年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 唐初 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(20887, "唐初", "陈子昂", "poem_title_1364527")'>陈子昂</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1364527_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1364527'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1364527'>命之不来也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1364527_comment'></div>圣人犹无可柰何。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1364527_comment'></div>况于贤者哉。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1364527_comment'></div>仆尝窃不自量。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1364527_comment'></div>谓以为得失在人。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1364527_comment'></div>欲揭闻见。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1364527_comment'></div>抗衡当代之士。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1364527_comment'></div>不知事有大谬。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1364527_comment'></div>异于此望者。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1364527_comment'></div>乃令人惭愧悔赧不自知。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1364527_comment'></div>大笑颠蹶。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1364527_comment'></div>怪其所以者尔。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1364527_comment'></div>虚已足下。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1364527_comment'></div>何可言邪。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1364527_comment'></div>夫道之将行也命也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1364527_comment'></div>道之将废也命也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1364527_comment'></div>子昂其如命何。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_16_1364527_comment'></div>雄笔雄笔。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_17_1364527_comment'></div>弃尔归吾东山。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_18_1364527_comment'></div>无汨我思。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_19_1364527_comment'></div>无乱我心。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_20_1364527_comment'></div>从此遁矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_21_1364527_comment'></div>属病不得面谈。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_22_1364527_comment'></div>书以述言。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_23_1364527_comment'></div>子昂白。</div><div id='poem_sentence_24_1364527_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=698&endYear=698')">698年</a>　居东都，守右拾遗。乞归前夕，赋诗送人出塞。作品：《送别出塞》<div id='poem_34743' id='poem_sentence_0_34743'>平生闻高义，书剑<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_0_34743", 34743, "Clauses/1/Comments/0")'>百夫雄</span>。<div id='poem_sentence_0_34743_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_1_34743'>言登青云去，非此白头翁。<div id='poem_sentence_1_34743_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_2_34743'>胡兵屯塞下，汉骑属<span class='inlineComment2'>（一作入）</span>云中。<div id='poem_sentence_2_34743_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_3_34743'>君为<span id='poem_sentence_4_34743'>单于不敢射，天子伫<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_4_34743", 34743, "Clauses/9/Comments/0")'>深功</span>。<div id='poem_sentence_4_34743_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_5_34743'>蜀山余方隐，良会何时同。<div id='poem_sentence_5_34743_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_6_34743'></div><div id='poem_sentence_6_34743_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=698&endYear=698')">698年</a>　居东都，守右拾遗。以父老，上表乞解官归侍，诏带官取给而归。<br /></div>

秭归

-----title
固原（平高）
-----detail
<div class='label1' id='c216ce5114cb47fa80912ffac1db76ab_label'><a href='javascript: DetailSwitch("c216ce5114cb47fa80912ffac1db76ab");'><span id='c216ce5114cb47fa80912ffac1db76ab_link' -----title
张掖
-----detail
<div class='label1' id='bf5b3f0b5f22450b87d3f52ad5c2663d_label'><a href='javascript: DetailSwitch("bf5b3f0b5f22450b87d3f52ad5c2663d");'><span id='bf5b3f0b5f22450b87d3f52ad5c2663d_link' class='switch'>—</span></a><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=686&endYear=686')">686年</a>，28岁</div><div id='bf5b3f0b5f22450b87d3f52ad5c2663d' class='detail'><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=686&endYear=686')">686年4月</a>　从军北征，四月军次张掖河，乔知之作《采玉篇》讥子昂误识药草，子昂作《荆玉篇》答之，并示王无竞。作品：《观荆玉篇并序》<span class='inlineComment2'>（王无竞（652-705），字仲烈，东莱人，仪凤二年举下笔成章科，授赵州栾城尉，历麟台正字，转右武卫仓曹参军、洛阳丞。累迁监察御史，垂拱二年，随乔知之征同罗、仆固，擢殿中侍御史，左迁太子舍人，预修《三教珠英》，神龙初，因诃诋权贵，出为苏州司马，后坐交张易之，再贬岭外，卒于广州。见孙逖《太子舍人王公墓志铭》、《旧唐书》卷一九○中、《新唐书》卷一○七本传。）</span><div id='poem_34736' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_34736' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/34736?labeling=true' target='_blank'>观荆玉篇</a><span class='authorDate'>（686年4月）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 唐初 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(20887, "唐初", "陈子昂", "poem_title_34736")'>陈子昂</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_34736_comment'></div><div class='titleComment' id='poem_preface_34736'>丙戌岁，余从左补阙乔公北征，夏四月，军幕次于张掖河（军幕舍于张掖河），河川草木，无他异者，惟有仙人杖，往往丛生。幽朔地寒，与中国稍异。予家世好服食，昔常饵之，乃此役也，而息意兹味。戍人有荐嘉蔬者，此物存焉。余倏尔而笑曰（余冁尔而笑曰）：「始者与此君别，不图至是而见之，岂非神明嘉惠，将欲扶吾寿也。」因为乔公昌言其能，实东莱王仲烈亦同旅舍，闻而大喜，甘心食之。已旬有五日矣，适有行人，自谓能知药者，谓乔公曰：「此白棘也。」公何谬哉！仲烈愕然而疑，亦曰：「吾怪其味甘（吾怪其味甜），今果如此。」乔公信是言，乃讥予，做《采玉篇》，谓宋人不识玉而宝王民石也。予心知必是，犹以独见之故，被夺于众人，乃喟然而叹曰：「嗟乎！人之大明者目也，心之至信者口也。夫目照五色，口分五味，玄黄甘苦，亦可断而不惑矣（亦何断而不惑矣），而路傍一议，二子增疑，况君臣之际，朋友之间乎？自是而观，则万物之情可见也。」感采玉咏，而做《观玉篇》以答之，并示仲烈，讥其失真也。</div><div id='poem_preface_34736_comment'></div><div class='titleComment' id='poem_allusion_34736'><span class='label'>引用典故：</span><span class='link' onclick='ShowAllusionComment(246, "poem_allusion_34736")'>三刖</span></div><div id='poem_allusion_34736_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_34736'><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_34736'>鸱夷双白玉，此玉有缁磷。<div id='poem_sentence_0_34736_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_1_34736'>悬之千金价，举世莫知真。<div id='poem_sentence_1_34736_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_2_34736'>丹青非异色，轻重有殊伦。<div id='poem_sentence_2_34736_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_3_34736", 34736, "Clauses/7/Comments/0")'>荆国</span>人。<div id='poem_sentence_3_34736_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_4_34736'></div><div id='poem_sentence_4_34736_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: -----title
额济纳旗（张掖）
-----detail
<div class='label1' id='8f8ccc361fe34a44a3958c9bad74b98b_label'><a href='javascript: DetailSwitch("8f8ccc361fe34a44a3958c9bad74b98b");'><span id='8f8ccc361fe34a44a3958c9bad74b98b_link' class='switch'>—</span></a><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=686&endYear=686')">686年</a>，28岁</div><div id='8f8ccc361fe34a44a3958c9bad74b98b' class='detail'><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=686&endYear=686')">686年</a>　从军北征，登塞上翁城，为文凭吊古之塞翁。作品：《吊塞上翁文》<span class='inlineComment2'>（按：陈文云“居延海南四百余里，有古城焉，土人云是塞上翁城。”居延海南四百余里，仍示出今内蒙古额济纳旗境内。）</span><div id='poem_1364566' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1364566' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1364566?labeling=true' target='_blank'>吊塞上翁文</a><span class='authorDate'>（686年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 唐初 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(20887, "唐初", "陈子昂", "poem_title_1364566")'>陈子昂</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1364566_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1364566'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1364566'>居延海南四百馀里。有古城焉。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1364566_comment'></div>土人云。是塞上翁城。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1364566_comment'></div>今为戍。其基扃<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_2_1364566", 1364566, "Clauses/5/Comments/0")'>趾迹</span>。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1364566_comment'></div>盖数千年也。丙戌岁兮。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1364566_comment'></div>我征匈奴。恭闻北叟。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1364566_comment'></div>托国此都。子尚于叟。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1364566_comment'></div>日月遐迈。及今来思。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1364566_comment'></div>实获心契。欣问于叟。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1364566_comment'></div>何德其愚。僻居幽漠。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1364566_comment'></div>浩与代殊。忘情逸马。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1364566_comment'></div>胡宁而知福。谢于邻人。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1364566_comment'></div>何达而不淑。丁男既存。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1364566_comment'></div>君子知复。人以为极也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1364566_comment'></div>伊怀兹土。既板且筑。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1364566_comment'></div>扃禁天崇。墉隍云矗。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1364566_comment'></div>今则荒秽。代亦不毓。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1364566_comment'></div>其故何哉。贤叟之德。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_16_1364566_comment'></div>登叟之堂。天道何远。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_17_1364566_comment'></div>而兹理茫茫。人代自故兮。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_18_1364566_comment'></div>邱垄崩荒。魂魄何独不归故乡。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_19_1364566_comment'></div>叟乎叟乎。我心之伤。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_20_1364566_comment'></div></div><div id='poem_sentence_21_1364566_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=686&endYear=686')">686年5月</a>　从军北征，五月师舍于同城，于古祠为军人画像作铭并序。作品：《燕然军人画像铭并序》<div id='poem_1364543' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1364543' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1364543?labeling=true' target='_blank'>燕然军人画像铭</a><span class='authorDate'>（686年5月）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 唐初 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(20887, "唐初", "陈子昂", "poem_title_1364543")'>陈子昂</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1364543_comment'></div><div class='titleComment' id='poem_preface_1364543'>龙集丙戌。有唐制匈奴五十六载。盖署其君长。以郡县畜之。荒服赖宁。古所莫记。是岁也。金微州都督仆固始桀骜惑乱其人。天子命左豹韬卫将军刘敬周发河西骑士。自居延海入以讨之。特敕左补阙乔知之摄侍御史护其军事。夏五月。师舍于同城。方绝大漠。以临浣海。君子曰。兵者凶器。仁者恶之。丑虏猖狂。厥自招咎。今至尊不得已而顺伐。尝闻西方之圣有能仁者。凶吉之业。各报以直。则使元恶授首。群氓不孤。兵无血刃。荒戎厎定。岂不在于大雄乎。诸将部校。佥曰允哉。将军乃饬躬率士卒。因古祠庙。图画形容。有古之弥勒像也。天人备容。丹青毕彩。盖以昭乎景福也。乃作铭曰。</div><div id='poem_preface_1364543_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1364543'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1364543'>耀天兵兮征荒服。绝云漠兮出元极。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1364543_comment'></div>白羽旆兮青云旗。箫鼓鸣兮士马悲。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1364543_comment'></div>愿左右兮浮屠道。备丹青兮妙天宝。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1364543_comment'></div>功既毕兮业既成。神之来兮福冥冥。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1364543_comment'></div></div><div id='poem_sentence_4_1364543_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=686&endYear=686')">686年</a>　从军北征，师舍于同城，乔知之因良谋难用，谗祸不测而心事重重，子昂登居延古城，赠诗以慰解。作品：《题居延古城赠乔十二知之》<div id='poem_34728' class='_poem'><div id='poem_sentence_7_1364464_comment'></div>零丁孤苦。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1364464_comment'></div>仅得成人。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1364464_comment'></div>老母悯臣孤蒙。<div id='poem_sentence_13_1364464_comment'></div>家贫无资。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1364464_comment'></div>纺绩以给束修。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1364464_comment'></div>衣褐并出母指。<div id='poem_sentence_51_1364464_comment'></div>最是良便。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_52_1364464_comment'></div>除此之际。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_53_1364464_comment'></div>未有剋期。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_54_1364464_comment'></div>臣谬齿王人。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_55_1364464_comment'></div>职在驱役。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_56_1364464_comment'></div>今岁奉使。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_57_1364464_comment'></div>巳至居延。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_58_1364464_comment'></div>单行虏庭。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_59_1364464_comment'></div>绝漠千里。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_60_1364464_comment'></div>臣虽万死。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_61_1364464_comment'></div>无答鸿恩。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_62_1364464_comment'></div>恐先朝露。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_63_1364464_comment'></div>有负眷知<span id='poem_sentence_66_1364464_comment'></div>哀臣孤苦。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_67_1364464_comment'></div>降鉴幽冥。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_68_1364464_comment'></div>使臣来年。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_69_1364464_comment'></div>得营葬具。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_70_1364464_comment'></div>斩草旧域。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_71_1364464_comment'></div>合骨先坟。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_72_1364464_comment'></div>保送羁魂。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_73_1364464_comment'></div>获申子道。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_74_1364464_comment'></div>乌鸟之志。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_75_1364464_comment'></div>获遂私情。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_76_1364464_comment'></div>迁窆事毕。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_77_1364464_comment'></div>驰影奔赴。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_78_1364464_comment'></div>虽即殒殁。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_79_1364464_comment'></div>廿心无憾。</div><div id='poem_sentence_80_1364464_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=686&endYear=686')">686年7月</a>　从军北征，在同城。为乔知之上表请击突厥。作品：《为乔补阙论突厥表》<div id='poem_1364463' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1364463' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1364463?labeling=true' target='_blank'>为乔补阙论突厥表</a><span class='authorDate'>（686年7月）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 唐初 · </span><a href='javascript: id='poem_content_1364463'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1364463'>臣某言。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1364463_comment'></div>臣以专蒙。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1364463_comment'></div>叨幸近侍。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1364463_comment'></div>陛下不以臣不肖。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1364463_comment'></div>特敕臣摄侍御史。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1364463_comment'></div><span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_5_1364463", 1364463, "Clauses/5/Comments/0")'>监护</span>燕然西军。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1364463_comment'></div>臣自违阙庭。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1364463_comment'></div>历涉秋夏。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1364463_comment'></div>徒居边徼。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1364463_comment'></div>无尺寸之功。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1364463_comment'></div>臣诚暗劣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1364463_comment'></div>孤负圣明。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1364463_comment'></div>然臣久在边隅。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1364463_comment'></div>夙夜勤灼。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1364463_comment'></div>莫不以蕃事为念。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1364463_comment'></div>俾按察之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1364463_comment'></div>比以突厥离乱事迹。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_16_1364463_comment'></div>参验委曲。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_17_1364463_comment'></div>穷问往来。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_18_1364463_comment'></div>窃有以得其真。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_19_1364463_comment'></div>莫不自为鲸鲵。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_20_1364463_comment'></div>递相吞食。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_21_1364463_comment'></div>流离残饿。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_22_1364463_comment'></div>莫知所归。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_23_1364463_comment'></div>臣诚愚不识事机。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_24_1364463_comment'></div>然窃以往古之变。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_25_1364463_comment'></div>考验于今。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_26_1364463_comment'></div>乃知天亡凶丑之时。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_27_1364463_comment'></div>陛下收功之日。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_28_1364463_comment'></div>然臣闻之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_29_1364463_comment'></div>难得易失者时也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_30_1364463_comment'></div>易遇难见者机也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_31_1364463_comment'></div>圣人所贵者。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_32_1364463_comment'></div>去祸于未萌。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_33_1364463_comment'></div>今陛下体上圣之资。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_34_1364463_comment'></div>开太平之化。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_35_1364463_comment'></div>匈奴为中国之患。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_36_1364463_comment'></div>自上代所苦久矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_37_1364463_comment'></div>合天降其灾。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_38_1364463_comment'></div>以授陛下。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_39_1364463_comment'></div>万代之业。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_40_1364463_comment'></div>在于今时。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_41_1364463_comment'></div>臣请以秦汉以来事迹證明之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_42_1364463_comment'></div>伏愿陛下少留圣听。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_43_1364463_comment'></div>寻绎省察。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_44_1364463_comment'></div>天下幸甚。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_45_1364463_comment'></div>臣闻始皇之时。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_46_1364463_comment'></div>并吞六国。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_47_1364463_comment'></div>制有天下。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_48_1364463_comment'></div>按剑叱咤。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_49_1364463_comment'></div>八荒奔驰。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_50_1364463_comment'></div>然匈奴彊梁。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_51_1364463_comment'></div>威不能服。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_52_1364463_comment'></div>牧马河内。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_53_1364463_comment'></div>以侵边疆。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_54_1364463_comment'></div>始皇赫然。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_55_1364463_comment'></div>使蒙恬将四十万众。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_56_1364463_comment'></div>北筑长城。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_57_1364463_comment'></div>因以逐胡。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_58_1364463_comment'></div>取其河南之地七百馀里。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_59_1364463_comment'></div>当时燕齐海岱。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_60_1364463_comment'></div>赢粮给费。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_61_1364463_comment'></div><span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_62_1364463", 1364463, "Clauses/62/Comments/0")'>徭役</span>烦苦。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_62_1364463_comment'></div>人以不堪。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_63_1364463_comment'></div>故长城未毕。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_64_1364463_comment'></div>而闾左之戌。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_65_1364463_comment'></div>巳为其患。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_66_1364463_comment'></div>二世而亡。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_67_1364463_comment'></div>莫不始于事胡也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_68_1364463_comment'></div>至汉兴。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_69_1364463_comment'></div>高祖受命。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_70_1364463_comment'></div>率群雄。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_71_1364463_comment'></div><span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_72_1364463", 1364463, "Clauses/72/Comments/0")'>乘利</span>便。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_72_1364463_comment'></div>以三十万众窘迫白登。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_73_1364463_comment'></div>七日被围。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_74_1364463_comment'></div>仅而获免。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_75_1364463_comment'></div>自是历吕太后至孝文帝。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_76_1364463_comment'></div>单于桀骜。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_77_1364463_comment'></div>益凌汉家。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_78_1364463_comment'></div>文帝徒以逊词。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_79_1364463_comment'></div>致献金帛。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_80_1364463_comment'></div>但求其善和而巳。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_81_1364463_comment'></div>不敢有图。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_82_1364463_comment'></div>贾谊所以哭之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_83_1364463_comment'></div>痛文帝以天下之盛。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_84_1364463_comment'></div>而卑事戎狄。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_85_1364463_comment'></div>以倒悬天下也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_86_1364463_comment'></div>至景帝时。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_87_1364463_comment'></div>边受其患。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_88_1364463_comment'></div>于是汉武践祚。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_89_1364463_comment'></div>以承六代鸿业。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_90_1364463_comment'></div>属乎文景元默之化。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_91_1364463_comment'></div>海内乂安。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_92_1364463_comment'></div>太仓之粟。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_93_1364463_comment'></div>红腐而不可食。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_94_1364463_comment'></div>内库之钱。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_95_1364463_comment'></div>贯朽而不可校。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_96_1364463_comment'></div>财力雄富。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_97_1364463_comment'></div>士马精彊。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_98_1364463_comment'></div>忿匈奴之骄慢。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_99_1364463_comment'></div>将报先帝之辱。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_100_1364463_comment'></div>遂使王恢韩安国将三十万众。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_101_1364463_comment'></div>以马邑诱单于。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_102_1364463_comment'></div>师出徒费。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_103_1364463_comment'></div>竟无毫发之功。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_104_1364463_comment'></div>于是大命六师。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_105_1364463_comment'></div>专以伐胡为务。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_106_1364463_comment'></div>首尾三十馀年。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_107_1364463_comment'></div>中国骚然。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_108_1364463_comment'></div>大受其弊。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_109_1364463_comment'></div>至于国用不足。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_110_1364463_comment'></div>军兴不给。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_111_1364463_comment'></div>租及六畜。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_112_1364463_comment'></div>算及船车。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_113_1364463_comment'></div>盗贼群兴。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_114_1364463_comment'></div>京师起乱。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_115_1364463_comment'></div>竟不能制单于之命。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_116_1364463_comment'></div>一日而臣服之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_117_1364463_comment'></div>汉宗衰残。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_118_1364463_comment'></div>几至覆社稷也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_119_1364463_comment'></div>故汉武晚年。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_120_1364463_comment'></div>厌兵革之弊。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_121_1364463_comment'></div>乃下哀痛之诏。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_122_1364463_comment'></div>罢轮台之游。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_123_1364463_comment'></div>封丞相为富民侯。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_124_1364463_comment'></div>将以苏中国也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_125_1364463_comment'></div>至宣帝代。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_126_1364463_comment'></div>罕复出师。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_127_1364463_comment'></div>属匈奴数穷。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_128_1364463_comment'></div>天降其祸。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_129_1364463_comment'></div>虚闾权渠单于病死。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_130_1364463_comment'></div>右贤王屠耆堂代立。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_131_1364463_comment'></div>骨肉大臣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_132_1364463_comment'></div>自不相服。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_133_1364463_comment'></div>又立虚闾权渠子为呼韩邪单于。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_134_1364463_comment'></div>击杀屠耆堂。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_135_1364463_comment'></div>诸名王贵人。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_136_1364463_comment'></div>各自分立为五单于。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_137_1364463_comment'></div>更相攻击。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_138_1364463_comment'></div>以至大乱。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_139_1364463_comment'></div>残虐死者。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_140_1364463_comment'></div>计万亿数。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_141_1364463_comment'></div>畜产耗减。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_142_1364463_comment'></div>十至八九。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_143_1364463_comment'></div>人以饥饿。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_144_1364463_comment'></div>相燔烧以求食。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_145_1364463_comment'></div>于是寄命无所。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_146_1364463_comment'></div>诸名王贵人右伊秩訾且渠当户以下。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_147_1364463_comment'></div>将兵五万。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_148_1364463_comment'></div>稽首来降。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_149_1364463_comment'></div>于北方晏然。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_150_1364463_comment'></div>靡有兵革之事。<div id='poem_sentence_153_1364463_comment'></div>臣窃以此观匈奴之形。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_154_1364463_comment'></div>察天时之变。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_155_1364463_comment'></div>盛衰存亡之机。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_156_1364463_comment'></div>事可见也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_157_1364463_comment'></div>然则匈奴不灭。<div id='poem_sentence_167_1364463_comment'></div>抚疮痍之人。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_168_1364463_comment'></div>不敢惕然有出师之意。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_169_1364463_comment'></div>然而未有<span id='poem_sentence_173_1364463_comment'></div>理乱有数。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_174_1364463_comment'></div>故曰圣人修备以待时。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_196_1364463_comment'></div>莫不一一臣所委察。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_197_1364463_comment'></div>比者归化。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_198_1364463_comment'></div>首尾相仍。<div id='poem_sentence_206_1364463_comment'></div>经今三年矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_207_1364463_comment'></div>野皆赤地。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_208_1364463_comment'></div>少有生草。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_209_1364463_comment'></div>以此羊马死耗。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_210_1364463_comment'></div>十至七八。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_218_1364463_comment'></div>或自相食。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_219_1364463_comment'></div>以活喉命。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_220_1364463_comment'></div>臣具<span class='inline' id='poem_sentence_240_1364463_comment'></div>行远图。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_241_1364463_comment'></div>大定北戎。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_274_1364463_comment'></div>德之大者。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_275_1364463_comment'></div>其何以加。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_276_1364463_comment'></div>若失此机。<div id='poem_sentence_279_1364463_comment'></div>独成千载之名。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_280_1364463_comment'></div>臣愚窃为陛下不取也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_281_1364463_comment'></div>伏见去月日敕。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_282_1364463_comment'></div>令同城权置安北都护府。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_289_1364463_comment'></div>制敌应变。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_290_1364463_comment'></div>未尝有遗。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_291_1364463_comment'></div>今陛下超然神鉴远照。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_292_1364463_comment'></div>实所谓圣明之见。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_293_1364463_comment'></div>睹于无形也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_294_1364463_comment'></div>臣比住同城。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_295_1364463_comment'></div>周观其地利。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_296_1364463_comment'></div>又博问谙知山川者。<div id='poem_sentence_299_1364463_comment'></div>皆是大碛。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_300_1364463_comment'></div>碛并石卤。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_301_1364463_comment'></div>水草不生。<div id='poem_sentence_325_1364463_comment'></div>可坐而取成。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_326_1364463_comment'></div>臣比来看国家兴兵。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_327_1364463_comment'></div>但循于常轨。<div 1364463, "Clauses/334/Comments/0")'>乘利</span>。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_334_1364463_comment'></div>轻于国威。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_335_1364463_comment'></div>兵愈出而事愈屈。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_336_1364463_comment'></div>盖是国家自过计于敌尔。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_337_1364463_comment'></div>故非小丑能有异图。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_340_1364463_comment'></div>但欲以今日之兵。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_341_1364463_comment'></div>今日之将。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_342_1364463_comment'></div>冀收功于异域。<div id='poem_sentence_349_1364463_comment'></div>小人非所敢谏。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_350_1364463_comment'></div>臣今监领后军某等。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_355_1364463_comment'></div>续以奏闻。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_356_1364463_comment'></div>伏愿陛下省臣此章。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_357_1364463_comment'></div>为国大计。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_358_1364463_comment'></div>傥万有可一中者。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_359_1364463_comment'></div>请与三事大夫熟图议之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_360_1364463_comment'></div>此亦万代一时也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_361_1364463_comment'></div>伏愿少留圣意。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_362_1364463_comment'></div>闲暇念之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_363_1364463_comment'></div>天下幸甚。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_364_1364463_comment'></div>陛下采臣刍荛。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_365_1364463_comment'></div>臣请执殳<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_366_1364463", 1364463, "Clauses/366/Comments/0")'>先驱</span>。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_366_1364463_comment'></div>为士卒<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_367_1364463", 1364463, "Clauses/367/Comments/0")'>启行</span>。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_367_1364463_comment'></div>横行匈奴之庭。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_368_1364463_comment'></div>归报陛下。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_369_1364463_comment'></div>臣死之日。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_370_1364463_comment'></div>庶无遗恨。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_371_1364463_comment'></div>不胜云云。</div><div id='poem_sentence_372_1364463_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=686&endYear=686')">686年7月</a>　从军北征，七月独南归，乔知之设帐饯别，作《拟古赠陈子昂》相送。<br /></div>
-----end

-----title
监利
-----detail
<div class='label1' id='ae4309b4ea074a5abc4c385386a90ea2_label'><a href='javascript: DetailSwitch("ae4309b4ea074a5abc4c385386a90ea2");'><span id='ae4309b4ea074a5abc4c385386a90ea2_link' class='switch'>—</span></a><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=694&endYear=694')">694年</a>，36岁</div><div id='ae4309b4ea074a5abc4c385386a90ea2' class='detail'><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=694&endYear=694')">694年</a>　服阕返都，过复州监利，望楚之高唐，发怀古之思。作品：《感遇 其二十八》<span class='inlineComment2'>（按：此诗彭谱云：“当是路过荆州（今）一带时所作”（《陈子昂诗注》48页），未详确系何地。今按：或为过湖北监利时所作。其一，诗云：“昔日章华宴，荆王乐荒淫”。章华，台名。《左传》昭公七年：“楚子成章华之台。”杜注：“台今在华容城内。”宋沈括《梦溪笔谈》卷四：“华容即今之监利县，非岳州之华容也，至今章华故台在县郭中，与杜预之说相符。”明清《监利县志》俱载章华台在县西北。“章台晓霁”被列为监利“容城八景”之一。验之今监利周老嘴镇（监利故县治）西3里天竺村有数平方公里古城址，散有大量秦汉以前砖块瓦砾，其地望与古籍章华台遗址大致相符。则楚灵王所营之离宫章华台，在今监利无疑，非其它歧说可比。  其二，诗云：“朅来高唐观 ,怅望云阳岑。”《文选·高唐赋序》：“昔者襄王与宋玉游于云梦之台，望高唐之观。”李善注：“《汉书音义》张揖曰：云梦，楚薮也，在南郡（荆州）华容（监利）县，其中有台馆。”《嘉庆重修一统志》：“四川夔州府：阳云台条：高唐观当在今荆州及汉阳境。”云阳岑，即阳云台，验之宋玉赋中“妾巫山之女也，为高唐之客，闻君游高唐……朝朝暮暮，阳台之下。旦朝视之，如言。”之语，知此云阳台、高唐观非今重庆巫山来鹤峰之“楚阳台”、“高唐观”也。   要之，“云梦之台”，“阳云台”，“楚阳台”“阳台”，实即章华台。高唐，或即章华台所在之古地名，高唐观，即章华台之台观建筑群。俱在今湖北监利。故子昂此诗，当作于返洛途中过监利时。）</span><div id='poem_34694' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_34694' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/34694?labeling=true' target='_blank'>感遇诗三十八首<span style='margin: 0 0.5em'> 其二十八 </span></a><span class='authorDate'>（694年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 唐初 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(20887, "唐初", "陈子昂", "poem_title_34694")'>陈子昂</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_34694_comment'></div><div class='titleComment' id='poem_allusion_34694'><span class='label'>引用典故：</span><span class='link' onclick='ShowAllusionComment(2370, "poem_allusion_34694")'>公子挟弹</span>　<span class='link' onclick='ShowAllusionComment(7651, "poem_allusion_34694")'>射兕云梦</span>　<span class='link' onclick='ShowAllusionComment(10515, "poem_allusion_34694")'>章华宴</span></div><div id='poem_allusion_34694_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_34694'><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_34694'>昔日<span class='link' onclick='ShowAllusionComment(10515, "poem_sentence_0_34694")'><span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_0_34694", 34694, "Clauses/0/Comments/1")'>章华</span>宴</span>，荆王乐荒淫。<div id='poem_sentence_0_34694_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_1_34694'>霓旌<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_1_34694", 34694, "Clauses/2/Comments/0")'>翠羽盖</span>，<span class='link' onclick='ShowAllusionComment(7651, "poem_sentence_1_34694")'>射兕云梦</span>林。<div id='poem_sentence_1_34694_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_2_34694'>朅来<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_2_34694", 34694, "Clauses/4/Comments/0")'>高唐观</span>，怅望云阳岑。<div id='poem_sentence_2_34694_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_3_34694'>雄图今何在，黄雀空哀吟。<div id='poem_sentence_3_34694_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' -----title
新乡
-----detail
<div class='label1' id='50926c5d68a2432ca9ce2a293c66c4a8_label'><a href='javascript: DetailSwitch("50926c5d68a2432ca9ce2a293c66c4a8");'><span id='50926c5d68a2432ca9ce2a293c66c4a8_link' class='switch'>—</span></a><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=696&endYear=696')">696年</a>，38岁</div><div id='50926c5d68a2432ca9ce2a293c66c4a8' class='detail'><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=696&endYear=696')">696年</a>　从军东征，次卫州新乡。先与出使天兵军之洛州参军宋之问约于新乡会面。及之问使还至新乡，子昂已先去，宋作《使往天兵军约与陈子昂新乡为期及还而不相遇》寄子昂。<br /></div>

<div class='label1' id='788a50c8289649fa91e795b8520e5222_label'><a href='javascript: DetailSwitch("788a50c8289649fa91e795b8520e5222");'><span id='788a50c8289649fa91e795b8520e5222_link' class='switch'>—</span></a><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=696&endYear=697')">696-697年</a>，38-39岁</div><div id='788a50c8289649fa91e795b8520e5222' class='detail'><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=696&endYear=696')">696年11月</a>　从军东征，次蓟城。著作郎崔融应召返洛，子昂赋蓟楼并序送融入都。作品：《登蓟城西北楼送崔著作融入都并序》<div id='poem_34685' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_34685' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/34685?labeling=true' target='_blank'>登蓟城西北楼送崔著作融入都</a><span class='authorDate'>（696年11月）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 唐初 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(20887, "唐初", "陈子昂", "poem_title_34685")'>陈子昂</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'>五言律诗</div></div><div id='poem_title_34685_comment'></div><div class='titleComment' id='poem_preface_34685'>仆尝倦游，伤别久矣，况登楼远国，衔酒故人，愤胡孽之侵边，从王师之出塞，元戎按甲，方刈鲜卑之垒，天子赐书，且有君相之召，而崔侯佩剑，即谒承明；群公负戈，方绝大漠；燕山北望，辽海东浮。云台与碣馆天殊，亭障共衣冠地隔，抚剑何道，长谣增叹，以身许国，我则当仁，论道匡君，子思报主，仲冬寒苦，幽朔初平。苍茫天兵之气，冥灭戎云之色，白羽一指，可扫九都。赤墀九重，伫观献凯，心期我愿斯遂。君恩共有（遂君之恩共有），策勋饮至，方同廊庙之欢；偃武櫜弓，借尔文儒之首。蓟丘故事，可以赠言，同赋登蓟楼送崔子云尔。</div><div id='poem_preface_34685_comment'></div><div class='titleComment' id='poem_allusion_34685'><span class='label'>引用典故：</span><span class='link' onclick='ShowAllusionComment(9048, "poem_allusion_34685")'>西南失朋</span></div><div id='poem_allusion_34685_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_34685'><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_34685'>蓟楼望燕国，负剑喜兹登。<div id='poem_sentence_0_34685_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_1_34685'>清规子方奏，单戟我无能。<div id='poem_sentence_1_34685_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_2_34685'>仲冬边风急，云汉复<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_2_34685", 34685, "Clauses/5/Comments/0")'>霜棱</span>。<div id='poem_sentence_2_34685_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_3_34685'>慷慨竟何道，西南恨失朋。<div id='poem_sentence_3_34685_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_4_34685'></div><div id='poem_sentence_4_34685_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=696&endYear=696')">696年</a>　在建安军幕，与安边使韩某唱酬。作品：《答韩使同在边》<span class='inlineComment2'>（按：子昂从武攸宜东征冬至蓟城后之行止履迹，考子昂诗文及《通鉴》可明大概。一月武攸宜与安东诸州刺史诸将约二月上旬六道并入（《为建安王与安东诸军州书》），二月与辽东都督高仇须约百道齐驱并海路东入（《为建安王与辽东书》），知此前武攸宜以幽州为大本营，大军一直未动。至三月一日方祭旗、兵发幽州（《祃牙文》），大军三月次渔阳，闻前军十数万已于十二日败亡硖石谷，三军震恐，不敢进。（事见《通鉴》卷二百零六。）武攸宜既不敢进，当仓惶退据幽州。验之《通鉴》又载契丹乘胜寇幽州，攸宜遣将击之不克，则知武攸宜大军在渔阳稍作停留即仓惶退据幽州无疑。四月六日硖石谷弃甲先遁之苏宏晖逃归，系狱之地在幽州（《谢衣表》），亦证幽州为武攸宜大本营，且此时大军已回幽州。此后大军与契丹在幽州相持直至六月三十日契丹在幽州败亡，孙万荣死潞水东（《通鉴》卷二百零六）。  要之，武攸宜行营自万岁通天元年冬至蓟城，即以幽州为大本营，除三月于渔阳作短暂停留外，其余皆在幽州，直至七月班师。陈子昂掌文书，随大军行止，履迹亦如是。）</span><div id='poem_34717' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_34717' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/34717?labeling=true' target='_blank'>答韩使同在边</a><span class='authorDate'>（696年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 唐初 · </span><a href='javascript: id='poem_content_34717'><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_34717'>汉家失中策，胡马屡南驱。<div id='poem_sentence_0_34717_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_1_34717'>闻诏安边使，曾是故人谟。<div id='poem_sentence_1_34717_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_2_34717'>废书怅怀古，负剑许<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_2_34717", 34717, "Clauses/5/Comments/0")'>良图</span>。<div id='poem_sentence_2_34717_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_3_34717'>出关岁方晏，乘障日多虞。<div id='poem_sentence_3_34717_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_4_34717'>虏入<span class='link' onclick='ShowAllusionComment(9581, "poem_sentence_4_34717")'>白登道</span>，烽交紫塞途。<div id='poem_sentence_4_34717_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_5_34717'>连兵屯北地，<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_5_34717", 34717, "Clauses/11/Comments/0")'>清野</span>备东胡。<div id='poem_sentence_5_34717_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_6_34717'>边城方晏闭，斥堠始昭苏。<div id='poem_sentence_6_34717_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_7_34717'>复闻韩长孺，辛苦事匈奴。<div id='poem_sentence_7_34717_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_8_34717'>雨雪颜容改，纵横才位孤。<div id='poem_sentence_8_34717_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_9_34717'>空怀老臣策，未获<span class='link' onclick='ShowAllusionComment(10540, "poem_sentence_9_34717")'>赵军租</span>。<div id='poem_sentence_9_34717_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_10_34717'>但蒙<span class='link' onclick='ShowAllusionComment(8738, "poem_sentence_10_34717")'>魏侯重</span>，不受谤书诬。<div id='poem_sentence_10_34717_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_11_34717'>当取<span class='link' onclick='ShowAllusionComment(4874, "poem_sentence_11_34717")'>金人祭</span>，还歌凯入都。<div id='poem_sentence_11_34717_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_12_34717'></div><div id='poem_sentence_12_34717_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=696&endYear=696')">696年</a>　在建安军幕，为军中草谢赐冬衣表。作品：《谢赐冬衣表》<span class='inlineComment2'>（按：子昂从武攸宜东征冬至蓟城后之行止履迹，考子昂诗文及《通鉴》可明大概。一月武攸宜与安东诸州刺史诸将约二月上旬六道并入（《为建安王与安东诸军州书》），二月与辽东都督高仇须约百道齐驱并海路东入（《为建安王与辽东书》），知此前武攸宜以幽州为大本营，大军一直未动。至三月一日方祭旗、兵发幽州（《祃牙文》），大军三月次渔阳，闻前军十数万已于十二日败亡硖石谷，三军震恐，不敢进。（事见《通鉴》卷二百零六。）武攸宜既不敢进，当仓惶退据幽州。验之《通鉴》又载契丹乘胜寇幽州，攸宜遣将击之不克，则知武攸宜大军在渔阳稍作停留即仓惶退据幽州无疑。四月六日硖石谷弃甲先遁之苏宏晖逃归，系狱之地在幽州（《谢衣表》），亦证幽州为武攸宜大本营，且此时大军已回幽州。此后大军与契丹在幽州相持直至六月三十日契丹在幽州败亡，孙万荣死潞水东（《通鉴》卷二百零六）。  要之，武攸宜行营自万岁通天元年冬至蓟城，即以幽州为大本营，除三月于渔阳作短暂停留外，其余皆在幽州，直至七月班师。陈子昂掌文书，随大军行止，履迹亦如是。）</span><div id='poem_1364476' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1364476' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1364476?labeling=true' target='_blank'>谢赐冬衣表</a><span class='authorDate'>（696年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 唐初 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(20887, "唐初", "陈子昂", "poem_title_1364476")'>陈子昂</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1364476_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1364476'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1364476'>臣某言。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1364476_comment'></div>中使某至。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1364476_comment'></div>伏奉某月日敕书。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1364476_comment'></div>慰问将士官吏僧道耆老等。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1364476_comment'></div>并赐臣手诏。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1364476_comment'></div>及冬衣两副。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1364476_comment'></div>大将等衣一十五副者。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1364476_comment'></div>天慈远致。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1364476_comment'></div>圣泽傍流。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1364476_comment'></div>海隅臣庶。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1364476_comment'></div>抃舞相庆。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1364476_comment'></div>臣某中谢。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1364476_comment'></div>伏维陛下道宏文武。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1364476_comment'></div>任切藩维。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1364476_comment'></div>远念戎旅之勤。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1364476_comment'></div>亟颁时节之赐。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1364476_comment'></div>臣以谬膺寄理。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_16_1364476_comment'></div>载涉炎凉。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_17_1364476_comment'></div>效绩无闻。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_18_1364476_comment'></div>负败将及。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_19_1364476_comment'></div>恩私每降。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_20_1364476_comment'></div>惭惧不宁。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_21_1364476_comment'></div>今又俯浃宸慈。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_22_1364476_comment'></div>曲延宠赉。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_23_1364476_comment'></div>当<span class='inline' id='poem_sentence_25_1364476_comment'></div>佳气集于城池。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_26_1364476_comment'></div>喜容生于草木。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_27_1364476_comment'></div>三军叶庆。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_28_1364476_comment'></div><span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_29_1364476", 1364476, "Clauses/29/Comments/0")'>万井</span>相欢。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_29_1364476_comment'></div>况臣荷宠逾涯。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_30_1364476_comment'></div>忝恩滋甚。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_31_1364476_comment'></div>萤烛无裨于景曜。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_32_1364476_comment'></div>畎浍徒愿于朝宗。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_33_1364476_comment'></div>悚踊遐方。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_34_1364476_comment'></div>感恋俱切。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_35_1364476_comment'></div>无任感恩荷惧屏营之至。</div><div id='poem_sentence_36_1364476_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=697&endYear=697')">697年1月</a>　在建安军幕。一月，为建安王武攸宜撰与安东诸军州书，约二月上旬互为掎角共破贼事。作品：《为建安王与安东诸军州书》<span class='inlineComment2'>（按：子昂从武攸宜东征冬至蓟城后之行止履迹，考子昂诗文及《通鉴》可明大概。一月武攸宜与安东诸州刺史诸将约二月上旬六道并入（《为建安王与安东诸军州书》），二月与辽东都督高仇须约百道齐驱并海路东入（《为建安王与辽东书》），知此前武攸宜以幽州为大本营，大军一直未动。至三月一日方祭旗、兵发幽州（《祃牙文》），大军三月次渔阳，闻前军十数万已于十二日败亡硖石谷，三军震恐，不敢进。（事见《通鉴》卷二百零六。）武攸宜既不敢进，当仓惶退据幽州。验之《通鉴》又载契丹乘胜寇幽州，攸宜遣将击之不克，则知武攸宜大军在渔阳稍作停留即仓惶退据幽州无疑。四月六日硖石谷弃甲先遁之苏宏晖逃归，系狱之地在幽州（《谢衣表》），亦证幽州为武攸宜大本营，且此时大军已回幽州。此后大军与契丹在幽州相持直至六月三十日契丹在幽州败亡，孙万荣死潞水东（《通鉴》卷二百零六）。  要之，武攸宜行营自万岁通天元年冬至蓟城，即以幽州为大本营，除三月于渔阳作短暂停留外，其余皆在幽州，直至七月班师。陈子昂掌文书，随大军行止，履迹亦如是。）</span><div id='poem_1364525' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1364525' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1364525?labeling=true' target='_blank'>为建安王与安东诸军州书</a><span class='authorDate'>（697年1月）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 唐初 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(20887, "唐初", "陈子昂", "poem_title_1364525")'>陈子昂</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1364525_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1364525'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1364525'>日月。清边道行军大总管建安郡王攸宜致书安东诸州刺史并诸将部校官属等。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1364525_comment'></div>初春犹寒。公等久统兵马。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1364525_comment'></div>勤国捍边。不至劳弊也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1364525_comment'></div>某如常。比贼中频有人出来。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1364525_comment'></div>异口同词。皆云逆贼李尽灭已死。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1364525_comment'></div>营州饥饿。人不聊生。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1364525_comment'></div>诸蕃首领百姓等。唯望官军。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1364525_comment'></div>即拟归顺。前后继至。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1364525_comment'></div>非止一人。某先使人向营州。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1364525_comment'></div>昨回。具得父老密状。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1364525_comment'></div>云贼势穷蹙。去正月上旬。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1364525_comment'></div>有妖星落孙万斩营中。其声如雷。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1364525_comment'></div>贼党离心。各以猜贰。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1364525_comment'></div>天殃如此。人事又然。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1364525_comment'></div>平殄凶渠。正在今日。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1364525_comment'></div>大军即以二月上旬。六道并入。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1364525_comment'></div>指期剋剪。同立大勋。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_16_1364525_comment'></div>请公等训励兵马。共为掎角。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_17_1364525_comment'></div>开国封侯。其机在此。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_18_1364525_comment'></div>幸各勉力。以图厥功。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_19_1364525_comment'></div>寻当更使人续往。先此<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_20_1364525", 1364525, "Clauses/41/Comments/0")'>不具</span>。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_20_1364525_comment'></div></div><div id='poem_sentence_21_1364525_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=697&endYear=697')">697年1月</a>　在建安军幕。一月，为建安王武攸宜撰答清边道总管王孝杰送俘虏获马等书。作品：《为建安王答王尚书送生口书》<span class='inlineComment2'>（按：子昂从武攸宜东征冬至蓟城后之行止履迹，考子昂诗文及《通鉴》可明大概。一月武攸宜与安东诸州刺史诸将约二月上旬六道并入（《为建安王与安东诸军州书》），二月与辽东都督高仇须约百道齐驱并海路东入（《为建安王与辽东书》），知此前武攸宜以幽州为大本营，大军一直未动。至三月一日方祭旗、兵发幽州（《祃牙文》），大军三月次渔阳，闻前军十数万已于十二日败亡硖石谷，三军震恐，不敢进。（事见《通鉴》卷二百零六。）武攸宜既不敢进，当仓惶退据幽州。验之《通鉴》又载契丹乘胜寇幽州，攸宜遣将击之不克，则知武攸宜大军在渔阳稍作停留即仓惶退据幽州无疑。四月六日硖石谷弃甲先遁之苏宏晖逃归，系狱之地在幽州（《谢衣表》），亦证幽州为武攸宜大本营，且此时大军已回幽州。此后大军与契丹在幽州相持直至六月三十日契丹在幽州败亡，孙万荣死潞水东（《通鉴》卷二百零六）。  要之，武攸宜行营自万岁通天元年冬至蓟城，即以幽州为大本营，除三月于渔阳作短暂停留外，其余皆在幽州，直至七月班师。陈子昂掌文书，随大军行止，履迹亦如是。）</span><div id='poem_1364523' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1364523' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1364523?labeling=true' target='_blank'>为建安王荅王尚书送生口书</a><span class='authorDate'>（697年1月）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 唐初 · </span><a href='javascript: id='poem_sentence_1_1364523_comment'></div>具如来状。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1364523_comment'></div>仰以欣快。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1364523_comment'></div>三军共之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1364523_comment'></div>狡寇逋诛。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1364523_comment'></div>此来擒馘。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1364523_comment'></div>师徒企踵。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1364523_comment'></div>争望先锋。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1364523_comment'></div>尚书远略英谋。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1364523_comment'></div>临机<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_10_1364523", 1364523, "Clauses/10/Comments/0")'>果断</span>。<div class='inline' "Clauses/12/Comments/0")'>枭首</span>伏辜。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1364523_comment'></div>在此诸军。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1364523_comment'></div>实增募勇。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_18_1364523_comment'></div>破竹之势。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_19_1364523_comment'></div>自此为阶。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_20_1364523_comment'></div>某方擐甲负戈。<div id='poem_sentence_28_1364523_comment'></div>裨将已下。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_29_1364523_comment'></div>各慰问之云云。</div><div id='poem_sentence_30_1364523_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a class='inlineComment2'>（按：子昂从武攸宜东征冬至蓟城后之行止履迹，考子昂诗文及《通鉴》可明大概。一月武攸宜与安东诸州刺史诸将约二月上旬六道并入（《为建安王与安东诸军州书》），二月与辽东都督高仇须约百道齐驱并海路东入（《为建安王与辽东书》），知此前武攸宜以幽州为大本营，大军一直未动。至三月一日方祭旗、兵发幽州（《祃牙文》），大军三月次渔阳，闻前军十数万已于十二日败亡硖石谷，三军震恐，不敢进。（事见《通鉴》卷二百零六。）武攸宜既不敢进，当仓惶退据幽州。验之《通鉴》又载契丹乘胜寇幽州，攸宜遣将击之不克，则知武攸宜大军在渔阳稍作停留即仓惶退据幽州无疑。四月六日硖石谷弃甲先遁之苏宏晖逃归，系狱之地在幽州（《谢衣表》），亦证幽州为武攸宜大本营，且此时大军已回幽州。此后大军与契丹在幽州相持直至六月三十日契丹在幽州败亡，孙万荣死潞水东（《通鉴》卷二百零六）。  要之，武攸宜行营自万岁通天元年冬至蓟城，即以幽州为大本营，除三月于渔阳作短暂停留外，其余皆在幽州，直至七月班师。陈子昂掌文书，随大军行止，履迹亦如是。）</span><div id='poem_1364524' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1364524' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a id='poem_sentence_1_1364524_comment'></div>非公等忠勇兼资。统率多算。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1364524_comment'></div>同心戮力。殉节忘躯。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1364524_comment'></div>以剋剪逋凶。扬国威武。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1364524_comment'></div>在此将士。闻公等殊战。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1364524_comment'></div>贼不当锋。莫不西望愤勇。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1364524_comment'></div>钦羡独剋。甚善甚善。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1364524_comment'></div>营州饥饿。人不聊生。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1364524_comment'></div>唯待官军。即拟归顺。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1364524_comment'></div>恨不得与诸公等共观诸将斩馘<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_14_1364524", 1364524, "Clauses/28/Comments/0")'>献俘</span>。旦夕严寒。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1364524_comment'></div>愿各休胜。契丹破了。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1364524_comment'></div>便望回兵。平殄默啜。<div class='inline'
