href='/Writing/1364522?labeling=true' target='_blank'>为建安王与辽东书</a><span class='authorDate'>（697年2月）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 唐初 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(20887, "唐初", "陈子昂", "poem_title_1364522")'>陈子昂</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1364522_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1364522'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1364522'>月日。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1364522_comment'></div>清边道大总管建安郡王攸宜致书于辽东州高都督蕃府。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1364522_comment'></div>贤甥某至。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1364522_comment'></div>仰知破逆贼孙万斩十有馀阵。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1364522_comment'></div>并生获夷贼一千人。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1364522_comment'></div>三军庆快。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1364522_comment'></div>万里同欢。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1364522_comment'></div>都督体英伟之才。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1364522_comment'></div>抱忠义之节。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1364522_comment'></div>遂能身先士卒。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1364522_comment'></div>为国讨雠。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1364522_comment'></div>以数百之兵。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1364522_comment'></div>当二万之寇。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1364522_comment'></div>指麾电扫。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1364522_comment'></div>逆党云销。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1364522_comment'></div>非都督智勇过人。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1364522_comment'></div>威名远振。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_16_1364522_comment'></div>谁能以少击众。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_17_1364522_comment'></div>陷丑摧凶。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_18_1364522_comment'></div>使国家无东顾之忧。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_19_1364522_comment'></div>是都督之力也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_20_1364522_comment'></div>贤甥俊酷似其舅。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_21_1364522_comment'></div>遂能与某等应机破敌。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_22_1364522_comment'></div>效节立功。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_23_1364522_comment'></div>此已各赏金带绯袍。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_24_1364522_comment'></div>薄荅诚效。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_25_1364522_comment'></div>更自录奏。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_26_1364522_comment'></div>拟加荣官。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_27_1364522_comment'></div>愿都督远知此意也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_28_1364522_comment'></div>今贼饥饿。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_29_1364522_comment'></div>灾舋日滋。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_30_1364522_comment'></div>天降其殃。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_31_1364522_comment'></div>尽灭已死。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_32_1364522_comment'></div>人厌其祸。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_33_1364522_comment'></div>万斩方诛。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_34_1364522_comment'></div>营州士人及城傍子弟。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_35_1364522_comment'></div>近送密款。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_36_1364522_comment'></div>准待官军。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_37_1364522_comment'></div>某令将蕃汉精兵四十万众剋取。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_38_1364522_comment'></div>某月日百道齐驱。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_39_1364522_comment'></div>分五万蕃汉精兵。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_40_1364522_comment'></div>令中郎将薛讷取海路东入。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_41_1364522_comment'></div>舟楫已具。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_42_1364522_comment'></div>来月亦发。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_43_1364522_comment'></div>请都督励兵秣马。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_44_1364522_comment'></div>以待此期。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_45_1364522_comment'></div>共登丸山。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_46_1364522_comment'></div>看殄凶虏。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_47_1364522_comment'></div>书勋竹帛。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_48_1364522_comment'></div>开国传家。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_49_1364522_comment'></div>是都督建功之日也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_50_1364522_comment'></div>中閒剋期同会。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_51_1364522_comment'></div>当更别使知闻。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_52_1364522_comment'></div>正属有军事。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_53_1364522_comment'></div>未能委曲。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_54_1364522_comment'></div>初春向暖。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_55_1364522_comment'></div>愿动静胜常。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_56_1364522_comment'></div><span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_57_1364522", 1364522, "Clauses/57/Comments/0")'>所是</span>都督官属及大首领并左右立功人等。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_57_1364522_comment'></div>并申此问。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_58_1364522_comment'></div>相见在近。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_59_1364522_comment'></div>豫以慰怀。</div><div id='poem_sentence_60_1364522_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=697&endYear=697')">697年2月</a>　在建安军幕。二月，前军总管王孝杰捕得投营白鼠，以为贼降之兆，书送中军。子昂为建安王草上奏表。作品：《奏白鼠表》<span class='inlineComment2'>（按：子昂从武攸宜东征冬至蓟城后之行止履迹，考子昂诗文及《通鉴》可明大概。一月武攸宜与安东诸州刺史诸将约二月上旬六道并入（《为建安王与安东诸军州书》），二月与辽东都督高仇须约百道齐驱并海路东入（《为建安王与辽东书》），知此前武攸宜以幽州为大本营，大军一直未动。至三月一日方祭旗、兵发幽州（《祃牙文》），大军三月次渔阳，闻前军十数万已于十二日败亡硖石谷，三军震恐，不敢进。（事见《通鉴》卷二百零六。）武攸宜既不敢进，当仓惶退据幽州。验之《通鉴》又载契丹乘胜寇幽州，攸宜遣将击之不克，则知武攸宜大军在渔阳稍作停留即仓惶退据幽州无疑。四月六日硖石谷弃甲先遁之苏宏晖逃归，系狱之地在幽州（《谢衣表》），亦证幽州为武攸宜大本营，且此时大军已回幽州。此后大军与契丹在幽州相持直至六月三十日契丹在幽州败亡，孙万荣死潞水东（《通鉴》卷二百零六）。  要之，武攸宜行营自万岁通天元年冬至蓟城，即以幽州为大本营，除三月于渔阳作短暂停留外，其余皆在幽州，直至七月班师。陈子昂掌文书，随大军行止，履迹亦如是。）</span><div id='poem_1364459' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1364459' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1364459?labeling=true' target='_blank'>奏白鼠表</a><span class='authorDate'>（697年2月）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 唐初 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(20887, "唐初", "陈子昂", "poem_title_1364459")'>陈子昂</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1364459_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1364459'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1364459'>臣某言。今月日。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1364459_comment'></div>臣等令中道前军总管王孝杰进军平州。十九日行次渔阳界。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1364459_comment'></div>昼有白鼠入营。孝杰捕得笼送者。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1364459_comment'></div>身如白雪。目似黄金。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1364459_comment'></div>顿首跧伏。帖若无气。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1364459_comment'></div>将士同见。皆谓贼降之徵。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1364459_comment'></div>臣闻鼠者坎精。孽胡之象。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1364459_comment'></div>穿窃为盗。凶贼之徒。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1364459_comment'></div>固合穴处野居。宵行昼伏。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1364459_comment'></div>今白日归命。素质伏辜。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1364459_comment'></div>天亡之徵。兆实先露。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1364459_comment'></div>自孝杰发后。再有贼中信来。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1364459_comment'></div>不谋同词。皆云尽灭病死。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1364459_comment'></div>亲离众溃。匪朝即夕。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1364459_comment'></div>臣训兵励勇。取乱侮亡。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1364459_comment'></div>昔宋剋鲜卑。苍鹅入幕。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1364459_comment'></div>今圣威远振。白鼠投营。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_16_1364459_comment'></div>休兆同符。实如灵契。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_17_1364459_comment'></div>凡在将士。孰不欢欣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_18_1364459_comment'></div>执馘献俘。期在不远。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_19_1364459_comment'></div></div><div id='poem_sentence_20_1364459_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=697&endYear=697')">697年2月</a>　在建安军幕。二月，前军总管王孝杰捕得投营白鼠，以为贼降之兆，书送中军，子昂为建安王撰回书。作品：《为建安王答王尚书》<span class='inlineComment2'>（按：子昂从武攸宜东征冬至蓟城后之行止履迹，考子昂诗文及《通鉴》可明大概。一月武攸宜与安东诸州刺史诸将约二月上旬六道并入（《为建安王与安东诸军州书》），二月与辽东都督高仇须约百道齐驱并海路东入（《为建安王与辽东书》），知此前武攸宜以幽州为大本营，大军一直未动。至三月一日方祭旗、兵发幽州（《祃牙文》），大军三月次渔阳，闻前军十数万已于十二日败亡硖石谷，三军震恐，不敢进。（事见《通鉴》卷二百零六。）武攸宜既不敢进，当仓惶退据幽州。验之《通鉴》又载契丹乘胜寇幽州，攸宜遣将击之不克，则知武攸宜大军在渔阳稍作停留即仓惶退据幽州无疑。四月六日硖石谷弃甲先遁之苏宏晖逃归，系狱之地在幽州（《谢衣表》），亦证幽州为武攸宜大本营，且此时大军已回幽州。此后大军与契丹在幽州相持直至六月三十日契丹在幽州败亡，孙万荣死潞水东（《通鉴》卷二百零六）。  要之，武攸宜行营自万岁通天元年冬至蓟城，即以幽州为大本营，除三月于渔阳作短暂停留外，其余皆在幽州，直至七月班师。陈子昂掌文书，随大军行止，履迹亦如是。）</span><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=697&endYear=697')">697年</a>　在建安军幕。武后赐厩马四匹，子昂为建安王武攸宜撰谢恩表。作品：《为建安王谢借马表》<span class='inlineComment2'>（按：子昂从武攸宜东征冬至蓟城后之行止履迹，考子昂诗文及《通鉴》可明大概。一月武攸宜与安东诸州刺史诸将约二月上旬六道并入（《为建安王与安东诸军州书》），二月与辽东都督高仇须约百道齐驱并海路东入（《为建安王与辽东书》），知此前武攸宜以幽州为大本营，大军一直未动。至三月一日方祭旗、兵发幽州（《祃牙文》），大军三月次渔阳，闻前军十数万已于十二日败亡硖石谷，三军震恐，不敢进。（事见《通鉴》卷二百零六。）武攸宜既不敢进，当仓惶退据幽州。验之《通鉴》又载契丹乘胜寇幽州，攸宜遣将击之不克，则知武攸宜大军在渔阳稍作停留即仓惶退据幽州无疑。四月六日硖石谷弃甲先遁之苏宏晖逃归，系狱之地在幽州（《谢衣表》），亦证幽州为武攸宜大本营，且此时大军已回幽州。此后大军与契丹在幽州相持直至六月三十日契丹在幽州败亡，孙万荣死潞水东（《通鉴》卷二百零六）。  要之，武攸宜行营自万岁通天元年冬至蓟城，即以幽州为大本营，除三月于渔阳作短暂停留外，其余皆在幽州，直至七月班师。陈子昂掌文书，随大军行止，履迹亦如是。）</span><div id='poem_1364477' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1364477' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1364477?labeling=true' target='_blank'>为建安王谢借马表</a><span class='authorDate'>（697年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 唐初 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(20887, "唐初", "陈子昂", "poem_title_1364477")'>陈子昂</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1364477_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1364477'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1364477'>臣攸宜言。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1364477_comment'></div>伏奉圣慈敕。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1364477_comment'></div>借臣厩马四匹。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1364477_comment'></div>星旗方列。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1364477_comment'></div>天马忽来。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1364477_comment'></div>祇拜恩荣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1364477_comment'></div>抃跃兼集。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1364477_comment'></div>臣名惭白马。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1364477_comment'></div>阵昧青龙。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1364477_comment'></div>徒凭庙胜之威。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1364477_comment'></div>窃总元戎之首。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1364477_comment'></div>皇师久露。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1364477_comment'></div>凶羯未孚。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1364477_comment'></div>方欲亲负干戈。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1364477_comment'></div>身先士卒。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1364477_comment'></div>金山深入。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1364477_comment'></div>期突厥之功。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_16_1364477_comment'></div><span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_17_1364477", 1364477, "Clauses/17/Comments/0")'>玉壶</span>遂临。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_17_1364477_comment'></div>叨得骏之赐。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_18_1364477_comment'></div>昔开东道。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_19_1364477_comment'></div>今见西来。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_20_1364477_comment'></div>感燕骨而长鸣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_21_1364477_comment'></div>君恩罔报。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_22_1364477_comment'></div>向朔云而骧首。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_23_1364477_comment'></div><span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_24_1364477", 1364477, "Clauses/24/Comments/0")'>蹋顿</span>方擒。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_24_1364477_comment'></div>坐驰千里。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_25_1364477_comment'></div>实愧三军。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_26_1364477_comment'></div>宠贵非图。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_27_1364477_comment'></div>荣多增惧。</div><div id='poem_sentence_28_1364477_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=697&endYear=697')">697年3月1日</a>　在建安军幕。三月一日，大军发幽州，祭旗，子昂为建安王武攸宜撰祃牙文。作品：《祃牙文》<span class='inlineComment2'>（按：子昂从武攸宜东征冬至蓟城后之行止履迹，考子昂诗文及《通鉴》可明大概。一月武攸宜与安东诸州刺史诸将约二月上旬六道并入（《为建安王与安东诸军州书》），二月与辽东都督高仇须约百道齐驱并海路东入（《为建安王与辽东书》），知此前武攸宜以幽州为大本营，大军一直未动。至三月一日方祭旗、兵发幽州（《祃牙文》），大军三月次渔阳，闻前军十数万已于十二日败亡硖石谷，三军震恐，不敢进。（事见《通鉴》卷二百零六。）武攸宜既不敢进，当仓惶退据幽州。验之《通鉴》又载契丹乘胜寇幽州，攸宜遣将击之不克，则知武攸宜大军在渔阳稍作停留即仓惶退据幽州无疑。四月六日硖石谷弃甲先遁之苏宏晖逃归，系狱之地在幽州（《谢衣表》），亦证幽州为武攸宜大本营，且此时大军已回幽州。此后大军与契丹在幽州相持直至六月三十日契丹在幽州败亡，孙万荣死潞水东（《通鉴》卷二百零六）。  要之，武攸宜行营自万岁通天元年冬至蓟城，即以幽州为大本营，除三月于渔阳作短暂停留外，其余皆在幽州，直至七月班师。陈子昂掌文书，随大军行止，履迹亦如是。）</span><div id='poem_1364563' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1364563' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1364563?labeling=true' target='_blank'>祃牙文</a><span class='authorDate'>（697年3月1日）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 唐初 · </span><a href='javascript: onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_1_1364563", 1364563, "Clauses/2/Comments/0")'>军牙</span>之神。盖先王作兵。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1364563_comment'></div>以讨有罪。奸慝窃命。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1364563_comment'></div>戎夷不龚。则必肆诸市朝。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1364563_comment'></div>大戮原野。我皇周子育万国。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1364563_comment'></div>宠绥百蛮。青云干吕。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1364563_comment'></div>白环入贡。久有年矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1364563_comment'></div>契丹凶羯。敢乱天常。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1364563_comment'></div>乃蜂聚丸山。豕食辽塞。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1364563_comment'></div><span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_9_1364563", 1364563, "Clauses/18/Comments/0")'>宴安鸩毒</span>。作为欃枪。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1364563_comment'></div>天厌其凶。国用致讨。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1364563_comment'></div>皇帝命我。肃将王诛。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1364563_comment'></div>今大军已集。吉辰协应。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1364563_comment'></div>旄头首建。羽旆前列。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1364563_comment'></div>夷貊咸威。将士听誓。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1364563_comment'></div>方俟天休命。为人殄灾。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1364563_comment'></div>惟尔有神。尚歼乃丑。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_16_1364563_comment'></div>召太一。会雷公。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_17_1364563_comment'></div>翼白虎。乘青龙。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_18_1364563_comment'></div>星流彗扫。永清朔裔。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_19_1364563_comment'></div>使兵不血刃。戎夏来同。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_20_1364563_comment'></div>以昭我天子之德。允乃神之功。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_21_1364563_comment'></div>岂非正直聪明哉。无纵大雠。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_22_1364563_comment'></div>以作神羞。急急如律令。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_23_1364563_comment'></div></div><div id='poem_sentence_24_1364563_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=697&endYear=697')">697年3月</a>　在建安军幕。三月，建安王武攸宜令中郎将薛讷分兵五万取海路东入，清边军海运度支大使虞部郎中王玄珪赢粮景从。子昂为王玄珪撰祭海神文。作品：《禜海文》<span class='inlineComment2'>（按：子昂从武攸宜东征冬至蓟城后之行止履迹，考子昂诗文及《通鉴》可明大概。一月武攸宜与安东诸州刺史诸将约二月上旬六道并入（《为建安王与安东诸军州书》），二月与辽东都督高仇须约百道齐驱并海路东入（《为建安王与辽东书》），知此前武攸宜以幽州为大本营，大军一直未动。至三月一日方祭旗、兵发幽州（《祃牙文》），大军三月次渔阳，闻前军十数万已于十二日败亡硖石谷，三军震恐，不敢进。（事见《通鉴》卷二百零六。）武攸宜既不敢进，当仓惶退据幽州。验之《通鉴》又载契丹乘胜寇幽州，攸宜遣将击之不克，则知武攸宜大军在渔阳稍作停留即仓惶退据幽州无疑。四月六日硖石谷弃甲先遁之苏宏晖逃归，系狱之地在幽州（《谢衣表》），亦证幽州为武攸宜大本营，且此时大军已回幽州。此后大军与契丹在幽州相持直至六月三十日契丹在幽州败亡，孙万荣死潞水东（《通鉴》卷二百零六）。 id='poem_sentence_16_1364564_comment'></div>楼船雾集。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_17_1364564_comment'></div>且欲浮碣石。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_18_1364564_comment'></div>淩方壶。<div href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=697&endYear=697')">697年</a>，39岁</div><div id='08d41ae5eec9436e983ebb3800145d4c' class='detail'><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=697&endYear=697')">697年</a>　在建安军幕。为建安王武攸宜撰祭故壮武将军左玉钤卫中候左三军营主苗君文。作品：《为建安王祭苗君文》<span class='inlineComment2'>（徐谱云此表当作于未捷之前。按：武攸宜大军三月次渔阳，闻前军十数万败亡硖石谷，三军震恐，不敢进。事见《通鉴》卷二百零六。当此之时，武攸宜当无余裕祭阵亡之苗君。武攸宜既不敢进，当仓惶退据幽州。验之《通鉴》又载契丹乘胜寇幽州，攸宜遣将击之不克，则知武攸宜大军在渔阳稍作停留即仓惶退据幽州无疑，其祭阵亡苗君之事，当在幽州与契丹相持之时。故定作此文之地在幽州。）</span><div id='poem_1364568' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1364568' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1364568?labeling=true' target='_blank'>为建安王祭苗君文</a><span href='/Writing/1364474?labeling=true' target='_blank'>为副大总管苏将军谢罪表</a><span class='authorDate'>（697年4月）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 唐初 · </span><a href='javascript: id='poem_sentence_15_1364474_comment'></div>臣妄以庸才。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_16_1364474_comment'></div>谬叨重任。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_17_1364474_comment'></div>不能深图远算。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_18_1364474_comment'></div>馘丑摧凶。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_19_1364474_comment'></div>以宣庙略之威。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_20_1364474_comment'></div>永息边人之患。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_21_1364474_comment'></div>属前军挫衄。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_22_1364474_comment'></div>士卒奔亡。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_23_1364474_comment'></div>臣复继驱驰。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_24_1364474_comment'></div>战斗交合。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_25_1364474_comment'></div>川谷地险。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_26_1364474_comment'></div>客主势殊。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_27_1364474_comment'></div>步马相悬。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_28_1364474_comment'></div>左右受敌。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_29_1364474_comment'></div>决命争死。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_30_1364474_comment'></div>力尽涂穷。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_31_1364474_comment'></div>遂以貔貅之师。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_32_1364474_comment'></div>衄于犬羊之众。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_33_1364474_comment'></div>诚宜刎首谢国。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_34_1364474_comment'></div>杀身报恩。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_35_1364474_comment'></div>陛下洪汤禹之仁。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_36_1364474_comment'></div>务宽大之典。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_37_1364474_comment'></div>愚臣同孟明之侣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_38_1364474_comment'></div>遂免严诛。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_39_1364474_comment'></div>白骨再荣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_40_1364474_comment'></div><span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_41_1364474", 1364474, "Clauses/41/Comments/0")'>丹慊</span>未泯。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_41_1364474_comment'></div>誓将枕戈尝胆。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_42_1364474_comment'></div>殄逆枭凶。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_43_1364474_comment'></div>躬为士卒之先。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_44_1364474_comment'></div>以雪殇魂之愤。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_45_1364474_comment'></div><span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_46_1364474", 1364474, "Clauses/46/Comments/0")'>肝脑涂地</span>。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_46_1364474_comment'></div>少答鸿私。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_47_1364474_comment'></div>不胜荷戴再生荣幸之至。</div><div id='poem_sentence_48_1364474_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=697&endYear=697')">697年4月</a>　在建安军幕。三月十二日，前军与契丹战于东硖石谷，王师败绩，王孝杰战死，苏宏晖弃甲先遁。太后遣使斩宏晖，使未至而宏晖已立功，因赦罪复官。子昂为其撰谢恩表。作品：《为副大总管屯营大将军苏宏晖谢表》<span class='inlineComment2'>（按：子昂从武攸宜东征冬至蓟城后之行止履迹，考子昂诗文及《通鉴》可明大概。一月武攸宜与安东诸州刺史诸将约二月上旬六道并入（《为建安王与安东诸军州书》），二月与辽东都督高仇须约百道齐驱并海路东入（《为建安王与辽东书》），知此前武攸宜以幽州为大本营，大军一直未动。至三月一日方祭旗、兵发幽州（《祃牙文》），大军三月次渔阳，闻前军十数万已于十二日败亡硖石谷，三军震恐，不敢进。（事见《通鉴》卷二百零六。）武攸宜既不敢进，当仓惶退据幽州。验之《通鉴》又载契丹乘胜寇幽州，攸宜遣将击之不克，则知武攸宜大军在渔阳稍作停留即仓惶退据幽州无疑。四月六日硖石谷弃甲先遁之苏宏晖逃归，系狱之地在幽州（《谢衣表》），亦证幽州为武攸宜大本营，且此时大军已回幽州。此后大军与契丹在幽州相持直至六月三十日契丹在幽州败亡，孙万荣死潞水东（《通鉴》卷二百零六）。  要之，武攸宜行营自万岁通天元年冬至蓟城，即以幽州为大本营，除三月于渔阳作短暂停留外，其余皆在幽州，直至七月班师。陈子昂掌文书，随大军行止，履迹亦如是。）</span><div id='poem_1364473' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1364473' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1364473?labeling=true' target='_blank'>为副大总管屯营大将军苏宏晖谢表</a><span class='authorDate'>（697年4月）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 唐初 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(20887, "唐初", "陈子昂", "poem_title_1364473")'>陈子昂</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1364473_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1364473'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1364473'>臣闻猃狁不恭。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1364473_comment'></div>周王致其大戮。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1364473_comment'></div>将军失律。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1364473_comment'></div>汉将被其严刑。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1364473_comment'></div>未有逆命骄天。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1364473_comment'></div>而逋舋鼓之罚。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1364473_comment'></div>亡师沮众。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1364473_comment'></div>遂宽<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_7_1364473", 1364473, "Clauses/7/Comments/0")'>载社</span>之诛。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1364473_comment'></div>伏惟天册金轮皇帝陛下肃恭上帝。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1364473_comment'></div>子育群生。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1364473_comment'></div>万国所以宅心。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1364473_comment'></div>百蛮由其屈膝。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1364473_comment'></div>而契丹凶狡。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1364473_comment'></div>敢窃陲边。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1364473_comment'></div>毒虐生灵。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1364473_comment'></div><span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_15_1364473", 1364473, "Clauses/15/Comments/0")'>暴殄天物</span>。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1364473_comment'></div>皇兵顺伐。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_16_1364473_comment'></div>仗仁义以共行。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_17_1364473_comment'></div>穷寇奸回。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_18_1364473_comment'></div>凭险阻而犹斗。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_19_1364473_comment'></div>臣等仁亏圣略。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_20_1364473_comment'></div>智昧<span class='link' id='poem_sentence_22_1364473_comment'></div>挫于犬羊之旅。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_23_1364473_comment'></div>诚合<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_24_1364473", 1364473, "Clauses/24/Comments/0")'>结缨</span>军垒。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_24_1364473_comment'></div>抵罪国章。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_25_1364473_comment'></div>陛下以尧舜深仁。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_26_1364473_comment'></div>且缓三苗之伐。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_27_1364473_comment'></div>禹汤罪巳。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_28_1364473_comment'></div>不与万方之辜。<div id='poem_sentence_30_1364473_comment'></div>更参授钺之任。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_31_1364473_comment'></div><span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_32_1364473", 1364473, "Clauses/32/Comments/0")'>死绥</span>之魄。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_32_1364473_comment'></div>复同挟纩之恩。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_33_1364473_comment'></div>四夷义以来苏。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_34_1364473_comment'></div>三军感而抃舞。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_35_1364473_comment'></div>痍疮再起。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_36_1364473_comment'></div>俘馘是图。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_37_1364473_comment'></div>将士同心。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_38_1364473_comment'></div>誓雪孟明之耻。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_39_1364473_comment'></div>殇魂共愤。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_40_1364473_comment'></div>思亢杜回之雠。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_41_1364473_comment'></div>臣等殉义忘生。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_42_1364473_comment'></div>报恩惟死。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_43_1364473_comment'></div>不任感激庆戴。</div><div id='poem_sentence_44_1364473_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=697&endYear=697')">697年4月</a>　在建安军幕。三月十二日，前军与契丹战于东硖石谷，王师败绩，王孝杰战死，苏宏晖弃甲先遁。太后遣使斩宏晖，使未至而宏晖已立功，因赦罪复官，赐衣勉之。子昂为其撰谢赐衣表。作品：《谢衣表》<span class='inlineComment2'>（按：子昂从武攸宜东征冬至蓟城后之行止履迹，考子昂诗文及《通鉴》可明大概。一月武攸宜与安东诸州刺史诸将约二月上旬六道并入（《为建安王与安东诸军州书》），二月与辽东都督高仇须约百道齐驱并海路东入（《为建安王与辽东书》），知此前武攸宜以幽州为大本营，大军一直未动。至三月一日方祭旗、兵发幽州（《祃牙文》），大军三月次渔阳，闻前军十数万已于十二日败亡硖石谷，三军震恐，不敢进。（事见《通鉴》卷二百零六。）武攸宜既不敢进，当仓惶退据幽州。验之《通鉴》又载契丹乘胜寇幽州，攸宜遣将击之不克，则知武攸宜大军在渔阳稍作停留即仓惶退据幽州无疑。四月六日硖石谷弃甲先遁之苏宏晖逃归，系狱之地在幽州（《谢衣表》），亦证幽州为武攸宜大本营，且此时大军已回幽州。此后大军与契丹在幽州相持直至六月三十日契丹在幽州败亡，孙万荣死潞水东（《通鉴》卷二百零六）。  要之，武攸宜行营自万岁通天元年冬至蓟城，即以幽州为大本营，除三月于渔阳作短暂停留外，其余皆在幽州，直至七月班师。陈子昂掌文书，随大军行止，履迹亦如是。）</span><div id='poem_1364475' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1364475' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1364475?labeling=true' target='_blank'>谢衣表</a><span class='authorDate'>（697年4月）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 唐初 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(20887, "唐初", "陈子昂", "poem_title_1364475")'>陈子昂</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1364475_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1364475'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1364475'>臣今月日。千骑田楷至。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1364475_comment'></div>伏奉恩敕。赐臣紫衫旱衫裤等一副。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1364475_comment'></div>臣万死骷骨。垂朽蒙荣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1364475_comment'></div>载战载殒。<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_3_1364475", 1364475, "Clauses/7/Comments/0")'>肝心涂地</span>。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1364475_comment'></div>中谢。臣以驽朽。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1364475_comment'></div>叨承重任。凭奉圣略。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1364475_comment'></div>诛讨元凶。实合震曜天威。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1364475_comment'></div>俘斩逆首。而智力浅短。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1364475_comment'></div>进退无规。被王孝杰陷锋于前。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1364475_comment'></div>臣则接战于后。躬先士卒。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1364475_comment'></div>苦斗山林。自辰至酉。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1364475_comment'></div>杀贼无数。嵓谷峻狭。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1364475_comment'></div>车乘相旋。被孝杰败兵。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1364475_comment'></div>回相冲突。逆贼乘便。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1364475_comment'></div>重袭臣军。士卒被伤。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1364475_comment'></div>子将多死。臣决命争首。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1364475_comment'></div>陷阵摧凶。日暮兵疲。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_16_1364475_comment'></div>疮痍相半。鸟散山谷。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_17_1364475_comment'></div>人无斗心。臣独无依。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_18_1364475_comment'></div>遂失师律。即欲刎颈阵下。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_19_1364475_comment'></div>委骨显诚。实恐身死尅伤。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_20_1364475_comment'></div>未雪国耻。所以含垢忍辱。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_21_1364475_comment'></div>图死阙庭。今月六日至幽州。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_22_1364475_comment'></div>即囚系狱户。延颈戢魄。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_23_1364475_comment'></div>惟待严刑。汤镬在前。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_24_1364475_comment'></div>分委灰土。岂谓天慈矜鉴。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_25_1364475_comment'></div>回宪增荣。以其<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_26_1364475", 1364475, "Clauses/53/Comments/0")'>伏锧</span>之魂。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_26_1364475_comment'></div>更辱赐衣之宠。烦冤踊跃。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_27_1364475_comment'></div>载兢载惶。泣血尝胆。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_28_1364475_comment'></div>誓复国雠。刻骨刻肌。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_29_1364475_comment'></div>敢忘天造。不胜巳死再生感戴欣跃之至。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_30_1364475_comment'></div></div><div id='poem_sentence_31_1364475_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=697&endYear=697')">697年</a>　在建安军幕。时前军相继陷没，三军震恐，子昂数谏而不纳，反遭黜降，徘徊郁结，因登蓟北楼，感燕昭乐毅之事，赋诗数首，寄终南隐居之卢藏用。作品：《蓟丘览古赠卢居士藏用七首并序》<span class='inlineComment2'>（卢藏用（？-713？）字子潜，行二，幽州范阳人。初举进士，不调，隐居终南、少室二山。长安中，召授左拾遗。神龙中，累转起居舍人，兼知制诰，俄迁中书舍人。景龙中，为吏部侍郎。又迁黄门侍郎、修文馆学士，转工部侍郎，迁尚书右丞。先天二年，因附太平公主，流岭南。改昭州司户参军，迁黔州长史，卒于始兴。《旧唐书·睿宗纪》谓坐太平公主、窦怀贞等谋逆时伏诛。年五十余。善属文，工书，好琴棋，与陈子昂、赵贞固友善，曾为陈子昂编集、撰序、作传。有《春秋后语》一○卷、《老子注》二卷、《庄子内外篇注》一二卷、《子书要略》一卷、文集三○卷，均已佚。《旧唐书》卷九四、《新唐书》卷一二三有传。参周祖譔《中国文学家大辞典》（唐五代卷）第126页卢藏用条。）</span><div id='poem_34660' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_34660' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/34660?labeling=true' target='_blank'>蓟丘览古赠卢居士藏用七首<span style='margin: 0 0.5em'> 其七 </span>郭隗<span class='inlineComment2'>（末缺）</span></a><span class='authorDate'>（697年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 唐初 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(20887, "唐初", "陈子昂", "poem_title_34660")'>陈子昂</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'>五言绝句</div></div><div id='poem_title_34660_comment'></div><div class='titleComment' id='poem_preface_34775'>丁酉岁，吾北征，出至蓟门，历观燕之旧都，其城池霸业，迹已芜没矣，乃慨然仰叹，忆昔乐生、邹子。群贤之游盛矣。因登蓟丘，作七诗以志之，寄终南卢居士，亦有轩辕之遗迹也。</div><div id='poem_preface_34775_comment'></div><div class='titleComment' id='poem_sentence_1_34770_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_2_34770'>自言幽燕客，<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_2_34770", 34770, id='poem_sentence_3_34770_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_4_34770'>避雠至海上，被役此边州。<div id='poem_sentence_4_34770_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_6_34770_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_7_34770'>何知七十战，白首<span class='link' onclick='ShowAllusionComment(961, "poem_sentence_7_34770")'>未封侯</span>。<div id='poem_sentence_7_34770_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_8_34770'></div><div id='poem_sentence_8_34770_comment'></div></div><div class='poemComment' id='poem_comment_34770'><a href='javascript: ShowPoemComment(34770)'>评注</a><span class='inlineComment4'>（点击查看或隐藏评注）</span></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=697&endYear=697')">697年7月</a>　在建安军幕。建安王武攸宜献食百舆，为武后祝寿。子昂为其撰献食表。作品：《为建安王献食表》<span class='inlineComment2'>（徐谱云表撰于七月庚午自幽州班师之前，未详何月。今按：武后生辰为正月二十三，其用周正，即十一月二十三。武攸宜七月于幽州进食献寿，除云路途月余，八月即可至，献寿已是过早，当不得再提前。之所以不待班师回京后再献，当为军旅外臣所献之物意义自不同，回朝后当不复再有献食百舆之便，故赶在班师之前献之。故定子昂此表作时为七月。）</span><div id='poem_1364461' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1364461' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1364461?labeling=true' target='_blank'>为建安王献食表</a><span class='authorDate'>（697年7月）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 唐初 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(20887, "唐初", "陈子昂", class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1364461'>臣谬藉葭莩。叨荣圭组。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1364461_comment'></div>元戎出塞。违凤扆而逾年。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1364461_comment'></div>班师入朝。拜鸾闱而有日。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1364461_comment'></div>策勋饮至。频承<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_3_1364461", 1364461, "Clauses/7/Comments/0")'>湛露</span>之恩。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1364461_comment'></div>献寿奉觞。未申<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_4_1364461", 1364461, "Clauses/9/Comments/0")'>行潦</span>之荐。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1364461_comment'></div>所以白茅微藉。愿享于钧台。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1364461_comment'></div><span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_6_1364461", 1364461, "Clauses/12/Comments/0")'>黄污</span>菲诚。思奉于瑶水。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1364461_comment'></div>谨辄献食一百舆。伏知金鸡瑞鼎。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1364461_comment'></div>盈上帝之珍羞。玉女<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_8_1364461", 1364461, "Clauses/17/Comments/0")'>行厨</span>。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1364461_comment'></div>尽群仙之品味。以兹菲薄。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1364461_comment'></div>有类蘋蘩。多惭在藻之欢。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1364461_comment'></div>窃有献芹之志。所愿皇慈俯纳。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1364461_comment'></div>丹慊获申。天子万年。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1364461_comment'></div>永庆南山之寿。微臣百拜。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1364461_comment'></div>长承北极之恩。无任诚恳之至。<div class='inline' ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=697&endYear=697')">697年7月24日</a>　在建安军幕。七月二十四日从武攸宜自幽州班师。<br /></div>

-----title
蓟县（渔阳）
-----detail
<div class='label1' id='f9acf9cb69f54d08bfdccb5e8b1ead3d_label'><a href='javascript: DetailSwitch("f9acf9cb69f54d08bfdccb5e8b1ead3d");'><span id='f9acf9cb69f54d08bfdccb5e8b1ead3d_link' class='switch'>—</span></a><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=697&endYear=697')">697年</a>，39岁</div><div id='f9acf9cb69f54d08bfdccb5e8b1ead3d' class='detail'><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=697&endYear=697')">697年3月</a>　在建安军幕。三月，次渔阳。前军与契丹战，大败，三军震恐，不敢进。子昂数谏武攸宜严立法制，且请分万人前驱破敌。不纳，且贬署军曹。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=697&endYear=697')">697年</a>　在建安军幕。三月，军次渔阳。前军王孝杰等于东硖石谷败亡。子昂为十余万阵亡将士作国殇文以痛之。作品：《国殇文》<span class='inlineComment2'>（按：三月子昂随武攸宜大军至渔阳，闻前军十数万将士殉亡。以子昂国士心性，未必等到有闲暇时方撰国殇文以痛之祭之。子昂作此文或在武攸宜震恐不敢进，子昂数谏而不纳之一、二天内，故定子昂作此文在渔阳。非退据幽州后。）</span><div id='poem_1364565' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1364565' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1364565?labeling=true' target='_blank'>国殇文</a><span class='authorDate'>（697年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 唐初 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(20887, "唐初", "陈子昂", "poem_title_1364565")'>陈子昂</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1364565_comment'></div><div class='titleComment' id='poem_preface_1364565'>丁酉岁三月庚辰。前将军尚书王孝杰败王师于榆关峡口。吾哀之。故有此作。</div><div id='poem_preface_1364565_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1364565'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1364565'>天未悔祸兮。炽此山戎。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1364565_comment'></div>虐老昏幼兮。人罹其穷。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1364565_comment'></div>帝用震怒兮。言剪其凶。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1364565_comment'></div>出金虎兮曜天锋。扫宇宙之甲。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1364565_comment'></div>驰燕蓟之冲。何士马之沸渭。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1364565_comment'></div>若云海之汹汹。荆吴少年。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1364565_comment'></div>韩魏劲卒。戈矛如林。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1364565_comment'></div>白羽若月。且欲蹈乌丸之垒。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1364565_comment'></div>刈赤山之旗。联青邱之缴。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1364565_comment'></div>封黄龙之尸。凶胡猖獗。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1364565_comment'></div>奸险是凭。蛇伏泥滓。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1364565_comment'></div>蚁斗邱陵。哀我将之<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_11_1364565", 1364565, "Clauses/23/Comments/0")'>仡勇</span>兮。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1364565_comment'></div>无算略以是膺。陷天井之死地。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1364565_comment'></div>属云骑以相腾。短兵既接。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1364565_comment'></div>长戟亦合。星流飙驰。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1364565_comment'></div>树离<span class='inlineComment2'>（一作杂）</span>山沓。智无所施其巧。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1364565_comment'></div>勇不能制其怯。顿金鼓之雄威。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_16_1364565_comment'></div>沦<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_17_1364565", 1364565, "Clauses/34/Comments/0")'>舆尸</span>之败业。呜呼哀哉。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_17_1364565_comment'></div>矢石既尽白日颓。主将已死士卒哀。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_18_1364565_comment'></div>徒手奋呼谁救哉。<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_19_1364565", 1364565, "Clauses/39/Comments/0")'>含愤</span>抗怒志未回。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_19_1364565_comment'></div>杀气凝兮苍云暮。虎豹慄兮殇魂惧。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_20_1364565_comment'></div>殇魂惧兮可柰何。恨非其死兮弃山阿。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_21_1364565_comment'></div>血流骨积殪荒楚。思归道远不得语。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_22_1364565_comment'></div>降不戮兮北不诛。殁不赏兮功不图。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_23_1364565_comment'></div>岂力士之未徇。诚师律之见孤。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_24_1364565_comment'></div>重曰。壮士虽死精魂用。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_25_1364565_comment'></div>凶丑尔雠不可纵。我闻强死能厉灾。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_26_1364565_comment'></div>古有结草抗杜回。苟前失之未远。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_27_1364565_comment'></div>傥<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_28_1364565", 1364565, "Clauses/56/Comments/0")'>冥雠</span>之在哉。呜呼魂兮念归来。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_28_1364565_comment'></div></div><div id='poem_sentence_29_1364565_comment'></div></div></div><br /></div>
-----end

宝鸡（陈仓）

ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=698&endYear=698')">698年</a>　归田途中，西至散关，赋诗答乔知之。作品：《西还至散关答乔补阙知之》<div id='poem_34735' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_34735' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a -----title
广汉（雒县）
-----detail
<div class='label1' id='88df8f3a7d464f2fbffe862cde7307f0_label'><a href='javascript: DetailSwitch("88df8f3a7d464f2fbffe862cde7307f0");'><span id='88df8f3a7d464f2fbffe862cde7307f0_link' class='switch'>—</span></a><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=699&endYear=699')">699年</a>，41岁</div><div id='88df8f3a7d464f2fbffe862cde7307f0' class='detail'><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=699&endYear=699')">699年</a>　归田侍养。采药歧岭，汉州雒县父老邀于途，请为县令张知古撰颂德碑。作品：《汉州雒县令张君吏人颂德碑》<span class='inlineComment2'>（按：文曰“我行千里，而得一贤”，又曰“子昂时因归宁，采药歧岭，父老乃载酒邀诸途，论府君之深仁，访生祠之故事，永我以典礼，博我以文章。”则子昂撰此碑之地，或为采药歧岭，入汉州，遇雒县父老，为其所请，亦为张县令高义所感，援笔而成。故系此文撰于汉州雒县界。）</span><div id='poem_1364548' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1364548' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1364548?labeling=true' target='_blank'>汉州雒县令张君吏人颂德碑</a><span class='authorDate'>（699年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 唐初 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(20887, "唐初", "陈子昂", "poem_title_1364548")'>陈子昂</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1364548_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1364548'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1364548'>至哉天子。在穆清之中。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1364548_comment'></div>端元默之化。万国日见。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1364548_comment'></div>百姓以亲。谁其昭宣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1364548_comment'></div>令长其任也。然则国有小大。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1364548_comment'></div>政有污隆。遭其和平。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1364548_comment'></div>则循理之功易。值其凋瘵。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1364548_comment'></div>则革弊之业难。况罹乎荐瘥。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1364548_comment'></div>救其涂炭。力倍于中。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1364548_comment'></div>而功不半之。利尽其仁。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1364548_comment'></div>而泽未全洽。则我府君当钦明之世。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1364548_comment'></div>承苛慝之烬。缉<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_10_1364548", 1364548, "Clauses/21/Comments/0")'>颓靡</span>之馀。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1364548_comment'></div>遂能抚宁矜残。淳耀<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_11_1364548", 1364548, "Clauses/23/Comments/0")'>敦懿</span>。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1364548_comment'></div>改制立宪。昭德显仁。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1364548_comment'></div>奇迹光乎曩贤。惠风穆于兹日。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1364548_comment'></div>我行千里。而得一贤。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1364548_comment'></div>传曰。夫用我者。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1364548_comment'></div>而岂徒哉。府君姓张氏。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_16_1364548_comment'></div>名知古。盖汉少傅留侯之裔也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_17_1364548_comment'></div>昔留侯得沧海力士。东报于秦。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_18_1364548_comment'></div>遇黄石老人。西归于汉。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_19_1364548_comment'></div>山河钟鼎。子孙保之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_20_1364548_comment'></div>代在关中。今为宜州人也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_21_1364548_comment'></div>高祖艺。周恒州司马。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_22_1364548_comment'></div>曾祖欢。隋许州司马。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_23_1364548_comment'></div>祖雄。唐并州榆次令。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_24_1364548_comment'></div>考琳。原州平原令。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_25_1364548_comment'></div>皆禀瑚琏之器。著经济之才。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_26_1364548_comment'></div>大位不跻。元德滋茂。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_27_1364548_comment'></div>其昭祉复袭于我府君。府君体英奇之姿。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_28_1364548_comment'></div>冲希默之量。齐敏内肃。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_29_1364548_comment'></div>端外融。夫其孝友睦姻。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_30_1364548_comment'></div>研几成务。深断守节之固。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_31_1364548_comment'></div>拨烦要之能。在于家邦。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_32_1364548_comment'></div>闻其政矣。起家补同州朝邑尉。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_33_1364548_comment'></div>历太州郑县尉左金吾卫仓曹参军洛州洛阳主簿。黄图左翊。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_34_1364548_comment'></div>豪侠所凑。赤墀佐理。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_35_1364548_comment'></div>实赖其能。又迁雍州明堂县丞。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_36_1364548_comment'></div>时皇帝恭默明台。清问下吏。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_37_1364548_comment'></div>西南矜寡有词上官曰。刺史沓贪而苛。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_38_1364548_comment'></div>县令威施而忍。奸宄因舋。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_39_1364548_comment'></div>群行敚𭤑。哀哉<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_40_1364548", 1364548, "Clauses/81/Comments/0")'>氓黎</span>。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_40_1364548_comment'></div>颠在荼毒。朝廷悯之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_41_1364548_comment'></div>帝曰俞。允哉。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_42_1364548_comment'></div>乃用敕抚此荒邑。噫嘻。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_43_1364548_comment'></div>昔者苛政未作。封境保安。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_44_1364548_comment'></div>兹都冲要。衿带全蜀。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_45_1364548_comment'></div>百濮兼错。万裔之泉。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_46_1364548_comment'></div>宝利珍货。尽四海矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_47_1364548_comment'></div>迨残猛聿至。蟊贼内讧。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_48_1364548_comment'></div>始于硕鼠之侵。终屠<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_49_1364548", 1364548, "Clauses/99/Comments/0")'>饿狼</span>之喙。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_49_1364548_comment'></div>杼轴既尽。郛邑殆空。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_50_1364548_comment'></div>悲夫仲尼云。苛政虐于猛虎。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_51_1364548_comment'></div>岂猛虎而已哉。我府君殷然始宣皇明。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_52_1364548_comment'></div>恭职事。巡省黄发。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_53_1364548_comment'></div>周爰令图。所以绥亡固存。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_54_1364548_comment'></div>蠲虐去暴。与百姓更始者。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_55_1364548_comment'></div>舆人斐然。乃作诵曰。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_56_1364548_comment'></div>我有圣帝抚令君。遭暴<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_57_1364548", 1364548, "Clauses/115/Comments/0")'>昏椓</span>茕寡纷。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_57_1364548_comment'></div>民户流散日月曛。君去来兮惠我仁。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_58_1364548_comment'></div>百姓苏矣见阳春。然不躬不亲。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_59_1364548_comment'></div>庶民不信。于是府君知人散久矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_60_1364548_comment'></div>黩于<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_61_1364548", 1364548, "Clauses/122/Comments/0")'>诈罔</span>。巳曰未遂。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_61_1364548_comment'></div>躬六曹之务。先<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_62_1364548", 1364548, "Clauses/125/Comments/0")'>五美</span>之训。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_62_1364548_comment'></div>下官敛手。<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_63_1364548", 1364548, "Clauses/127/Comments/0")'>牟食</span>革心。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_63_1364548_comment'></div>人始翕如也。初官户在版图者万有五千馀家。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_64_1364548_comment'></div>历政<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_65_1364548", 1364548, "Clauses/130/Comments/0")'>侵残</span>。逃者过半。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_65_1364548_comment'></div>岁月永久。庐井<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_66_1364548", 1364548, "Clauses/133/Comments/0")'>湮芜</span>。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_66_1364548_comment'></div>蟏蛸在堂。蟋蟀空叹。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_67_1364548_comment'></div>先是有敕。天下逃人归复旧业者。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_68_1364548_comment'></div>免当年租庸。公以柔远能迩。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_69_1364548_comment'></div>政之大端。乃下令曰。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_70_1364548_comment'></div>于戏。天子诚悯斯人。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_71_1364548_comment'></div>是用命我。其讫有济。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_72_1364548_comment'></div>若逋不及惠。幽不能明。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_73_1364548_comment'></div>吾之罪人。部内有逃越他境。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_74_1364548_comment'></div>能相率归者。免一岁租及征徭。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_75_1364548_comment'></div>若茕嫠贫窭不能自济者。当别议优之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_76_1364548_comment'></div>其长正耆老。可明喻此诚。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_77_1364548_comment'></div>使被幽谷。令既下。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_78_1364548_comment'></div>克己示信。或有逃者。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_79_1364548_comment'></div>引首而归。公亲循宁慰。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_80_1364548_comment'></div>赡理其业。于是小大悦赉。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_81_1364548_comment'></div>远近承风。四封诸通。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_82_1364548_comment'></div>一朝景附。夫负妻戴子。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_83_1364548_comment'></div>荷蓑提笠。首尾郊郭者。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_84_1364548_comment'></div>凡七千馀家。熙乎若鸿雁之得春也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_85_1364548_comment'></div>既至矣。则劳来之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_86_1364548_comment'></div>既止矣。则安辑之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_87_1364548_comment'></div>或三年。或十年。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_88_1364548_comment'></div>旧馆已无。乔木犹在。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_89_1364548_comment'></div>公缉屋涂室。薙陌开阡。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_90_1364548_comment'></div>为其并疆。人得其居矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_91_1364548_comment'></div>田畯失业。农野榛荒。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_92_1364548_comment'></div>此邦膏腴。利在江浸。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_93_1364548_comment'></div>有金雁白鱼二水。是其朝云。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_94_1364548_comment'></div>泽麓无虞。沟畛填塞。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_95_1364548_comment'></div>公浚其涂洫。川浍始通。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_96_1364548_comment'></div>人得就耕矣。流亡初复。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_97_1364548_comment'></div><span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_98_1364548", 1364548, "Clauses/196/Comments/0")'>贫鞠</span>兼半。<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_98_1364548", 1364548, "Clauses/197/Comments/0")'>食不糊口</span>。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_98_1364548_comment'></div>力未赡农。公又假富资贫。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_99_1364548_comment'></div>耦耕分种。助其铚刈。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_100_1364548_comment'></div>岁以有年。人得其食矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_101_1364548_comment'></div>曩者征税横敚。商旅不行。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_102_1364548_comment'></div>贸迁有无。廛肆半绝。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_103_1364548_comment'></div>公阜其货财。交易复通。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_104_1364548_comment'></div>日中<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_105_1364548", 1364548, "Clauses/210/Comments/0")'>噬嗑</span>。人得其利矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_105_1364548_comment'></div>乃种树畜牧。蚕渔工贾。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_106_1364548_comment'></div>什伯之器。车服之庸。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_107_1364548_comment'></div>婚姻之时。丧祭之礼。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_108_1364548_comment'></div>莫不尽为度数。制其权衡。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_109_1364548_comment'></div>征赋既均。千室如一。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_110_1364548_comment'></div>于是百姓允赖。鼓舞而歌。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_111_1364548_comment'></div>其歌诗凡六章。题曰逃还乐。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_112_1364548_comment'></div>其首章盖言天子之德也。其二章悯前政之虐也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_113_1364548_comment'></div>其三章喜公惠之至也。其四章言逃还之乐也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_114_1364548_comment'></div>其五章美公化行而奸慝不兴也。其六章善政令均平赋敛不淫也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_115_1364548_comment'></div>时日月会于龙狵。岁功成平。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_116_1364548_comment'></div>孟冬。百嘉备蒸。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_117_1364548_comment'></div>品物咸乂。府君乃稽版籍。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_118_1364548_comment'></div>考幽明。亲巡乎邦庐。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_119_1364548_comment'></div>存问乎鳏耄。黄耇稚齿。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_120_1364548_comment'></div>山原之民。乃接手赓歌。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_121_1364548_comment'></div>迎拥马首。累乎道路者以百千辈。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_122_1364548_comment'></div>昼肆酒。夜联烛。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_123_1364548_comment'></div>群舞蹈咏。迎途饯郊。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_124_1364548_comment'></div>皆歌前六章。庆公惠也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_125_1364548_comment'></div>是以封内欢康。境外萌动。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_126_1364548_comment'></div>企公德美。有若神明。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_127_1364548_comment'></div>府君尝因公事至成都。成都之民。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_128_1364548_comment'></div>驾肩相瞩。盖籍甚其异也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_129_1364548_comment'></div>封人有丧者庐于墓侧。鞠然在疚。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_130_1364548_comment'></div>负土成坟。公亲从寮吏。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_131_1364548_comment'></div>吊其苫席。自是礼让行焉。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_132_1364548_comment'></div>学校兴焉。长史河南窦公。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_133_1364548_comment'></div>旌别尚贤。廉居政。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_134_1364548_comment'></div>以公甄理颓弊。跻美中和。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_135_1364548_comment'></div>历政逋亡。一朝狎至。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_136_1364548_comment'></div>遂表其状。奏之于阙庭。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_137_1364548_comment'></div>属獯鬻孔亟。戎车未暇。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_138_1364548_comment'></div>郊垒既夷。邦宪清穆。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_139_1364548_comment'></div>刺史南阳张公。幨帏卧理。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_140_1364548_comment'></div>宽猛以济。儒术兼优。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_141_1364548_comment'></div>吏畏独坐。人歌来暮。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_142_1364548_comment'></div>甄综品鉴。物无遗才。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_143_1364548_comment'></div>又以公保邦乂民。胜残去杀。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_144_1364548_comment'></div>重理前秩。升闻宸扆。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_145_1364548_comment'></div>夫升闻者。岂循良而已哉。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_146_1364548_comment'></div>盖激清励贪。耸善惩恶。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_147_1364548_comment'></div>祈元嘉命。优公宠章。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_148_1364548_comment'></div>于是乡旄邦彦。华发杼首。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_149_1364548_comment'></div>或名淹玉垒。家擅铜山。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_150_1364548_comment'></div>如王宏马靖等若干人。皆以政洽仁显功著颂宣扬。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_151_1364548_comment'></div>金帛嘉止。不日而至。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_152_1364548_comment'></div>至则国肥矣。去则民瘠矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_153_1364548_comment'></div>况我邦族。其将畴依。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_154_1364548_comment'></div>兄弟睦亲。不可以从往也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_155_1364548_comment'></div>筐篚玉帛。不足以永贶也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_156_1364548_comment'></div>隔千里而不昧。与百姓而长存。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_157_1364548_comment'></div>非刻金石。列图象。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_158_1364548_comment'></div>扬宏懿。崇耿光。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_159_1364548_comment'></div>则喁然众情。孰克慰满。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_160_1364548_comment'></div>于是乃从旅凿巉岩。自金水之山。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_161_1364548_comment'></div>得玉玫之石。农夫田妇。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_162_1364548_comment'></div>担扛力运。皆惧公往。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_163_1364548_comment'></div>遗像莫瞻。共琢之磨之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_164_1364548_comment'></div>议之谋之。子昂时因归宁。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_165_1364548_comment'></div>采药岐领。父老乃载酒邀诸途。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_166_1364548_comment'></div>论府君之深仁。访生祠之故事。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_167_1364548_comment'></div>永我以典礼。博我以文章。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_168_1364548_comment'></div>夫千里一贤。义者所贵。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_169_1364548_comment'></div>今百城一理。公独有之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_170_1364548_comment'></div>不熙其烈光。以示当世。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_171_1364548_comment'></div>则孱弱者胡以激节。贪垢者曷以悛心。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_172_1364548_comment'></div>敢因此义。乃氓谣而作颂曰<span class='inlineComment2'>（颂缺）</span>。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_173_1364548_comment'></div></div><div id='poem_sentence_174_1364548_comment'></div></div></div><br /></div>
